<s> but if we say   of human origin   we are afraid of the people  for they all hold that john was a prophet  </s>
<s> so they answered jesus   we dont know   then he said   neither will i tell you by what authority i am doing these things </s>
<s>  what do you think  there was a man who had two sons  he went to the first and said   son  go and work today in the vineyard  </s>
<s>   i will not   he answered  but later he changed his mind and went </s>
<s>  then the father went to the other son and said the same thing  he answered   i will  sir   but he did not go </s>
<s>  which of the two did what his father wanted    the first   they answered  jesus said to them   truly i tell you  the tax collectors and the prostitutes are entering the kingdom of god ahead of you </s>
<s> for john came to you to show you the way of righteousness  and you did not believe him  but the tax collectors and the prostitutes did  and even after you saw this  you did not repent and believe him </s>
<s>  listen to another parable  there was a landowner who planted a vineyard  he put a wall round it  dug a winepress in it and built a watchtower  then he rented the vineyard to some farmers and moved to another place </s>
<s> when the harvest time approached  he sent his servants to the tenants to collect his fruit </s>
<s>  the tenants seized his servants  they beat one  killed another  and stoned a third </s>
<s> then he sent other servants to them  more than the first time  and the tenants treated them in the same way </s>
<s> last of all  he sent his son to them   they will respect my son   he said </s>
<s>  but when the tenants saw the son  they said to each other   this is the heir  come  lets kill him and take his inheritance  </s>
<s> so they took him and threw him out of the vineyard and killed him </s>
<s>  therefore  when the owner of the vineyard comes  what will he do to those tenants  </s>
<s>  he will bring those wretches to a wretched end   they replied   and he will rent the vineyard to other tenants  who will give him his share of the crop at harvest time  </s>
<s> jesus said to them   have you never read in the scriptures    the stone the builders rejected has become the cornerstone  the lord has done this  and it is marvellous in our eyes  </s>
<s>  therefore i tell you that the kingdom of god will be taken away from you and given to a people who will produce its fruit </s>
<s> anyone who falls on this stone will be broken to pieces  anyone on whom it falls will be crushed  </s>
<s> when the chief priests and the pharisees heard jesus parables  they knew he was talking about them </s>
<s> they looked for a way to arrest him  but they were afraid of the crowd because the people held that he was a prophet </s>
<s> jesus spoke to them again in parables  saying </s>
<s>  the kingdom of heaven is like a king who prepared a wedding banquet for his son </s>
<s> he sent his servants to those who had been invited to the banquet to tell them to come  but they refused to come </s>
<s>  then he sent some more servants and said   tell those who have been invited that i have prepared my dinner  my oxen and fattened cattle have been slaughtered  and everything is ready  come to the wedding banquet  </s>
<s>  but they paid no attention and went off  one to his field  another to his business </s>
<s> the rest seized his servants  illtreated them and killed them </s>
<s> the king was enraged  he sent his army and destroyed those murderers and burned their city </s>
<s>  then he said to his servants   the wedding banquet is ready  but those i invited did not deserve to come </s>
<s> so go to the street corners and invite to the banquet anyone you find  </s>
<s> so the servants went out into the streets and gathered all the people they could find  the bad as well as the good  and the wedding hall was filled with guests </s>
<s>  but when the king came in to see the guests  he noticed a man there who was not wearing wedding clothes </s>
<s> he asked   how did you get in here without wedding clothes  friend   the man was speechless </s>
<s>  then the king told the attendants   tie him hand and foot  and throw him outside  into the darkness  where there will be weeping and gnashing of teeth  </s>

<s> now there were seven brothers among us  the first one married and died  and since he had no children  he left his wife to his brother </s>
<s> the same thing happened to the second and third brother  right on down to the seventh </s>
<s> finally  the woman died </s>

<s> at the resurrection people will neither marry nor be given in marriage  they will be like the angels in heaven </s>

<s>  i am the god of abraham  the god of isaac  and the god of jacob   he is not the god of the dead but of the living  </s>

<s> and the second is like it   love your neighbour as yourself  </s>
<s> all the law and the prophets hang on these two commandments  </s>

<s>  i have sinned   he said   for i have betrayed innocent blood    what is that to us   they replied   thats your responsibility  </s>
<s> so judas threw the money into the temple and left  then he went away and hanged himself </s>
<s> the chief priests picked up the coins and said   it is against the law to put this into the treasury  since it is blood money  </s>
<s> so they decided to use the money to buy the potters field as a burial place for foreigners </s>
<s> that is why it has been called the field of blood to this day </s>
<s> then what was spoken by jeremiah the prophet was fulfilled   they took the thirty pieces of silver  the price set on him by the people of israel </s>
<s> and they used them to buy the potters field  as the lord commanded me  </s>
<s> meanwhile jesus stood before the governor  and the governor asked him   are you the king of the jews    you have said so   jesus replied </s>
<s> when he was accused by the chief priests and the elders  he gave no answer </s>
<s> then pilate asked him   dont you hear the testimony they are bringing against you  </s>
<s> but jesus made no reply  not even to a single charge  to the great amazement of the governor </s>
<s> now it was the governors custom at the festival to release a prisoner chosen by the crowd </s>
<s> at that time they had a wellknown prisoner whose name was jesus barabbas </s>
<s> so when the crowd had gathered  pilate asked them   which one do you want me to release to you  jesus barabbas  or jesus who is called the messiah  </s>
<s> for he knew it was out of selfinterest that they had handed jesus over to him </s>
<s> while pilate was sitting on the judges seat  his wife sent him this message   dont have anything to do with that innocent man  for i have suffered a great deal today in a dream because of him  </s>
<s> but the chief priests and the elders persuaded the crowd to ask for barabbas and to have jesus executed </s>
<s>  which of the two do you want me to release to you   asked the governor   barabbas   they answered </s>
<s>  what shall i do  then  with jesus who is called the messiah   pilate asked  they all answered   crucify him  </s>
<s>  why  what crime has he committed   asked pilate  but they shouted all the louder   crucify him  </s>
<s> when pilate saw that he was getting nowhere  but that instead an uproar was starting  he took water and washed his hands in front of the crowd   i am innocent of this mans blood   he said   it is your responsibility  </s>
<s> all the people answered   his blood is on us and on our children  </s>
<s> then he released barabbas to them  but he had jesus flogged  and handed him over to be crucified </s>
<s> then the governors soldiers took jesus into the praetorium and gathered the whole company of soldiers round him </s>
<s> they stripped him and put a scarlet robe on him </s>
<s> and then twisted together a crown of thorns and set it on his head  they put a staff in his right hand  then they knelt in front of him and mocked him   hail  king of the jews   they said </s>
<s> they spat on him  and took the staff and struck him on the head again and again </s>
<s> after they had mocked him  they took off the robe and put his own clothes on him  then they led him away to crucify him </s>
<s> as they were going out  they met a man from cyrene  named simon  and they forced him to carry the cross </s>
<s> they came to a place called golgotha  which means  the place of the skull  </s>
<s> there they offered jesus wine to drink  mixed with gall  but after tasting it  he refused to drink it </s>
<s> when they had crucified him  they divided up his clothes by casting lots </s>
<s> and sitting down  they kept watch over him there </s>
<s> above his head they placed the written charge against him  this is jesus  the king of the jews </s>
<s> two rebels were crucified with him  one on his right and one on his left </s>
<s> those who passed by hurled insults at him  shaking their heads</s>
<s> and saying   you who are going to destroy the temple and build it in three days  save yourself  come down from the cross  if you are the son of god  </s>
<s> in the same way the chief priests  the teachers of the law and the elders mocked him </s>
<s>  he saved others   they said   but he cant save himself  hes the king of israel  let him come down now from the cross  and we will believe in him </s>
<s> he trusts in god  let god rescue him now if he wants him  for he said   i am the son of god   </s>
<s> in the same way the rebels who were crucified with him also heaped insults on him </s>
<s> from noon until three in the afternoon darkness came over all the land </s>
<s> about three in the afternoon jesus cried out in a loud voice   eli  eli  lema sabachthani    which means  my god  my god  why have you forsaken me    </s>
<s> when some of those standing there heard this  they said   hes calling elijah  </s>
<s> immediately one of them ran and got a sponge  he filled it with wine vinegar  put it on a staff  and offered it to jesus to drink </s>
<s> the rest said   now leave him alone  lets see if elijah comes to save him  </s>
<s> and when jesus had cried out again in a loud voice  he gave up his spirit </s>
<s> at that moment the curtain of the temple was torn in two from top to bottom  the earth shook  the rocks split</s>
<s> and the tombs broke open  the bodies of many holy people who had died were raised to life </s>
<s> they came out of the tombs after jesus resurrection and went into the holy city and appeared to many people </s>
<s> when the centurion and those with him who were guarding jesus saw the earthquake and all that had happened  they were terrified  and exclaimed   surely he was the son of god  </s>
<s> many women were there  watching from a distance  they had followed jesus from galilee to care for his needs </s>
<s> among them were mary magdalene  mary the mother of james and joseph  and the mother of zebedees sons </s>
<s> as evening approached  there came a rich man from arimathea  named joseph  who had himself become a disciple of jesus </s>
<s> going to pilate  he asked for jesus body  and pilate ordered that it be given to him </s>
<s> joseph took the body  wrapped it in a clean linen cloth </s>
<s> and placed it in his own new tomb that he had cut out of the rock  he rolled a big stone in front of the entrance to the tomb and went away </s>
<s> mary magdalene and the other mary were sitting there opposite the tomb </s>
<s> the next day  the one after preparation day  the chief priests and the pharisees went to pilate </s>
<s>  sir   they said   we remember that while he was still alive that deceiver said   after three days i will rise again  </s>
<s> so give the order for the tomb to be made secure until the third day  otherwise  his disciples may come and steal the body and tell the people that he has been raised from the dead  this last deception will be worse than the first  </s>
<s>  take a guard   pilate answered   go  make the tomb as secure as you know how  </s>
<s> so they went and made the tomb secure by putting a seal on the stone and posting the guard </s>
<s> after the sabbath  at dawn on the first day of the week  mary magdalene and the other mary went to look at the tomb </s>
<s> there was a violent earthquake  for an angel of the lord came down from heaven and  going to the tomb  rolled back the stone and sat on it </s>
<s> his appearance was like lightning  and his clothes were white as snow </s>
<s> the guards were so afraid of him that they shook and became like dead men </s>
<s> the angel said to the women   do not be afraid  for i know that you are looking for jesus  who was crucified </s>
<s> he is not here  he has risen  just as he said  come and see the place where he lay </s>
<s> then go quickly and tell his disciples   he has risen from the dead and is going ahead of you into galilee  there you will see him   now i have told you  </s>
<s> so the women hurried away from the tomb  afraid yet filled with joy  and ran to tell his disciples </s>
<s> suddenly jesus met them   greetings   he said  they came to him  clasped his feet and worshipped him </s>
<s> then jesus said to them   do not be afraid  go and tell my brothers to go to galilee  there they will see me  </s>
<s> while the women were on their way  some of the guards went into the city and reported to the chief priests everything that had happened </s>
<s> when the chief priests had met with the elders and devised a plan  they gave the soldiers a large sum of money </s>
<s> telling them   you are to say   his disciples came during the night and stole him away while we were asleep  </s>
<s> if this report gets to the governor  we will satisfy him and keep you out of trouble  </s>
<s> so the soldiers took the money and did as they were instructed  and this story has been widely circulated among the jews to this very day </s>
<s> then the eleven disciples went to galilee  to the mountain where jesus had told them to go </s>
<s> when they saw him  they worshipped him  but some doubted </s>
<s> then jesus came to them and said   all authority in heaven and on earth has been given to me </s>
<s> therefore go and make disciples of all nations  baptising them in the name of the father and of the son and of the holy spirit </s>
<s> and teaching them to obey everything i have commanded you  and surely i am with you always  to the very end of the age  </s>
<s> the beginning of the good news about jesus the messiah  the son of god </s>
<s> as it is written in isaiah the prophet   i will send my messenger ahead of you  who will prepare your way </s>
<s>  a voice of one calling in the wilderness   prepare the way for the lord  make straight paths for him   </s>
<s> at that time jesus came from nazareth in galilee and was baptised by john in the jordan </s>
<s> just as jesus was coming up out of the water  he saw heaven being torn open and the spirit descending on him like a dove </s>
<s> and a voice came from heaven   you are my son  whom i love  with you i am well pleased  </s>
<s> at once the spirit sent him out into the wilderness </s>
<s> and he was in the wilderness for forty days  being tempted by satan  he was with the wild animals  and angels attended him </s>
<s> after john was put in prison  jesus went into galilee  proclaiming the good news of god </s>
<s>  the time has come   he said   the kingdom of god has come near  repent and believe the good news  </s>
<s> as jesus walked beside the sea of galilee  he saw simon and his brother andrew casting a net into the lake  for they were fishermen </s>
<s>  come  follow me   jesus said   and i will send you out to fish for people  </s>
<s> at once they left their nets and followed him </s>
<s> when he had gone a little farther  he saw james son of zebedee and his brother john in a boat  preparing their nets </s>
<s> without delay he called them  and they left their father zebedee in the boat with the hired men and followed him </s>
<s> they went to capernaum  and when the sabbath came  jesus went into the synagogue and began to teach </s>
<s> the people were amazed at his teaching  because he taught them as one who had authority  not as the teachers of the law </s>
<s> just then a man in their synagogue who was possessed by an impure spirit cried out </s>
<s>  what do you want with us  jesus of nazareth  have you come to destroy us  i know who you are  the holy one of god  </s>
<s>  be quiet   said jesus sternly   come out of him  </s>
<s> the impure spirit shook the man violently and came out of him with a shriek </s>
<s> the people were all so amazed that they asked each other   what is this  a new teaching  and with authority  he even gives orders to impure spirits and they obey him  </s>
<s> news about him spread quickly over the whole region of galilee </s>
<s> as soon as they left the synagogue  they went with james and john to the home of simon and andrew </s>
<s> simons motherinlaw was in bed with a fever  and they immediately told jesus about her </s>
<s> so he went to her  took her hand and helped her up  the fever left her and she began to wait on them </s>
<s> that evening after sunset the people brought to jesus all who were ill and demonpossessed </s>
<s> the whole town gathered at the door </s>
<s> and jesus healed many who had various diseases  he also drove out many demons  but he would not let the demons speak because they knew who he was </s>
<s> very early in the morning  while it was still dark  jesus got up  left the house and went off to a solitary place  where he prayed </s>
<s> simon and his companions went to look for him </s>
<s> and when they found him  they exclaimed   everyone is looking for you  </s>
<s> jesus replied   let us go somewhere else  to the nearby villages  so that i can preach there also  that is why i have come  </s>
<s> so he travelled throughout galilee  preaching in their synagogues and driving out demons </s>
<s> a man with leprosy came to him and begged him on his knees   if you are willing  you can make me clean  </s>
<s> jesus was indignant  he reached out his hand and touched the man   i am willing   he said   be clean  </s>
<s> immediately the leprosy left him and he was cleansed </s>
<s> jesus sent him away at once with a strong warning </s>
<s>  see that you dont tell this to anyone  but go  show yourself to the priest and offer the sacrifices that moses commanded for your cleansing  as a testimony to them  </s>
<s> instead he went out and began to talk freely  spreading the news  as a result  jesus could no longer enter a town openly but stayed outside in lonely places  yet the people still came to him from everywhere </s>
<s> a few days later  when jesus again entered capernaum  the people heard that he had come home </s>
<s> they gathered in such large numbers that there was no room left  not even outside the door  and he preached the word to them </s>
<s> some men came  bringing to him a paralysed man  carried by four of them </s>
<s> since they could not get him to jesus because of the crowd  they made an opening in the roof above jesus by digging through it and then lowered the mat the man was lying on </s>
<s> when jesus saw their faith  he said to the paralysed man   son  your sins are forgiven  </s>
<s> now some teachers of the law were sitting there  thinking to themselves </s>
<s>  why does this fellow talk like that  hes blaspheming  who can forgive sins but god alone  </s>
<s> immediately jesus knew in his spirit that this was what they were thinking in their hearts  and he said to them   why are you thinking these things </s>
<s> which is easier  to say to this paralysed man   your sins are forgiven   or to say   get up  take your mat and walk  </s>
<s> but i want you to know that the son of man has authority on earth to forgive sins   so he said to the man </s>
<s>  i tell you  get up  take your mat and go home  </s>
<s> he got up  took his mat and walked out in full view of them all  this amazed everyone and they praised god  saying   we have never seen anything like this  </s>
<s> once again jesus went out beside the lake  a large crowd came to him  and he began to teach them </s>
<s> as he walked along  he saw levi son of alphaeus sitting at the tax collectors booth   follow me   jesus told him  and levi got up and followed him </s>
<s> while jesus was having dinner at levis house  many tax collectors and sinners were eating with him and his disciples  for there were many who followed him </s>
<s> when the teachers of the law who were pharisees saw him eating with the sinners and tax collectors  they asked his disciples   why does he eat with tax collectors and sinners  </s>
<s> on hearing this  jesus said to them   it is not the healthy who need a doctor  but those who are ill  i have not come to call the righteous  but sinners  </s>
<s> now johns disciples and the pharisees were fasting  some people came and asked jesus   how is it that johns disciples and the disciples of the pharisees are fasting  but yours are not  </s>
<s> jesus answered   how can the guests of the bridegroom fast while he is with them  they cannot  so long as they have him with them </s>
<s> but the time will come when the bridegroom will be taken from them  and on that day they will fast </s>
<s>  no one sews a patch of unshrunk cloth on an old garment  otherwise  the new piece will pull away from the old  making the tear worse </s>
<s> and no one pours new wine into old wineskins  otherwise  the wine will burst the skins  and both the wine and the wineskins will be ruined  no  they pour new wine into new wineskins  </s>
<s> one sabbath jesus was going through the cornfields  and as his disciples walked along  they began to pick some ears of corn </s>
<s> the pharisees said to him   look  why are they doing what is unlawful on the sabbath  </s>
<s> he answered   have you never read what david did when he and his companions were hungry and in need </s>
<s> in the days of abiathar the high priest  he entered the house of god and ate the consecrated bread  which is lawful only for priests to eat  and he also gave some to his companions  </s>
<s> then he said to them   the sabbath was made for man  not man for the sabbath </s>
<s> so the son of man is lord even of the sabbath  </s>
<s> another time jesus went into the synagogue  and a man with a shrivelled hand was there </s>
<s> some of them were looking for a reason to accuse jesus  so they watched him closely to see if he would heal him on the sabbath </s>
<s> jesus said to the man with the shrivelled hand   stand up in front of everyone  </s>
<s> then jesus asked them   which is lawful on the sabbath  to do good or to do evil  to save life or to kill   but they remained silent </s>
<s> he looked around at them in anger and  deeply distressed at their stubborn hearts  said to the man   stretch out your hand   he stretched it out  and his hand was completely restored </s>
<s> then the pharisees went out and began to plot with the herodians how they might kill jesus </s>
<s> jesus withdrew with his disciples to the lake  and a large crowd from galilee followed </s>
<s> when they heard all he was doing  many people came to him from judea  jerusalem  idumea  and the regions across the jordan and around tyre and sidon </s>
<s> because of the crowd he told his disciples to have a small boat ready for him  to keep the people from crowding him </s>
<s> for he had healed many  so that those with diseases were pushing forward to touch him </s>
<s> whenever the impure spirits saw him  they fell down before him and cried out   you are the son of god  </s>
<s> but he gave them strict orders not to tell others about him </s>
<s> jesus went up on a mountainside and called to him those he wanted  and they came to him </s>
<s> he appointed twelve that they might be with him and that he might send them out to preach</s>
<s> and to have authority to drive out demons </s>
<s> these are the twelve he appointed  simon  to whom he gave the name peter  </s>
<s> james son of zebedee and his brother john  to them he gave the name boanerges  which means  sons of thunder  </s>
<s> andrew  philip  bartholomew  matthew  thomas  james son of alphaeus  thaddaeus  simon the zealot</s>
<s> and judas iscariot  who betrayed him </s>
<s> then jesus entered a house  and again a crowd gathered  so that he and his disciples were not even able to eat </s>
<s> when his family heard about this  they went to take charge of him  for they said   he is out of his mind  </s>
<s> and the teachers of the law who came down from jerusalem said   he is possessed by beelzebul  by the prince of demons he is driving out demons  </s>
<s> so jesus called them over to him and began to speak to them in parables   how can satan drive out satan </s>
<s> if a kingdom is divided against itself  that kingdom cannot stand </s>
<s> if a house is divided against itself  that house cannot stand </s>
<s> and if satan opposes himself and is divided  he cannot stand  his end has come </s>
<s> in fact  no one can enter a strong mans house without first tying him up  then he can plunder the strong mans house </s>
<s> truly i tell you  people can be forgiven all their sins and every slander they utter </s>
<s> but whoever blasphemes against the holy spirit will never be forgiven  they are guilty of an eternal sin  </s>
<s> he said this because they were saying   he has an impure spirit  </s>
<s> then jesus mother and brothers arrived  standing outside  they sent someone in to call him </s>
<s> a crowd was sitting round him  and they told him   your mother and brothers are outside looking for you  </s>
<s>  who are my mother and my brothers   he asked </s>
<s> then he looked at those seated in a circle round him and said   here are my mother and my brothers </s>
<s> whoever does gods will is my brother and sister and mother  </s>
<s> again jesus began to teach by the lake  the crowd that gathered round him was so large that he got into a boat and sat in it out on the lake  while all the people were along the shore at the waters edge </s>
<s> he taught them many things by parables  and in his teaching said </s>
<s>  listen  a farmer went out to sow his seed </s>
<s> as he was scattering the seed  some fell along the path  and the birds came and ate it up </s>
<s> some fell on rocky places  where it did not have much soil  it sprang up quickly  because the soil was shallow </s>
<s> but when the sun came up  the plants were scorched  and they withered because they had no root </s>
<s> other seed fell among thorns  which grew up and choked the plants  so that they did not bear grain </s>
<s> still other seed fell on good soil  it came up  grew and produced a crop  some multiplying thirty  some sixty  some a hundred times  </s>
<s> then jesus said   whoever has ears to hear  let them hear  </s>
<s> when he was alone  the twelve and the others around him asked him about the parables </s>
<s> he told them   the secret of the kingdom of god has been given to you  but to those on the outside everything is said in parables</s>
<s> so that    they may be ever seeing but never perceiving  and ever hearing but never understanding  otherwise they might turn and be forgiven   </s>
<s> then jesus said to them   dont you understand this parable  how then will you understand any parable </s>
<s> the farmer sows the word </s>
<s> some people are like seed along the path  where the word is sown  as soon as they hear it  satan comes and takes away the word that was sown in them </s>
<s> others  like seed sown on rocky places  hear the word and at once receive it with joy </s>
<s> but since they have no root  they last only a short time  when trouble or persecution comes because of the word  they quickly fall away </s>
<s> still others  like seed sown among thorns  hear the word </s>
<s> but the worries of this life  the deceitfulness of wealth and the desires for other things come in and choke the word  making it unfruitful </s>
<s> others  like seed sown on good soil  hear the word  accept it  and produce a crop  some thirty  some sixty  some a hundred times what was sown  </s>
<s> he said to them   do you bring in a lamp to put it under a bowl or a bed  instead  dont you put it on its stand </s>
<s> for whatever is hidden is meant to be disclosed  and whatever is concealed is meant to be brought out into the open </s>
<s> if anyone has ears to hear  let them hear  </s>
<s>  consider carefully what you hear   he continued   with the measure you use  it will be measured to you  and even more </s>
<s> whoever has will be given more  whoever does not have  even what they have will be taken from them  </s>
<s> he also said   this is what the kingdom of god is like  a man scatters seed on the ground </s>
<s> night and day  whether he sleeps or gets up  the seed sprouts and grows  though he does not know how </s>
<s> all by itself the soil produces corn  first the stalk  then the ear  then the full grain in the ear </s>
<s> as soon as the corn is ripe  he puts the sickle to it  because the harvest has come  </s>
<s> again he said   what shall we say the kingdom of god is like  or what parable shall we use to describe it </s>
<s> it is like a mustard seed  which is the smallest of all seeds on earth </s>
<s> yet when planted  it grows and becomes the largest of all garden plants  with such big branches that the birds can perch in its shade  </s>
<s> with many similar parables jesus spoke the word to them  as much as they could understand </s>
<s> he did not say anything to them without using a parable  but when he was alone with his own disciples  he explained everything </s>
<s> that day when evening came  he said to his disciples   let us go over to the other side  </s>
<s> leaving the crowd behind  they took him along  just as he was  in the boat  there were also other boats with him </s>
<s> a furious squall came up  and the waves broke over the boat  so that it was nearly swamped </s>
<s> jesus was in the stern  sleeping on a cushion  the disciples woke him and said to him   teacher  dont you care if we drown  </s>
<s> he got up  rebuked the wind and said to the waves   quiet  be still   then the wind died down and it was completely calm </s>
<s> he said to his disciples   why are you so afraid  do you still have no faith  </s>
<s> they were terrified and asked each other   who is this  even the wind and the waves obey him  </s>
<s> they went across the lake to the region of the gerasenes </s>
<s> when jesus got out of the boat  a man with an impure spirit came from the tombs to meet him </s>
<s> this man lived in the tombs  and no one could bind him anymore  not even with a chain </s>
<s> for he had often been chained hand and foot  but he tore the chains apart and broke the irons on his feet  no one was strong enough to subdue him </s>
<s> night and day among the tombs and in the hills he would cry out and cut himself with stones </s>
<s> when he saw jesus from a distance  he ran and fell on his knees in front of him </s>
<s> he shouted at the top of his voice   what do you want with me  jesus  son of the most high god  in gods name dont torture me  </s>
<s> for jesus had said to him   come out of this man  you impure spirit  </s>
<s> then jesus asked him   what is your name    my name is legion   he replied   for we are many  </s>
<s> and he begged jesus again and again not to send them out of the area </s>
<s> a large herd of pigs was feeding on the nearby hillside </s>
<s> the demons begged jesus   send us among the pigs  allow us to go into them  </s>
<s> he gave them permission  and the impure spirits came out and went into the pigs  the herd  about two thousand in number  rushed down the steep bank into the lake and were drowned </s>
<s> those tending the pigs ran off and reported this in the town and countryside  and the people went out to see what had happened </s>
<s> when they came to jesus  they saw the man who had been possessed by the legion of demons  sitting there  dressed and in his right mind  and they were afraid </s>
<s> those who had seen it told the people what had happened to the demonpossessed man  and told about the pigs as well </s>
<s> then the people began to plead with jesus to leave their region </s>
<s> as jesus was getting into the boat  the man who had been demonpossessed begged to go with him </s>
<s> jesus did not let him  but said   go home to your own people and tell them how much the lord has done for you  and how he has had mercy on you  </s>
<s> so the man went away and began to tell in the decapolis how much jesus had done for him  and all the people were amazed </s>
<s> when jesus had again crossed over by boat to the other side of the lake  a large crowd gathered round him while he was by the lake </s>
<s> then one of the synagogue leaders  named jairus  came  and when he saw jesus  he fell at his feet </s>
<s> he pleaded earnestly with him   my little daughter is dying  please come and put your hands on her so that she will be healed and live  </s>
<s> so jesus went with him  a large crowd followed and pressed round him </s>
<s> and a woman was there who had been subject to bleeding for twelve years </s>

<s> when she heard about jesus  she came up behind him in the crowd and touched his cloak </s>
<s> because she thought   if i just touch his clothes  i will be healed  </s>
<s> immediately her bleeding stopped and she felt in her body that she was freed from her suffering </s>
<s> at once jesus realised that power had gone out from him  he turned round in the crowd and asked   who touched my clothes  </s>
<s>  you see the people crowding against you   his disciples answered   and yet you can ask   who touched me   </s>
<s> but jesus kept looking around to see who had done it </s>
<s> then the woman  knowing what had happened to her  came and fell at his feet and  trembling with fear  told him the whole truth </s>

<s> others said   he is elijah   and still others claimed   he is a prophet  like one of the prophets of long ago  </s>

<s> and saw some of his disciples eating food with hands that were defiled  that is  unwashed </s>
<s>  the pharisees and all the jews do not eat unless they give their hands a ceremonial washing  holding to the tradition of the elders </s>
<s> when they come from the marketplace they do not eat unless they wash  and they observe many other traditions  such as the washing of cups  pitchers and kettles  </s>
<s> so the pharisees and teachers of the law asked jesus   why dont your disciples live according to the tradition of the elders instead of eating their food with defiled hands  </s>

<s> and he continued   you have a fine way of setting aside the commands of god in order to observe your own traditions </s>
<s> for moses said   honour your father and mother   and   anyone who curses their father or mother is to be put to death  </s>
<s> but you say that if anyone declares that what might have been used to help their father or mother is corban  that is  devoted to god  </s>
<s> then you no longer let them do anything for their father or mother </s>
<s> thus you nullify the word of god by your tradition that you have handed down  and you do many things like that  </s>
<s> again jesus called the crowd to him and said   listen to me  everyone  and understand this </s>
<s> nothing outside a person can defile them by going into them  rather  it is what comes out of a person that defiles them   </s>
<s> </s>
<s> after he had left the crowd and entered the house  his disciples asked him about this parable </s>
<s>  are you so dull   he asked   dont you see that nothing that enters a person from the outside can defile them </s>
<s> for it doesnt go into their heart but into their stomach  and then out of the body    in saying this  jesus declared all foods clean  </s>
<s> he went on   what comes out of a person is what defiles them </s>

<s> then they came to jericho  as jesus and his disciples  together with a large crowd  were leaving the city  a blind man  bartimaeus  which means  son of timaeus   was sitting by the roadside begging </s>
<s> when he heard that it was jesus of nazareth  he began to shout   jesus  son of david  have mercy on me  </s>
<s> many rebuked him and told him to be quiet  but he shouted all the more   son of david  have mercy on me  </s>
<s> jesus stopped and said   call him   so they called to the blind man   cheer up  on your feet  hes calling you  </s>
<s> throwing his cloak aside  he jumped to his feet and came to jesus </s>
<s>  what do you want me to do for you   jesus asked him  the blind man said   rabbi  i want to see  </s>
<s>  go   said jesus   your faith has healed you   immediately he received his sight and followed jesus along the road </s>
<s> as they approached jerusalem and came to bethphage and bethany at the mount of olives  jesus sent two of his disciples </s>
<s> saying to them   go to the village ahead of you  and just as you enter it  you will find a colt tied there  which no one has ever ridden  untie it and bring it here </s>
<s> if anyone asks you   why are you doing this   say   the lord needs it and will send it back here shortly   </s>
<s> they went and found a colt outside in the street  tied at a doorway  as they untied it </s>
<s> some people standing there asked   what are you doing  untying that colt  </s>
<s> they answered as jesus had told them to  and the people let them go </s>
<s> when they brought the colt to jesus and threw their cloaks over it  he sat on it </s>
<s> many people spread their cloaks on the road  while others spread branches they had cut in the fields </s>
<s> those who went ahead and those who followed shouted   hosanna    blessed is he who comes in the name of the lord  </s>
<s>  blessed is the coming kingdom of our father david    hosanna in the highest heaven  </s>
<s> jesus entered jerusalem and went into the temple courts  he looked around at everything  but since it was already late  he went out to bethany with the twelve </s>
<s> the next day as they were leaving bethany  jesus was hungry </s>
<s> seeing in the distance a figtree in leaf  he went to find out if it had any fruit  when he reached it  he found nothing but leaves  because it was not the season for figs </s>
<s> then he said to the tree   may no one ever eat fruit from you again   and his disciples heard him say it </s>
<s> on reaching jerusalem  jesus entered the temple courts and began driving out those who were buying and selling there  he overturned the tables of the moneychangers and the benches of those selling doves </s>
<s> and would not allow anyone to carry merchandise through the temple courts </s>
<s> and as he taught them  he said   is it not written   my house will be called a house of prayer for all nations   but you have made it  a den of robbers   </s>
<s> the chief priests and the teachers of the law heard this and began looking for a way to kill him  for they feared him  because the whole crowd was amazed at his teaching </s>
<s> when evening came  jesus and his disciples went out of the city </s>
<s> in the morning  as they went along  they saw the figtree withered from the roots </s>
<s> peter remembered and said to jesus   rabbi  look  the figtree you cursed has withered  </s>
<s>  have faith in god   jesus answered </s>
<s>  truly i tell you  if anyone says to this mountain   go  throw yourself into the sea   and does not doubt in their heart but believes that what they say will happen  it will be done for them </s>
<s> therefore i tell you  whatever you ask for in prayer  believe that you have received it  and it will be yours </s>
<s> and when you stand praying  if you hold anything against anyone  forgive them  so that your father in heaven may forgive you your sins   </s>
<s> </s>
<s> they arrived again in jerusalem  and while jesus was walking in the temple courts  the chief priests  the teachers of the law and the elders came to him </s>
<s>  by what authority are you doing these things   they asked   and who gave you authority to do this  </s>
<s> jesus replied   i will ask you one question  answer me  and i will tell you by what authority i am doing these things </s>
<s> johns baptism  was it from heaven  or of human origin  tell me  </s>
<s> they discussed it among themselves and said   if we say   from heaven   he will ask   then why didnt you believe him  </s>
<s> but if we say   of human origin     they feared the people  for everyone held that john really was a prophet  </s>
<s> so they answered jesus   we dont know   jesus said   neither will i tell you by what authority i am doing these things  </s>
<s> jesus then began to speak to them in parables   a man planted a vineyard  he put a wall round it  dug a pit for the winepress and built a watchtower  then he rented the vineyard to some farmers and moved to another place </s>
<s> at harvest time he sent a servant to the tenants to collect from them some of the fruit of the vineyard </s>
<s> but they seized him  beat him and sent him away emptyhanded </s>
<s> then he sent another servant to them  they struck this man on the head and treated him shamefully </s>
<s> he sent still another  and that one they killed  he sent many others  some of them they beat  others they killed </s>
<s>  he had one left to send  a son  whom he loved  he sent him last of all  saying   they will respect my son  </s>
<s>  but the tenants said to one another   this is the heir  come  lets kill him  and the inheritance will be ours  </s>
<s> so they took him and killed him  and threw him out of the vineyard </s>
<s>  what then will the owner of the vineyard do  he will come and kill those tenants and give the vineyard to others </s>
<s> havent you read this passage of scripture    the stone the builders rejected has become the cornerstone </s>
<s> the lord has done this  and it is marvellous in our eyes   </s>
<s> then the chief priests  the teachers of the law and the elders looked for a way to arrest him because they knew he had spoken the parable against them  but they were afraid of the crowd  so they left him and went away </s>
<s> later they sent some of the pharisees and herodians to jesus to catch him in his words </s>
<s> they came to him and said   teacher  we know that you are a man of integrity  you arent swayed by others  because you pay no attention to who they are  but you teach the way of god in accordance with the truth  is it right to pay the polltax to caesar or not </s>
<s> should we pay or shouldnt we   but jesus knew their hypocrisy   why are you trying to trap me   he asked   bring me a denarius and let me look at it  </s>
<s> they brought the coin  and he asked them   whose image is this  and whose inscription    caesars   they replied </s>
<s> then jesus said to them   give back to caesar what is caesars and to god what is gods   and they were amazed at him </s>
<s> then the sadducees  who say there is no resurrection  came to him with a question </s>
<s>  teacher   they said   moses wrote for us that if a mans brother dies and leaves a wife but no children  the man must marry the widow and raise up offspring for his brother </s>
<s> now there were seven brothers  the first one married and died without leaving any children </s>
<s> the second one married the widow  but he also died  leaving no child  it was the same with the third </s>
<s> in fact  none of the seven left any children  last of all  the woman died too </s>
<s> at the resurrection whose wife will she be  since the seven were married to her  </s>
<s> jesus replied   are you not in error because you do not know the scriptures or the power of god </s>
<s> when the dead rise  they will neither marry nor be given in marriage  they will be like the angels in heaven </s>
<s> now about the dead rising  have you not read in the book of moses  in the account of the burning bush  how god said to him   i am the god of abraham  the god of isaac  and the god of jacob  </s>
<s> he is not the god of the dead  but of the living  you are badly mistaken  </s>
<s> one of the teachers of the law came and heard them debating  noticing that jesus had given them a good answer  he asked him   of all the commandments  which is the most important  </s>
<s>  the most important one   answered jesus   is this   hear  o israel  the lord our god  the lord is one </s>
<s> love the lord your god with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind and with all your strength  </s>
<s> the second is this   love your neighbour as yourself   there is no commandment greater than these  </s>
<s>  well said  teacher   the man replied   you are right in saying that god is one and there is no other but him </s>
<s> to love him with all your heart  with all your understanding and with all your strength  and to love your neighbour as yourself is more important than all burnt offerings and sacrifices  </s>
<s> when jesus saw that he had answered wisely  he said to him   you are not far from the kingdom of god   and from then on no one dared ask him any more questions </s>
<s> while jesus was teaching in the temple courts  he asked   why do the teachers of the law say that the messiah is the son of david </s>
<s> david himself  speaking by the holy spirit  declared    the lord said to my lord   sit at my right hand until i put your enemies under your feet    the large crowd listened to him with delight </s>
<s> as he taught  jesus said   watch out for the teachers of the law  they like to walk around in flowing robes and be greeted with respect in the marketplaces </s>
<s> and have the most important seats in the synagogues and the places of honour at banquets </s>
<s> they devour widows houses and for a show make lengthy prayers  these men will be punished most severely  </s>
<s> jesus sat down opposite the place where the offerings were put and watched the crowd putting their money into the temple treasury  many rich people threw in large amounts </s>
<s> but a poor widow came and put in two very small copper coins  worth only a few pence </s>
<s> calling his disciples to him  jesus said   truly i tell you  this poor widow has put more into the treasury than all the others </s>
<s> they all gave out of their wealth  but she  out of her poverty  put in everything  all she had to live on  </s>
<s> as jesus was leaving the temple  one of his disciples said to him   look  teacher  what massive stones  what magnificent buildings  </s>
<s>  do you see all these great buildings   replied jesus   not one stone here will be left on another  every one will be thrown down  </s>
<s> as jesus was sitting on the mount of olives opposite the temple  peter  james  john and andrew asked him privately </s>
<s>  tell us  when will these things happen  and what will be the sign that they are all about to be fulfilled  </s>
<s> jesus said to them   watch out that no one deceives you </s>
<s> many will come in my name  claiming   i am he   and will deceive many </s>
<s> when you hear of wars and rumours of wars  do not be alarmed  such things must happen  but the end is still to come </s>
<s> nation will rise against nation  and kingdom against kingdom  there will be earthquakes in various places  and famines  these are the beginning of birthpains </s>
<s>  you must be on your guard  you will be handed over to the local councils and flogged in the synagogues  on account of me you will stand before governors and kings as witnesses to them </s>
<s> and the gospel must first be preached to all nations </s>
<s> whenever you are arrested and brought to trial  do not worry beforehand about what to say  just say whatever is given you at the time  for it is not you speaking  but the holy spirit </s>
<s>  brother will betray brother to death  and a father his child  children will rebel against their parents and have them put to death </s>
<s> everyone will hate you because of me  but the one who stands firm to the end will be saved </s>
<s>  when you see  the abomination that causes desolation  standing where it does not belong  let the reader understand  then let those who are in judea flee to the mountains </s>
<s> let no one on the housetop go down or enter the house to take anything out </s>
<s> let no one in the field go back to get their cloak </s>
<s> how dreadful it will be in those days for pregnant women and nursing mothers </s>
<s> pray that this will not take place in winter </s>
<s> because those will be days of distress unequalled from the beginning  when god created the world  until now  and never to be equalled again </s>
<s>  if the lord had not cut short those days  no one would survive  but for the sake of the elect  whom he has chosen  he has shortened them </s>
<s> at that time if anyone says to you   look  here is the messiah   or   look  there he is   do not believe it </s>
<s> for false messiahs and false prophets will appear and perform signs and wonders to deceive  if possible  even the elect </s>
<s> so be on your guard  i have told you everything in advance </s>
<s>  but in those days  following that distress    the sun will be darkened  and the moon will not give its light </s>
<s> the stars will fall from the sky  and the heavenly bodies will be shaken  </s>
<s>  at that time people will see the son of man coming in clouds with great power and glory </s>
<s> and he will send his angels and gather his elect from the four winds  from the ends of the earth to the ends of the heavens </s>
<s>  now learn this lesson from the figtree  as soon as its twigs get tender and its leaves come out  you know that summer is near </s>
<s> even so  when you see these things happening  you know that it is near  right at the door </s>
<s> truly i tell you  this generation will certainly not pass away until all these things have happened </s>
<s> heaven and earth will pass away  but my words will never pass away </s>
<s>  but about that day or hour no one knows  not even the angels in heaven  nor the son  but only the father </s>
<s> be on guard  be alert  you do not know when that time will come </s>
<s> its like a man going away  he leaves his house and puts his servants in charge  each with their assigned task  and tells the one at the door to keep watch </s>
<s>  therefore keep watch because you do not know when the owner of the house will come back  whether in the evening  or at midnight  or when the cock crows  or at dawn </s>
<s> if he comes suddenly  do not let him find you sleeping </s>
<s> what i say to you  i say to everyone   watch   </s>
<s> now the passover and the festival of unleavened bread were only two days away  and the chief priests and the teachers of the law were scheming to arrest jesus secretly and kill him </s>
<s>  but not during the festival   they said   or the people may riot  </s>
<s> while he was in bethany  reclining at the table in the home of simon the leper  a woman came with an alabaster jar of very expensive perfume  made of pure nard  she broke the jar and poured the perfume on his head </s>
<s> some of those present were saying indignantly to one another   why this waste of perfume </s>
<s> it could have been sold for more than a years wages and the money given to the poor   and they rebuked her harshly </s>
<s>  leave her alone   said jesus   why are you bothering her  she has done a beautiful thing to me </s>
<s> the poor you will always have with you  and you can help them any time you want  but you will not always have me </s>
<s> she did what she could  she poured perfume on my body beforehand to prepare for my burial </s>
<s> truly i tell you  wherever the gospel is preached throughout the world  what she has done will also be told  in memory of her  </s>

<s> then he returned to his disciples and found them sleeping   simon   he said to peter   are you asleep  couldnt you keep watch for one hour </s>

<s> when he came back  he again found them sleeping  because their eyes were heavy  they did not know what to say to him </s>

<s> he fled naked  leaving his garment behind </s>

<s> but jesus still made no reply  and pilate was amazed </s>

<s> knowing it was out of selfinterest that the chief priests had handed jesus over to him </s>

<s> they crucified two rebels with him  one on his right and one on his left  </s>
<s> </s>

<s> joseph of arimathea  a prominent member of the council  who was himself waiting for the kingdom of god  went boldly to pilate and asked for jesus body </s>

<s> but when they looked up  they saw that the stone  which was very large  had been rolled away </s>
<s> as they entered the tomb  they saw a young man dressed in a white robe sitting on the right side  and they were alarmed </s>
<s>  dont be alarmed   he said   you are looking for jesus the nazarene  who was crucified  he has risen  he is not here  see the place where they laid him </s>
<s> but go  tell his disciples and peter   he is going ahead of you into galilee  there you will see him  just as he told you   </s>
<s> trembling and bewildered  the women went out and fled from the tomb  they said nothing to anyone  because they were afraid </s>
<s> when jesus rose early on the first day of the week  he appeared first to mary magdalene  out of whom he had driven seven demons </s>
<s> she went and told those who had been with him and who were mourning and weeping </s>
<s> when they heard that jesus was alive and that she had seen him  they did not believe it </s>
<s> afterwards jesus appeared in a different form to two of them while they were walking in the country </s>
<s> these returned and reported it to the rest  but they did not believe them either </s>
<s> later jesus appeared to the eleven as they were eating  he rebuked them for their lack of faith and their stubborn refusal to believe those who had seen him after he had risen </s>
<s> he said to them   go into all the world and preach the gospel to all creation </s>
<s> whoever believes and is baptised will be saved  but whoever does not believe will be condemned </s>
<s> and these signs will accompany those who believe  in my name they will drive out demons  they will speak in new tongues </s>
<s> they will pick up snakes with their hands  and when they drink deadly poison  it will not hurt them at all  they will place their hands on people who are ill  and they will get well  </s>
<s> after the lord jesus had spoken to them  he was taken up into heaven and he sat at the right hand of god </s>
<s> then the disciples went out and preached everywhere  and the lord worked with them and confirmed his word by the signs that accompanied it </s>
<s> many have undertaken to draw up an account of the things that have been fulfilled among us </s>
<s> just as they were handed down to us by those who from the first were eye witnesses and servants of the word </s>
<s> with this in mind  since i myself have carefully investigated everything from the beginning  i too decided to write an orderly account for you  most excellent theophilus </s>
<s> so that you may know the certainty of the things you have been taught </s>
<s> in the time of herod king of judea there was a priest named zechariah  who belonged to the priestly division of abijah  his wife elizabeth was also a descendant of aaron </s>
<s> both of them were righteous in the sight of god  observing all the lords commands and decrees blamelessly </s>
<s> but they were childless because elizabeth was not able to conceive  and they were both very old </s>
<s> once when zechariahs division was on duty and he was serving as priest before god </s>
<s> he was chosen by lot  according to the custom of the priesthood  to go into the temple of the lord and burn incense </s>
<s> and when the time for the burning of incense came  all the assembled worshippers were praying outside </s>
<s> then an angel of the lord appeared to him  standing at the right side of the altar of incense </s>
<s> when zechariah saw him  he was startled and was gripped with fear </s>
<s> but the angel said to him   do not be afraid  zechariah  your prayer has been heard  your wife elizabeth will bear you a son  and you are to call him john </s>
<s> he will be a joy and delight to you  and many will rejoice because of his birth </s>
<s> for he will be great in the sight of the lord  he is never to take wine or other fermented drink  and he will be filled with the holy spirit even before he is born </s>
<s> he will bring back many of the people of israel to the lord their god </s>
<s> and he will go on before the lord  in the spirit and power of elijah  to turn the hearts of the parents to their children and the disobedient to the wisdom of the righteous  to make ready a people prepared for the lord  </s>
<s> zechariah asked the angel   how can i be sure of this  i am an old man and my wife is well on in years  </s>
<s> the angel said to him   i am gabriel  i stand in the presence of god  and i have been sent to speak to you and to tell you this good news </s>
<s> and now you will be silent and not able to speak until the day this happens  because you did not believe my words  which will come true at their appointed time  </s>
<s> meanwhile  the people were waiting for zechariah and wondering why he stayed so long in the temple </s>
<s> when he came out  he could not speak to them  they realised he had seen a vision in the temple  for he kept making signs to them but remained unable to speak </s>
<s> when his time of service was completed  he returned home </s>
<s> after this his wife elizabeth became pregnant and for five months remained in seclusion </s>
<s>  the lord has done this for me   she said   in these days he has shown his favour and taken away my disgrace among the people  </s>
<s> in the sixth month of elizabeths pregnancy  god sent the angel gabriel to nazareth  a town in galilee </s>
<s> to a virgin pledged to be married to a man named joseph  a descendant of david  the virgins name was mary </s>
<s> the angel went to her and said   greetings  you who are highly favoured  the lord is with you  </s>
<s> mary was greatly troubled at his words and wondered what kind of greeting this might be </s>
<s> but the angel said to her   do not be afraid  mary  you have found favour with god </s>
<s> you will conceive and give birth to a son  and you are to call him jesus </s>
<s> he will be great and will be called the son of the most high  the lord god will give him the throne of his father david </s>
<s> and he will reign over jacobs descendants for ever  his kingdom will never end  </s>
<s>  how will this be   mary asked the angel   since i am a virgin  </s>
<s> the angel answered   the holy spirit will come on you  and the power of the most high will overshadow you  so the holy one to be born will be called the son of god </s>
<s> even elizabeth your relative is going to have a child in her old age  and she who was said to be unable to conceive is in her sixth month </s>
<s> for no word from god will ever fail  </s>
<s>  i am the lords servant   mary answered   may your word to me be fulfilled   then the angel left her </s>
<s> at that time mary got ready and hurried to a town in the hill country of judea </s>
<s> where she entered zechariahs home and greeted elizabeth </s>
<s> when elizabeth heard marys greeting  the baby leaped in her womb  and elizabeth was filled with the holy spirit </s>
<s> in a loud voice she exclaimed   blessed are you among women  and blessed is the child you will bear </s>
<s> but why am i so favoured  that the mother of my lord should come to me </s>
<s> as soon as the sound of your greeting reached my ears  the baby in my womb leaped for joy </s>
<s> blessed is she who has believed that the lord would fulfil his promises to her  </s>
<s> and mary said </s>
<s> mary stayed with elizabeth for about three months and then returned home </s>
<s> when it was time for elizabeth to have her baby  she gave birth to a son </s>
<s> her neighbours and relatives heard that the lord had shown her great mercy  and they shared her joy </s>
<s> on the eighth day they came to circumcise the child  and they were going to name him after his father zechariah </s>
<s> but his mother spoke up and said   no  he is to be called john  </s>
<s> they said to her   there is no one among your relatives who has that name  </s>
<s> then they made signs to his father  to find out what he would like to name the child </s>
<s> he asked for a writing tablet  and to everyones astonishment he wrote   his name is john  </s>
<s> immediately his mouth was opened and his tongue set free  and he began to speak  praising god </s>
<s> all the neighbours were filled with awe  and throughout the hill country of judea people were talking about all these things </s>
<s> everyone who heard this wondered about it  asking   what then is this child going to be   for the lords hand was with him </s>
<s> his father zechariah was filled with the holy spirit and prophesied </s>
<s> and the child grew and became strong in spirit  and he lived in the wilderness until he appeared publicly to israel </s>
<s> in those days caesar augustus issued a decree that a census should be taken of the entire roman world </s>
<s>  this was the first census that took place while quirinius was governor of syria  </s>
<s> and everyone went to their own town to register </s>
<s> so joseph also went up from the town of nazareth in galilee to judea  to bethlehem the town of david  because he belonged to the house and line of david </s>
<s> he went there to register with mary  who was pledged to be married to him and was expecting a child </s>
<s> while they were there  the time came for the baby to be born </s>
<s> and she gave birth to her firstborn  a son  she wrapped him in cloths and placed him in a manger  because there was no guest room available for them </s>
<s> and there were shepherds living out in the fields near by  keeping watch over their flocks at night </s>
<s> an angel of the lord appeared to them  and the glory of the lord shone around them  and they were terrified </s>
<s> but the angel said to them   do not be afraid  i bring you good news that will cause great joy for all the people </s>
<s> today in the town of david a saviour has been born to you  he is the messiah  the lord </s>
<s> this will be a sign to you  you will find a baby wrapped in cloths and lying in a manger  </s>
<s> suddenly a great company of the heavenly host appeared with the angel  praising god and saying </s>
<s>  glory to god in the highest heaven  and on earth peace to those on whom his favour rests  </s>
<s> when the angels had left them and gone into heaven  the shepherds said to one another   lets go to bethlehem and see this thing that has happened  which the lord has told us about  </s>
<s> so they hurried off and found mary and joseph  and the baby  who was lying in the manger </s>
<s> when they had seen him  they spread the word concerning what had been told them about this child </s>
<s> and all who heard it were amazed at what the shepherds said to them </s>
<s> but mary treasured up all these things and pondered them in her heart </s>
<s> the shepherds returned  glorifying and praising god for all the things they had heard and seen  which were just as they had been told </s>
<s> on the eighth day  when it was time to circumcise the child  he was named jesus  the name the angel had given him before he was conceived </s>
<s> when the time came for the purification rites required by the law of moses  joseph and mary took him to jerusalem to present him to the lord</s>
<s>  as it is written in the law of the lord   every firstborn male is to be consecrated to the lord  </s>
<s> and to offer a sacrifice in keeping with what is said in the law of the lord   a pair of doves or two young pigeons </s>
<s> now there was a man in jerusalem called simeon  who was righteous and devout  he was waiting for the consolation of israel  and the holy spirit was on him </s>
<s> it had been revealed to him by the holy spirit that he would not die before he had seen the lords messiah </s>
<s> moved by the spirit  he went into the temple courts  when the parents brought in the child jesus to do for him what the custom of the law required </s>
<s> simeon took him in his arms and praised god  saying </s>
<s> the childs father and mother marvelled at what was said about him </s>
<s> then simeon blessed them and said to mary  his mother   this child is destined to cause the falling and rising of many in israel  and to be a sign that will be spoken against </s>
<s> so that the thoughts of many hearts will be revealed  and a sword will pierce your own soul too  </s>
<s> there was also a prophet  anna  the daughter of penuel  of the tribe of asher  she was very old  she had lived with her husband seven years after her marriage </s>
<s> and then was a widow until she was eightyfour  she never left the temple but worshipped night and day  fasting and praying </s>
<s> coming up to them at that very moment  she gave thanks to god and spoke about the child to all who were looking forward to the redemption of jerusalem </s>
<s> when joseph and mary had done everything required by the law of the lord  they returned to galilee to their own town of nazareth </s>
<s> and the child grew and became strong  he was filled with wisdom  and the grace of god was on him </s>
<s> every year jesus parents went to jerusalem for the festival of the passover </s>
<s> when he was twelve years old  they went up to the festival  according to the custom </s>
<s> after the festival was over  while his parents were returning home  the boy jesus stayed behind in jerusalem  but they were unaware of it </s>
<s> thinking he was in their company  they travelled on for a day  then they began looking for him among their relatives and friends </s>
<s> when they did not find him  they went back to jerusalem to look for him </s>
<s> after three days they found him in the temple courts  sitting among the teachers  listening to them and asking them questions </s>
<s> everyone who heard him was amazed at his understanding and his answers </s>
<s> when his parents saw him  they were astonished  his mother said to him   son  why have you treated us like this  your father and i have been anxiously searching for you  </s>
<s>  why were you searching for me   he asked   didnt you know i had to be in my fathers house  </s>
<s> but they did not understand what he was saying to them </s>
<s> then he went down to nazareth with them and was obedient to them  but his mother treasured all these things in her heart </s>
<s> and jesus grew in wisdom and stature  and in favour with god and man </s>
<s> in the fifteenth year of the reign of tiberius caesar  when pontius pilate was governor of judea  herod tetrarch of galilee  his brother philip tetrarch of iturea and traconitis  and lysanias tetrarch of abilene </s>
<s> during the highpriesthood of annas and caiaphas  the word of god came to john son of zechariah in the wilderness </s>
<s> he went into all the country around the jordan  preaching a baptism of repentance for the forgiveness of sins </s>
<s> as it is written in the book of the words of isaiah the prophet   a voice of one calling in the wilderness   prepare the way for the lord  make straight paths for him </s>
<s> every valley shall be filled in  every mountain and hill made low  the crooked roads shall become straight  the rough ways smooth </s>
<s> and all people will see gods salvation   </s>
<s> john said to the crowds coming out to be baptised by him   you brood of vipers  who warned you to flee from the coming wrath </s>
<s> produce fruit in keeping with repentance  and do not begin to say to yourselves   we have abraham as our father   for i tell you that out of these stones god can raise up children for abraham </s>
<s> the axe has been laid to the root of the trees  and every tree that does not produce good fruit will be cut down and thrown into the fire  </s>
<s>  what should we do then   the crowd asked </s>
<s> john answered   anyone who has two shirts should share with the one who has none  and anyone who has food should do the same  </s>
<s> even tax collectors came to be baptised   teacher   they asked   what should we do  </s>
<s>  dont collect any more than you are required to   he told them </s>
<s> then some soldiers asked him   and what should we do   he replied   dont extort money and dont accuse people falsely  be content with your pay  </s>
<s> the people were waiting expectantly and were all wondering in their hearts if john might possibly be the messiah </s>
<s> john answered them all   i baptise you with water  but one who is more powerful than i will come  the straps of whose sandals i am not worthy to untie  he will baptise you with the holy spirit and fire </s>
<s> his winnowing fork is in his hand to clear his threshingfloor and to gather the wheat into his barn  but he will burn up the chaff with unquenchable fire  </s>
<s> and with many other words john exhorted the people and proclaimed the good news to them </s>
<s> but when john rebuked herod the tetrarch because of his marriage to herodias  his brothers wife  and all the other evil things he had done </s>
<s> herod added this to them all  he locked john up in prison </s>
<s> when all the people were being baptised  jesus was baptised too  and as he was praying  heaven was opened</s>
<s> and the holy spirit descended on him in bodily form like a dove  and a voice came from heaven   you are my son  whom i love  with you i am well pleased  </s>
<s> now jesus himself was about thirty years old when he began his ministry  he was the son  so it was thought  of joseph </s>
<s> jesus  full of the holy spirit  left the jordan and was led by the spirit into the wilderness </s>
<s> where for forty days he was tempted by the devil  he ate nothing during those days  and at the end of them he was hungry </s>
<s> the devil said to him   if you are the son of god  tell this stone to become bread  </s>
<s> jesus answered   it is written   man shall not live on bread alone   </s>
<s> the devil led him up to a high place and showed him in an instant all the kingdoms of the world </s>
<s> and he said to him   i will give you all their authority and splendour  it has been given to me  and i can give it to anyone i want to </s>
<s> if you worship me  it will all be yours  </s>
<s> jesus answered   it is written   worship the lord your god and serve him only   </s>
<s> the devil led him to jerusalem and had him stand on the highest point of the temple   if you are the son of god   he said   throw yourself down from here </s>
<s> for it is written    he will command his angels concerning you to guard you carefully </s>
<s> they will lift you up in their hands  so that you will not strike your foot against a stone   </s>
<s> jesus answered   it is said   do not put the lord your god to the test   </s>
<s> when the devil had finished all this tempting  he left him until an opportune time </s>
<s> jesus returned to galilee in the power of the spirit  and news about him spread through the whole countryside </s>
<s> he was teaching in their synagogues  and everyone praised him </s>
<s> he went to nazareth  where he had been brought up  and on the sabbath day he went into the synagogue  as was his custom  he stood up to read </s>
<s> and the scroll of the prophet isaiah was handed to him  unrolling it  he found the place where it is written </s>
<s>  the spirit of the lord is on me  because he has anointed me to proclaim good news to the poor  he has sent me to proclaim freedom for the prisoners and recovery of sight for the blind  to set the oppressed free </s>
<s> to proclaim the year of the lords favour  </s>
<s> then he rolled up the scroll  gave it back to the attendant and sat down  the eyes of everyone in the synagogue were fastened on him </s>
<s> he began by saying to them   today this scripture is fulfilled in your hearing  </s>
<s> all spoke well of him and were amazed at the gracious words that came from his lips   isnt this josephs son   they asked </s>
<s> jesus said to them   surely you will quote this proverb to me   physician  heal yourself   and you will tell me   do here in your home town what we have heard that you did in capernaum   </s>
<s>  truly i tell you   he continued   no prophet is accepted in his home town </s>
<s> i assure you that there were many widows in israel in elijahs time  when the sky was shut for three and a half years and there was a severe famine throughout the land </s>
<s> yet elijah was not sent to any of them  but to a widow in zarephath in the region of sidon </s>
<s> and there were many in israel with leprosy in the time of elisha the prophet  yet not one of them was cleansed  only naaman the syrian  </s>
<s> all the people in the synagogue were furious when they heard this </s>
<s> they got up  drove him out of the town  and took him to the brow of the hill on which the town was built  in order to throw him off the cliff </s>
<s> but he walked right through the crowd and went on his way </s>
<s> then he went down to capernaum  a town in galilee  and on the sabbath he taught the people </s>
<s> they were amazed at his teaching  because his words had authority </s>
<s> in the synagogue there was a man possessed by a demon  an impure spirit  he cried out at the top of his voice </s>
<s>  go away  what do you want with us  jesus of nazareth  have you come to destroy us  i know who you are  the holy one of god  </s>
<s>  be quiet   jesus said sternly   come out of him   then the demon threw the man down before them all and came out without injuring him </s>
<s> all the people were amazed and said to each other   what words these are  with authority and power he gives orders to impure spirits and they come out  </s>
<s> and the news about him spread throughout the surrounding area </s>
<s> jesus left the synagogue and went to the home of simon  now simons motherinlaw was suffering from a high fever  and they asked jesus to help her </s>
<s> so he bent over her and rebuked the fever  and it left her  she got up at once and began to wait on them </s>
<s> at sunset  the people brought to jesus all who had various kinds of illness  and laying his hands on each one  he healed them </s>
<s> moreover  demons came out of many people  shouting   you are the son of god   but he rebuked them and would not allow them to speak  because they knew he was the messiah </s>
<s> at daybreak  jesus went out to a solitary place  the people were looking for him and when they came to where he was  they tried to keep him from leaving them </s>
<s> but he said   i must proclaim the good news of the kingdom of god to the other towns also  because that is why i was sent  </s>
<s> and he kept on preaching in the synagogues of judea </s>
<s> one day as jesus was standing by the lake of gennesaret  the people were crowding round him and listening to the word of god </s>
<s> he saw at the waters edge two boats  left there by the fishermen  who were washing their nets </s>
<s> he got into one of the boats  the one belonging to simon  and asked him to put out a little from the shore  then he sat down and taught the people from the boat </s>
<s> when he had finished speaking  he said to simon   put out into deep water  and let down the nets for a catch  </s>
<s> simon answered   master  weve worked hard all night and havent caught anything  but because you say so  i will let down the nets  </s>
<s> when they had done so  they caught such a large number of fish that their nets began to break </s>
<s> so they signalled to their partners in the other boat to come and help them  and they came and filled both boats so full that they began to sink </s>
<s> when simon peter saw this  he fell at jesus knees and said   go away from me  lord  i am a sinful man  </s>
<s> for he and all his companions were astonished at the catch of fish they had taken </s>
<s> and so were james and john  the sons of zebedee  simons partners  then jesus said to simon   dont be afraid  from now on you will fish for people  </s>
<s> so they pulled their boats up on shore  left everything and followed him </s>
<s> while jesus was in one of the towns  a man came along who was covered with leprosy  when he saw jesus  he fell with his face to the ground and begged him   lord  if you are willing  you can make me clean  </s>
<s> jesus reached out his hand and touched the man   i am willing   he said   be clean   and immediately the leprosy left him </s>
<s> then jesus ordered him   dont tell anyone  but go  show yourself to the priest and offer the sacrifices that moses commanded for your cleansing  as a testimony to them  </s>
<s> yet the news about him spread all the more  so that crowds of people came to hear him and to be healed of their illnesses </s>
<s> but jesus often withdrew to lonely places and prayed </s>
<s> one day jesus was teaching  and pharisees and teachers of the law were sitting there  they had come from every village of galilee and from judea and jerusalem  and the power of the lord was with jesus to heal those who were ill </s>
<s> some men came carrying a paralysed man on a mat and tried to take him into the house to lay him before jesus </s>
<s> when they could not find a way to do this because of the crowd  they went up on the roof and lowered him on his mat through the tiles into the middle of the crowd  right in front of jesus </s>
<s> when jesus saw their faith  he said   friend  your sins are forgiven  </s>
<s> the pharisees and the teachers of the law began thinking to themselves   who is this fellow who speaks blasphemy  who can forgive sins but god alone  </s>
<s> jesus knew what they were thinking and asked   why are you thinking these things in your hearts </s>
<s> which is easier  to say   your sins are forgiven   or to say   get up and walk  </s>
<s> but i want you to know that the son of man has authority on earth to forgive sins   so he said to the paralysed man   i tell you  get up  take your mat and go home  </s>
<s> immediately he stood up in front of them  took what he had been lying on and went home praising god </s>
<s> everyone was amazed and gave praise to god  they were filled with awe and said   we have seen remarkable things today  </s>
<s> after this  jesus went out and saw a tax collector by the name of levi sitting at his tax booth   follow me   jesus said to him </s>
<s> and levi got up  left everything and followed him </s>
<s> then levi held a great banquet for jesus at his house  and a large crowd of tax collectors and others were eating with them </s>
<s> but the pharisees and the teachers of the law who belonged to their sect complained to his disciples   why do you eat and drink with tax collectors and sinners  </s>
<s> jesus answered them   it is not the healthy who need a doctor  but those who are ill </s>
<s> i have not come to call the righteous  but sinners to repentance  </s>
<s> they said to him   johns disciples often fast and pray  and so do the disciples of the pharisees  but yours go on eating and drinking  </s>
<s> jesus answered   can you make the friends of the bridegroom fast while he is with them </s>
<s> but the time will come when the bridegroom will be taken from them  in those days they will fast  </s>
<s> he told them this parable   no one tears a piece out of a new garment to patch an old one  otherwise  they will have torn the new garment  and the patch from the new will not match the old </s>
<s> and no one pours new wine into old wineskins  otherwise  the new wine will burst the skins  the wine will run out and the wineskins will be ruined </s>
<s> no  new wine must be poured into new wineskins </s>
<s> and no one after drinking old wine wants the new  for they say   the old is better   </s>
<s> one sabbath jesus was going through the cornfields  and his disciples began to pick some ears of corn  rub them in their hands and eat the grain </s>
