<s> some of the pharisees asked   why are you doing what is unlawful on the sabbath  </s>
<s> jesus answered them   have you never read what david did when he and his companions were hungry </s>
<s> he entered the house of god  and taking the consecrated bread  he ate what is lawful only for priests to eat  and he also gave some to his companions  </s>
<s> then jesus said to them   the son of man is lord of the sabbath  </s>
<s> on another sabbath he went into the synagogue and was teaching  and a man was there whose right hand was shrivelled </s>
<s> the pharisees and the teachers of the law were looking for a reason to accuse jesus  so they watched him closely to see if he would heal on the sabbath </s>
<s> but jesus knew what they were thinking and said to the man with the shrivelled hand   get up and stand in front of everyone   so he got up and stood there </s>
<s> then jesus said to them   i ask you  which is lawful on the sabbath  to do good or to do evil  to save life or to destroy it  </s>
<s> he looked round at them all  and then said to the man   stretch out your hand   he did so  and his hand was completely restored </s>
<s> but the pharisees and the teachers of the law were furious and began to discuss with one another what they might do to jesus </s>
<s> one of those days jesus went out to a mountainside to pray  and spent the night praying to god </s>
<s> when morning came  he called his disciples to him and chose twelve of them  whom he also designated apostles </s>
<s> simon  whom he named peter   his brother andrew  james  john  philip  bartholomew </s>
<s> matthew  thomas  james son of alphaeus  simon who was called the zealot </s>
<s> judas son of james  and judas iscariot  who became a traitor </s>
<s> he went down with them and stood on a level place  a large crowd of his disciples was there and a great number of people from all over judea  from jerusalem  and from the coastal region around tyre and sidon </s>
<s> who had come to hear him and to be healed of their diseases  those troubled by impure spirits were cured </s>
<s> and the people all tried to touch him  because power was coming from him and healing them all </s>
<s> looking at his disciples  he said   blessed are you who are poor  for yours is the kingdom of god </s>
<s> blessed are you who hunger now  for you will be satisfied  blessed are you who weep now  for you will laugh </s>
<s> blessed are you when people hate you  when they exclude you and insult you and reject your name as evil </s>
<s>  rejoice in that day and leap for joy  because great is your reward in heaven  for that is how their ancestors treated the prophets </s>
<s>  but woe to you who are rich  for you have already received your comfort </s>
<s> woe to you who are well fed now  for you will go hungry  woe to you who laugh now  for you will mourn and weep </s>
<s> woe to you when everyone speaks well of you  for that is how their ancestors treated the false prophets </s>
<s>  but to you who are listening i say  love your enemies  do good to those who hate you </s>
<s> bless those who curse you  pray for those who illtreat you </s>
<s> if someone slaps you on one cheek  turn to them the other also  if someone takes your coat  do not withhold your shirt from them </s>
<s> give to everyone who asks you  and if anyone takes what belongs to you  do not demand it back </s>
<s> do to others as you would have them do to you </s>
<s>  if you love those who love you  what credit is that to you  even sinners love those who love them </s>
<s> and if you do good to those who are good to you  what credit is that to you  even sinners do that </s>
<s> and if you lend to those from whom you expect repayment  what credit is that to you  even sinners lend to sinners  expecting to be repaid in full </s>
<s> but love your enemies  do good to them  and lend to them without expecting to get anything back  then your reward will be great  and you will be children of the most high  because he is kind to the ungrateful and wicked </s>
<s> be merciful  just as your father is merciful </s>
<s>  do not judge  and you will not be judged  do not condemn  and you will not be condemned  forgive  and you will be forgiven </s>
<s> give  and it will be given to you  a good measure  pressed down  shaken together and running over  will be poured into your lap  for with the measure you use  it will be measured to you  </s>
<s> he also told them this parable   can the blind lead the blind  will they not both fall into a pit </s>
<s> the student is not above the teacher  but everyone who is fully trained will be like their teacher </s>
<s>  why do you look at the speck of sawdust in your brothers eye and pay no attention to the plank in your own eye </s>
<s> how can you say to your brother   brother  let me take the speck out of your eye   when you yourself fail to see the plank in your own eye  you hypocrite  first take the plank out of your eye  and then you will see clearly to remove the speck from your brothers eye </s>
<s>  no good tree bears bad fruit  nor does a bad tree bear good fruit </s>
<s> each tree is recognised by its own fruit  people do not pick figs from thornbushes  or grapes from briers </s>
<s> a good man brings good things out of the good stored up in his heart  and an evil man brings evil things out of the evil stored up in his heart  for the mouth speaks what the heart is full of </s>
<s>  why do you call me   lord  lord   and do not do what i say </s>
<s> as for everyone who comes to me and hears my words and puts them into practice  i will show you what they are like </s>
<s> they are like a man building a house  who dug down deep and laid the foundation on rock  when the flood came  the torrent struck that house but could not shake it  because it was well built </s>
<s> but the one who hears my words and does not put them into practice is like a man who built a house on the ground without a foundation  the moment the torrent struck that house  it collapsed and its destruction was complete  </s>
<s> when jesus had finished saying all this to the people who were listening  he entered capernaum </s>
<s> there a centurions servant  whom his master valued highly  was ill and about to die </s>
<s> the centurion heard of jesus and sent some elders of the jews to him  asking him to come and heal his servant </s>
<s> when they came to jesus  they pleaded earnestly with him   this man deserves to have you do this </s>
<s> because he loves our nation and has built our synagogue  </s>
<s> so jesus went with them  he was not far from the house when the centurion sent friends to say to him   lord  dont trouble yourself  for i do not deserve to have you come under my roof </s>
<s> that is why i did not even consider myself worthy to come to you  but say the word  and my servant will be healed </s>
<s> for i myself am a man under authority  with soldiers under me  i tell this one   go   and he goes  and that one   come   and he comes  i say to my servant   do this   and he does it  </s>
<s> when jesus heard this  he was amazed at him  and turning to the crowd following him  he said   i tell you  i have not found such great faith even in israel  </s>
<s> then the men who had been sent returned to the house and found the servant well </s>
<s> soon afterwards  jesus went to a town called nain  and his disciples and a large crowd went along with him </s>
<s> as he approached the town gate  a dead person was being carried out  the only son of his mother  and she was a widow  and a large crowd from the town was with her </s>
<s> when the lord saw her  his heart went out to her and he said   dont cry  </s>
<s> then he went up and touched the bier they were carrying him on  and the bearers stood still  he said   young man  i say to you  get up  </s>
<s> the dead man sat up and began to talk  and jesus gave him back to his mother </s>
<s> they were all filled with awe and praised god   a great prophet has appeared among us   they said   god has come to help his people  </s>
<s> this news about jesus spread throughout judea and the surrounding country </s>
<s> johns disciples told him about all these things  calling two of them </s>
<s> he sent them to the lord to ask   are you the one who is to come  or should we expect someone else  </s>
<s> when the men came to jesus  they said   john the baptist sent us to you to ask   are you the one who is to come  or should we expect someone else   </s>
<s> at that very time jesus cured many who had diseases  illnesses and evil spirits  and gave sight to many who were blind </s>
<s> so he replied to the messengers   go back and report to john what you have seen and heard  the blind receive sight  the lame walk  those who have leprosy are cleansed  the deaf hear  the dead are raised  and the good news is proclaimed to the poor </s>
<s> blessed is anyone who does not stumble on account of me  </s>
<s> after johns messengers left  jesus began to speak to the crowd about john   what did you go out into the wilderness to see  a reed swayed by the wind </s>
<s> if not  what did you go out to see  a man dressed in fine clothes  no  those who wear expensive clothes and indulge in luxury are in palaces </s>
<s> but what did you go out to see  a prophet  yes  i tell you  and more than a prophet </s>
<s> this is the one about whom it is written    i will send my messenger ahead of you  who will prepare your way before you  </s>
<s> i tell you  among those born of women there is no one greater than john  yet the one who is least in the kingdom of god is greater than he  </s>
<s>  all the people  even the tax collectors  when they heard jesus words  acknowledged that gods way was right  because they had been baptised by john </s>
<s> but the pharisees and the experts in the law rejected gods purpose for themselves  because they had not been baptised by john  </s>
<s> jesus went on to say   to what  then  can i compare the people of this generation  what are they like </s>
<s> they are like children sitting in the marketplace and calling out to each other    we played the pipe for you  and you did not dance  we sang a dirge  and you did not cry  </s>
<s> when one of the pharisees invited jesus to have dinner with him  he went to the pharisees house and reclined at the table </s>
<s> a woman in that town who lived a sinful life learned that jesus was eating at the pharisees house  so she came there with an alabaster jar of perfume </s>
<s> as she stood behind him at his feet weeping  she began to wet his feet with her tears  then she wiped them with her hair  kissed them and poured perfume on them </s>
<s> when the pharisee who had invited him saw this  he said to himself   if this man were a prophet  he would know who is touching him and what kind of woman she is  that she is a sinner  </s>
<s> jesus answered him   simon  i have something to tell you    tell me  teacher   he said </s>
<s>  two people owed money to a certain moneylender  one owed him five hundred denarii  and the other fifty </s>
<s> neither of them had the money to pay him back  so he forgave the debts of both  now which of them will love him more  </s>
<s> simon replied   i suppose the one who had the bigger debt forgiven    you have judged correctly   jesus said </s>
<s> then he turned towards the woman and said to simon   do you see this woman  i came into your house  you did not give me any water for my feet  but she wet my feet with her tears and wiped them with her hair </s>
<s> you did not give me a kiss  but this woman  from the time i entered  has not stopped kissing my feet </s>
<s> you did not put oil on my head  but she has poured perfume on my feet </s>
<s> therefore  i tell you  her many sins have been forgiven  as her great love has shown  but whoever has been forgiven little loves little  </s>
<s> then jesus said to her   your sins are forgiven  </s>
<s> the other guests began to say among themselves   who is this who even forgives sins  </s>
<s> jesus said to the woman   your faith has saved you  go in peace  </s>
<s> after this  jesus travelled about from one town and village to another  proclaiming the good news of the kingdom of god  the twelve were with him </s>
<s> and also some women who had been cured of evil spirits and diseases  mary  called magdalene  from whom seven demons had come out </s>
<s> joanna the wife of chuza  the manager of herods household  susanna  and many others  these women were helping to support them out of their own means </s>
<s> while a large crowd was gathering and people were coming to jesus from town after town  he told this parable </s>
<s>  a farmer went out to sow his seed  as he was scattering the seed  some fell along the path  it was trampled on  and the birds ate it up </s>
<s> some fell on rocky ground  and when it came up  the plants withered because they had no moisture </s>
<s> other seed fell among thorns  which grew up with it and choked the plants </s>
<s> still other seed fell on good soil  it came up and yielded a crop  a hundred times more than was sown   when he said this  he called out   whoever has ears to hear  let them hear  </s>
<s> his disciples asked him what this parable meant </s>
<s> he said   the knowledge of the secrets of the kingdom of god has been given to you  but to others i speak in parables  so that    though seeing  they may not see  though hearing  they may not understand  </s>
<s>  this is the meaning of the parable  the seed is the word of god </s>
<s> those along the path are the ones who hear  and then the devil comes and takes away the word from their hearts  so that they may not believe and be saved </s>
<s> those on the rocky ground are the ones who receive the word with joy when they hear it  but they have no root  they believe for a while  but in the time of testing they fall away </s>
<s> the seed that fell among thorns stands for those who hear  but as they go on their way they are choked by lifes worries  riches and pleasures  and they do not mature </s>
<s> but the seed on good soil stands for those with a noble and good heart  who hear the word  retain it  and by persevering produce a crop </s>
<s>  no one lights a lamp and hides it in a clay jar or puts it under a bed  instead  they put it on a stand  so that those who come in can see the light </s>
<s> for there is nothing hidden that will not be disclosed  and nothing concealed that will not be known or brought out into the open </s>
<s> therefore consider carefully how you listen  whoever has will be given more  whoever does not have  even what they think they have will be taken from them  </s>
<s> now jesus mother and brothers came to see him  but they were not able to get near him because of the crowd </s>
<s> someone told him   your mother and brothers are standing outside  wanting to see you  </s>
<s> he replied   my mother and brothers are those who hear gods word and put it into practice  </s>
<s> one day jesus said to his disciples   let us go over to the other side of the lake   so they got into a boat and set out </s>
<s> as they sailed  he fell asleep  a squall came down on the lake  so that the boat was being swamped  and they were in great danger </s>
<s> the disciples went and woke him  saying   master  master  were going to drown   he got up and rebuked the wind and the raging waters  the storm subsided  and all was calm </s>
<s>  where is your faith   he asked his disciples  in fear and amazement they asked one another   who is this  he commands even the winds and the water  and they obey him  </s>
<s> they sailed to the region of the gerasenes  which is across the lake from galilee </s>
<s> when jesus stepped ashore  he was met by a demonpossessed man from the town  for a long time this man had not worn clothes or lived in a house  but had lived in the tombs </s>
<s> when he saw jesus  he cried out and fell at his feet  shouting at the top of his voice   what do you want with me  jesus  son of the most high god  i beg you  dont torture me  </s>
<s> for jesus had commanded the impure spirit to come out of the man  many times it had seized him  and though he was chained hand and foot and kept under guard  he had broken his chains and had been driven by the demon into solitary places </s>
<s> jesus asked him   what is your name    legion   he replied  because many demons had gone into him </s>
<s> and they begged jesus repeatedly not to order them to go into the abyss </s>
<s> a large herd of pigs was feeding there on the hillside  the demons begged jesus to let them go into the pigs  and he gave them permission </s>
<s> when the demons came out of the man  they went into the pigs  and the herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake and was drowned </s>
<s> when those tending the pigs saw what had happened  they ran off and reported this in the town and countryside </s>
<s> and the people went out to see what had happened  when they came to jesus  they found the man from whom the demons had gone out  sitting at jesus feet  dressed and in his right mind  and they were afraid </s>
<s> those who had seen it told the people how the demonpossessed man had been cured </s>
<s> then all the people of the region of the gerasenes asked jesus to leave them  because they were overcome with fear  so he got into the boat and left </s>
<s> the man from whom the demons had gone out begged to go with him  but jesus sent him away  saying </s>
<s>  return home and tell how much god has done for you   so the man went away and told all over the town how much jesus had done for him </s>
<s> now when jesus returned  a crowd welcomed him  for they were all expecting him </s>
<s> then a man named jairus  a synagogue leader  came and fell at jesus feet  pleading with him to come to his house</s>
<s> because his only daughter  a girl of about twelve  was dying  as jesus was on his way  the crowds almost crushed him </s>
<s> and a woman was there who had been subject to bleeding for twelve years  but no one could heal her </s>
<s> she came up behind him and touched the edge of his cloak  and immediately her bleeding stopped </s>
<s>  who touched me   jesus asked  when they all denied it  peter said   master  the people are crowding and pressing against you  </s>
<s> but jesus said   someone touched me  i know that power has gone out from me  </s>
<s> then the woman  seeing that she could not go unnoticed  came trembling and fell at his feet  in the presence of all the people  she told why she had touched him and how she had been instantly healed </s>
<s> then he said to her   daughter  your faith has healed you  go in peace  </s>
<s> while jesus was still speaking  someone came from the house of jairus  the synagogue leader   your daughter is dead   he said   dont bother the teacher anymore  </s>
<s> hearing this  jesus said to jairus   dont be afraid  just believe  and she will be healed  </s>
<s> when he arrived at the house of jairus  he did not let anyone go in with him except peter  john and james  and the childs father and mother </s>
<s> meanwhile  all the people were wailing and mourning for her   stop wailing   jesus said   she is not dead but asleep  </s>
<s> they laughed at him  knowing that she was dead </s>
<s> but he took her by the hand and said   my child  get up  </s>
<s> her spirit returned  and at once she stood up  then jesus told them to give her something to eat </s>
<s> her parents were astonished  but he ordered them not to tell anyone what had happened </s>
<s> when jesus had called the twelve together  he gave them power and authority to drive out all demons and to cure diseases </s>
<s> and he sent them out to proclaim the kingdom of god and to heal those who were ill </s>
<s> he told them   take nothing for the journey  no staff  no bag  no bread  no money  no extra shirt </s>
<s> whatever house you enter  stay there until you leave that town </s>
<s> if people do not welcome you  leave their town and shake the dust off your feet as a testimony against them  </s>
<s> so they set out and went from village to village  proclaiming the good news and healing people everywhere </s>
<s> now herod the tetrarch heard about all that was going on  and he was perplexed because some were saying that john had been raised from the dead </s>
<s> others that elijah had appeared  and still others that one of the prophets of long ago had come back to life </s>
<s> but herod said   i beheaded john  who  then  is this i hear such things about   and he tried to see him </s>
<s> when the apostles returned  they reported to jesus what they had done  then he took them with him and they withdrew by themselves to a town called bethsaida </s>
<s> but the crowds learned about it and followed him  he welcomed them and spoke to them about the kingdom of god  and healed those who needed healing </s>
<s> late in the afternoon the twelve came to him and said   send the crowd away so they can go to the surrounding villages and countryside and find food and lodging  because we are in a remote place here  </s>
<s> he replied   you give them something to eat   they answered   we have only five loaves of bread and two fish  unless we go and buy food for all this crowd  </s>
<s>  about five thousand men were there   but he said to his disciples   make them sit down in groups of about fifty each  </s>
<s> the disciples did so  and everyone sat down </s>
<s> taking the five loaves and the two fish and looking up to heaven  he gave thanks and broke them  then he gave them to the disciples to distribute to the people </s>
<s> they all ate and were satisfied  and the disciples picked up twelve basketfuls of broken pieces that were left over </s>
<s> once when jesus was praying in private and his disciples were with him  he asked them   who do the crowds say i am  </s>
<s> they replied   some say john the baptist  others say elijah  and still others  that one of the prophets of long ago has come back to life  </s>
<s>  but what about you   he asked   who do you say i am   peter answered   gods messiah  </s>
<s> jesus strictly warned them not to tell this to anyone </s>
<s> and he said   the son of man must suffer many things and be rejected by the elders  the chief priests and the teachers of the law  and he must be killed and on the third day be raised to life  </s>
<s> then he said to them all   whoever wants to be my disciple must deny themselves and take up their cross daily and follow me </s>
<s> for whoever wants to save their life will lose it  but whoever loses their life for me will save it </s>
<s> what good is it for someone to gain the whole world  and yet lose or forfeit their very self </s>
<s> whoever is ashamed of me and my words  the son of man will be ashamed of them when he comes in his glory and in the glory of the father and of the holy angels </s>
<s>  truly i tell you  some who are standing here will not taste death before they see the kingdom of god  </s>
<s> about eight days after jesus said this  he took peter  john and james with him and went up onto a mountain to pray </s>
<s> as he was praying  the appearance of his face changed  and his clothes became as bright as a flash of lightning </s>
<s> two men  moses and elijah  appeared in glorious splendour  talking with jesus </s>
<s> they spoke about his departure  which he was about to bring to fulfilment at jerusalem </s>
<s> peter and his companions were very sleepy  but when they became fully awake  they saw his glory and the two men standing with him </s>
<s> as the men were leaving jesus  peter said to him   master  it is good for us to be here  let us put up three shelters  one for you  one for moses and one for elijah    he did not know what he was saying  </s>
<s> while he was speaking  a cloud appeared and covered them  and they were afraid as they entered the cloud </s>
<s> a voice came from the cloud  saying   this is my son  whom i have chosen  listen to him  </s>
<s> when the voice had spoken  they found that jesus was alone  the disciples kept this to themselves and did not tell anyone at that time what they had seen </s>
<s> the next day  when they came down from the mountain  a large crowd met him </s>
<s> a man in the crowd called out   teacher  i beg you to look at my son  for he is my only child </s>
<s> a spirit seizes him and he suddenly screams  it throws him into convulsions so that he foams at the mouth  it scarcely ever leaves him and is destroying him </s>
<s> i begged your disciples to drive it out  but they could not  </s>
<s>  you unbelieving and perverse generation   jesus replied   how long shall i stay with you and put up with you  bring your son here  </s>
<s> even while the boy was coming  the demon threw him to the ground in a convulsion  but jesus rebuked the impure spirit  healed the boy and gave him back to his father </s>
<s> and they were all amazed at the greatness of god  while everyone was marvelling at all that jesus did  he said to his disciples </s>
<s>  listen carefully to what i am about to tell you  the son of man is going to be delivered into the hands of men  </s>
<s> but they did not understand what this meant  it was hidden from them  so that they did not grasp it  and they were afraid to ask him about it </s>
<s> an argument started among the disciples as to which of them would be the greatest </s>
<s> jesus  knowing their thoughts  took a little child and made him stand beside him </s>
<s> then he said to them   whoever welcomes this little child in my name welcomes me  and whoever welcomes me welcomes the one who sent me  for it is the one who is least among you all who is the greatest  </s>
<s>  master   said john   we saw someone driving out demons in your name and we tried to stop him  because he is not one of us  </s>
<s>  do not stop him   jesus said   for whoever is not against you is for you  </s>
<s> as the time approached for him to be taken up to heaven  jesus resolutely set out for jerusalem </s>
<s> and he sent messengers on ahead  who went into a samaritan village to get things ready for him </s>
<s> but the people there did not welcome him  because he was heading for jerusalem </s>
<s> when the disciples james and john saw this  they asked   lord  do you want us to call fire down from heaven to destroy them  </s>
<s> but jesus turned and rebuked them </s>
<s> then he and his disciples went to another village </s>
<s> as they were walking along the road  a man said to him   i will follow you wherever you go  </s>
<s> jesus replied   foxes have dens and birds have nests  but the son of man has nowhere to lay his head  </s>
<s> he said to another man   follow me   but he replied   lord  first let me go and bury my father  </s>
<s> jesus said to him   let the dead bury their own dead  but you go and proclaim the kingdom of god  </s>
<s> still another said   i will follow you  lord  but first let me go back and say goodbye to my family  </s>
<s> jesus replied   no one who puts a hand to the plough and looks back is fit for service in the kingdom of god  </s>
<s> after this the lord appointed seventytwo others and sent them two by two ahead of him to every town and place where he was about to go </s>
<s> he told them   the harvest is plentiful  but the workers are few  ask the lord of the harvest  therefore  to send out workers into his harvest field </s>
<s> go  i am sending you out like lambs among wolves </s>
<s> do not take a purse or bag or sandals  and do not greet anyone on the road </s>
<s>  when you enter a house  first say   peace to this house  </s>
<s> if someone who promotes peace is there  your peace will rest on them  if not  it will return to you </s>
<s> stay there  eating and drinking whatever they give you  for the worker deserves his wages  do not move around from house to house </s>
<s>  when you enter a town and are welcomed  eat what is offered to you </s>
<s> heal those there who are ill and tell them   the kingdom of god has come near to you  </s>
<s> but when you enter a town and are not welcomed  go into its streets and say </s>
<s>  even the dust of your town we wipe from our feet as a warning to you  yet be sure of this  the kingdom of god has come near  </s>
<s> i tell you  it will be more bearable on that day for sodom than for that town </s>
<s>  woe to you  chorazin  woe to you  bethsaida  for if the miracles that were performed in you had been performed in tyre and sidon  they would have repented long ago  sitting in sackcloth and ashes </s>
<s> but it will be more bearable for tyre and sidon at the judgment than for you </s>
<s> and you  capernaum  will you be lifted to the heavens  no  you will go down to hades </s>
<s>  whoever listens to you listens to me  whoever rejects you rejects me  but whoever rejects me rejects him who sent me  </s>
<s> the seventytwo returned with joy and said   lord  even the demons submit to us in your name  </s>
<s> he replied   i saw satan fall like lightning from heaven </s>
<s> i have given you authority to trample on snakes and scorpions and to overcome all the power of the enemy  nothing will harm you </s>
<s> however  do not rejoice that the spirits submit to you  but rejoice that your names are written in heaven  </s>
<s> at that time jesus  full of joy through the holy spirit  said   i praise you  father  lord of heaven and earth  because you have hidden these things from the wise and learned  and revealed them to little children  yes  father  for this is what you were pleased to do </s>
<s>  all things have been committed to me by my father  no one knows who the son is except the father  and no one knows who the father is except the son and those to whom the son chooses to reveal him  </s>
<s> then he turned to his disciples and said privately   blessed are the eyes that see what you see </s>
<s> for i tell you that many prophets and kings wanted to see what you see but did not see it  and to hear what you hear but did not hear it  </s>
<s> on one occasion an expert in the law stood up to test jesus   teacher   he asked   what must i do to inherit eternal life  </s>
<s>  what is written in the law   he replied   how do you read it  </s>
<s> he answered    love the lord your god with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your strength and with all your mind   and   love your neighbour as yourself   </s>
<s>  you have answered correctly   jesus replied   do this and you will live  </s>
<s> but he wanted to justify himself  so he asked jesus   and who is my neighbour  </s>
<s> in reply jesus said   a man was going down from jerusalem to jericho  when he was attacked by robbers  they stripped him of his clothes  beat him and went away  leaving him halfdead </s>
<s> a priest happened to be going down the same road  and when he saw the man  he passed by on the other side </s>
<s> so too  a levite  when he came to the place and saw him  passed by on the other side </s>
<s> but a samaritan  as he travelled  came where the man was  and when he saw him  he took pity on him </s>
<s> he went to him and bandaged his wounds  pouring on oil and wine  then he put the man on his own donkey  brought him to an inn and took care of him </s>
<s> the next day he took out two denarii and gave them to the innkeeper   look after him   he said   and when i return  i will reimburse you for any extra expense you may have  </s>
<s>  which of these three do you think was a neighbour to the man who fell into the hands of robbers  </s>
<s> the expert in the law replied   the one who had mercy on him   jesus told him   go and do likewise  </s>
<s> as jesus and his disciples were on their way  he came to a village where a woman named martha opened her home to him </s>
<s> she had a sister called mary  who sat at the lords feet listening to what he said </s>
<s> but martha was distracted by all the preparations that had to be made  she came to him and asked   lord  dont you care that my sister has left me to do the work by myself  tell her to help me  </s>
<s>  martha  martha   the lord answered   you are worried and upset about many things </s>
<s> but few things are needed  or indeed only one  mary has chosen what is better  and it will not be taken away from her  </s>
<s> one day jesus was praying in a certain place  when he finished  one of his disciples said to him   lord  teach us to pray  just as john taught his disciples  </s>
<s> he said to them   when you pray  say    father  hallowed be your name  your kingdom come </s>
<s> give us each day our daily bread </s>
<s> forgive us our sins  for we also forgive everyone who sins against us  and lead us not into temptation   </s>
<s> then jesus said to them   suppose you have a friend  and you go to him at midnight and say   friend  lend me three loaves of bread </s>
<s> a friend of mine on a journey has come to me  and i have no food to offer him  </s>
<s> and suppose the one inside answers   dont bother me  the door is already locked  and my children and i are in bed  i cant get up and give you anything  </s>
<s> i tell you  even though he will not get up and give you the bread because of friendship  yet because of your shameless audacity he will surely get up and give you as much as you need </s>
<s>  so i say to you  ask and it will be given to you  seek and you will find  knock and the door will be opened to you </s>
<s> for everyone who asks receives  the one who seeks finds  and to the one who knocks  the door will be opened </s>
<s>  which of you fathers  if your son asks for a fish  will give him a snake instead </s>
<s> or if he asks for an egg  will give him a scorpion </s>
<s> if you then  though you are evil  know how to give good gifts to your children  how much more will your father in heaven give the holy spirit to those who ask him  </s>
<s> jesus was driving out a demon that was mute  when the demon left  the man who had been mute spoke  and the crowd was amazed </s>
<s> but some of them said   by beelzebul  the prince of demons  he is driving out demons  </s>
<s> others tested him by asking for a sign from heaven </s>
<s> jesus knew their thoughts and said to them   any kingdom divided against itself will be ruined  and a house divided against itself will fall </s>
<s> if satan is divided against himself  how can his kingdom stand  i say this because you claim that i drive out demons by beelzebul </s>
<s> now if i drive out demons by beelzebul  by whom do your followers drive them out  so then  they will be your judges </s>
<s> but if i drive out demons by the finger of god  then the kingdom of god has come upon you </s>
<s>  when a strong man  fully armed  guards his own house  his possessions are safe </s>
<s> but when someone stronger attacks and overpowers him  he takes away the armour in which the man trusted and divides up his plunder </s>
<s>  whoever is not with me is against me  and whoever does not gather with me scatters </s>
<s>  when an impure spirit comes out of a person  it goes through arid places seeking rest and does not find it  then it says   i will return to the house i left  </s>
<s> when it arrives  it finds the house swept clean and put in order </s>
<s> then it goes and takes seven other spirits more wicked than itself  and they go in and live there  and the final condition of that person is worse than the first  </s>
<s> as jesus was saying these things  a woman in the crowd called out   blessed is the mother who gave you birth and nursed you  </s>
<s> he replied   blessed rather are those who hear the word of god and obey it  </s>
<s> as the crowds increased  jesus said   this is a wicked generation  it asks for a sign  but none will be given it except the sign of jonah </s>
<s> for as jonah was a sign to the ninevites  so also will the son of man be to this generation </s>
<s> the queen of the south will rise at the judgment with the people of this generation and condemn them  for she came from the ends of the earth to listen to solomons wisdom  and now something greater than solomon is here </s>
<s> the men of nineveh will stand up at the judgment with this generation and condemn it  for they repented at the preaching of jonah  and now something greater than jonah is here </s>
<s>  no one lights a lamp and puts it in a place where it will be hidden  or under a bowl  instead they put it on its stand  so that those who come in may see the light </s>
<s> your eye is the lamp of your body  when your eyes are healthy  your whole body also is full of light  but when they are unhealthy  your body also is full of darkness </s>
<s> see to it  then  that the light within you is not darkness </s>
<s> therefore  if your whole body is full of light  and no part of it dark  it will be just as full of light as when a lamp shines its light on you  </s>
<s> when jesus had finished speaking  a pharisee invited him to eat with him  so he went in and reclined at the table </s>
<s> but the pharisee was surprised when he noticed that jesus did not first wash before the meal </s>
<s> then the lord said to him   now then  you pharisees clean the outside of the cup and dish  but inside you are full of greed and wickedness </s>
<s> you foolish people  did not the one who made the outside make the inside also </s>
<s> but now as for what is inside you  be generous to the poor  and everything will be clean for you </s>
<s>  woe to you pharisees  because you give god a tenth of your mint  rue and all other kinds of garden herbs  but you neglect justice and the love of god  you should have practised the latter without leaving the former undone </s>
<s>  woe to you pharisees  because you love the most important seats in the synagogues and respectful greetings in the marketplaces </s>
<s>  woe to you  because you are like unmarked graves  which people walk over without knowing it  </s>
<s> one of the experts in the law answered him   teacher  when you say these things  you insult us also  </s>
<s> jesus replied   and you experts in the law  woe to you  because you load people down with burdens they can hardly carry  and you yourselves will not lift one finger to help them </s>
<s>  woe to you  because you build tombs for the prophets  and it was your ancestors who killed them </s>
<s> so you testify that you approve of what your ancestors did  they killed the prophets  and you build their tombs </s>
<s> because of this  god in his wisdom said   i will send them prophets and apostles  some of whom they will kill and others they will persecute  </s>
<s> therefore this generation will be held responsible for the blood of all the prophets that has been shed since the beginning of the world </s>
<s> from the blood of abel to the blood of zechariah  who was killed between the altar and the sanctuary  yes  i tell you  this generation will be held responsible for it all </s>
<s>  woe to you experts in the law  because you have taken away the key to knowledge  you yourselves have not entered  and you have hindered those who were entering  </s>
<s> when jesus went outside  the pharisees and the teachers of the law began to oppose him fiercely and to besiege him with questions </s>
<s> waiting to catch him in something he might say </s>
<s> meanwhile  when a crowd of many thousands had gathered  so that they were trampling on one another  jesus began to speak first to his disciples  saying   be on your guard against the yeast of the pharisees  which is hypocrisy </s>
<s> there is nothing concealed that will not be disclosed  or hidden that will not be made known </s>
<s> what you have said in the dark will be heard in the daylight  and what you have whispered in the ear in the inner rooms will be proclaimed from the roofs </s>
<s>  i tell you  my friends  do not be afraid of those who kill the body and after that can do no more </s>
<s> but i will show you whom you should fear  fear him who  after your body has been killed  has authority to throw you into hell  yes  i tell you  fear him </s>
<s> are not five sparrows sold for two pennies  yet not one of them is forgotten by god </s>
<s> indeed  the very hairs of your head are all numbered  dont be afraid  you are worth more than many sparrows </s>
<s>  i tell you  whoever publicly acknowledges me before others  the son of man will also acknowledge before the angels of god </s>
<s> but whoever disowns me before others will be disowned before the angels of god </s>
<s> and everyone who speaks a word against the son of man will be forgiven  but anyone who blasphemes against the holy spirit will not be forgiven </s>
<s>  when you are brought before synagogues  rulers and authorities  do not worry about how you will defend yourselves or what you will say </s>
<s> for the holy spirit will teach you at that time what you should say  </s>
<s> someone in the crowd said to him   teacher  tell my brother to divide the inheritance with me  </s>
<s> jesus replied   man  who appointed me a judge or an arbiter between you  </s>
<s> then he said to them   watch out  be on your guard against all kinds of greed  life does not consist in an abundance of possessions  </s>
<s> and he told them this parable   the ground of a certain rich man yielded an abundant harvest </s>
<s> he thought to himself   what shall i do  i have no place to store my crops  </s>
<s>  then he said   this is what ill do  i will tear down my barns and build bigger ones  and there i will store my surplus grain </s>
<s> and ill say to myself   you have plenty of grain laid up for many years  take life easy  eat  drink and be merry   </s>
<s>  but god said to him   you fool  this very night your life will be demanded from you  then who will get what you have prepared for yourself  </s>
<s>  this is how it will be with whoever stores up things for themselves but is not rich towards god  </s>
<s> then jesus said to his disciples   therefore i tell you  do not worry about your life  what you will eat  or about your body  what you will wear </s>
<s> for life is more than food  and the body more than clothes </s>
<s> consider the ravens  they do not sow or reap  they have no storeroom or barn  yet god feeds them  and how much more valuable you are than birds </s>
<s> who of you by worrying can add a single hour to your life </s>
<s> since you cannot do this very little thing  why do you worry about the rest </s>
<s>  consider how the wild flowers grow  they do not labour or spin  yet i tell you  not even solomon in all his splendour was dressed like one of these </s>
<s> if that is how god clothes the grass of the field  which is here today  and tomorrow is thrown into the fire  how much more will he clothe you  you of little faith </s>
<s> and do not set your heart on what you will eat or drink  do not worry about it </s>
<s> for the pagan world runs after all such things  and your father knows that you need them </s>
<s> but seek his kingdom  and these things will be given to you as well </s>
<s>  do not be afraid  little flock  for your father has been pleased to give you the kingdom </s>
<s> sell your possessions and give to the poor  provide purses for yourselves that will not wear out  a treasure in heaven that will never fail  where no thief comes near and no moth destroys </s>
<s> for where your treasure is  there your heart will be also </s>
<s>  be dressed ready for service and keep your lamps burning </s>
<s> like servants waiting for their master to return from a wedding banquet  so that when he comes and knocks they can immediately open the door for him </s>
<s> it will be good for those servants whose master finds them watching when he comes  truly i tell you  he will dress himself to serve  will make them recline at the table and will come and wait on them </s>
<s> it will be good for those servants whose master finds them ready  even if he comes in the middle of the night or towards daybreak </s>
<s> but understand this  if the owner of the house had known at what hour the thief was coming  he would not have let his house be broken into </s>
<s> you also must be ready  because the son of man will come at an hour when you do not expect him  </s>
<s> peter asked   lord  are you telling this parable to us  or to everyone  </s>
<s> the lord answered   who then is the faithful and wise manager  whom the master puts in charge of his servants to give them their food allowance at the proper time </s>
<s> it will be good for that servant whom the master finds doing so when he returns </s>
<s> truly i tell you  he will put him in charge of all his possessions </s>
<s> but suppose the servant says to himself   my master is taking a long time in coming   and he then begins to beat the other servants  both men and women  and to eat and drink and get drunk </s>
<s> the master of that servant will come on a day when he does not expect him and at an hour he is not aware of  he will cut him to pieces and assign him a place with the unbelievers </s>
<s>  the servant who knows the masters will and does not get ready or does not do what the master wants will be beaten with many blows </s>
<s> but the one who does not know and does things deserving punishment will be beaten with few blows  from everyone who has been given much  much will be demanded  and from the one who has been entrusted with much  much more will be asked </s>
<s>  i have come to bring fire on the earth  and how i wish it were already kindled </s>
<s> but i have a baptism to undergo  and what constraint i am under until it is completed </s>
<s> do you think i came to bring peace on earth  no  i tell you  but division </s>
<s> from now on there will be five in one family divided against each other  three against two and two against three </s>
<s> they will be divided  father against son and son against father  mother against daughter and daughter against mother  motherinlaw against daughterinlaw and daughterinlaw against motherinlaw  </s>
<s> he said to the crowd   when you see a cloud rising in the west  immediately you say   its going to rain   and it does </s>
<s> and when the south wind blows  you say   its going to be hot   and it is </s>
<s> hypocrites  you know how to interpret the appearance of the earth and the sky  how is it that you dont know how to interpret this present time </s>
<s>  why dont you judge for yourselves what is right </s>
<s> as you are going with your adversary to the magistrate  try hard to be reconciled on the way  or your adversary may drag you off to the judge  and the judge turn you over to the officer  and the officer throw you into prison </s>
<s> i tell you  you will not get out until you have paid the last penny  </s>
<s> now there were some present at that time who told jesus about the galileans whose blood pilate had mixed with their sacrifices </s>
<s> jesus answered   do you think that these galileans were worse sinners than all the other galileans because they suffered this way </s>
<s> i tell you  no  but unless you repent  you too will all perish </s>
<s> or those eighteen who died when the tower in siloam fell on them  do you think they were more guilty than all the others living in jerusalem </s>
<s> i tell you  no  but unless you repent  you too will all perish  </s>
<s> then he told this parable   a man had a figtree growing in his vineyard  and he went to look for fruit on it but did not find any </s>
<s> so he said to the man who took care of the vineyard   for three years now ive been coming to look for fruit on this figtree and havent found any  cut it down  why should it use up the soil  </s>
<s>   sir   the man replied   leave it alone for one more year  and ill dig round it and fertilise it </s>
<s> if it bears fruit next year  fine  if not  then cut it down   </s>
<s> on a sabbath jesus was teaching in one of the synagogues </s>
<s> and a woman was there who had been crippled by a spirit for eighteen years  she was bent over and could not straighten up at all </s>
<s> when jesus saw her  he called her forward and said to her   woman  you are set free from your infirmity  </s>
<s> then he put his hands on her  and immediately she straightened up and praised god </s>
<s> indignant because jesus had healed on the sabbath  the synagogue leader said to the people   there are six days for work  so come and be healed on those days  not on the sabbath  </s>
<s> the lord answered him   you hypocrites  doesnt each of you on the sabbath untie your ox or donkey from the stall and lead it out to give it water </s>
<s> then should not this woman  a daughter of abraham  whom satan has kept bound for eighteen long years  be set free on the sabbath day from what bound her  </s>
<s> when he said this  all his opponents were humiliated  but the people were delighted with all the wonderful things he was doing </s>
<s> then jesus asked   what is the kingdom of god like  what shall i compare it to </s>
<s> it is like a mustard seed  which a man took and planted in his garden  it grew and became a tree  and the birds perched in its branches  </s>
<s> again he asked   what shall i compare the kingdom of god to </s>
<s> it is like yeast that a woman took and mixed into about thirty kilograms of flour until it worked all through the dough  </s>
<s> then jesus went through the towns and villages  teaching as he made his way to jerusalem </s>
<s> someone asked him   lord  are only a few people going to be saved   he said to them </s>
<s>  make every effort to enter through the narrow door  because many  i tell you  will try to enter and will not be able to </s>
<s> once the owner of the house gets up and closes the door  you will stand outside knocking and pleading   sir  open the door for us    but he will answer   i dont know you or where you come from  </s>
<s>  then you will say   we ate and drank with you  and you taught in our streets  </s>
<s>  but he will reply   i dont know you or where you come from  away from me  all you evildoers  </s>
<s>  there will be weeping there  and gnashing of teeth  when you see abraham  isaac and jacob and all the prophets in the kingdom of god  but you yourselves thrown out </s>
<s> people will come from east and west and north and south  and will take their places at the feast in the kingdom of god </s>
<s> indeed there are those who are last who will be first  and first who will be last  </s>
<s> at that time some pharisees came to jesus and said to him   leave this place and go somewhere else  herod wants to kill you  </s>
<s> he replied   go and tell that fox   i will keep on driving out demons and healing people today and tomorrow  and on the third day i will reach my goal  </s>
<s> in any case  i must press on today and tomorrow and the next day  for surely no prophet can die outside jerusalem </s>
<s>  jerusalem  jerusalem  you who kill the prophets and stone those sent to you  how often i have longed to gather your children together  as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings  and you were not willing </s>
<s> look  your house is left to you desolate  i tell you  you will not see me again until you say   blessed is he who comes in the name of the lord   </s>
<s> one sabbath  when jesus went to eat in the house of a prominent pharisee  he was being carefully watched </s>
<s> there in front of him was a man suffering from abnormal swelling of his body </s>
<s> jesus asked the pharisees and experts in the law   is it lawful to heal on the sabbath or not  </s>
<s> but they remained silent  so taking hold of the man  he healed him and sent him on his way </s>
<s> then he asked them   if one of you has a child or an ox that falls into a well on the sabbath day  will you not immediately pull it out  </s>
<s> and they had nothing to say </s>
<s> when he noticed how the guests picked the places of honour at the table  he told them this parable </s>
<s>  when someone invites you to a wedding feast  do not take the place of honour  for a person more distinguished than you may have been invited </s>
<s> if so  the host who invited both of you will come and say to you   give this person your seat   then  humiliated  you will have to take the least important place </s>
<s> but when you are invited  take the lowest place  so that when your host comes  he will say to you   friend  move up to a better place   then you will be honoured in the presence of all the other guests </s>
<s> for all those who exalt themselves will be humbled  and those who humble themselves will be exalted  </s>
<s> then jesus said to his host   when you give a luncheon or dinner  do not invite your friends  your brothers or sisters  your relatives  or your rich neighbours  if you do  they may invite you back and so you will be repaid </s>
<s> but when you give a banquet  invite the poor  the crippled  the lame  the blind </s>
<s> and you will be blessed  although they cannot repay you  you will be repaid at the resurrection of the righteous  </s>
<s> when one of those at the table with him heard this  he said to jesus   blessed is the one who will eat at the feast in the kingdom of god  </s>
<s> jesus replied   a certain man was preparing a great banquet and invited many guests </s>
<s> at the time of the banquet he sent his servant to tell those who had been invited   come  for everything is now ready  </s>
<s>  but they all alike began to make excuses  the first said   i have just bought a field  and i must go and see it  please excuse me  </s>
<s>  another said   i have just bought five yoke of oxen  and im on my way to try them out  please excuse me  </s>
<s>  still another said   i have just got married  so i cant come  </s>
<s>  the servant came back and reported this to his master  then the owner of the house became angry and ordered his servant   go out quickly into the streets and alleys of the town and bring in the poor  the crippled  the blind and the lame  </s>
<s>   sir   the servant said   what you ordered has been done  but there is still room  </s>
<s>  then the master told his servant   go out to the roads and country lanes and compel them to come in  so that my house will be full </s>
<s> i tell you  not one of those who were invited will get a taste of my banquet   </s>
<s> large crowds were travelling with jesus  and turning to them he said </s>
<s>  if anyone comes to me and does not hate father and mother  wife and children  brothers and sisters  yes  even their own life  such a person cannot be my disciple </s>
<s> and whoever does not carry their cross and follow me cannot be my disciple </s>
<s>  suppose one of you wants to build a tower  wont you first sit down and estimate the cost to see if you have enough money to complete it </s>
<s> for if you lay the foundation and are not able to finish it  everyone who sees it will ridicule you </s>
<s> saying   this person began to build and wasnt able to finish  </s>
<s>  or suppose a king is about to go to war against another king  wont he first sit down and consider whether he is able with ten thousand men to oppose the one coming against him with twenty thousand </s>
<s> if he is not able  he will send a delegation while the other is still a long way off and will ask for terms of peace </s>
<s> in the same way  those of you who do not give up everything you have cannot be my disciples </s>
<s>  salt is good  but if it loses its saltiness  how can it be made salty again </s>
<s> it is fit neither for the soil nor for the manure heap  it is thrown out   whoever has ears to hear  let them hear  </s>
<s> now the tax collectors and sinners were all gathering round to hear jesus </s>
<s> but the pharisees and the teachers of the law muttered   this man welcomes sinners  and eats with them  </s>
<s> then jesus told them this parable </s>
<s>  suppose one of you has a hundred sheep and loses one of them  doesnt he leave the ninetynine in the open country and go after the lost sheep until he finds it </s>
<s> and when he finds it  he joyfully puts it on his shoulders</s>
<s> and goes home  then he calls his friends and neighbours together and says   rejoice with me  i have found my lost sheep  </s>
<s> i tell you that in the same way there will be more rejoicing in heaven over one sinner who repents than over ninetynine righteous people who do not need to repent </s>
<s>  or suppose a woman has ten silver coins and loses one  doesnt she light a lamp  sweep the house and search carefully until she finds it </s>
<s> and when she finds it  she calls her friends and neighbours together and says   rejoice with me  i have found my lost coin  </s>
<s> in the same way  i tell you  there is rejoicing in the presence of the angels of god over one sinner who repents  </s>
<s> jesus continued   there was a man who had two sons </s>
<s> the younger one said to his father   father  give me my share of the estate   so he divided his property between them </s>
<s>  not long after that  the younger son got together all he had  set off for a distant country and there squandered his wealth in wild living </s>
<s> after he had spent everything  there was a severe famine in that whole country  and he began to be in need </s>
<s> so he went and hired himself out to a citizen of that country  who sent him to his fields to feed pigs </s>
<s> he longed to fill his stomach with the pods that the pigs were eating  but no one gave him anything </s>
<s>  when he came to his senses  he said   how many of my fathers hired servants have food to spare  and here i am starving to death </s>
<s> i will set out and go back to my father and say to him  father  i have sinned against heaven and against you </s>
<s> i am no longer worthy to be called your son  make me like one of your hired servants  </s>
<s> so he got up and went to his father   but while he was still a long way off  his father saw him and was filled with compassion for him  he ran to his son  threw his arms round him and kissed him </s>
<s>  the son said to him   father  i have sinned against heaven and against you  i am no longer worthy to be called your son  </s>
<s>  but the father said to his servants   quick  bring the best robe and put it on him  put a ring on his finger and sandals on his feet </s>
<s> bring the fattened calf and kill it  lets have a feast and celebrate </s>
<s> for this son of mine was dead and is alive again  he was lost and is found   so they began to celebrate </s>
<s>  meanwhile  the elder son was in the field  when he came near the house  he heard music and dancing </s>
<s> so he called one of the servants and asked him what was going on </s>
<s>  your brother has come   he replied   and your father has killed the fattened calf because he has him back safe and sound  </s>
<s>  the elder brother became angry and refused to go in  so his father went out and pleaded with him </s>
<s> but he answered his father   look  all these years ive been slaving for you and never disobeyed your orders  yet you never gave me even a young goat so i could celebrate with my friends </s>
<s> but when this son of yours who has squandered your property with prostitutes comes home  you kill the fattened calf for him  </s>
<s>   my son   the father said   you are always with me  and everything i have is yours </s>

<s> jesus told his disciples   there was a rich man whose manager was accused of wasting his possessions </s>

<s> then came the day of unleavened bread on which the passover lamb had to be sacrificed </s>

<s>  where do you want us to prepare for it   they asked </s>
<s> he replied   as you enter the city  a man carrying a jar of water will meet you  follow him to the house that he enters </s>
<s> and say to the owner of the house   the teacher asks  where is the guest room  where i may eat the passover with my disciples  </s>
<s> he will show you a large room upstairs  all furnished  make preparations there  </s>
<s> they left and found things just as jesus had told them  so they prepared the passover </s>
<s> when the hour came  jesus and his apostles reclined at the table </s>
<s> and he said to them   i have eagerly desired to eat this passover with you before i suffer </s>
<s> for i tell you  i will not eat it again until it finds fulfilment in the kingdom of god  </s>
<s> after taking the cup  he gave thanks and said   take this and divide it among you </s>
<s> for i tell you i will not drink again from the fruit of the vine until the kingdom of god comes  </s>
<s> and he took bread  gave thanks and broke it  and gave it to them  saying   this is my body given for you  do this in remembrance of me  </s>
<s> in the same way  after the supper he took the cup  saying   this cup is the new covenant in my blood  which is poured out for you </s>
<s> but the hand of him who is going to betray me is with mine on the table </s>
<s> the son of man will go as it has been decreed  but woe to that man who betrays him  </s>
<s> they began to question among themselves which of them it might be who would do this </s>
<s> a dispute also arose among them as to which of them was considered to be greatest </s>
<s> jesus said to them   the kings of the gentiles lord it over them  and those who exercise authority over them call themselves benefactors </s>
<s> but you are not to be like that  instead  the greatest among you should be like the youngest  and the one who rules like the one who serves </s>
<s> for who is greater  the one who is at the table or the one who serves  is it not the one who is at the table  but i am among you as one who serves </s>
<s> you are those who have stood by me in my trials </s>
<s> and i confer on you a kingdom  just as my father conferred one on me </s>
<s> so that you may eat and drink at my table in my kingdom and sit on thrones  judging the twelve tribes of israel </s>
<s>  simon  simon  satan has asked to sift all of you as wheat </s>
<s> but i have prayed for you  simon  that your faith may not fail  and when you have turned back  strengthen your brothers  </s>
<s> but he replied   lord  i am ready to go with you to prison and to death  </s>
<s> jesus answered   i tell you  peter  before the cock crows today  you will deny three times that you know me  </s>
<s> then jesus asked them   when i sent you without purse  bag or sandals  did you lack anything    nothing   they answered </s>
<s> he said to them   but now if you have a purse  take it  and also a bag  and if you dont have a sword  sell your cloak and buy one </s>
<s> it is written   and he was numbered with the transgressors   and i tell you that this must be fulfilled in me  yes  what is written about me is reaching its fulfilment  </s>
<s> the disciples said   see  lord  here are two swords    thats enough   he replied </s>
<s> jesus went out as usual to the mount of olives  and his disciples followed him </s>
<s> on reaching the place  he said to them   pray that you will not fall into temptation  </s>
<s> he withdrew about a stones throw beyond them  knelt down and prayed </s>
<s>  father  if you are willing  take this cup from me  yet not my will  but yours be done  </s>
<s> an angel from heaven appeared to him and strengthened him </s>
<s> and being in anguish  he prayed more earnestly  and his sweat was like drops of blood falling to the ground </s>
<s> when he rose from prayer and went back to the disciples  he found them asleep  exhausted from sorrow </s>
<s>  why are you sleeping   he asked them   get up and pray so that you will not fall into temptation  </s>
<s> while he was still speaking a crowd came up  and the man who was called judas  one of the twelve  was leading them  he approached jesus to kiss him </s>
<s> but jesus asked him   judas  are you betraying the son of man with a kiss  </s>
<s> when jesus followers saw what was going to happen  they said   lord  should we strike with our swords  </s>
<s> and one of them struck the servant of the high priest  cutting off his right ear </s>
<s> but jesus answered   no more of this   and he touched the mans ear and healed him </s>
<s> then jesus said to the chief priests  the officers of the temple guard  and the elders  who had come for him   am i leading a rebellion  that you have come with swords and clubs </s>
<s> every day i was with you in the temple courts  and you did not lay a hand on me  but this is your hour  when darkness reigns  </s>
<s> then seizing him  they led him away and took him into the house of the high priest  peter followed at a distance </s>
<s> and when some there had kindled a fire in the middle of the courtyard and had sat down together  peter sat down with them </s>
<s> a servantgirl saw him seated there in the firelight  she looked closely at him and said   this man was with him  </s>
<s> but he denied it   woman  i dont know him   he said </s>
<s> a little later someone else saw him and said   you also are one of them    man  i am not   peter replied </s>
<s> about an hour later another asserted   certainly this fellow was with him  for he is a galilean  </s>
<s> peter replied   man  i dont know what youre talking about   just as he was speaking  the cock crowed </s>
<s> the lord turned and looked straight at peter  then peter remembered the word the lord had spoken to him   before the cock crows today  you will disown me three times  </s>
<s> and he went outside and wept bitterly </s>
<s> the men who were guarding jesus began mocking and beating him </s>
<s> they blindfolded him and demanded   prophesy  who hit you  </s>
<s> and they said many other insulting things to him </s>
<s> at daybreak the council of the elders of the people  both the chief priests and the teachers of the law  met together  and jesus was led before them </s>
<s>  if you are the messiah   they said   tell us   jesus answered   if i tell you  you will not believe me </s>
<s> and if i asked you  you would not answer </s>
<s> but from now on  the son of man will be seated at the right hand of the mighty god  </s>
<s> they all asked   are you then the son of god   he replied   you say that i am  </s>
<s> then they said   why do we need any more testimony  we have heard it from his own lips  </s>
<s> then the whole assembly rose and led him off to pilate </s>
<s> and they began to accuse him  saying   we have found this man subverting our nation  he opposes payment of taxes to caesar and claims to be messiah  a king  </s>
<s> so pilate asked jesus   are you the king of the jews    you have said so   jesus replied </s>
<s> then pilate announced to the chief priests and the crowd   i find no basis for a charge against this man  </s>
<s> but they insisted   he stirs up the people all over judea by his teaching  he started in galilee and has come all the way here  </s>
<s> on hearing this  pilate asked if the man was a galilean </s>
<s> when he learned that jesus was under herods jurisdiction  he sent him to herod  who was also in jerusalem at that time </s>
<s> when herod saw jesus  he was greatly pleased  because for a long time he had been wanting to see him  from what he had heard about him  he hoped to see him perform a sign of some sort </s>
<s> he plied him with many questions  but jesus gave him no answer </s>
<s> the chief priests and the teachers of the law were standing there  vehemently accusing him </s>
<s> then herod and his soldiers ridiculed and mocked him  dressing him in an elegant robe  they sent him back to pilate </s>
<s> that day herod and pilate became friends  before this they had been enemies </s>
<s> pilate called together the chief priests  the rulers and the people </s>
<s> and said to them   you brought me this man as one who was inciting the people to rebellion  i have examined him in your presence and have found no basis for your charges against him </s>
<s> neither has herod  for he sent him back to us  as you can see  he has done nothing to deserve death </s>
<s> therefore  i will punish him and then release him   </s>
<s> </s>
<s> but the whole crowd shouted   away with this man  release barabbas to us  </s>
<s>  barabbas had been thrown into prison for an insurrection in the city  and for murder  </s>
<s> wanting to release jesus  pilate appealed to them again </s>
<s> but they kept shouting   crucify him  crucify him  </s>
<s> for the third time he spoke to them   why  what crime has this man committed  i have found in him no grounds for the death penalty  therefore i will have him punished and then release him  </s>
<s> but with loud shouts they insistently demanded that he be crucified  and their shouts prevailed </s>
<s> so pilate decided to grant their demand </s>
<s> he released the man who had been thrown into prison for insurrection and murder  the one they asked for  and surrendered jesus to their will </s>
<s> as the soldiers led him away  they seized simon from cyrene  who was on his way in from the country  and put the cross on him and made him carry it behind jesus </s>
<s> a large number of people followed him  including women who mourned and wailed for him </s>
<s> jesus turned and said to them   daughters of jerusalem  do not weep for me  weep for yourselves and for your children </s>
<s> for the time will come when you will say   blessed are the childless women  the wombs that never bore and the breasts that never nursed  </s>
<s> then   they will say to the mountains   fall on us   and to the hills   cover us   </s>
<s> two other men  both criminals  were also led out with him to be executed </s>
<s> when they came to the place called the skull  they crucified him there  along with the criminals  one on his right  the other on his left </s>
<s> jesus said   father  forgive them  for they do not know what they are doing   and they divided up his clothes by casting lots </s>
<s> the people stood watching  and the rulers even sneered at him  they said   he saved others  let him save himself if he is gods messiah  the chosen one  </s>
<s> the soldiers also came up and mocked him  they offered him wine vinegar</s>
<s> and said   if you are the king of the jews  save yourself  </s>
<s> there was a written notice above him  which read  this is the king of the jews </s>
<s> one of the criminals who hung there hurled insults at him   arent you the messiah  save yourself and us  </s>
<s> but the other criminal rebuked him   dont you fear god   he said   since you are under the same sentence </s>
<s> we are punished justly  for we are getting what our deeds deserve  but this man has done nothing wrong  </s>
<s> then he said   jesus  remember me when you come into your kingdom  </s>
<s> jesus answered him   truly i tell you  today you will be with me in paradise  </s>
<s> it was now about noon  and darkness came over the whole land until three in the afternoon </s>
<s> for the sun stopped shining  and the curtain of the temple was torn in two </s>
<s> jesus called out with a loud voice   father  into your hands i commit my spirit   when he had said this  he breathed his last </s>
<s> the centurion  seeing what had happened  praised god and said   surely this was a righteous man  </s>
<s> when all the people who had gathered to witness this sight saw what took place  they beat their breasts and went away </s>
<s> but all those who knew him  including the women who had followed him from galilee  stood at a distance  watching these things </s>
<s> now there was a man named joseph  a member of the council  a good and upright man </s>
<s> who had not consented to their decision and action  he came from the judean town of arimathea  and he himself was waiting for the kingdom of god </s>
<s> going to pilate  he asked for jesus body </s>
<s> then he took it down  wrapped it in linen cloth and placed it in a tomb cut in the rock  one in which no one had yet been laid </s>
<s> it was preparation day  and the sabbath was about to begin </s>
<s> the women who had come with jesus from galilee followed joseph and saw the tomb and how his body was laid in it </s>
<s> then they went home and prepared spices and perfumes  but they rested on the sabbath in obedience to the commandment </s>
<s> on the first day of the week  very early in the morning  the women took the spices they had prepared and went to the tomb </s>
<s> they found the stone rolled away from the tomb </s>
<s> but when they entered  they did not find the body of the lord jesus </s>
<s> while they were wondering about this  suddenly two men in clothes that gleamed like lightning stood beside them </s>
<s> in their fright the women bowed down with their faces to the ground  but the men said to them   why do you look for the living among the dead </s>
<s> he is not here  he has risen  remember how he told you  while he was still with you in galilee </s>
<s>  the son of man must be delivered over to the hands of sinners  be crucified and on the third day be raised again   </s>
<s> then they remembered his words </s>
<s> when they came back from the tomb  they told all these things to the eleven and to all the others </s>
<s> it was mary magdalene  joanna  mary the mother of james  and the others with them who told this to the apostles </s>
<s> but they did not believe the women  because their words seemed to them like nonsense </s>
<s> peter  however  got up and ran to the tomb  bending over  he saw the strips of linen lying by themselves  and he went away  wondering to himself what had happened </s>
<s> now that same day two of them were going to a village called emmaus  about seven miles from jerusalem </s>
<s> they were talking with each other about everything that had happened </s>
<s> as they talked and discussed these things with each other  jesus himself came up and walked along with them </s>
<s> but they were kept from recognising him </s>
<s> he asked them   what are you discussing together as you walk along   they stood still  their faces downcast </s>
<s> one of them  named cleopas  asked him   are you the only one visiting jerusalem who does not know the things that have happened there in these days  </s>
<s>  what things   he asked   about jesus of nazareth   they replied   he was a prophet  powerful in word and deed before god and all the people </s>
<s> the chief priests and our rulers handed him over to be sentenced to death  and they crucified him </s>
<s> but we had hoped that he was the one who was going to redeem israel  and what is more  it is the third day since all this took place </s>
<s> in addition  some of our women amazed us  they went to the tomb early this morning</s>
<s> but didnt find his body  they came and told us that they had seen a vision of angels  who said he was alive </s>
<s> then some of our companions went to the tomb and found it just as the women had said  but they did not see jesus  </s>
<s> he said to them   how foolish you are  and how slow to believe all that the prophets have spoken </s>
<s> did not the messiah have to suffer these things and then enter his glory  </s>
<s> and beginning with moses and all the prophets  he explained to them what was said in all the scriptures concerning himself </s>
<s> as they approached the village to which they were going  jesus continued on as if he were going further </s>
<s> but they urged him strongly   stay with us  for it is nearly evening  the day is almost over   so he went in to stay with them </s>
<s> when he was at the table with them  he took bread  gave thanks  broke it and began to give it to them </s>
<s> then their eyes were opened and they recognised him  and he disappeared from their sight </s>
<s> they asked each other   were not our hearts burning within us while he talked with us on the road and opened the scriptures to us  </s>
<s> they got up and returned at once to jerusalem  there they found the eleven and those with them  assembled together</s>
<s> and saying   it is true  the lord has risen and has appeared to simon  </s>
