<s> while they were still talking about this  jesus himself stood among them and said to them   peace be with you  </s>
<s> they were startled and frightened  thinking they saw a ghost </s>
<s> he said to them   why are you troubled  and why do doubts rise in your minds </s>
<s> look at my hands and my feet  it is i myself  touch me and see  a ghost does not have flesh and bones  as you see i have  </s>
<s> when he had said this  he showed them his hands and feet </s>
<s> and while they still did not believe it because of joy and amazement  he asked them   do you have anything here to eat  </s>
<s> they gave him a piece of broiled fish </s>
<s> and he took it and ate it in their presence </s>
<s> he said to them   this is what i told you while i was still with you  everything must be fulfilled that is written about me in the law of moses  the prophets and the psalms  </s>
<s> then he opened their minds so they could understand the scriptures </s>
<s> he told them   this is what is written  the messiah will suffer and rise from the dead on the third day </s>
<s> and repentance for the forgiveness of sins will be preached in his name to all nations  beginning at jerusalem </s>
<s> you are witnesses of these things </s>
<s> i am going to send you what my father has promised  but stay in the city until you have been clothed with power from on high  </s>
<s> when he had led them out to the vicinity of bethany  he lifted up his hands and blessed them </s>
<s> while he was blessing them  he left them and was taken up into heaven </s>
<s> then they worshipped him and returned to jerusalem with great joy </s>
<s> and they stayed continually at the temple  praising god </s>
<s> in the beginning was the word  and the word was with god  and the word was god </s>
<s> he was with god in the beginning </s>
<s> through him all things were made  without him nothing was made that has been made </s>
<s> in him was life  and that life was the light of all mankind </s>
<s> the light shines in the darkness  and the darkness has not overcome it </s>
<s> there was a man sent from god whose name was john </s>
<s> he came as a witness to testify concerning that light  so that through him all might believe </s>
<s> he himself was not the light  he came only as a witness to the light </s>
<s> the true light that gives light to everyone was coming into the world </s>
<s> he was in the world  and though the world was made through him  the world did not recognise him </s>
<s> he came to that which was his own  but his own did not receive him </s>
<s> yet to all who did receive him  to those who believed in his name  he gave the right to become children of god </s>
<s> children born not of natural descent  nor of human decision or a husbands will  but born of god </s>
<s> the word became flesh and made his dwelling among us  we have seen his glory  the glory of the one and only son  who came from the father  full of grace and truth </s>
<s>  john testified concerning him  he cried out  saying   this is the one i spoke about when i said   he who comes after me has surpassed me because he was before me    </s>
<s> out of his fullness we have all received grace in place of grace already given </s>
<s> for the law was given through moses  grace and truth came through jesus christ </s>
<s> no one has ever seen god  but the one and only son  who is himself god and is in the closest relationship with the father  has made him known </s>
<s> now this was johns testimony when the jewish leaders in jerusalem sent priests and levites to ask him who he was </s>
<s> he did not fail to confess  but confessed freely   i am not the messiah  </s>
<s> they asked him   then who are you  are you elijah   he said   i am not    are you the prophet   he answered   no  </s>
<s> finally they said   who are you  give us an answer to take back to those who sent us  what do you say about yourself  </s>
<s> john replied in the words of isaiah the prophet   i am the voice of one calling in the wilderness   make straight the way for the lord   </s>
<s> now the pharisees who had been sent</s>
<s> questioned him   why then do you baptise if you are not the messiah  nor elijah  nor the prophet  </s>
<s>  i baptise with water   john replied   but among you stands one you do not know </s>
<s> he is the one who comes after me  the straps of whose sandals i am not worthy to untie  </s>
<s> this all happened at bethany on the other side of the jordan  where john was baptising </s>
<s> the next day john saw jesus coming towards him and said   look  the lamb of god  who takes away the sin of the world </s>
<s> this is the one i meant when i said   a man who comes after me has surpassed me because he was before me  </s>
<s> i myself did not know him  but the reason i came baptising with water was that he might be revealed to israel  </s>
<s> then john gave this testimony   i saw the spirit come down from heaven as a dove and remain on him </s>
<s> and i myself did not know him  but the one who sent me to baptise with water told me   the man on whom you see the spirit come down and remain is the one who will baptise with the holy spirit  </s>
<s> i have seen and i testify that this is gods chosen one  </s>
<s> the next day john was there again with two of his disciples </s>
<s> when he saw jesus passing by  he said   look  the lamb of god  </s>
<s> when the two disciples heard him say this  they followed jesus </s>
<s> turning round  jesus saw them following and asked   what do you want   they said   rabbi  which means  teacher    where are you staying  </s>
<s>  come   he replied   and you will see   so they went and saw where he was staying  and they spent that day with him  it was about four in the afternoon </s>
<s> andrew  simon peters brother  was one of the two who heard what john had said and who had followed jesus </s>
<s> the first thing andrew did was to find his brother simon and tell him   we have found the messiah  that is  the christ  </s>
<s> and he brought him to jesus  jesus looked at him and said   you are simon son of john  you will be called cephas  which  when translated  is peter  </s>

<s> philip  like andrew and peter  was from the town of bethsaida </s>
<s> philip found nathanael and told him   we have found the one moses wrote about in the law  and about whom the prophets also wrote  jesus of nazareth  the son of joseph  </s>
<s>  nazareth  can anything good come from there   nathanael asked   come and see   said philip </s>
<s> when jesus saw nathanael approaching  he said of him   here truly is an israelite in whom there is no deceit  </s>
<s>  how do you know me   nathanael asked  jesus answered   i saw you while you were still under the figtree before philip called you  </s>
<s> then nathanael declared   rabbi  you are the son of god  you are the king of israel  </s>
<s> jesus said   you believe because i told you i saw you under the figtree  you will see greater things than that  </s>
<s> he then added   very truly i tell you  you will see  heaven open  and the angels of god ascending and descending on  the son of man  </s>
<s> on the third day a wedding took place at cana in galilee  jesus mother was there </s>
<s> and jesus and his disciples had also been invited to the wedding </s>
<s> when the wine was gone  jesus mother said to him   they have no more wine  </s>
<s>  woman  why do you involve me   jesus replied   my hour has not yet come  </s>
<s> his mother said to the servants   do whatever he tells you  </s>
<s> nearby stood six stone water jars  the kind used by the jews for ceremonial washing  each holding from eighty to a hundred and twenty litres </s>
<s> jesus said to the servants   fill the jars with water  so they filled them to the brim </s>
<s> then he told them   now draw some out and take it to the master of the banquet   they did so </s>
<s> and the master of the banquet tasted the water that had been turned into wine  he did not realise where it had come from  though the servants who had drawn the water knew  then he called the bridegroom aside</s>
<s> and said   everyone brings out the choice wine first and then the cheaper wine after the guests have had too much to drink  but you have saved the best till now  </s>
<s> what jesus did here in cana of galilee was the first of the signs through which he revealed his glory  and his disciples believed in him </s>
<s> after this he went down to capernaum with his mother and brothers and his disciples  there they stayed for a few days </s>
<s> when it was almost time for the jewish passover  jesus went up to jerusalem </s>
<s> in the temple courts he found people selling cattle  sheep and doves  and others sitting at tables exchanging money </s>
<s> so he made a whip out of cords  and drove all from the temple courts  both sheep and cattle  he scattered the coins of the moneychangers and overturned their tables </s>
<s> to those who sold doves he said   get these out of here  stop turning my fathers house into a market  </s>
<s> his disciples remembered that it is written   zeal for your house will consume me  </s>
<s> the jews then responded to him   what sign can you show us to prove your authority to do all this  </s>
<s> jesus answered them   destroy this temple  and i will raise it again in three days  </s>
<s> they replied   it has taken fortysix years to build this temple  and you are going to raise it in three days  </s>
<s> but the temple he had spoken of was his body </s>
<s> after he was raised from the dead  his disciples recalled what he had said  then they believed the scripture and the words that jesus had spoken </s>
<s> now while he was in jerusalem at the passover festival  many people saw the signs he was performing and believed in his name </s>
<s> but jesus would not entrust himself to them  for he knew all people </s>
<s> he did not need any testimony about mankind  for he knew what was in each person </s>
<s> now there was a pharisee  a man named nicodemus who was a member of the jewish ruling council </s>
<s> he came to jesus at night and said   rabbi  we know that you are a teacher who has come from god  for no one could perform the signs you are doing if god were not with him  </s>
<s> jesus replied   very truly i tell you  no one can see the kingdom of god unless they are born again  </s>
<s>  how can someone be born when they are old   nicodemus asked   surely they cannot enter a second time into their mothers womb to be born  </s>
<s> jesus answered   very truly i tell you  no one can enter the kingdom of god unless they are born of water and the spirit </s>
<s> flesh gives birth to flesh  but the spirit gives birth to spirit </s>
<s> you should not be surprised at my saying   you must be born again  </s>
<s> the wind blows wherever it pleases  you hear its sound  but you cannot tell where it comes from or where it is going  so it is with everyone born of the spirit  </s>
<s>  how can this be   nicodemus asked </s>
<s>  you are israels teacher   said jesus   and do you not understand these things </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  we speak of what we know  and we testify to what we have seen  but still you people do not accept our testimony </s>
<s> i have spoken to you of earthly things and you do not believe  how then will you believe if i speak of heavenly things </s>
<s> no one has ever gone into heaven except the one who came from heaven  the son of man </s>
<s> just as moses lifted up the snake in the wilderness  so the son of man must be lifted up </s>
<s> that everyone who believes may have eternal life in him  </s>
<s> for god so loved the world that he gave his one and only son  that whoever believes in him shall not perish but have eternal life </s>
<s> for god did not send his son into the world to condemn the world  but to save the world through him </s>
<s> whoever believes in him is not condemned  but whoever does not believe stands condemned already because they have not believed in the name of gods one and only son </s>
<s> this is the verdict  light has come into the world  but people loved darkness instead of light because their deeds were evil </s>
<s> everyone who does evil hates the light  and will not come into the light for fear that their deeds will be exposed </s>
<s> but whoever lives by the truth comes into the light  so that it may be seen plainly that what they have done has been done in the sight of god </s>
<s> after this  jesus and his disciples went out into the judean countryside  where he spent some time with them  and baptised </s>
<s> now john also was baptising at aenon near salim  because there was plenty of water  and people were coming and being baptised </s>
<s>  this was before john was put in prison  </s>
<s> an argument developed between some of johns disciples and a certain jew over the matter of ceremonial washing </s>
<s> they came to john and said to him   rabbi  that man who was with you on the other side of the jordan  the one you testified about  look  he is baptising  and everyone is going to him  </s>
<s> to this john replied   a person can receive only what is given them from heaven </s>
<s> you yourselves can testify that i said   i am not the messiah but am sent ahead of him  </s>
<s> the bride belongs to the bridegroom  the friend who attends the bridegroom waits and listens for him  and is full of joy when he hears the bridegrooms voice  that joy is mine  and it is now complete </s>
<s> he must become greater  i must become less  </s>
<s> the one who comes from above is above all  the one who is from the earth belongs to the earth  and speaks as one from the earth  the one who comes from heaven is above all </s>
<s> he testifies to what he has seen and heard  but no one accepts his testimony </s>
<s> whoever has accepted it has certified that god is truthful </s>
<s> for the one whom god has sent speaks the words of god  for god gives the spirit without limit </s>
<s> the father loves the son and has placed everything in his hands </s>
<s> whoever believes in the son has eternal life  but whoever rejects the son will not see life  for gods wrath remains on them </s>
<s> now jesus learned that the pharisees had heard that he was gaining and baptising more disciples than john </s>
<s> although in fact it was not jesus who baptised  but his disciples </s>
<s> so he left judea and went back once more to galilee </s>
<s> now he had to go through samaria </s>
<s> so he came to a town in samaria called sychar  near the plot of ground jacob had given to his son joseph </s>
<s> jacobs well was there  and jesus  tired as he was from the journey  sat down by the well  it was about noon </s>
<s> when a samaritan woman came to draw water  jesus said to her   will you give me a drink  </s>
<s>  his disciples had gone into the town to buy food  </s>
<s> the samaritan woman said to him   you are a jew and i am a samaritan woman  how can you ask me for a drink    for jews do not associate with samaritans  </s>
<s> jesus answered her   if you knew the gift of god and who it is that asks you for a drink  you would have asked him and he would have given you living water  </s>
<s>  sir   the woman said   you have nothing to draw with and the well is deep  where can you get this living water </s>
<s> are you greater than our father jacob  who gave us the well and drank from it himself  as did also his sons and his livestock  </s>
<s> jesus answered   everyone who drinks this water will be thirsty again </s>
<s> but whoever drinks the water i give them will never thirst  indeed  the water i give them will become in them a spring of water welling up to eternal life  </s>
<s> the woman said to him   sir  give me this water so that i wont get thirsty and have to keep coming here to draw water  </s>
<s> he told her   go  call your husband and come back  </s>
<s>  i have no husband   she replied  jesus said to her   you are right when you say you have no husband </s>
<s> the fact is  you have had five husbands  and the man you now have is not your husband  what you have just said is quite true  </s>
<s>  sir   the woman said   i can see that you are a prophet </s>
<s> our ancestors worshipped on this mountain  but you jews claim that the place where we must worship is in jerusalem  </s>
<s>  woman   jesus replied   believe me  a time is coming when you will worship the father neither on this mountain nor in jerusalem </s>
<s> you samaritans worship what you do not know  we worship what we do know  for salvation is from the jews </s>
<s> yet a time is coming and has now come when the true worshippers will worship the father in the spirit and in truth  for they are the kind of worshippers the father seeks </s>
<s> god is spirit  and his worshippers must worship in the spirit and in truth  </s>
<s> the woman said   i know that messiah  called christ   is coming  when he comes  he will explain everything to us  </s>
<s> then jesus declared   i  the one speaking to you  i am he  </s>
<s> just then his disciples returned and were surprised to find him talking with a woman  but no one asked   what do you want   or  why are you talking with her  </s>
<s> then  leaving her water jar  the woman went back to the town and said to the people </s>
<s>  come  see a man who told me everything ive ever done  could this be the messiah  </s>
<s> they came out of the town and made their way towards him </s>
<s> meanwhile his disciples urged him   rabbi  eat something  </s>
<s> but he said to them   i have food to eat that you know nothing about  </s>
<s> then his disciples said to each other   could someone have brought him food  </s>
<s>  my food   said jesus   is to do the will of him who sent me and to finish his work </s>
<s> dont you have a saying   its still four months until harvest   i tell you  open your eyes and look at the fields  they are ripe for harvest </s>
<s> even now the one who reaps draws a wage and harvests a crop for eternal life  so that the sower and the reaper may be glad together </s>
<s> thus the saying  one sows and another reaps  is true </s>
<s> i sent you to reap what you have not worked for  others have done the hard work  and you have reaped the benefits of their labour  </s>
<s> many of the samaritans from that town believed in him because of the womans testimony   he told me everything ive ever done  </s>
<s> so when the samaritans came to him  they urged him to stay with them  and he stayed two days </s>
<s> and because of his words many more became believers </s>
<s> they said to the woman   we no longer believe just because of what you said  now we have heard for ourselves  and we know that this man really is the saviour of the world  </s>
<s> after the two days he left for galilee </s>
<s>  now jesus himself had pointed out that a prophet has no honour in his own country  </s>
<s> when he arrived in galilee  the galileans welcomed him  they had seen all that he had done in jerusalem at the passover festival  for they also had been there </s>
<s> once more he visited cana in galilee  where he had turned the water into wine  and there was a certain royal official whose son lay ill at capernaum </s>
<s> when this man heard that jesus had arrived in galilee from judea  he went to him and begged him to come and heal his son  who was close to death </s>
<s>  unless you people see signs and wonders   jesus told him   you will never believe  </s>
<s> the royal official said   sir  come down before my child dies  </s>
<s>  go   jesus replied   your son will live   the man took jesus at his word and departed </s>
<s> while he was still on the way  his servants met him with the news that his boy was living </s>
<s> when he enquired as to the time when his son got better  they said to him   yesterday  at one in the afternoon  the fever left him  </s>
<s> then the father realised that this was the exact time at which jesus had said to him   your son will live   so he and his whole household believed </s>
<s> this was the second sign jesus performed after coming from judea to galilee </s>
<s> some time later  jesus went up to jerusalem for one of the jewish festivals </s>
<s> now there is in jerusalem near the sheep gate a pool  which in aramaic is called bethesda and which is surrounded by five covered colonnades </s>
<s> here a great number of disabled people used to lie  the blind  the lame  the paralysed  </s>
<s> </s>
<s> one who was there had been an invalid for thirtyeight years </s>
<s> when jesus saw him lying there and learned that he had been in this condition for a long time  he asked him   do you want to get well  </s>
<s>  sir   the invalid replied   i have no one to help me into the pool when the water is stirred  while i am trying to get in  someone else goes down ahead of me  </s>
<s> then jesus said to him   get up  pick up your mat and walk  </s>
<s> at once the man was cured  he picked up his mat and walked  the day on which this took place was a sabbath </s>
<s> and so the jewish leaders said to the man who had been healed   it is the sabbath  the law forbids you to carry your mat  </s>
<s> but he replied   the man who made me well said to me   pick up your mat and walk   </s>
<s> so they asked him   who is this fellow who told you to pick it up and walk  </s>
<s> the man who was healed had no idea who it was  for jesus had slipped away into the crowd that was there </s>
<s> later jesus found him at the temple and said to him   see  you are well again  stop sinning or something worse may happen to you  </s>
<s> the man went away and told the jewish leaders that it was jesus who had made him well </s>
<s> so  because jesus was doing these things on the sabbath  the jewish leaders began to persecute him </s>
<s> in his defence jesus said to them   my father is always at his work to this very day  and i too am working  </s>
<s> for this reason they tried all the more to kill him  not only was he breaking the sabbath  but he was even calling god his own father  making himself equal with god </s>
<s> jesus gave them this answer   very truly i tell you  the son can do nothing by himself  he can do only what he sees his father doing  because whatever the father does the son also does </s>
<s> for the father loves the son and shows him all he does  yes  and he will show him even greater works than these  so that you will be amazed </s>
<s> for just as the father raises the dead and gives them life  even so the son gives life to whom he is pleased to give it </s>
<s> moreover  the father judges no one  but has entrusted all judgment to the son </s>
<s> that all may honour the son just as they honour the father  whoever does not honour the son does not honour the father  who sent him </s>
<s>  very truly i tell you  whoever hears my word and believes him who sent me has eternal life and will not be judged but has crossed over from death to life </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  a time is coming and has now come when the dead will hear the voice of the son of god and those who hear will live </s>
<s> for as the father has life in himself  so he has granted the son also to have life in himself </s>
<s> and he has given him authority to judge because he is the son of man </s>
<s>  do not be amazed at this  for a time is coming when all who are in their graves will hear his voice</s>
<s> and come out  those who have done what is good will rise to live  and those who have done what is evil will rise to be condemned </s>
<s> by myself i can do nothing  i judge only as i hear  and my judgment is just  for i seek not to please myself but him who sent me </s>
<s>  if i testify about myself  my testimony is not true </s>
<s> there is another who testifies in my favour  and i know that his testimony about me is true </s>
<s>  you have sent to john and he has testified to the truth </s>
<s> not that i accept human testimony  but i mention it that you may be saved </s>
<s> john was a lamp that burned and gave light  and you chose for a time to enjoy his light </s>
<s>  i have testimony weightier than that of john  for the works that the father has given me to finish  the very works that i am doing  testify that the father has sent me </s>
<s> and the father who sent me has himself testified concerning me  you have never heard his voice nor seen his form </s>
<s> nor does his word dwell in you  for you do not believe the one he sent </s>
<s> you study the scriptures diligently because you think that in them you have eternal life  these are the very scriptures that testify about me </s>
<s> yet you refuse to come to me to have life </s>
<s>  i do not accept glory from human beings </s>
<s> but i know you  i know that you do not have the love of god in your hearts </s>
<s> i have come in my fathers name  and you do not accept me  but if someone else comes in his own name  you will accept him </s>
<s> how can you believe since you accept glory from one another but do not seek the glory that comes from the only god </s>
<s>  but do not think i will accuse you before the father  your accuser is moses  on whom your hopes are set </s>
<s> if you believed moses  you would believe me  for he wrote about me </s>
<s> but since you do not believe what he wrote  how are you going to believe what i say  </s>
<s> some time after this  jesus crossed to the far shore of the sea of galilee  that is  the sea of tiberias  </s>
<s> and a great crowd of people followed him because they saw the signs he had performed by healing those who were ill </s>
<s> then jesus went up on a mountainside and sat down with his disciples </s>
<s> the jewish passover festival was near </s>
<s> when jesus looked up and saw a great crowd coming towards him  he said to philip   where shall we buy bread for these people to eat  </s>
<s> he asked this only to test him  for he already had in mind what he was going to do </s>
<s> philip answered him   it would take more than half a years wages to buy enough bread for each one to have a bite  </s>
<s> another of his disciples  andrew  simon peters brother  spoke up </s>
<s>  here is a boy with five small barley loaves and two small fish  but how far will they go among so many  </s>
<s> jesus said   make the people sit down   there was plenty of grass in that place  and they sat down  about five thousand men were there  </s>
<s> jesus then took the loaves  gave thanks  and distributed to those who were seated as much as they wanted  he did the same with the fish </s>
<s> when they had all had enough to eat  he said to his disciples   gather the pieces that are left over  let nothing be wasted  </s>
<s> so they gathered them and filled twelve baskets with the pieces of the five barley loaves left over by those who had eaten </s>
<s> after the people saw the sign jesus performed  they began to say   surely this is the prophet who is to come into the world  </s>
<s> jesus  knowing that they intended to come and make him king by force  withdrew again to a mountain by himself </s>
<s> when evening came  his disciples went down to the lake </s>
<s> where they got into a boat and set off across the lake for capernaum  by now it was dark  and jesus had not yet joined them </s>
<s> a strong wind was blowing and the waters grew rough </s>
<s> when they had rowed about three or four miles  they saw jesus approaching the boat  walking on the water  and they were frightened </s>
<s> but he said to them   it is i  dont be afraid  </s>
<s> then they were willing to take him into the boat  and immediately the boat reached the shore where they were heading </s>
<s> the next day the crowd that had stayed on the opposite shore of the lake realised that only one boat had been there  and that jesus had not entered it with his disciples  but that they had gone away alone </s>
<s> then some boats from tiberias landed near the place where the people had eaten the bread after the lord had given thanks </s>
<s> once the crowd realised that neither jesus nor his disciples were there  they got into the boats and went to capernaum in search of jesus </s>
<s> when they found him on the other side of the lake  they asked him   rabbi  when did you get here  </s>
<s> jesus answered   very truly i tell you  you are looking for me  not because you saw the signs i performed but because you ate the loaves and had your fill </s>
<s> do not work for food that spoils  but for food that endures to eternal life  which the son of man will give you  for on him god the father has placed his seal of approval  </s>
<s> then they asked him   what must we do to do the works god requires  </s>
<s> jesus answered   the work of god is this  to believe in the one he has sent  </s>
<s> so they asked him   what sign then will you give that we may see it and believe you  what will you do </s>
<s> our ancestors ate the manna in the wilderness  as it is written   he gave them bread from heaven to eat   </s>
<s> jesus said to them   very truly i tell you  it is not moses who has given you the bread from heaven  but it is my father who gives you the true bread from heaven </s>
<s> for the bread of god is the bread that comes down from heaven and gives life to the world  </s>
<s>  sir   they said   always give us this bread  </s>
<s> then jesus declared   i am the bread of life  whoever comes to me will never go hungry  and whoever believes in me will never be thirsty </s>
<s> but as i told you  you have seen me and still you do not believe </s>
<s> all those the father gives me will come to me  and whoever comes to me i will never drive away </s>
<s> for i have come down from heaven not to do my will but to do the will of him who sent me </s>
<s> and this is the will of him who sent me  that i shall lose none of all those he has given me  but raise them up at the last day </s>
<s> for my fathers will is that everyone who looks to the son and believes in him shall have eternal life  and i will raise them up at the last day  </s>
<s> at this the jews there began to grumble about him because he said   i am the bread that came down from heaven  </s>
<s> they said   is this not jesus  the son of joseph  whose father and mother we know  how can he now say   i came down from heaven   </s>
<s>  stop grumbling among yourselves   jesus answered </s>
<s>  no one can come to me unless the father who sent me draws them  and i will raise them up at the last day </s>
<s> it is written in the prophets   they will all be taught by god   everyone who has heard the father and learned from him comes to me </s>
<s> no one has seen the father except the one who is from god  only he has seen the father </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  the one who believes has eternal life </s>
<s> i am the bread of life </s>
<s> your ancestors ate the manna in the wilderness  yet they died </s>
<s> but here is the bread that comes down from heaven  which anyone may eat and not die </s>
<s> i am the living bread that came down from heaven  whoever eats this bread will live for ever  this bread is my flesh  which i will give for the life of the world  </s>
<s> then the jews began to argue sharply among themselves   how can this man give us his flesh to eat  </s>
<s> jesus said to them   very truly i tell you  unless you eat the flesh of the son of man and drink his blood  you have no life in you </s>
<s> whoever eats my flesh and drinks my blood has eternal life  and i will raise them up at the last day </s>
<s> for my flesh is real food and my blood is real drink </s>
<s> whoever eats my flesh and drinks my blood remains in me  and i in them </s>
<s> just as the living father sent me and i live because of the father  so the one who feeds on me will live because of me </s>
<s> this is the bread that came down from heaven  your ancestors ate manna and died  but whoever feeds on this bread will live for ever  </s>
<s> he said this while teaching in the synagogue in capernaum </s>
<s> on hearing it  many of his disciples said   this is a hard teaching  who can accept it  </s>
<s> aware that his disciples were grumbling about this  jesus said to them   does this offend you </s>
<s> then what if you see the son of man ascend to where he was before </s>
<s> the spirit gives life  the flesh counts for nothing  the words i have spoken to you  they are full of the spirit and life </s>
<s> yet there are some of you who do not believe   for jesus had known from the beginning which of them did not believe and who would betray him </s>
<s> he went on to say   this is why i told you that no one can come to me unless the father has enabled them  </s>
<s> from this time many of his disciples turned back and no longer followed him </s>
<s>  you do not want to leave too  do you   jesus asked the twelve </s>
<s> simon peter answered him   lord  to whom shall we go  you have the words of eternal life </s>
<s> we have come to believe and to know that you are the holy one of god  </s>
<s> then jesus replied   have i not chosen you  the twelve  yet one of you is a devil  </s>
<s>  he meant judas  the son of simon iscariot  who  though one of the twelve  was later to betray him  </s>
<s> after this  jesus went around in galilee  he did not want to go about in judea because the jewish leaders there were looking for a way to kill him </s>
<s> but when the jewish festival of tabernacles was near </s>
<s> jesus brothers said to him   leave galilee and go to judea  so that your disciples there may see the works you do </s>
<s> no one who wants to become a public figure acts in secret  since you are doing these things  show yourself to the world  </s>
<s> for even his own brothers did not believe in him </s>
<s> therefore jesus told them   my time is not yet here  for you any time will do </s>
<s> the world cannot hate you  but it hates me because i testify that its works are evil </s>
<s> you go to the festival  i am not going up to this festival  because my time has not yet fully come  </s>
<s> after he had said this  he stayed in galilee </s>
<s> however  after his brothers had left for the festival  he went also  not publicly  but in secret </s>
<s> now at the festival the jewish leaders were watching for jesus and asking   where is he  </s>
<s> among the crowds there was widespread whispering about him  some said   he is a good man   others replied   no  he deceives the people  </s>
<s> but no one would say anything publicly about him for fear of the leaders </s>
<s> not until halfway through the festival did jesus go up to the temple courts and begin to teach </s>
<s> the jews there were amazed and asked   how did this man get such learning without having been taught  </s>
<s> jesus answered   my teaching is not my own  it comes from the one who sent me </s>
<s> anyone who chooses to do the will of god will find out whether my teaching comes from god or whether i speak on my own </s>
<s> whoever speaks on their own does so to gain personal glory  but he who seeks the glory of the one who sent him is a man of truth  there is nothing false about him </s>
<s> has not moses given you the law  yet not one of you keeps the law  why are you trying to kill me  </s>
<s>  you are demonpossessed   the crowd answered   who is trying to kill you  </s>
<s> jesus said to them   i did one miracle  and you are all amazed </s>
<s> yet  because moses gave you circumcision  though actually it did not come from moses  but from the patriarchs   you circumcise a boy on the sabbath </s>
<s> now if a boy can be circumcised on the sabbath so that the law of moses may not be broken  why are you angry with me for healing a mans whole body on the sabbath </s>
<s> stop judging by mere appearances  but instead judge correctly  </s>
<s> at that point some of the people of jerusalem began to ask   isnt this the man they are trying to kill </s>
<s> here he is  speaking publicly  and they are not saying a word to him  have the authorities really concluded that he is the messiah </s>
<s> but we know where this man is from  when the messiah comes  no one will know where he is from  </s>
<s> then jesus  still teaching in the temple courts  cried out   yes  you know me  and you know where i am from  i am not here on my own authority  but he who sent me is true  you do not know him </s>
<s> but i know him because i am from him and he sent me  </s>
<s> at this they tried to seize him  but no one laid a hand on him  because his hour had not yet come </s>
<s> still  many in the crowd believed in him  they said   when the messiah comes  will he perform more signs than this man  </s>
<s> the pharisees heard the crowd whispering such things about him  then the chief priests and the pharisees sent temple guards to arrest him </s>
<s> jesus said   i am with you for only a short time  and then i am going to the one who sent me </s>
<s> you will look for me  but you will not find me  and where i am  you cannot come  </s>
<s> the jews said to one another   where does this man intend to go that we cannot find him  will he go where our people live scattered among the greeks  and teach the greeks </s>
<s> what did he mean when he said   you will look for me  but you will not find me   and  where i am  you cannot come   </s>
<s> on the last and greatest day of the festival  jesus stood and said in a loud voice   let anyone who is thirsty come to me and drink </s>
<s> whoever believes in me  as scripture has said  rivers of living water will flow from within them  </s>
<s> by this he meant the spirit  whom those who believed in him were later to receive  up to that time the spirit had not been given  since jesus had not yet been glorified </s>
<s> on hearing his words  some of the people said   surely this man is the prophet  </s>
<s> others said   he is the messiah   still others asked   how can the messiah come from galilee </s>
<s> does not scripture say that the messiah will come from davids descendants and from bethlehem  the town where david lived  </s>
<s> thus the people were divided because of jesus </s>
<s> some wanted to seize him  but no one laid a hand on him </s>
<s> finally the temple guards went back to the chief priests and the pharisees  who asked them   why didnt you bring him in  </s>
<s>  no one ever spoke the way this man does   the guards replied </s>
<s>  you mean he has deceived you also   the pharisees retorted </s>
<s>  have any of the rulers or of the pharisees believed in him </s>
<s> no  but this mob that knows nothing of the law  there is a curse on them  </s>
<s> nicodemus  who had gone to jesus earlier and who was one of their own number  asked </s>
<s>  does our law condemn a man without first hearing him to find out what he has been doing  </s>
<s> they replied   are you from galilee  too  look into it  and you will find that a prophet does not come out of galilee  </s>
<s> then they all went home </s>
<s> but jesus went to the mount of olives </s>
<s> at dawn he appeared again in the temple courts  where all the people gathered round him  and he sat down to teach them </s>
<s> the teachers of the law and the pharisees brought in a woman caught in adultery  they made her stand before the group</s>
<s> and said to jesus   teacher  this woman was caught in the act of adultery </s>
<s> in the law moses commanded us to stone such women  now what do you say  </s>
<s> they were using this question as a trap  in order to have a basis for accusing him  but jesus bent down and started to write on the ground with his finger </s>
<s> when they kept on questioning him  he straightened up and said to them   let any one of you who is without sin be the first to throw a stone at her  </s>
<s> again he stooped down and wrote on the ground </s>
<s> at this  those who heard began to go away one at a time  the older ones first  until only jesus was left  with the woman still standing there </s>
<s> jesus straightened up and asked her   woman  where are they  has no one condemned you  </s>
<s>  no one  sir   she said   then neither do i condemn you   jesus declared   go now and leave your life of sin  </s>
<s> when jesus spoke again to the people  he said   i am the light of the world  whoever follows me will never walk in darkness  but will have the light of life  </s>
<s> the pharisees challenged him   here you are  appearing as your own witness  your testimony is not valid  </s>
<s> jesus answered   even if i testify on my own behalf  my testimony is valid  for i know where i came from and where i am going  but you have no idea where i come from or where i am going </s>
<s> you judge by human standards  i pass judgment on no one </s>
<s> but if i do judge  my decisions are true  because i am not alone  i stand with the father  who sent me </s>
<s> in your own law it is written that the testimony of two witnesses is true </s>
<s> i am one who testifies for myself  my other witness is the father  who sent me  </s>
<s> then they asked him   where is your father    you do not know me or my father   jesus replied   if you knew me  you would know my father also  </s>
<s> he spoke these words while teaching in the temple courts near the place where the offerings were put  yet no one seized him  because his hour had not yet come </s>
<s> once more jesus said to them   i am going away  and you will look for me  and you will die in your sin  where i go  you cannot come  </s>
<s> this made the jews ask   will he kill himself  is that why he says   where i go  you cannot come   </s>
<s> but he continued   you are from below  i am from above  you are of this world  i am not of this world </s>
<s> i told you that you would die in your sins  if you do not believe that i am he  you will indeed die in your sins  </s>
<s>  who are you   they asked   just what i have been telling you from the beginning   jesus replied </s>
<s>  i have much to say in judgment of you  but he who sent me is trustworthy  and what i have heard from him i tell the world  </s>
<s> they did not understand that he was telling them about his father </s>
<s> so jesus said   when you have lifted up the son of man  then you will know that i am he and that i do nothing on my own but speak just what the father has taught me </s>
<s> the one who sent me is with me  he has not left me alone  for i always do what pleases him  </s>
<s> even as he spoke  many believed in him </s>
<s> to the jews who had believed him  jesus said   if you hold to my teaching  you are really my disciples </s>
<s> then you will know the truth  and the truth will set you free  </s>
<s> they answered him   we are abrahams descendants and have never been slaves of anyone  how can you say that we shall be set free  </s>
<s> jesus replied   very truly i tell you  everyone who sins is a slave to sin </s>
<s> now a slave has no permanent place in the family  but a son belongs to it for ever </s>
<s> so if the son sets you free  you will be free indeed </s>
<s> i know you are abrahams descendants  yet you are looking for a way to kill me  because you have no room for my word </s>
<s> i am telling you what i have seen in the fathers presence  and you are doing what you have heard from your father  </s>
<s>  abraham is our father   they answered   if you were abrahams children   said jesus   then you would do what abraham did </s>
<s> as it is  you are looking for a way to kill me  a man who has told you the truth that i heard from god  abraham did not do such things </s>
<s> you are doing the works of your own father    we are not illegitimate children   they protested   the only father we have is god himself  </s>
<s> jesus said to them   if god were your father  you would love me  for i have come here from god  i have not come on my own  god sent me </s>
<s> why is my language not clear to you  because you are unable to hear what i say </s>
<s> you belong to your father  the devil  and you want to carry out your fathers desires  he was a murderer from the beginning  not holding to the truth  for there is no truth in him  when he lies  he speaks his native language  for he is a liar and the father of lies </s>
<s> yet because i tell the truth  you do not believe me </s>
<s> can any of you prove me guilty of sin  if i am telling the truth  why dont you believe me </s>
<s> whoever belongs to god hears what god says  the reason you do not hear is that you do not belong to god  </s>
<s> the jews answered him   arent we right in saying that you are a samaritan and demonpossessed  </s>
<s>  i am not possessed by a demon   said jesus   but i honour my father and you dishonour me </s>
<s> i am not seeking glory for myself  but there is one who seeks it  and he is the judge </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  whoever obeys my word will never see death  </s>
<s> at this they exclaimed   now we know that you are demonpossessed  abraham died and so did the prophets  yet you say that whoever obeys your word will never taste death </s>
<s> are you greater than our father abraham  he died  and so did the prophets  who do you think you are  </s>
<s> jesus replied   if i glorify myself  my glory means nothing  my father  whom you claim as your god  is the one who glorifies me </s>
<s> though you do not know him  i know him  if i said i did not  i would be a liar like you  but i do know him and obey his word </s>
<s> your father abraham rejoiced at the thought of seeing my day  he saw it and was glad  </s>
<s>  you are not yet fifty years old   they said to him   and you have seen abraham  </s>
<s>  very truly i tell you   jesus answered   before abraham was born  i am  </s>
<s> at this  they picked up stones to stone him  but jesus hid himself  slipping away from the temple grounds </s>
<s> as he went along  he saw a man blind from birth </s>
<s> his disciples asked him   rabbi  who sinned  this man or his parents  that he was born blind  </s>
<s>  neither this man nor his parents sinned   said jesus   but this happened so that the works of god might be displayed in him </s>
<s> as long as it is day  we must do the works of him who sent me  night is coming  when no one can work </s>
<s> while i am in the world  i am the light of the world  </s>
<s> after saying this  he spat on the ground  made some mud with the saliva  and put it on the mans eyes </s>
<s>  go   he told him   wash in the pool of siloam  this word means  sent   so the man went and washed  and came home seeing </s>
<s> his neighbours and those who had formerly seen him begging asked   isnt this the same man who used to sit and beg  </s>
<s> some claimed that he was  others said   no  he only looks like him   but he himself insisted   i am the man  </s>
<s>  how then were your eyes opened   they asked </s>
<s> he replied   the man they call jesus made some mud and put it on my eyes  he told me to go to siloam and wash  so i went and washed  and then i could see  </s>
<s>  where is this man   they asked him   i dont know   he said </s>
<s> they brought to the pharisees the man who had been blind </s>
<s> now the day on which jesus had made the mud and opened the mans eyes was a sabbath </s>
<s> therefore the pharisees also asked him how he had received his sight   he put mud on my eyes   the man replied   and i washed  and now i see  </s>
<s> some of the pharisees said   this man is not from god  for he does not keep the sabbath   but others asked   how can a sinner perform such signs   so they were divided </s>
<s> then they turned again to the blind man   what have you to say about him  it was your eyes he opened   the man replied   he is a prophet  </s>
<s> they still did not believe that he had been blind and had received his sight until they sent for the mans parents </s>
<s>  is this your son   they asked   is this the one you say was born blind  how is it that now he can see  </s>
<s>  we know he is our son   the parents answered   and we know he was born blind </s>
<s> but how he can see now  or who opened his eyes  we dont know  ask him  he is of age  he will speak for himself  </s>
<s> his parents said this because they were afraid of the jewish leaders  who already had decided that anyone who acknowledged that jesus was the messiah would be put out of the synagogue </s>
<s> that was why his parents said   he is of age  ask him  </s>
<s> a second time they summoned the man who had been blind   give glory to god by telling the truth   they said   we know this man is a sinner  </s>
<s> he replied   whether he is a sinner or not  i dont know  one thing i do know  i was blind but now i see  </s>
<s> then they asked him   what did he do to you  how did he open your eyes  </s>
<s> he answered   i have told you already and you did not listen  why do you want to hear it again  do you want to become his disciples too  </s>
<s> then they hurled insults at him and said   you are this fellows disciple  we are disciples of moses </s>
<s> we know that god spoke to moses  but as for this fellow  we dont even know where he comes from  </s>
<s> the man answered   now that is remarkable  you dont know where he comes from  yet he opened my eyes </s>
<s> we know that god does not listen to sinners  he listens to the godly person who does his will </s>
<s> nobody has ever heard of opening the eyes of a man born blind </s>
<s> if this man were not from god  he could do nothing  </s>
<s> to this they replied   you were steeped in sin at birth  how dare you lecture us   and they threw him out </s>
<s> jesus heard that they had thrown him out  and when he found him  he said   do you believe in the son of man  </s>
<s>  who is he  sir   the man asked   tell me so that i may believe in him  </s>
<s> jesus said   you have now seen him  in fact  he is the one speaking with you  </s>
<s> then the man said   lord  i believe   and he worshipped him </s>
<s> jesus said   for judgment i have come into this world  so that the blind will see and those who see will become blind  </s>
<s> some pharisees who were with him heard him say this and asked   what  are we blind too  </s>
<s> jesus said   if you were blind  you would not be guilty of sin  but now that you claim you can see  your guilt remains </s>
<s>  very truly i tell you pharisees  anyone who does not enter the sheepfold by the gate  but climbs in by some other way  is a thief and a robber </s>
<s> the one who enters by the gate is the shepherd of the sheep </s>
<s> the gatekeeper opens the gate for him  and the sheep listen to his voice  he calls his own sheep by name and leads them out </s>
<s> when he has brought out all his own  he goes on ahead of them  and his sheep follow him because they know his voice </s>
<s> but they will never follow a stranger  in fact  they will run away from him because they do not recognise a strangers voice  </s>
<s> jesus used this figure of speech  but the pharisees did not understand what he was telling them </s>
<s> therefore jesus said again   very truly i tell you  i am the gate for the sheep </s>
<s> all who have come before me are thieves and robbers  but the sheep have not listened to them </s>
<s> i am the gate  whoever enters through me will be saved  they will come in and go out  and find pasture </s>
<s> the thief comes only to steal and kill and destroy  i have come that they may have life  and have it to the full </s>
<s>  i am the good shepherd  the good shepherd lays down his life for the sheep </s>
<s> the hired hand is not the shepherd and does not own the sheep  so when he sees the wolf coming  he abandons the sheep and runs away  then the wolf attacks the flock and scatters it </s>
<s> the man runs away because he is a hired hand and cares nothing for the sheep </s>
<s>  i am the good shepherd  i know my sheep and my sheep know me </s>
<s> just as the father knows me and i know the father  and i lay down my life for the sheep </s>
<s> i have other sheep that are not of this sheepfold  i must bring them also  they too will listen to my voice  and there shall be one flock and one shepherd </s>
<s> the reason my father loves me is that i lay down my life  only to take it up again </s>
<s> no one takes it from me  but i lay it down of my own accord  i have authority to lay it down and authority to take it up again  this command i received from my father  </s>
<s> the jews who heard these words were again divided </s>
<s> many of them said   he is demonpossessed and raving mad  why listen to him  </s>
<s> but others said   these are not the sayings of a man possessed by a demon  can a demon open the eyes of the blind  </s>
<s> then came the festival of dedication at jerusalem  it was winter </s>
<s> and jesus was in the temple courts walking in solomons colonnade </s>
<s> the jews who were there gathered round him  saying   how long will you keep us in suspense  if you are the messiah  tell us plainly  </s>
<s> jesus answered   i did tell you  but you do not believe  the works i do in my fathers name testify about me </s>
<s> but you do not believe because you are not my sheep </s>
<s> my sheep listen to my voice  i know them  and they follow me </s>
<s> i give them eternal life  and they shall never perish  no one will snatch them out of my hand </s>
<s> my father  who has given them to me  is greater than all  no one can snatch them out of my fathers hand </s>
<s> i and the father are one  </s>
<s> again his jewish opponents picked up stones to stone him </s>
<s> but jesus said to them   i have shown you many good works from the father  for which of these do you stone me  </s>
<s>  we are not stoning you for any good work   they replied   but for blasphemy  because you  a mere man  claim to be god  </s>
<s> jesus answered them   is it not written in your law   i have said you are  gods  </s>
<s> if he called them  gods   to whom the word of god came  and scripture cannot be set aside </s>
<s> what about the one whom the father set apart as his very own and sent into the world  why then do you accuse me of blasphemy because i said   i am gods son  </s>
<s> do not believe me unless i do the works of my father </s>
<s> but if i do them  even though you do not believe me  believe the works  that you may know and understand that the father is in me  and i in the father  </s>
<s> again they tried to seize him  but he escaped their grasp </s>
<s> then jesus went back across the jordan to the place where john had been baptising in the early days  there he stayed </s>
<s> and many people came to him  they said   though john never performed a sign  all that john said about this man was true  </s>
<s> and in that place many believed in jesus </s>
<s> now a man named lazarus was ill  he was from bethany  the village of mary and her sister martha </s>
<s>  this mary  whose brother lazarus now lay ill  was the same one who poured perfume on the lord and wiped his feet with her hair  </s>
<s> so the sisters sent word to jesus   lord  the one you love is ill  </s>
<s> when he heard this  jesus said   this illness will not end in death  no  it is for gods glory so that gods son may be glorified through it  </s>
<s> now jesus loved martha and her sister and lazarus </s>
<s> so when he heard that lazarus was ill  he stayed where he was two more days </s>
<s> and then he said to his disciples   let us go back to judea  </s>
<s>  but rabbi   they said   a short while ago the jews there tried to stone you  and yet you are going back  </s>
<s> jesus answered   are there not twelve hours of daylight  anyone who walks in the daytime will not stumble  for they see by this worlds light </s>
<s> it is when a person walks at night that they stumble  for they have no light  </s>
<s> after he had said this  he went on to tell them   our friend lazarus has fallen asleep  but i am going there to wake him up  </s>
<s> his disciples replied   lord  if he sleeps  he will get better  </s>
<s> jesus had been speaking of his death  but his disciples thought he meant natural sleep </s>
<s> so then he told them plainly   lazarus is dead </s>
<s> and for your sake i am glad i was not there  so that you may believe  but let us go to him  </s>
<s> then thomas  also known as didymus  said to the rest of the disciples   let us also go  that we may die with him  </s>
<s> on his arrival  jesus found that lazarus had already been in the tomb for four days </s>
<s> now bethany was less than two miles from jerusalem </s>
<s> and many jews had come to martha and mary to comfort them in the loss of their brother </s>
<s> when martha heard that jesus was coming  she went out to meet him  but mary stayed at home </s>
<s>  lord   martha said to jesus   if you had been here  my brother would not have died </s>
<s> but i know that even now god will give you whatever you ask  </s>
<s> jesus said to her   your brother will rise again  </s>
<s> martha answered   i know he will rise again in the resurrection at the last day  </s>
<s> jesus said to her   i am the resurrection and the life  the one who believes in me will live  even though they die </s>
<s> and whoever lives by believing in me will never die  do you believe this  </s>
<s>  yes  lord   she replied   i believe that you are the messiah  the son of god  who is to come into the world  </s>
<s> after she had said this  she went back and called her sister mary aside   the teacher is here   she said   and is asking for you  </s>
<s> when mary heard this  she got up quickly and went to him </s>
<s> now jesus had not yet entered the village  but was still at the place where martha had met him </s>
<s> when the jews who had been with mary in the house  comforting her  noticed how quickly she got up and went out  they followed her  supposing she was going to the tomb to mourn there </s>
<s> when mary reached the place where jesus was and saw him  she fell at his feet and said   lord  if you had been here  my brother would not have died  </s>
<s> when jesus saw her weeping  and the jews who had come along with her also weeping  he was deeply moved in spirit and troubled </s>
<s>  where have you laid him   he asked   come and see  lord   they replied </s>
<s> jesus wept </s>
<s> then the jews said   see how he loved him  </s>
<s> but some of them said   could not he who opened the eyes of the blind man have kept this man from dying  </s>
<s> jesus  once more deeply moved  came to the tomb  it was a cave with a stone laid across the entrance </s>
<s>  take away the stone   he said   but  lord   said martha  the sister of the dead man   by this time there is a bad odour  for he has been there four days  </s>
<s> then jesus said   did i not tell you that if you believe  you will see the glory of god  </s>
<s> so they took away the stone  then jesus looked up and said   father  i thank you that you have heard me </s>
<s> i knew that you always hear me  but i said this for the benefit of the people standing here  that they may believe that you sent me  </s>
<s> when he had said this  jesus called in a loud voice   lazarus  come out  </s>
<s> the dead man came out  his hands and feet wrapped with strips of linen  and a cloth round his face  jesus said to them   take off the grave clothes and let him go  </s>
<s> therefore many of the jews who had come to visit mary  and had seen what jesus did  believed in him </s>
<s> but some of them went to the pharisees and told them what jesus had done </s>
<s> then the chief priests and the pharisees called a meeting of the sanhedrin   what are we accomplishing   they asked   here is this man performing many signs </s>
<s> if we let him go on like this  everyone will believe in him  and then the romans will come and take away both our temple and our nation  </s>
<s> then one of them  named caiaphas  who was high priest that year  spoke up   you know nothing at all </s>
<s> you do not realise that it is better for you that one man die for the people than that the whole nation perish  </s>
<s> he did not say this on his own  but as high priest that year he prophesied that jesus would die for the jewish nation </s>
<s> and not only for that nation but also for the scattered children of god  to bring them together and make them one </s>
<s> so from that day on they plotted to take his life </s>
<s> therefore jesus no longer moved about publicly among the people of judea  instead he withdrew to a region near the wilderness  to a village called ephraim  where he stayed with his disciples </s>
<s> when it was almost time for the jewish passover  many went up from the country to jerusalem for their ceremonial cleansing before the passover </s>
<s> they kept looking for jesus  and as they stood in the temple courts they asked one another   what do you think  isnt he coming to the festival at all  </s>
<s> but the chief priests and the pharisees had given orders that anyone who found out where jesus was should report it so that they might arrest him </s>
<s> six days before the passover  jesus came to bethany  where lazarus lived  whom jesus had raised from the dead </s>
<s> here a dinner was given in jesus honour  martha served  while lazarus was among those reclining at the table with him </s>
<s> then mary took about half a litre of pure nard  an expensive perfume  she poured it on jesus feet and wiped his feet with her hair  and the house was filled with the fragrance of the perfume </s>
<s> but one of his disciples  judas iscariot  who was later to betray him  objected </s>
<s>  why wasnt this perfume sold and the money given to the poor  it was worth a years wages  </s>
<s> he did not say this because he cared about the poor but because he was a thief  as keeper of the money bag  he used to help himself to what was put into it </s>
<s>  leave her alone   jesus replied   it was intended that she should save this perfume for the day of my burial </s>
<s> you will always have the poor among you  but you will not always have me  </s>
<s> meanwhile a large crowd of jews found out that jesus was there and came  not only because of him but also to see lazarus  whom he had raised from the dead </s>
<s> so the chief priests made plans to kill lazarus as well </s>
<s> for on account of him many of the jews were going over to jesus and believing in him </s>
<s> the next day the great crowd that had come for the festival heard that jesus was on his way to jerusalem </s>
<s> they took palm branches and went out to meet him  shouting   hosanna    blessed is he who comes in the name of the lord    blessed is the king of israel  </s>
<s>  do not be afraid  daughter zion  see  your king is coming  seated on a donkeys colt  </s>
<s> at first his disciples did not understand all this  only after jesus was glorified did they realise that these things had been written about him and that these things had been done to him </s>
<s> now the crowd that was with him when he called lazarus from the tomb and raised him from the dead continued to spread the word </s>
<s> many people  because they had heard that he had performed this sign  went out to meet him </s>
<s> so the pharisees said to one another   see  this is getting us nowhere  look how the whole world has gone after him  </s>
<s> now there were some greeks among those who went up to worship at the festival </s>
<s> they came to philip  who was from bethsaida in galilee  with a request   sir   they said   we would like to see jesus  </s>
<s> philip went to tell andrew  andrew and philip in turn told jesus </s>
<s> jesus replied   the hour has come for the son of man to be glorified </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  unless a grain of wheat falls to the ground and dies  it remains only a single seed  but if it dies  it produces many seeds </s>
<s> anyone who loves their life will lose it  while anyone who hates their life in this world will keep it for eternal life </s>
<s> whoever serves me must follow me  and where i am  my servant also will be  my father will honour the one who serves me </s>
<s>  now my soul is troubled  and what shall i say   father  save me from this hour   no  it was for this very reason i came to this hour </s>
<s> father  glorify your name   then a voice came from heaven   i have glorified it  and will glorify it again  </s>
<s> the crowd that was there and heard it said it had thundered  others said an angel had spoken to him </s>
<s> jesus said   this voice was for your benefit  not mine </s>
<s> now is the time for judgment on this world  now the prince of this world will be driven out </s>
<s> and i  when i am lifted up from the earth  will draw all people to myself  </s>
<s> he said this to show the kind of death he was going to die </s>
<s> the crowd spoke up   we have heard from the law that the messiah will remain for ever  so how can you say   the son of man must be lifted up   who is this  son of man   </s>
<s> then jesus told them   you are going to have the light just a little while longer  walk while you have the light  before darkness overtakes you  whoever walks in the dark does not know where they are going </s>
<s> believe in the light while you have the light  so that you may become children of light   when he had finished speaking  jesus left and hid himself from them </s>
<s> even after jesus had performed so many signs in their presence  they still would not believe in him </s>
<s> this was to fulfil the word of isaiah the prophet   lord  who has believed our message and to whom has the arm of the lord been revealed  </s>
<s> for this reason they could not believe  because  as isaiah says elsewhere </s>
<s>  he has blinded their eyes and hardened their hearts  so they can neither see with their eyes  nor understand with their hearts  nor turn  and i would heal them  </s>
<s> yet at the same time many even among the leaders believed in him  but because of the pharisees they would not openly acknowledge their faith for fear they would be put out of the synagogue </s>
<s> for they loved human praise more than praise from god </s>
<s> then jesus cried out   whoever believes in me does not believe in me only  but in the one who sent me </s>
<s> the one who looks at me is seeing the one who sent me </s>
<s> i have come into the world as a light  so that no one who believes in me should stay in darkness </s>
<s>  if anyone hears my words but does not keep them  i do not judge that person  for i did not come to judge the world  but to save the world </s>
<s> there is a judge for the one who rejects me and does not accept my words  the very words i have spoken will condemn them at the last day </s>
<s> for i did not speak on my own  but the father who sent me commanded me to say all that i have spoken </s>
<s> i know that his command leads to eternal life  so whatever i say is just what the father has told me to say  </s>
<s> it was just before the passover festival  jesus knew that the hour had come for him to leave this world and go to the father  having loved his own who were in the world  he loved them to the end </s>
<s> the evening meal was in progress  and the devil had already prompted judas  the son of simon iscariot  to betray jesus </s>
<s> jesus knew that the father had put all things under his power  and that he had come from god and was returning to god </s>
<s> so he got up from the meal  took off his outer clothing  and wrapped a towel round his waist </s>
<s> after that  he poured water into a basin and began to wash his disciples feet  drying them with the towel that was wrapped round him </s>
<s> he came to simon peter  who said to him   lord  are you going to wash my feet  </s>
<s> jesus replied   you do not realise now what i am doing  but later you will understand  </s>
<s>  no   said peter   you shall never wash my feet   jesus answered   unless i wash you  you have no part with me  </s>
<s>  then  lord   simon peter replied   not just my feet but my hands and my head as well  </s>
<s> jesus answered   those who have had a bath need only to wash their feet  their whole body is clean  and you are clean  though not every one of you  </s>
<s> for he knew who was going to betray him  and that was why he said not every one was clean </s>
<s> when he had finished washing their feet  he put on his clothes and returned to his place   do you understand what i have done for you   he asked them </s>
<s>  you call me  teacher  and  lord   and rightly so  for that is what i am </s>
<s> now that i  your lord and teacher  have washed your feet  you also should wash one anothers feet </s>
<s> i have set you an example that you should do as i have done for you </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  no servant is greater than his master  nor is a messenger greater than the one who sent him </s>
<s> now that you know these things  you will be blessed if you do them </s>
<s>  i am not referring to all of you  i know those i have chosen  but this is to fulfil this passage of scripture   he who shared my bread has turned against me  </s>
<s>  i am telling you now before it happens  so that when it does happen you will believe that i am who i am </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  whoever accepts anyone i send accepts me  and whoever accepts me accepts the one who sent me  </s>
<s> after he had said this  jesus was troubled in spirit and testified   very truly i tell you  one of you is going to betray me  </s>
<s> his disciples stared at one another  at a loss to know which of them he meant </s>
<s> one of them  the disciple whom jesus loved  was reclining next to him </s>
<s> simon peter motioned to this disciple and said   ask him which one he means  </s>
<s> leaning back against jesus  he asked him   lord  who is it  </s>
<s> jesus answered   it is the one to whom i will give this piece of bread when i have dipped it in the dish   then  dipping the piece of bread  he gave it to judas  the son of simon iscariot </s>
<s> as soon as judas took the bread  satan entered into him  so jesus told him   what you are about to do  do quickly  </s>
<s> but no one at the meal understood why jesus said this to him </s>
<s> since judas had charge of the money  some thought jesus was telling him to buy what was needed for the festival  or to give something to the poor </s>
<s> as soon as judas had taken the bread  he went out  and it was night </s>
<s> when he was gone  jesus said   now the son of man is glorified and god is glorified in him </s>
<s> if god is glorified in him  god will glorify the son in himself  and will glorify him at once </s>
<s>  my children  i will be with you only a little longer  you will look for me  and just as i told the jews  so i tell you now  where i am going  you cannot come </s>
<s>  a new command i give you  love one another  as i have loved you  so you must love one another </s>
<s> by this everyone will know that you are my disciples  if you love one another  </s>
<s> simon peter asked him   lord  where are you going   jesus replied   where i am going  you cannot follow now  but you will follow later  </s>
<s> peter asked   lord  why cant i follow you now  i will lay down my life for you  </s>
<s> then jesus answered   will you really lay down your life for me  very truly i tell you  before the cock crows  you will disown me three times </s>
<s>  do not let your hearts be troubled  you believe in god  believe also in me </s>
<s> my fathers house has many rooms  if that were not so  would i have told you that i am going there to prepare a place for you </s>
<s> and if i go and prepare a place for you  i will come back and take you to be with me that you also may be where i am </s>
<s> you know the way to the place where i am going  </s>
<s> thomas said to him   lord  we dont know where you are going  so how can we know the way  </s>
<s> jesus answered   i am the way and the truth and the life  no one comes to the father except through me </s>
<s> if you really know me  you will know my father as well  from now on  you do know him and have seen him  </s>
<s> philip said   lord  show us the father and that will be enough for us  </s>
<s> jesus answered   dont you know me  philip  even after i have been among you such a long time  anyone who has seen me has seen the father  how can you say   show us the father  </s>
<s> dont you believe that i am in the father  and that the father is in me  the words i say to you i do not speak on my own authority  rather  it is the father  living in me  who is doing his work </s>
<s> believe me when i say that i am in the father and the father is in me  or at least believe on the evidence of the works themselves </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  whoever believes in me will do the works i have been doing  and they will do even greater things than these  because i am going to the father </s>
<s> and i will do whatever you ask in my name  so that the father may be glorified in the son </s>
<s> you may ask me for anything in my name  and i will do it </s>
<s>  if you love me  keep my commands </s>
<s> and i will ask the father  and he will give you another advocate to help you and be with you for ever </s>
<s> the spirit of truth  the world cannot accept him  because it neither sees him nor knows him  but you know him  for he lives with you and will be in you </s>
<s> i will not leave you as orphans  i will come to you </s>
<s> before long  the world will not see me any more  but you will see me  because i live  you also will live </s>
<s> on that day you will realise that i am in my father  and you are in me  and i am in you </s>
<s> whoever has my commands and keeps them is the one who loves me  the one who loves me will be loved by my father  and i too will love them and show myself to them  </s>
<s> then judas  not judas iscariot  said   but  lord  why do you intend to show yourself to us and not to the world  </s>
<s> jesus replied   anyone who loves me will obey my teaching  my father will love them  and we will come to them and make our home with them </s>
<s> anyone who does not love me will not obey my teaching  these words you hear are not my own  they belong to the father who sent me </s>
<s>  all this i have spoken while still with you </s>
<s> but the advocate  the holy spirit  whom the father will send in my name  will teach you all things and will remind you of everything i have said to you </s>
<s> peace i leave with you  my peace i give you  i do not give to you as the world gives  do not let your hearts be troubled and do not be afraid </s>
<s>  you heard me say   i am going away and i am coming back to you   if you loved me  you would be glad that i am going to the father  for the father is greater than i </s>
<s> i have told you now before it happens  so that when it does happen you will believe </s>
<s> i will not say much more to you  for the prince of this world is coming  he has no hold over me </s>
<s> but he comes so that the world may learn that i love the father and do exactly what my father has commanded me   come now  let us leave </s>
<s>  i am the true vine  and my father is the gardener </s>
<s> he cuts off every branch in me that bears no fruit  while every branch that does bear fruit he prunes so that it will be even more fruitful </s>
<s> you are already clean because of the word i have spoken to you </s>
<s> remain in me  as i also remain in you  no branch can bear fruit by itself  it must remain in the vine  neither can you bear fruit unless you remain in me </s>
<s>  i am the vine  you are the branches  if you remain in me and i in you  you will bear much fruit  apart from me you can do nothing </s>
<s> if you do not remain in me  you are like a branch that is thrown away and withers  such branches are picked up  thrown into the fire and burned </s>
<s> if you remain in me and my words remain in you  ask whatever you wish  and it will be done for you </s>
<s> this is to my fathers glory  that you bear much fruit  showing yourselves to be my disciples </s>
<s>  as the father has loved me  so have i loved you  now remain in my love </s>
<s> if you keep my commands  you will remain in my love  just as i have kept my fathers commands and remain in his love </s>
<s> i have told you this so that my joy may be in you and that your joy may be complete </s>
<s> my command is this  love each other as i have loved you </s>
<s> greater love has no one than this  to lay down ones life for ones friends </s>
<s> you are my friends if you do what i command </s>
<s> i no longer call you servants  because a servant does not know his masters business  instead  i have called you friends  for everything that i learned from my father i have made known to you </s>
<s> you did not choose me  but i chose you and appointed you so that you might go and bear fruit  fruit that will last  and so that whatever you ask in my name the father will give you </s>
<s> this is my command  love each other </s>
<s>  if the world hates you  keep in mind that it hated me first </s>
<s> if you belonged to the world  it would love you as its own  as it is  you do not belong to the world  but i have chosen you out of the world  that is why the world hates you </s>
<s> remember what i told you   a servant is not greater than his master   if they persecuted me  they will persecute you also  if they obeyed my teaching  they will obey yours also </s>
<s> they will treat you this way because of my name  for they do not know the one who sent me </s>
<s> if i had not come and spoken to them  they would not be guilty of sin  but now they have no excuse for their sin </s>
<s> whoever hates me hates my father as well </s>
<s> if i had not done among them the works no one else did  they would not be guilty of sin  as it is  they have seen  and yet they have hated both me and my father </s>
<s> but this is to fulfil what is written in their law   they hated me without reason  </s>
<s>  when the advocate comes  whom i will send to you from the father  the spirit of truth who goes out from the father  he will testify about me </s>
<s> and you also must testify  for you have been with me from the beginning </s>
<s>  all this i have told you so that you will not fall away </s>
<s> they will put you out of the synagogue  in fact  the time is coming when anyone who kills you will think they are offering a service to god </s>
<s> they will do such things because they have not known the father or me </s>
<s> i have told you this  so that when their time comes you will remember that i warned you about them  i did not tell you this from the beginning because i was with you </s>
<s> but now i am going to him who sent me  none of you asks me   where are you going  </s>
<s> rather  you are filled with grief because i have said these things </s>
<s> but very truly i tell you  it is for your good that i am going away  unless i go away  the advocate will not come to you  but if i go  i will send him to you </s>
<s> when he comes  he will prove the world to be in the wrong about sin and righteousness and judgment </s>
<s> about sin  because people do not believe in me </s>
<s> about righteousness  because i am going to the father  where you can see me no longer </s>
<s> and about judgment  because the prince of this world now stands condemned </s>
<s>  i have much more to say to you  more than you can now bear </s>
<s> but when he  the spirit of truth  comes  he will guide you into all the truth  he will not speak on his own  he will speak only what he hears  and he will tell you what is yet to come </s>
<s> he will glorify me because it is from me that he will receive what he will make known to you </s>
<s> all that belongs to the father is mine  that is why i said the spirit will receive from me what he will make known to you  </s>
<s> jesus went on to say   in a little while you will see me no more  and then after a little while you will see me  </s>
<s> at this  some of his disciples said to one another   what does he mean by saying   in a little while you will see me no more  and then after a little while you will see me   and  because i am going to the father   </s>
<s> they kept asking   what does he mean by  a little while   we dont understand what he is saying  </s>
