<s> jesus saw that they wanted to ask him about this  so he said to them   are you asking one another what i meant when i said   in a little while you will see me no more  and then after a little while you will see me  </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  you will weep and mourn while the world rejoices  you will grieve  but your grief will turn to joy </s>
<s> a woman giving birth to a child has pain because her time has come  but when her baby is born she forgets the anguish because of her joy that a child is born into the world </s>
<s> so with you  now is your time of grief  but i will see you again and you will rejoice  and no one will take away your joy </s>
<s> in that day you will no longer ask me anything  very truly i tell you  my father will give you whatever you ask in my name </s>
<s> until now you have not asked for anything in my name  ask and you will receive  and your joy will be complete </s>
<s>  though i have been speaking figuratively  a time is coming when i will no longer use this kind of language but will tell you plainly about my father </s>
<s> in that day you will ask in my name  i am not saying that i will ask the father on your behalf </s>
<s> no  the father himself loves you because you have loved me and have believed that i came from god </s>
<s> i came from the father and entered the world  now i am leaving the world and going back to the father  </s>
<s> then jesus disciples said   now you are speaking clearly and without figures of speech </s>
<s> now we can see that you know all things and that you do not even need to have anyone ask you questions  this makes us believe that you came from god  </s>
<s>  do you now believe   jesus replied </s>
<s>  a time is coming and in fact has come when you will be scattered  each to your own home  you will leave me all alone  yet i am not alone  for my father is with me </s>
<s>  i have told you these things  so that in me you may have peace  in this world you will have trouble  but take heart  i have overcome the world  </s>
<s> after jesus said this  he looked towards heaven and prayed   father  the hour has come  glorify your son  that your son may glorify you </s>
<s> for you granted him authority over all people that he might give eternal life to all those you have given him </s>
<s> now this is eternal life  that they know you  the only true god  and jesus christ  whom you have sent </s>
<s> i have brought you glory on earth by finishing the work you gave me to do </s>
<s> and now  father  glorify me in your presence with the glory i had with you before the world began </s>
<s>  i have revealed you to those whom you gave me out of the world  they were yours  you gave them to me and they have obeyed your word </s>
<s> now they know that everything you have given me comes from you </s>
<s> for i gave them the words you gave me and they accepted them  they knew with certainty that i came from you  and they believed that you sent me </s>
<s> i pray for them  i am not praying for the world  but for those you have given me  for they are yours </s>
<s> all i have is yours  and all you have is mine  and glory has come to me through them </s>
<s> i will remain in the world no longer  but they are still in the world  and i am coming to you  holy father  protect them by the power of your name  the name you gave me  so that they may be one as we are one </s>
<s> while i was with them  i protected them and kept them safe by that name you gave me  none has been lost except the one doomed to destruction so that scripture would be fulfilled </s>
<s>  i am coming to you now  but i say these things while i am still in the world  so that they may have the full measure of my joy within them </s>
<s> i have given them your word and the world has hated them  for they are not of the world any more than i am of the world </s>
<s> my prayer is not that you take them out of the world but that you protect them from the evil one </s>
<s> they are not of the world  even as i am not of it </s>
<s> sanctify them by the truth  your word is truth </s>
<s> as you sent me into the world  i have sent them into the world </s>
<s> for them i sanctify myself  that they too may be truly sanctified </s>
<s>  my prayer is not for them alone  i pray also for those who will believe in me through their message </s>
<s> that all of them may be one  father  just as you are in me and i am in you  may they also be in us so that the world may believe that you have sent me </s>
<s> i have given them the glory that you gave me  that they may be one as we are one </s>
<s> i in them and you in me  so that they may be brought to complete unity  then the world will know that you sent me and have loved them even as you have loved me </s>
<s>  father  i want those you have given me to be with me where i am  and to see my glory  the glory you have given me because you loved me before the creation of the world </s>
<s>  righteous father  though the world does not know you  i know you  and they know that you have sent me </s>
<s> i have made you known to them  and will continue to make you known in order that the love you have for me may be in them and that i myself may be in them  </s>
<s> when he had finished praying  jesus left with his disciples and crossed the kidron valley  on the other side there was a garden  and he and his disciples went into it </s>
<s> now judas  who betrayed him  knew the place  because jesus had often met there with his disciples </s>
<s> so judas came to the garden  guiding a detachment of soldiers and some officials from the chief priests and the pharisees  they were carrying torches  lanterns and weapons </s>
<s> jesus  knowing all that was going to happen to him  went out and asked them   who is it you want  </s>
<s>  jesus of nazareth   they replied   i am he   jesus said   and judas the traitor was standing there with them  </s>
<s> when jesus said   i am he   they drew back and fell to the ground </s>
<s> again he asked them   who is it you want    jesus of nazareth   they said </s>
<s> jesus answered   i told you that i am he  if you are looking for me  then let these men go  </s>
<s> this happened so that the words he had spoken would be fulfilled   i have not lost one of those you gave me  </s>
<s> then simon peter  who had a sword  drew it and struck the high priests servant  cutting off his right ear   the servants name was malchus  </s>
<s> jesus commanded peter   put your sword away  shall i not drink the cup the father has given me  </s>
<s> then the detachment of soldiers with its commander and the jewish officials arrested jesus  they bound him</s>
<s> and brought him first to annas  who was the fatherinlaw of caiaphas  the high priest that year </s>
<s> caiaphas was the one who had advised the jewish leaders that it would be good if one man died for the people </s>
<s> simon peter and another disciple were following jesus  because this disciple was known to the high priest  he went with jesus into the high priests courtyard </s>
<s> but peter had to wait outside at the door  the other disciple  who was known to the high priest  came back  spoke to the servantgirl on duty there and brought peter in </s>
<s>  you arent one of this mans disciples too  are you   she asked peter  he replied   i am not  </s>
<s> it was cold  and the servants and officials stood round a fire they had made to keep warm  peter also was standing with them  warming himself </s>
<s> meanwhile  the high priest questioned jesus about his disciples and his teaching </s>
<s>  i have spoken openly to the world   jesus replied   i always taught in synagogues or at the temple  where all the jews come together  i said nothing in secret </s>
<s> why question me  ask those who heard me  surely they know what i said  </s>
<s> when jesus said this  one of the officials near by slapped him in the face   is this the way you answer the high priest   he demanded </s>
<s>  if i said something wrong   jesus replied   testify as to what is wrong  but if i spoke the truth  why did you strike me  </s>
<s> then annas sent him bound to caiaphas the high priest </s>
<s> meanwhile  simon peter was still standing there warming himself  so they asked him   you arent one of his disciples too  are you   he denied it  saying   i am not  </s>
<s> one of the high priests servants  a relative of the man whose ear peter had cut off  challenged him   didnt i see you with him in the garden  </s>
<s> again peter denied it  and at that moment a cock began to crow </s>
<s> then the jewish leaders took jesus from caiaphas to the palace of the roman governor  by now it was early morning  and to avoid ceremonial uncleanness they did not enter the palace  because they wanted to be able to eat the passover </s>
<s> so pilate came out to them and asked   what charges are you bringing against this man  </s>
<s>  if he were not a criminal   they replied   we would not have handed him over to you  </s>
<s> pilate said   take him yourselves and judge him by your own law    but we have no right to execute anyone   they objected </s>
<s> this took place to fulfil what jesus had said about the kind of death he was going to die </s>
<s> pilate then went back inside the palace  summoned jesus and asked him   are you the king of the jews  </s>
<s>  is that your own idea   jesus asked   or did others talk to you about me  </s>
<s>  am i a jew   pilate replied   your own people and chief priests handed you over to me  what is it you have done  </s>
<s> jesus said   my kingdom is not of this world  if it were  my servants would fight to prevent my arrest by the jewish leaders  but now my kingdom is from another place  </s>
<s>  you are a king  then   said pilate  jesus answered   you say that i am a king  in fact  the reason i was born and came into the world is to testify to the truth  everyone on the side of truth listens to me  </s>
<s>  what is truth   retorted pilate  with this he went out again to the jews gathered there and said   i find no basis for a charge against him </s>
<s> but it is your custom for me to release to you one prisoner at the time of the passover  do you want me to release  the king of the jews   </s>
<s> they shouted back   no  not him  give us barabbas   now barabbas had taken part in an uprising </s>
<s> then pilate took jesus and had him flogged </s>
<s> the soldiers twisted together a crown of thorns and put it on his head  they clothed him in a purple robe</s>
<s> and went up to him again and again  saying   hail  king of the jews   and they slapped him in the face </s>
<s> once more pilate came out and said to the jews gathered there   look  i am bringing him out to you to let you know that i find no basis for a charge against him  </s>
<s> when jesus came out wearing the crown of thorns and the purple robe  pilate said to them   here is the man  </s>
<s> as soon as the chief priests and their officials saw him  they shouted   crucify  crucify   but pilate answered   you take him and crucify him  as for me  i find no basis for a charge against him  </s>
<s> the jewish leaders insisted   we have a law  and according to that law he must die  because he claimed to be the son of god  </s>
<s> when pilate heard this  he was even more afraid </s>
<s> and he went back inside the palace   where do you come from   he asked jesus  but jesus gave him no answer </s>
<s>  do you refuse to speak to me   pilate said   dont you realise i have power either to free you or to crucify you  </s>
<s> jesus answered   you would have no power over me if it were not given to you from above  therefore the one who handed me over to you is guilty of a greater sin  </s>
<s> from then on  pilate tried to set jesus free  but the jewish leaders kept shouting   if you let this man go  you are no friend of caesar  anyone who claims to be a king opposes caesar  </s>
<s> when pilate heard this  he brought jesus out and sat down on the judges seat at a place known as the stone pavement  which in aramaic is gabbatha  </s>
<s> it was the day of preparation of the passover  it was about noon   here is your king   pilate said to the jews </s>
<s> but they shouted   take him away  take him away  crucify him    shall i crucify your king   pilate asked   we have no king but caesar   the chief priests answered </s>
<s> finally pilate handed him over to them to be crucified  so the soldiers took charge of jesus </s>
<s> carrying his own cross  he went out to the place of the skull  which in aramaic is called golgotha  </s>
<s> there they crucified him  and with him two others  one on each side and jesus in the middle </s>
<s> pilate had a notice prepared and fastened to the cross  it read  jesus of nazareth  the king of the jews </s>
<s> many of the jews read this sign  for the place where jesus was crucified was near the city  and the sign was written in aramaic  latin and greek </s>
<s> the chief priests of the jews protested to pilate   do not write  the king of the jews   but that this man claimed to be king of the jews  </s>
<s> pilate answered   what i have written  i have written  </s>
<s> when the soldiers crucified jesus  they took his clothes  dividing them into four shares  one for each of them  with the undergarment remaining  this garment was seamless  woven in one piece from top to bottom </s>
<s>  lets not tear it   they said to one another   lets decide by lot who will get it   this happened that the scripture might be fulfilled that said   they divided my clothes among them and cast lots for my garment  </s>
<s> near the cross of jesus stood his mother  his mothers sister  mary the wife of clopas  and mary magdalene </s>
<s> when jesus saw his mother there  and the disciple whom he loved standing near by  he said to her   woman  here is your son  </s>
<s> and to the disciple   here is your mother   from that time on  this disciple took her into his home </s>
<s> later  knowing that everything had now been finished  and so that scripture would be fulfilled  jesus said   i am thirsty  </s>
<s> a jar of wine vinegar was there  so they soaked a sponge in it  put the sponge on a stalk of the hyssop plant  and lifted it to jesus lips </s>
<s> when he had received the drink  jesus said   it is finished   with that  he bowed his head and gave up his spirit </s>
<s> now it was the day of preparation  and the next day was to be a special sabbath  because the jewish leaders did not want the bodies left on the crosses during the sabbath  they asked pilate to have the legs broken and the bodies taken down </s>
<s> the soldiers therefore came and broke the legs of the first man who had been crucified with jesus  and then those of the other </s>
<s> but when they came to jesus and found that he was already dead  they did not break his legs </s>
<s> instead  one of the soldiers pierced jesus side with a spear  bringing a sudden flow of blood and water </s>
<s> the man who saw it has given testimony  and his testimony is true  he knows that he tells the truth  and he testifies so that you also may believe </s>
<s> these things happened so that the scripture would be fulfilled   not one of his bones will be broken  </s>
<s> and  as another scripture says   they will look on the one they have pierced  </s>
<s> later  joseph of arimathea asked pilate for the body of jesus  now joseph was a disciple of jesus  but secretly because he feared the jewish leaders  with pilates permission  he came and took the body away </s>
<s> he was accompanied by nicodemus  the man who earlier had visited jesus at night  nicodemus brought a mixture of myrrh and aloes  about thirtyfive kilograms </s>
<s> taking jesus body  the two of them wrapped it  with the spices  in strips of linen  this was in accordance with jewish burial customs </s>
<s> at the place where jesus was crucified  there was a garden  and in the garden a new tomb  in which no one had ever been laid </s>
<s> because it was the jewish day of preparation and since the tomb was near by  they laid jesus there </s>
<s> early on the first day of the week  while it was still dark  mary magdalene went to the tomb and saw that the stone had been removed from the entrance </s>
<s> so she came running to simon peter and the other disciple  the one jesus loved  and said   they have taken the lord out of the tomb  and we dont know where they have put him  </s>
<s> so peter and the other disciple started for the tomb </s>
<s> both were running  but the other disciple outran peter and reached the tomb first </s>
<s> he bent over and looked in at the strips of linen lying there but did not go in </s>
<s> then simon peter came along behind him and went straight into the tomb  he saw the strips of linen lying there </s>
<s> as well as the cloth that had been wrapped round jesus head  the cloth was still lying in its place  separate from the linen </s>
<s> finally the other disciple  who had reached the tomb first  also went inside  he saw and believed </s>
<s>  they still did not understand from scripture that jesus had to rise from the dead  </s>
<s> then the disciples went back to where they were staying </s>
<s> now mary stood outside the tomb crying  as she wept  she bent over to look into the tomb</s>
<s> and saw two angels in white  seated where jesus body had been  one at the head and the other at the foot </s>
<s> they asked her   woman  why are you crying    they have taken my lord away   she said   and i dont know where they have put him  </s>
<s> at this  she turned round and saw jesus standing there  but she did not realise that it was jesus </s>
<s> he asked her   woman  why are you crying  who is it you are looking for   thinking he was the gardener  she said   sir  if you have carried him away  tell me where you have put him  and i will get him  </s>
<s> jesus said to her   mary   she turned towards him and cried out in aramaic   rabboni    which means  teacher  </s>
<s> jesus said   do not hold on to me  for i have not yet ascended to the father  go instead to my brothers and tell them   i am ascending to my father and your father  to my god and your god   </s>
<s> mary magdalene went to the disciples with the news   i have seen the lord   and she told them that he had said these things to her </s>
<s> on the evening of that first day of the week  when the disciples were together  with the doors locked for fear of the jewish leaders  jesus came and stood among them and said   peace be with you  </s>
<s> after he said this  he showed them his hands and side  the disciples were overjoyed when they saw the lord </s>
<s> again jesus said   peace be with you  as the father has sent me  i am sending you  </s>
<s> and with that he breathed on them and said   receive the holy spirit </s>
<s> if you forgive anyones sins  their sins are forgiven  if you do not forgive them  they are not forgiven  </s>
<s> now thomas  also known as didymus   one of the twelve  was not with the disciples when jesus came </s>
<s> so the other disciples told him   we have seen the lord   but he said to them   unless i see the nail marks in his hands and put my finger where the nails were  and put my hand into his side  i will not believe  </s>
<s> a week later his disciples were in the house again  and thomas was with them  though the doors were locked  jesus came and stood among them and said   peace be with you  </s>
<s> then he said to thomas   put your finger here  see my hands  reach out your hand and put it into my side  stop doubting and believe  </s>
<s> thomas said to him   my lord and my god  </s>
<s> then jesus told him   because you have seen me  you have believed  blessed are those who have not seen and yet have believed  </s>
<s> jesus performed many other signs in the presence of his disciples  which are not recorded in this book </s>
<s> but these are written that you may believe that jesus is the messiah  the son of god  and that by believing you may have life in his name </s>
<s> afterwards jesus appeared again to his disciples  by the sea of galilee  it happened this way </s>
<s> simon peter  thomas  also known as didymus   nathanael from cana in galilee  the sons of zebedee  and two other disciples were together </s>
<s>  im going out to fish   simon peter told them  and they said   well go with you   so they went out and got into the boat  but that night they caught nothing </s>
<s> early in the morning  jesus stood on the shore  but the disciples did not realise that it was jesus </s>
<s> he called out to them   friends  havent you any fish    no   they answered </s>
<s> he said   throw your net on the right side of the boat and you will find some   when they did  they were unable to haul the net in because of the large number of fish </s>
<s> then the disciple whom jesus loved said to peter   it is the lord   as soon as simon peter heard him say   it is the lord   he wrapped his outer garment round him  for he had taken it off  and jumped into the water </s>
<s> the other disciples followed in the boat  towing the net full of fish  for they were not far from shore  about a hundred metres </s>
<s> when they landed  they saw a fire of burning coals there with fish on it  and some bread </s>
<s> jesus said to them   bring some of the fish you have just caught  </s>
<s> so simon peter climbed back into the boat and dragged the net ashore  it was full of large fish  153  but even with so many the net was not torn </s>
<s> jesus said to them   come and have breakfast   none of the disciples dared ask him   who are you   they knew it was the lord </s>
<s> jesus came  took the bread and gave it to them  and did the same with the fish </s>
<s> this was now the third time jesus appeared to his disciples after he was raised from the dead </s>
<s> when they had finished eating  jesus said to simon peter   simon son of john  do you love me more than these    yes  lord   he said   you know that i love you   jesus said   feed my lambs  </s>
<s> again jesus said   simon son of john  do you love me   he answered   yes  lord  you know that i love you   jesus said   take care of my sheep  </s>
<s> the third time he said to him   simon son of john  do you love me   peter was hurt because jesus asked him the third time   do you love me   he said   lord  you know all things  you know that i love you   jesus said   feed my sheep </s>
<s> very truly i tell you  when you were younger you dressed yourself and went where you wanted  but when you are old you will stretch out your hands  and someone else will dress you and lead you where you do not want to go  </s>
<s> jesus said this to indicate the kind of death by which peter would glorify god  then he said to him   follow me  </s>
<s> peter turned and saw that the disciple whom jesus loved was following them   this was the one who had leaned back against jesus at the supper and had said   lord  who is going to betray you   </s>
<s> when peter saw him  he asked   lord  what about him  </s>
<s> jesus answered   if i want him to remain alive until i return  what is that to you  you must follow me  </s>
<s> because of this  the rumour spread among the believers that this disciple would not die  but jesus did not say that he would not die  he only said   if i want him to remain alive until i return  what is that to you  </s>
<s> this is the disciple who testifies to these things and who wrote them down  we know that his testimony is true </s>
<s> jesus did many other things as well  if every one of them were written down  i suppose that even the whole world would not have room for the books that would be written </s>
<s> in my former book  theophilus  i wrote about all that jesus began to do and to teach</s>
<s> until the day he was taken up to heaven  after giving instructions through the holy spirit to the apostles he had chosen </s>
<s> after his suffering  he presented himself to them and gave many convincing proofs that he was alive  he appeared to them over a period of forty days and spoke about the kingdom of god </s>
<s> on one occasion  while he was eating with them  he gave them this command   do not leave jerusalem  but wait for the gift my father promised  which you have heard me speak about </s>
<s> for john baptised with water  but in a few days you will be baptised with the holy spirit  </s>
<s> then they gathered round him and asked him   lord  are you at this time going to restore the kingdom to israel  </s>
<s> he said to them   it is not for you to know the times or dates the father has set by his own authority </s>
<s> but you will receive power when the holy spirit comes on you  and you will be my witnesses in jerusalem  and in all judea and samaria  and to the ends of the earth  </s>
<s> after he said this  he was taken up before their very eyes  and a cloud hid him from their sight </s>
<s> they were looking intently up into the sky as he was going  when suddenly two men dressed in white stood beside them </s>
<s>  men of galilee   they said   why do you stand here looking into the sky  this same jesus  who has been taken from you into heaven  will come back in the same way you have seen him go into heaven  </s>
<s> then the apostles returned to jerusalem from the hill called the mount of olives  a sabbath days walk from the city </s>
<s> when they arrived  they went upstairs to the room where they were staying  those present were peter  john  james and andrew  philip and thomas  bartholomew and matthew  james son of alphaeus and simon the zealot  and judas son of james </s>
<s> they all joined together constantly in prayer  along with the women and mary the mother of jesus  and with his brothers </s>
<s> in those days peter stood up among the believers  a group numbering about a hundred and twenty </s>
<s> and said   brothers and sisters  the scripture had to be fulfilled in which the holy spirit spoke long ago through david concerning judas  who served as guide for those who arrested jesus </s>
<s> he was one of our number and shared in our ministry  </s>
<s>  with the payment he received for his wickedness  judas bought a field  there he fell headlong  his body burst open and all his intestines spilled out </s>
<s> everyone in jerusalem heard about this  so they called that field in their language akeldama  that is  field of blood  </s>
<s>  for   said peter   it is written in the book of psalms    may his place be deserted  let there be no one to dwell in it     may another take his place of leadership  </s>
<s> so they nominated two men  joseph called barsabbas  also known as justus  and matthias </s>
<s> then they prayed   lord  you know everyones heart  show us which of these two you have chosen</s>
<s> to take over this apostolic ministry  which judas left to go where he belongs  </s>
<s> then they cast lots  and the lot fell to matthias  so he was added to the eleven apostles </s>
<s> when the day of pentecost came  they were all together in one place </s>
<s> suddenly a sound like the blowing of a violent wind came from heaven and filled the whole house where they were sitting </s>
<s> they saw what seemed to be tongues of fire that separated and came to rest on each of them </s>
<s> all of them were filled with the holy spirit and began to speak in other tongues as the spirit enabled them </s>
<s> now there were staying in jerusalem godfearing jews from every nation under heaven </s>
<s> when they heard this sound  a crowd came together in bewilderment  because each one heard their own language being spoken </s>
<s> utterly amazed  they asked   arent all these who are speaking galileans </s>
<s> then how is it that each of us hears them in our native language </s>
<s> parthians  medes and elamites  residents of mesopotamia  judea and cappadocia  pontus and asia </s>
<s> phrygia and pamphylia  egypt and the parts of libya near cyrene  visitors from rome</s>
<s>  both jews and converts to judaism   cretans and arabs  we hear them declaring the wonders of god in our own tongues  </s>
<s> amazed and perplexed  they asked one another   what does this mean  </s>
<s> some  however  made fun of them and said   they have had too much wine  </s>
<s> then peter stood up with the eleven  raised his voice and addressed the crowd   fellow jews and all of you who live in jerusalem  let me explain this to you  listen carefully to what i say </s>
<s> these people are not drunk  as you suppose  its only nine in the morning </s>
<s> no  this is what was spoken by the prophet joel </s>
<s>   in the last days  god says  i will pour out my spirit on all people  your sons and daughters will prophesy  your young men will see visions  your old men will dream dreams </s>
<s> even on my servants  both men and women  i will pour out my spirit in those days  and they will prophesy </s>
<s> i will show wonders in the heavens above and signs on the earth below  blood and fire and billows of smoke </s>
<s> the sun will be turned to darkness and the moon to blood before the coming of the great and glorious day of the lord </s>
<s> and everyone who calls on the name of the lord will be saved  </s>
<s>  fellow israelites  listen to this  jesus of nazareth was a man accredited by god to you by miracles  wonders and signs  which god did among you through him  as you yourselves know </s>
<s> this man was handed over to you by gods deliberate plan and foreknowledge  and you  with the help of wicked men  put him to death by nailing him to the cross </s>
<s> but god raised him from the dead  freeing him from the agony of death  because it was impossible for death to keep its hold on him </s>
<s> david said about him    i saw the lord always before me  because he is at my right hand  i will not be shaken </s>
<s> therefore my heart is glad and my tongue rejoices  my body also will rest in hope </s>
<s> because you will not abandon me to the realm of the dead  you will not let your holy one see decay </s>
<s> you have made known to me the paths of life  you will fill me with joy in your presence  </s>
<s>  fellow israelites  i can tell you confidently that the patriarch david died and was buried  and his tomb is here to this day </s>
<s> but he was a prophet and knew that god had promised him on oath that he would place one of his descendants on his throne </s>
<s> seeing what was to come  he spoke of the resurrection of the messiah  that he was not abandoned to the realm of the dead  nor did his body see decay </s>
<s> god has raised this jesus to life  and we are all witnesses of it </s>
<s> exalted to the right hand of god  he has received from the father the promised holy spirit and has poured out what you now see and hear </s>
<s> for david did not ascend to heaven  and yet he said    the lord said to my lord   sit at my right hand</s>
<s> until i make your enemies a footstool for your feet   </s>
<s>  therefore let all israel be assured of this  god has made this jesus  whom you crucified  both lord and messiah  </s>
<s> when the people heard this  they were cut to the heart and said to peter and the other apostles   brothers  what shall we do  </s>
<s> peter replied   repent and be baptised  every one of you  in the name of jesus christ for the forgiveness of your sins  and you will receive the gift of the holy spirit </s>
<s> the promise is for you and your children and for all who are far off  for all whom the lord our god will call  </s>
<s> with many other words he warned them  and he pleaded with them   save yourselves from this corrupt generation  </s>
<s> those who accepted his message were baptised  and about three thousand were added to their number that day </s>
<s> they devoted themselves to the apostles teaching and to fellowship  to the breaking of bread and to prayer </s>
<s> everyone was filled with awe at the many wonders and signs performed by the apostles </s>
<s> all the believers were together and had everything in common </s>
<s> they sold property and possessions to give to anyone who had need </s>
<s> every day they continued to meet together in the temple courts  they broke bread in their homes and ate together with glad and sincere hearts </s>
<s> praising god and enjoying the favour of all the people  and the lord added to their number daily those who were being saved </s>
<s> one day peter and john were going up to the temple at the time of prayer  at three in the afternoon </s>
<s> now a man who was lame from birth was being carried to the temple gate called beautiful  where he was put every day to beg from those going into the temple courts </s>
<s> when he saw peter and john about to enter  he asked them for money </s>
<s> peter looked straight at him  as did john  then peter said   look at us  </s>
<s> so the man gave them his attention  expecting to get something from them </s>
<s> then peter said   silver or gold i do not have  but what i do have i give you  in the name of jesus christ of nazareth  walk  </s>
<s> taking him by the right hand  he helped him up  and instantly the mans feet and ankles became strong </s>
<s> he jumped to his feet and began to walk  then he went with them into the temple courts  walking and jumping  and praising god </s>
<s> when all the people saw him walking and praising god </s>
<s> they recognised him as the same man who used to sit begging at the temple gate called beautiful  and they were filled with wonder and amazement at what had happened to him </s>
<s> while the man held on to peter and john  all the people were astonished and came running to them in the place called solomons colonnade </s>
<s> when peter saw this  he said to them   fellow israelites  why does this surprise you  why do you stare at us as if by our own power or godliness we had made this man walk </s>
<s> the god of abraham  isaac and jacob  the god of our fathers  has glorified his servant jesus  you handed him over to be killed  and you disowned him before pilate  though he had decided to let him go </s>
<s> you disowned the holy and righteous one and asked that a murderer be released to you </s>
<s> you killed the author of life  but god raised him from the dead  we are witnesses of this </s>
<s> by faith in the name of jesus  this man whom you see and know was made strong  it is jesus name and the faith that comes through him that has completely healed him  as you can all see </s>
<s>  now  fellow israelites  i know that you acted in ignorance  as did your leaders </s>
<s> but this is how god fulfilled what he had foretold through all the prophets  saying that his messiah would suffer </s>
<s> repent  then  and turn to god  so that your sins may be wiped out  that times of refreshing may come from the lord </s>
<s> and that he may send the messiah  who has been appointed for you  even jesus </s>
<s> heaven must receive him until the time comes for god to restore everything  as he promised long ago through his holy prophets </s>
<s> for moses said   the lord your god will raise up for you a prophet like me from among your own people  you must listen to everything he tells you </s>
<s> anyone who does not listen to him will be completely cut off from their people  </s>
<s>  indeed  beginning with samuel  all the prophets who have spoken have foretold these days </s>
<s> and you are heirs of the prophets and of the covenant god made with your fathers  he said to abraham   through your offspring all peoples on earth will be blessed  </s>
<s> when god raised up his servant  he sent him first to you to bless you by turning each of you from your wicked ways  </s>
<s> the priests and the captain of the temple guard and the sadducees came up to peter and john while they were speaking to the people </s>
<s> they were greatly disturbed because the apostles were teaching the people  proclaiming in jesus the resurrection of the dead </s>
<s> they seized peter and john and  because it was evening  they put them in jail until the next day </s>
<s> but many who heard the message believed  so the number of men who believed grew to about five thousand </s>
<s> the next day the rulers  the elders and the teachers of the law met in jerusalem </s>
<s> annas the high priest was there  and so were caiaphas  john  alexander and others of the high priests family </s>
<s> they had peter and john brought before them and began to question them   by what power or what name did you do this  </s>
<s> then peter  filled with the holy spirit  said to them   rulers and elders of the people </s>
<s> if we are being called to account today for an act of kindness shown to a man who was lame and are being asked how he was healed </s>
<s> then know this  you and all the people of israel  it is by the name of jesus christ of nazareth  whom you crucified but whom god raised from the dead  that this man stands before you healed </s>
<s> jesus is   the stone you builders rejected  which has become the cornerstone  </s>
<s> when they saw the courage of peter and john and realised that they were unschooled  ordinary men  they were astonished and they took note that these men had been with jesus </s>
<s> but since they could see the man who had been healed standing there with them  there was nothing they could say </s>
<s> so they ordered them to withdraw from the sanhedrin and then conferred together </s>
<s>  what are we going to do with these men   they asked   everyone living in jerusalem knows they have performed a notable sign  and we cannot deny it </s>
<s> but to stop this thing from spreading any further among the people  we must warn them to speak no longer to anyone in this name  </s>
<s> then they called them in again and commanded them not to speak or teach at all in the name of jesus </s>
<s> but peter and john replied   which is right in gods eyes  to listen to you  or to him  you be the judges </s>
<s> as for us  we cannot help speaking about what we have seen and heard  </s>
<s> after further threats they let them go  they could not decide how to punish them  because all the people were praising god for what had happened </s>
<s> for the man who was miraculously healed was over forty years old </s>
<s> on their release  peter and john went back to their own people and reported all that the chief priests and the elders had said to them </s>
<s> when they heard this  they raised their voices together in prayer to god   sovereign lord   they said   you made the heavens and the earth and the sea  and everything in them </s>
<s> you spoke by the holy spirit through the mouth of your servant  our father david    why do the nations rage and the peoples plot in vain </s>
<s> the kings of the earth rise up and the rulers band together against the lord and against his anointed one  </s>
<s> after they prayed  the place where they were meeting was shaken  and they were all filled with the holy spirit and spoke the word of god boldly </s>
<s> all the believers were one in heart and mind  no one claimed that any of their possessions was their own  but they shared everything they had </s>
<s> with great power the apostles continued to testify to the resurrection of the lord jesus  and gods grace was so powerfully at work in them all</s>
<s> that there was no needy person among them  for from time to time those who owned land or houses sold them  brought the money from the sales</s>
<s> and put it at the apostles feet  and it was distributed to anyone who had need </s>
<s> joseph  a levite from cyprus  whom the apostles called barnabas  which means  son of encouragement  </s>
<s> sold a field he owned and brought the money and put it at the apostles feet </s>
<s> now a man named ananias  together with his wife sapphira  also sold a piece of property </s>
<s> with his wifes full knowledge he kept back part of the money for himself  but brought the rest and put it at the apostles feet </s>
<s> then peter said   ananias  how is it that satan has so filled your heart that you have lied to the holy spirit and have kept for yourself some of the money you received for the land </s>
<s> didnt it belong to you before it was sold  and after it was sold  wasnt the money at your disposal  what made you think of doing such a thing  you have not lied just to human beings but to god  </s>
<s> when ananias heard this  he fell down and died  and great fear seized all who heard what had happened </s>
<s> then some young men came forward  wrapped up his body  and carried him out and buried him </s>
<s> about three hours later his wife came in  not knowing what had happened </s>
<s> peter asked her   tell me  is this the price you and ananias got for the land    yes   she said   that is the price  </s>
<s> peter said to her   how could you conspire to test the spirit of the lord  listen  the feet of the men who buried your husband are at the door  and they will carry you out also  </s>
<s> at that moment she fell down at his feet and died  then the young men came in and  finding her dead  carried her out and buried her beside her husband </s>
<s> great fear seized the whole church and all who heard about these events </s>
<s> the apostles performed many signs and wonders among the people  and all the believers used to meet together in solomons colonnade </s>
<s> no one else dared join them  even though they were highly regarded by the people </s>
<s> nevertheless  more and more men and women believed in the lord and were added to their number </s>
<s> as a result  people brought those who were ill into the streets and laid them on beds and mats so that at least peters shadow might fall on some of them as he passed by </s>
<s> crowds gathered also from the towns around jerusalem  bringing those who were ill and those tormented by impure spirits  and all of them were healed </s>
<s> then the high priest and all his associates  who were members of the party of the sadducees  were filled with jealousy </s>
<s> they arrested the apostles and put them in the public jail </s>
<s> but during the night an angel of the lord opened the doors of the jail and brought them out </s>
<s>  go  stand in the temple courts   he said   and tell the people all about this new life  </s>
<s> at daybreak they entered the temple courts  as they had been told  and began to teach the people  when the high priest and his associates arrived  they called together the sanhedrin  the full assembly of the elders of israel  and sent to the jail for the apostles </s>
<s> but on arriving at the jail  the officers did not find them there  so they went back and reported </s>
<s>  we found the jail securely locked  with the guards standing at the doors  but when we opened them  we found no one inside  </s>
<s> on hearing this report  the captain of the temple guard and the chief priests were at a loss  wondering what this might lead to </s>
<s> then someone came and said   look  the men you put in jail are standing in the temple courts teaching the people  </s>
<s> at that  the captain went with his officers and brought the apostles  they did not use force  because they feared that the people would stone them </s>
<s> the apostles were brought in and made to appear before the sanhedrin to be questioned by the high priest </s>
<s>  we gave you strict orders not to teach in this name   he said   yet you have filled jerusalem with your teaching and are determined to make us guilty of this mans blood  </s>
<s> peter and the other apostles replied   we must obey god rather than human beings </s>
<s> the god of our ancestors raised jesus from the dead  whom you killed by hanging him on a cross </s>
<s> god exalted him to his own right hand as prince and saviour that he might bring israel to repentance and forgive their sins </s>
<s> we are witnesses of these things  and so is the holy spirit  whom god has given to those who obey him  </s>
<s> when they heard this  they were furious and wanted to put them to death </s>
<s> but a pharisee named gamaliel  a teacher of the law  who was honoured by all the people  stood up in the sanhedrin and ordered that the men be put outside for a little while </s>
<s> then he addressed the sanhedrin   men of israel  consider carefully what you intend to do to these men </s>
<s> some time ago theudas appeared  claiming to be somebody  and about four hundred men rallied to him  he was killed  all his followers were dispersed  and it all came to nothing </s>
<s> after him  judas the galilean appeared in the days of the census and led a band of people in revolt  he too was killed  and all his followers were scattered </s>
<s> therefore  in the present case i advise you  leave these men alone  let them go  for if their purpose or activity is of human origin  it will fail </s>
<s> but if it is from god  you will not be able to stop these men  you will only find yourselves fighting against god  </s>
<s> his speech persuaded them  they called the apostles in and had them flogged  then they ordered them not to speak in the name of jesus  and let them go </s>
<s> the apostles left the sanhedrin  rejoicing because they had been counted worthy of suffering disgrace for the name </s>
<s> day after day  in the temple courts and from house to house  they never stopped teaching and proclaiming the good news that jesus is the messiah </s>
<s> in those days when the number of disciples was increasing  the hellenistic jews among them complained against the hebraic jews because their widows were being overlooked in the daily distribution of food </s>
<s> so the twelve gathered all the disciples together and said   it would not be right for us to neglect the ministry of the word of god in order to wait on tables </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  choose seven men from among you who are known to be full of the spirit and wisdom  we will turn this responsibility over to them</s>
<s> and will give our attention to prayer and the ministry of the word  </s>
<s> this proposal pleased the whole group  they chose stephen  a man full of faith and of the holy spirit  also philip  procorus  nicanor  timon  parmenas  and nicolas from antioch  a convert to judaism </s>
<s> they presented these men to the apostles  who prayed and laid their hands on them </s>
<s> so the word of god spread  the number of disciples in jerusalem increased rapidly  and a large number of priests became obedient to the faith </s>
<s> now stephen  a man full of gods grace and power  performed great wonders and signs among the people </s>
<s> opposition arose  however  from members of the synagogue of the freedmen  as it was called   jews of cyrene and alexandria as well as the provinces of cilicia and asia  who began to argue with stephen </s>
<s> but they could not stand up against the wisdom the spirit gave him as he spoke </s>
<s> then they secretly persuaded some men to say   we have heard stephen speak blasphemous words against moses and against god  </s>
<s> so they stirred up the people and the elders and the teachers of the law  they seized stephen and brought him before the sanhedrin </s>
<s> they produced false witnesses  who testified   this fellow never stops speaking against this holy place and against the law </s>
<s> for we have heard him say that this jesus of nazareth will destroy this place and change the customs moses handed down to us  </s>
<s> all who were sitting in the sanhedrin looked intently at stephen  and they saw that his face was like the face of an angel </s>
<s> then the high priest asked stephen   are these charges true  </s>
<s> to this he replied   brothers and fathers  listen to me  the god of glory appeared to our father abraham while he was still in mesopotamia  before he lived in harran </s>
<s>  leave your country and your people   god said   and go to the land i will show you  </s>
<s>  so he left the land of the chaldeans and settled in harran  after the death of his father  god sent him to this land where you are now living </s>
<s> he gave him no inheritance here  not even enough ground to set his foot on  but god promised him that he and his descendants after him would possess the land  even though at that time abraham had no child </s>
<s> god spoke to him in this way   for four hundred years your descendants will be strangers in a country not their own  and they will be enslaved and illtreated </s>
<s> but i will punish the nation they serve as slaves   god said   and afterwards they will come out of that country and worship me in this place  </s>
<s> then he gave abraham the covenant of circumcision  and abraham became the father of isaac and circumcised him eight days after his birth  later isaac became the father of jacob  and jacob became the father of the twelve patriarchs </s>
<s>  because the patriarchs were jealous of joseph  they sold him as a slave into egypt  but god was with him</s>
<s> and rescued him from all his troubles  he gave joseph wisdom and enabled him to gain the goodwill of pharaoh king of egypt  so pharaoh made him ruler over egypt and all his palace </s>
<s>  then a famine struck all egypt and canaan  bringing great suffering  and our ancestors could not find food </s>
<s> when jacob heard that there was grain in egypt  he sent our forefathers on their first visit </s>
<s> on their second visit  joseph told his brothers who he was  and pharaoh learned about josephs family </s>
<s> after this  joseph sent for his father jacob and his whole family  seventyfive in all </s>
<s> then jacob went down to egypt  where he and our ancestors died </s>
<s> their bodies were brought back to shechem and placed in the tomb that abraham had bought from the sons of hamor at shechem for a certain sum of money </s>
<s>  as the time drew near for god to fulfil his promise to abraham  the number of our people in egypt had greatly increased </s>
<s> then  a new king  to whom joseph meant nothing  came to power in egypt  </s>
<s> he dealt treacherously with our people and oppressed our ancestors by forcing them to throw out their newborn babies so that they would die </s>
<s>  at that time moses was born  and he was no ordinary child  for three months he was cared for by his family </s>
<s> when he was placed outside  pharaohs daughter took him and brought him up as her own son </s>
<s> moses was educated in all the wisdom of the egyptians and was powerful in speech and action </s>
<s>  when moses was forty years old  he decided to visit his own people  the israelites </s>
<s> he saw one of them being illtreated by an egyptian  so he went to his defence and avenged him by killing the egyptian </s>
<s> moses thought that his own people would realise that god was using him to rescue them  but they did not </s>
<s> the next day moses came upon two israelites who were fighting  he tried to reconcile them by saying   men  you are brothers  why do you want to hurt each other  </s>
<s>  but the man who was illtreating the other pushed moses aside and said   who made you ruler and judge over us </s>
<s> are you thinking of killing me as you killed the egyptian yesterday  </s>
<s> when moses heard this  he fled to midian  where he settled as a foreigner and had two sons </s>
<s>  after forty years had passed  an angel appeared to moses in the flames of a burning bush in the desert near mount sinai </s>
<s> when he saw this  he was amazed at the sight  as he went over to get a closer look  he heard the lord say </s>
<s>  i am the god of your fathers  the god of abraham  isaac and jacob   moses trembled with fear and did not dare to look </s>
<s>  then the lord said to him   take off your sandals  for the place where you are standing is holy ground </s>
<s> i have indeed seen the oppression of my people in egypt  i have heard their groaning and have come down to set them free  now come  i will send you back to egypt  </s>
<s>  this is the same moses they had rejected with the words   who made you ruler and judge   he was sent to be their ruler and deliverer by god himself  through the angel who appeared to him in the bush </s>
<s> he led them out of egypt and performed wonders and signs in egypt  at the red sea and for forty years in the wilderness </s>
<s>  this is the moses who told the israelites   god will raise up for you a prophet like me from your own people  </s>
<s> he was in the assembly in the wilderness  with the angel who spoke to him on mount sinai  and with our ancestors  and he received living words to pass on to us </s>
<s>  but our ancestors refused to obey him  instead  they rejected him and in their hearts turned back to egypt </s>
<s> they told aaron   make us gods who will go before us  as for this fellow moses who led us out of egypt  we dont know what has happened to him  </s>
<s> that was the time they made an idol in the form of a calf  they brought sacrifices to it and revelled in what their own hands had made </s>
<s> but god turned away from them and gave them over to the worship of the sun  moon and stars  this agrees with what is written in the book of the prophets    did you bring me sacrifices and offerings for forty years in the wilderness  people of israel </s>
<s> you have taken up the tabernacle of molek and the star of your god rephan  the idols you made to worship  therefore i will send you into exile  beyond babylon </s>
<s>  our ancestors had the tabernacle of the covenant law with them in the wilderness  it had been made as god directed moses  according to the pattern he had seen </s>
<s> after receiving the tabernacle  our ancestors under joshua brought it with them when they took the land from the nations god drove out before them  it remained in the land until the time of david </s>
<s> who enjoyed gods favour and asked that he might provide a dwellingplace for the god of jacob </s>
<s> but it was solomon who built a house for him </s>
<s>  however  the most high does not live in houses made by human hands  as the prophet says </s>
<s>   heaven is my throne  and the earth is my footstool  what kind of house will you build for me  or where will my resting place be </s>
<s> has not my hand made all these things  </s>
<s>  you stiffnecked people  your hearts and ears are still uncircumcised  you are just like your ancestors  you always resist the holy spirit </s>
<s> was there ever a prophet your ancestors did not persecute  they even killed those who predicted the coming of the righteous one  and now you have betrayed and murdered him </s>
<s> you who have received the law that was given through angels but have not obeyed it  </s>
<s> when the members of the sanhedrin heard this  they were furious and gnashed their teeth at him </s>
<s> but stephen  full of the holy spirit  looked up to heaven and saw the glory of god  and jesus standing at the right hand of god </s>
<s>  look   he said   i see heaven open and the son of man standing at the right hand of god  </s>
<s> at this they covered their ears and  yelling at the top of their voices  they all rushed at him </s>
<s> dragged him out of the city and began to stone him  meanwhile  the witnesses laid their coats at the feet of a young man named saul </s>
<s> while they were stoning him  stephen prayed   lord jesus  receive my spirit  </s>
<s> then he fell on his knees and cried out   lord  do not hold this sin against them   when he had said this  he fell asleep </s>
<s> and saul approved of their killing him  on that day a great persecution broke out against the church in jerusalem  and all except the apostles were scattered throughout judea and samaria </s>
<s> godly men buried stephen and mourned deeply for him </s>
<s> but saul began to destroy the church  going from house to house  he dragged off both men and women and put them in prison </s>
<s> those who had been scattered preached the word wherever they went </s>
<s> philip went down to a city in samaria and proclaimed the messiah there </s>
<s> when the crowds heard philip and saw the signs he performed  they all paid close attention to what he said </s>
<s> for with shrieks  impure spirits came out of many  and many who were paralysed or lame were healed </s>
<s> so there was great joy in that city </s>
<s> now for some time a man named simon had practised sorcery in the city and amazed all the people of samaria  he boasted that he was someone great </s>
<s> and all the people  both high and low  gave him their attention and exclaimed   this man is rightly called the great power of god  </s>
<s> they followed him because he had amazed them for a long time with his sorcery </s>
<s> but when they believed philip as he proclaimed the good news of the kingdom of god and the name of jesus christ  they were baptised  both men and women </s>
<s> simon himself believed and was baptised  and he followed philip everywhere  astonished by the great signs and miracles he saw </s>
<s> when the apostles in jerusalem heard that samaria had accepted the word of god  they sent peter and john to samaria </s>
<s> when they arrived  they prayed for the new believers there that they might receive the holy spirit </s>
<s> because the holy spirit had not yet come on any of them  they had simply been baptised in the name of the lord jesus </s>
<s> then peter and john placed their hands on them  and they received the holy spirit </s>
<s> when simon saw that the spirit was given at the laying on of the apostles hands  he offered them money</s>
<s> and said   give me also this ability so that everyone on whom i lay my hands may receive the holy spirit  </s>
<s> peter answered   may your money perish with you  because you thought you could buy the gift of god with money </s>
<s> you have no part or share in this ministry  because your heart is not right before god </s>
<s> repent of this wickedness and pray to the lord in the hope that he may forgive you for having such a thought in your heart </s>
<s> for i see that you are full of bitterness and captive to sin  </s>
<s> then simon answered   pray to the lord for me so that nothing you have said may happen to me  </s>
<s> after they had further proclaimed the word of the lord and testified about jesus  peter and john returned to jerusalem  preaching the gospel in many samaritan villages </s>
<s> now an angel of the lord said to philip   go south to the road  the desert road  that goes down from jerusalem to gaza  </s>
<s> so he started out  and on his way he met an ethiopian eunuch  an important official in charge of all the treasury of the kandake  which means  queen of the ethiopians   this man had gone to jerusalem to worship </s>
<s> and on his way home was sitting in his chariot reading the book of isaiah the prophet </s>
<s> the spirit told philip   go to that chariot and stay near it  </s>
<s> then philip ran up to the chariot and heard the man reading isaiah the prophet   do you understand what you are reading   philip asked </s>
<s>  how can i   he said   unless someone explains it to me   so he invited philip to come up and sit with him </s>
<s> this is the passage of scripture the eunuch was reading   he was led like a sheep to the slaughter  and as a lamb before its shearer is silent  so he did not open his mouth </s>
<s> in his humiliation he was deprived of justice  who can speak of his descendants  for his life was taken from the earth  </s>
<s> the eunuch asked philip   tell me  please  who is the prophet talking about  himself or someone else  </s>
<s> then philip began with that very passage of scripture and told him the good news about jesus </s>
<s> as they travelled along the road  they came to some water and the eunuch said   look  here is water  what can stand in the way of my being baptised   </s>
<s> </s>
<s> and he gave orders to stop the chariot  then both philip and the eunuch went down into the water and philip baptised him </s>
<s> when they came up out of the water  the spirit of the lord suddenly took philip away  and the eunuch did not see him again  but went on his way rejoicing </s>
<s> philip  however  appeared at azotus and travelled about  preaching the gospel in all the towns until he reached caesarea </s>
<s> meanwhile  saul was still breathing out murderous threats against the lords disciples  he went to the high priest</s>
<s> and asked him for letters to the synagogues in damascus  so that if he found any there who belonged to the way  whether men or women  he might take them as prisoners to jerusalem </s>
<s> as he neared damascus on his journey  suddenly a light from heaven flashed around him </s>
<s> he fell to the ground and heard a voice say to him   saul  saul  why do you persecute me  </s>
<s>  who are you  lord   saul asked   i am jesus  whom you are persecuting   he replied </s>
<s>  now get up and go into the city  and you will be told what you must do  </s>
<s> the men travelling with saul stood there speechless  they heard the sound but did not see anyone </s>
<s> saul got up from the ground  but when he opened his eyes he could see nothing  so they led him by the hand into damascus </s>
<s> for three days he was blind  and did not eat or drink anything </s>
<s> in damascus there was a disciple named ananias  the lord called to him in a vision   ananias    yes  lord   he answered </s>
<s> the lord told him   go to the house of judas on straight street and ask for a man from tarsus named saul  for he is praying </s>
<s> in a vision he has seen a man named ananias come and place his hands on him to restore his sight  </s>
<s>  lord   ananias answered   i have heard many reports about this man and all the harm he has done to your holy people in jerusalem </s>
<s> and he has come here with authority from the chief priests to arrest all who call on your name  </s>
<s> but the lord said to ananias   go  this man is my chosen instrument to proclaim my name to the gentiles and their kings and to the people of israel </s>
<s> i will show him how much he must suffer for my name  </s>
<s> then ananias went to the house and entered it  placing his hands on saul  he said   brother saul  the lord  jesus  who appeared to you on the road as you were coming here  has sent me so that you may see again and be filled with the holy spirit  </s>
<s> immediately  something like scales fell from sauls eyes  and he could see again  he got up and was baptised </s>
<s> and after taking some food  he regained his strength  saul spent several days with the disciples in damascus </s>
<s> at once he began to preach in the synagogues that jesus is the son of god </s>
<s> all those who heard him were astonished and asked   isnt he the man who caused havoc in jerusalem among those who call on this name  and hasnt he come here to take them as prisoners to the chief priests  </s>
<s> yet saul grew more and more powerful and baffled the jews living in damascus by proving that jesus is the messiah </s>
<s> after many days had gone by  there was a conspiracy among the jews to kill him </s>
<s> but saul learned of their plan  day and night they kept close watch on the city gates in order to kill him </s>
<s> but his followers took him by night and lowered him in a basket through an opening in the wall </s>
<s> when he came to jerusalem  he tried to join the disciples  but they were all afraid of him  not believing that he really was a disciple </s>
<s> but barnabas took him and brought him to the apostles  he told them how saul on his journey had seen the lord and that the lord had spoken to him  and how in damascus he had preached fearlessly in the name of jesus </s>
<s> so saul stayed with them and moved about freely in jerusalem  speaking boldly in the name of the lord </s>
<s> he talked and debated with the hellenistic jews  but they tried to kill him </s>
<s> when the believers learned of this  they took him down to caesarea and sent him off to tarsus </s>
<s> then the church throughout judea  galilee and samaria enjoyed a time of peace and was strengthened  living in the fear of the lord and encouraged by the holy spirit  it increased in numbers </s>
<s> as peter travelled about the country  he went to visit the lords people who lived in lydda </s>
<s> there he found a man named aeneas  who was paralysed and had been bedridden for eight years </s>
<s>  aeneas   peter said to him   jesus christ heals you  get up and roll up your mat   immediately aeneas got up </s>
<s> all those who lived in lydda and sharon saw him and turned to the lord </s>
<s> in joppa there was a disciple named tabitha  in greek her name is dorcas   she was always doing good and helping the poor </s>
<s> about that time she became ill and died  and her body was washed and placed in an upstairs room </s>
<s> lydda was near joppa  so when the disciples heard that peter was in lydda  they sent two men to him and urged him   please come at once  </s>
<s> peter went with them  and when he arrived he was taken upstairs to the room  all the widows stood round him  crying and showing him the robes and other clothing that dorcas had made while she was still with them </s>
<s> peter sent them all out of the room  then he got down on his knees and prayed  turning towards the dead woman  he said   tabitha  get up   she opened her eyes  and seeing peter she sat up </s>
<s> he took her by the hand and helped her to her feet  then he called for the believers  especially the widows  and presented her to them alive </s>
<s> this became known all over joppa  and many people believed in the lord </s>
<s> peter stayed in joppa for some time with a tanner named simon </s>
<s> at caesarea there was a man named cornelius  a centurion in what was known as the italian regiment </s>
<s> he and all his family were devout and godfearing  he gave generously to those in need and prayed to god regularly </s>
<s> one day at about three in the afternoon he had a vision  he distinctly saw an angel of god  who came to him and said   cornelius  </s>
<s> cornelius stared at him in fear   what is it  lord   he asked  the angel answered   your prayers and gifts to the poor have come up as a memorial offering before god </s>
<s> now send men to joppa to bring back a man named simon who is called peter </s>
<s> he is staying with simon the tanner  whose house is by the sea  </s>
<s> when the angel who spoke to him had gone  cornelius called two of his servants and a devout soldier who was one of his attendants </s>
<s> he told them everything that had happened and sent them to joppa </s>
<s> about noon the following day as they were on their journey and approaching the city  peter went up on the roof to pray </s>
<s> he became hungry and wanted something to eat  and while the meal was being prepared  he fell into a trance </s>
<s> he saw heaven opened and something like a large sheet being let down to earth by its four corners </s>
<s> it contained all kinds of fourfooted animals  as well as reptiles and birds </s>
<s> then a voice told him   get up  peter  kill and eat  </s>
<s>  surely not  lord   peter replied   i have never eaten anything impure or unclean  </s>
<s> the voice spoke to him a second time   do not call anything impure that god has made clean  </s>
<s> this happened three times  and immediately the sheet was taken back to heaven </s>
<s> while peter was wondering about the meaning of the vision  the men sent by cornelius found out where simons house was and stopped at the gate </s>
<s> they called out  asking if simon who was known as peter was staying there </s>
<s> while peter was still thinking about the vision  the spirit said to him   simon  three men are looking for you </s>
<s> so get up and go downstairs  do not hesitate to go with them  for i have sent them  </s>
<s> peter went down and said to the men   im the one youre looking for  why have you come  </s>
<s> the men replied   we have come from cornelius the centurion  he is a righteous and godfearing man  who is respected by all the jewish people  a holy angel told him to ask you to come to his house so that he could hear what you have to say  </s>
<s> then peter invited the men into the house to be his guests  the next day peter started out with them  and some of the believers from joppa went along </s>
<s> the following day he arrived in caesarea  cornelius was expecting them and had called together his relatives and close friends </s>
<s> as peter entered the house  cornelius met him and fell at his feet in reverence </s>
<s> but peter made him get up   stand up   he said   i am only a man myself  </s>
<s> while talking with him  peter went inside and found a large gathering of people </s>
<s> he said to them   you are well aware that it is against our law for a jew to associate with or visit a gentile  but god has shown me that i should not call anyone impure or unclean </s>
<s> so when i was sent for  i came without raising any objection  may i ask why you sent for me  </s>
<s> cornelius answered   three days ago i was in my house praying at this hour  at three in the afternoon  suddenly a man in shining clothes stood before me</s>
<s> and said   cornelius  god has heard your prayer and remembered your gifts to the poor </s>
<s> send to joppa for simon who is called peter  he is a guest in the home of simon the tanner  who lives by the sea  </s>
<s> so i sent for you immediately  and it was good of you to come  now we are all here in the presence of god to listen to everything the lord has commanded you to tell us  </s>
<s> then peter began to speak   i now realise how true it is that god does not show favouritism</s>
<s> but accepts from every nation the one who fears him and does what is right </s>
<s> you know the message god sent to the people of israel  announcing the good news of peace through jesus christ  who is lord of all </s>
<s> you know what has happened throughout the province of judea  beginning in galilee after the baptism that john preached </s>
<s> how god anointed jesus of nazareth with the holy spirit and power  and how he went around doing good and healing all who were under the power of the devil  because god was with him </s>
<s>  we are witnesses of everything he did in the country of the jews and in jerusalem  they killed him by hanging him on a cross </s>
<s> but god raised him from the dead on the third day and caused him to be seen </s>
<s> he was not seen by all the people  but by witnesses whom god had already chosen  by us who ate and drank with him after he rose from the dead </s>
<s> he commanded us to preach to the people and to testify that he is the one whom god appointed as judge of the living and the dead </s>
<s> all the prophets testify about him that everyone who believes in him receives forgiveness of sins through his name  </s>
<s> while peter was still speaking these words  the holy spirit came on all who heard the message </s>
<s> the circumcised believers who had come with peter were astonished that the gift of the holy spirit had been poured out even on gentiles </s>
<s> for they heard them speaking in tongues and praising god  then peter said </s>
<s>  surely no one can stand in the way of their being baptised with water  they have received the holy spirit just as we have  </s>
<s> so he ordered that they be baptised in the name of jesus christ  then they asked peter to stay with them for a few days </s>
<s> the apostles and the believers throughout judea heard that the gentiles also had received the word of god </s>
<s> so when peter went up to jerusalem  the circumcised believers criticised him</s>
<s> and said   you went into the house of uncircumcised men and ate with them  </s>
<s> starting from the beginning  peter told them the whole story </s>
<s>  i was in the city of joppa praying  and in a trance i saw a vision  i saw something like a large sheet being let down from heaven by its four corners  and it came down to where i was </s>
<s> i looked into it and saw fourfooted animals of the earth  wild beasts  reptiles and birds </s>
<s> then i heard a voice telling me   get up  peter  kill and eat  </s>
<s>  i replied   surely not  lord  nothing impure or unclean has ever entered my mouth  </s>
<s>  the voice spoke from heaven a second time   do not call anything impure that god has made clean  </s>
<s> this happened three times  and then it was all pulled up to heaven again </s>
<s>  right then three men who had been sent to me from caesarea stopped at the house where i was staying </s>
<s> the spirit told me to have no hesitation about going with them  these six brothers also went with me  and we entered the mans house </s>
<s> he told us how he had seen an angel appear in his house and say   send to joppa for simon who is called peter </s>
<s> he will bring you a message through which you and all your household will be saved  </s>
<s>  as i began to speak  the holy spirit came on them as he had come on us at the beginning </s>
<s> then i remembered what the lord had said   john baptised with water  but you will be baptised with the holy spirit  </s>
<s> so if god gave them the same gift he gave us who believed in the lord jesus christ  who was i to think that i could stand in gods way  </s>
<s> when they heard this  they had no further objections and praised god  saying   so then  even to gentiles god has granted repentance that leads to life  </s>
<s> now those who had been scattered by the persecution that broke out when stephen was killed travelled as far as phoenicia  cyprus and antioch  spreading the word only among jews </s>
<s> some of them  however  men from cyprus and cyrene  went to antioch and began to speak to greeks also  telling them the good news about the lord jesus </s>
<s> the lords hand was with them  and a great number of people believed and turned to the lord </s>
<s> news of this reached the church in jerusalem  and they sent barnabas to antioch </s>
<s> when he arrived and saw what the grace of god had done  he was glad and encouraged them all to remain true to the lord with all their hearts </s>
<s> he was a good man  full of the holy spirit and faith  and a great number of people were brought to the lord </s>
<s> then barnabas went to tarsus to look for saul </s>
<s> and when he found him  he brought him to antioch  so for a whole year barnabas and saul met with the church and taught great numbers of people  the disciples were called christians first at antioch </s>
<s> during this time some prophets came down from jerusalem to antioch </s>
<s> one of them  named agabus  stood up and through the spirit predicted that a severe famine would spread over the entire roman world   this happened during the reign of claudius  </s>
<s> the disciples  as each one was able  decided to provide help for the brothers and sisters living in judea </s>
<s> this they did  sending their gift to the elders by barnabas and saul </s>
<s> it was about this time that king herod arrested some who belonged to the church  intending to persecute them </s>
<s> he had james  the brother of john  put to death with the sword </s>
<s> when he saw that this met with approval among the jews  he proceeded to seize peter also  this happened during the festival of unleavened bread </s>
<s> after arresting him  he put him in prison  handing him over to be guarded by four squads of four soldiers each  herod intended to bring him out for public trial after the passover </s>
<s> so peter was kept in prison  but the church was earnestly praying to god for him </s>
<s> the night before herod was to bring him to trial  peter was sleeping between two soldiers  bound with two chains  and sentries stood guard at the entrance </s>
<s> suddenly an angel of the lord appeared and a light shone in the cell  he struck peter on the side and woke him up   quick  get up   he said  and the chains fell off peters wrists </s>
<s> then the angel said to him   put on your clothes and sandals   and peter did so   wrap your cloak round you and follow me   the angel told him </s>
<s> peter followed him out of the prison  but he had no idea that what the angel was doing was really happening  he thought he was seeing a vision </s>
<s> they passed the first and second guards and came to the iron gate leading to the city  it opened for them by itself  and they went through it  when they had walked the length of one street  suddenly the angel left him </s>
<s> then peter came to himself and said   now i know without a doubt that the lord has sent his angel and rescued me from herods clutches and from everything the jewish people were hoping would happen  </s>
<s> when this had dawned on him  he went to the house of mary the mother of john  also called mark  where many people had gathered and were praying </s>
<s> peter knocked at the outer entrance  and a servant named rhoda came to answer the door </s>
<s> when she recognised peters voice  she was so overjoyed she ran back without opening it and exclaimed   peter is at the door  </s>
<s>  youre out of your mind   they told her  when she kept insisting that it was so  they said   it must be his angel  </s>
<s> but peter kept on knocking  and when they opened the door and saw him  they were astonished </s>
<s> peter motioned with his hand for them to be quiet and described how the lord had brought him out of prison   tell james and the other brothers and sisters about this   he said  and then he left for another place </s>
<s> in the morning  there was no small commotion among the soldiers as to what had become of peter </s>
<s> after herod had a thorough search made for him and did not find him  he crossexamined the guards and ordered that they be executed  then herod went from judea to caesarea and stayed there </s>
<s> he had been quarrelling with the people of tyre and sidon  they now joined together and sought an audience with him  after securing the support of blastus  a trusted personal servant of the king  they asked for peace  because they depended on the kings country for their food supply </s>
<s> on the appointed day herod  wearing his royal robes  sat on his throne and delivered a public address to the people </s>
<s> they shouted   this is the voice of a god  not of a man  </s>
<s> immediately  because herod did not give praise to god  an angel of the lord struck him down  and he was eaten by worms and died </s>
<s> but the word of god continued to spread and flourish </s>
<s> when barnabas and saul had finished their mission  they returned from jerusalem  taking with them john  also called mark </s>
<s> now in the church at antioch there were prophets and teachers  barnabas  simeon called niger  lucius of cyrene  manaen  who had been brought up with herod the tetrarch  and saul </s>
<s> while they were worshipping the lord and fasting  the holy spirit said   set apart for me barnabas and saul for the work to which i have called them  </s>
<s> so after they had fasted and prayed  they placed their hands on them and sent them off </s>
<s> the two of them  sent on their way by the holy spirit  went down to seleucia and sailed from there to cyprus </s>
<s> when they arrived at salamis  they proclaimed the word of god in the jewish synagogues  john was with them as their helper </s>
<s> they travelled through the whole island until they came to paphos  there they met a jewish sorcerer and false prophet named barjesus </s>
<s> who was an attendant of the proconsul  sergius paulus  the proconsul  an intelligent man  sent for barnabas and saul because he wanted to hear the word of god </s>
<s> but elymas the sorcerer  for that is what his name means  opposed them and tried to turn the proconsul from the faith </s>
<s> then saul  who was also called paul  filled with the holy spirit  looked straight at elymas and said </s>
<s>  you are a child of the devil and an enemy of everything that is right  you are full of all kinds of deceit and trickery  will you never stop perverting the right ways of the lord </s>
<s> now the hand of the lord is against you  you are going to be blind for a time  not even able to see the light of the sun   immediately mist and darkness came over him  and he groped about  seeking someone to lead him by the hand </s>
