<s> when the proconsul saw what had happened  he believed  for he was amazed at the teaching about the lord </s>
<s> from paphos  paul and his companions sailed to perga in pamphylia  where john left them to return to jerusalem </s>
<s> from perga they went on to pisidian antioch  on the sabbath they entered the synagogue and sat down </s>
<s> after the reading from the law and the prophets  the leaders of the synagogue sent word to them  saying   brothers  if you have a word of exhortation for the people  please speak  </s>
<s> standing up  paul motioned with his hand and said   fellow israelites and you gentiles who worship god  listen to me </s>
<s> the god of the people of israel chose our ancestors  he made the people prosper during their stay in egypt  with mighty power he led them out of that country </s>
<s> for about forty years he endured their conduct in the wilderness </s>
<s> and he overthrew seven nations in canaan  giving their land to his people as their inheritance </s>
<s> all this took about 450 years   after this  god gave them judges until the time of samuel the prophet </s>
<s> then the people asked for a king  and he gave them saul son of kish  of the tribe of benjamin  who ruled for forty years </s>
<s> after removing saul  he made david their king  god testified concerning him   i have found david son of jesse  a man after my own heart  he will do everything i want him to do  </s>
<s>  from this mans descendants god has brought to israel the saviour jesus  as he promised </s>
<s> before the coming of jesus  john preached repentance and baptism to all the people of israel </s>
<s> as john was completing his work  he said   who do you suppose i am  i am not the one you are looking for  but there is one coming after me whose sandals i am not worthy to untie  </s>
<s>  fellow children of abraham and you godfearing gentiles  it is to us that this message of salvation has been sent </s>
<s> the people of jerusalem and their rulers did not recognise jesus  yet in condemning him they fulfilled the words of the prophets that are read every sabbath </s>
<s> though they found no proper ground for a death sentence  they asked pilate to have him executed </s>
<s> when they had carried out all that was written about him  they took him down from the cross and laid him in a tomb </s>
<s> but god raised him from the dead </s>
<s> and for many days he was seen by those who had travelled with him from galilee to jerusalem  they are now his witnesses to our people </s>
<s>  we tell you the good news  what god promised our ancestors</s>
<s> he has fulfilled for us  their children  by raising up jesus  as it is written in the second psalm    you are my son  today i have become your father     i will give you the holy and sure blessings promised to david     you will not let your holy one see decay  </s>
<s>  now when david had served gods purpose in his own generation  he fell asleep  he was buried with his ancestors and his body decayed </s>
<s> but the one whom god raised from the dead did not see decay </s>
<s>  therefore  my friends  i want you to know that through jesus the forgiveness of sins is proclaimed to you </s>
<s> through him everyone who believes is set free from every sin  a justification you were not able to obtain under the law of moses </s>
<s> take care that what the prophets have said does not happen to you </s>
<s>   look  you scoffers  wonder and perish  for i am going to do something in your days that you would never believe  even if someone told you   </s>
<s> as paul and barnabas were leaving the synagogue  the people invited them to speak further about these things on the next sabbath </s>
<s> when the congregation was dismissed  many of the jews and devout converts to judaism followed paul and barnabas  who talked with them and urged them to continue in the grace of god </s>
<s> on the next sabbath almost the whole city gathered to hear the word of the lord </s>
<s> when the jews saw the crowds  they were filled with jealousy  they began to contradict what paul was saying and heaped abuse on him </s>
<s> then paul and barnabas answered them boldly   we had to speak the word of god to you first  since you reject it and do not consider yourselves worthy of eternal life  we now turn to the gentiles </s>
<s> for this is what the lord has commanded us    i have made you a light for the gentiles  that you may bring salvation to the ends of the earth   </s>
<s> when the gentiles heard this  they were glad and honoured the word of the lord  and all who were appointed for eternal life believed </s>
<s> the word of the lord spread through the whole region </s>
<s> but the jewish leaders incited the godfearing women of high standing and the leading men of the city  they stirred up persecution against paul and barnabas  and expelled them from their region </s>
<s> so they shook the dust off their feet as a warning to them and went to iconium </s>
<s> and the disciples were filled with joy and with the holy spirit </s>
<s> at iconium paul and barnabas went as usual into the jewish synagogue  there they spoke so effectively that a great number of jews and greeks believed </s>
<s> but the jews who refused to believe stirred up the other gentiles and poisoned their minds against the brothers </s>
<s> so paul and barnabas spent considerable time there  speaking boldly for the lord  who confirmed the message of his grace by enabling them to perform signs and wonders </s>
<s> the people of the city were divided  some sided with the jews  others with the apostles </s>
<s> there was a plot afoot among both gentiles and jews  together with their leaders  to illtreat them and stone them </s>
<s> but they found out about it and fled to the lycaonian cities of lystra and derbe and to the surrounding country </s>
<s> where they continued to preach the gospel </s>
<s> in lystra there sat a man who was lame  he had been that way from birth and had never walked </s>
<s> he listened to paul as he was speaking  paul looked directly at him  saw that he had faith to be healed</s>
<s> and called out   stand up on your feet   at that  the man jumped up and began to walk </s>
<s> when the crowd saw what paul had done  they shouted in the lycaonian language   the gods have come down to us in human form  </s>
<s> barnabas they called zeus  and paul they called hermes because he was the chief speaker </s>
<s> the priest of zeus  whose temple was just outside the city  brought bulls and wreaths to the city gates because he and the crowd wanted to offer sacrifices to them </s>
<s> but when the apostles barnabas and paul heard of this  they tore their clothes and rushed out into the crowd  shouting </s>
<s>  friends  why are you doing this  we too are only human  like you  we are bringing you good news  telling you to turn from these worthless things to the living god  who made the heavens and the earth and the sea and everything in them </s>
<s> in the past  he let all nations go their own way </s>
<s> yet he has not left himself without testimony  he has shown kindness by giving you rain from heaven and crops in their seasons  he provides you with plenty of food and fills your hearts with joy  </s>
<s> even with these words  they had difficulty keeping the crowd from sacrificing to them </s>
<s> then some jews came from antioch and iconium and won the crowd over  they stoned paul and dragged him outside the city  thinking he was dead </s>
<s> but after the disciples had gathered round him  he got up and went back into the city  the next day he and barnabas left for derbe </s>
<s> they preached the gospel in that city and won a large number of disciples  then they returned to lystra  iconium and antioch </s>
<s> strengthening the disciples and encouraging them to remain true to the faith   we must go through many hardships to enter the kingdom of god   they said </s>
<s> paul and barnabas appointed elders for them in each church and  with prayer and fasting  committed them to the lord  in whom they had put their trust </s>
<s> after going through pisidia  they came into pamphylia </s>
<s> and when they had preached the word in perga  they went down to attalia </s>
<s> from attalia they sailed back to antioch  where they had been committed to the grace of god for the work they had now completed </s>
<s> on arriving there  they gathered the church together and reported all that god had done through them and how he had opened a door of faith to the gentiles </s>
<s> and they stayed there a long time with the disciples </s>
<s> certain people came down from judea to antioch and were teaching the believers   unless you are circumcised  according to the custom taught by moses  you cannot be saved  </s>
<s> this brought paul and barnabas into sharp dispute and debate with them  so paul and barnabas were appointed  along with some other believers  to go up to jerusalem to see the apostles and elders about this question </s>
<s> the church sent them on their way  and as they travelled through phoenicia and samaria  they told how the gentiles had been converted  this news made all the believers very glad </s>
<s> when they came to jerusalem  they were welcomed by the church and the apostles and elders  to whom they reported everything god had done through them </s>
<s> then some of the believers who belonged to the party of the pharisees stood up and said   the gentiles must be circumcised and required to keep the law of moses  </s>
<s> the apostles and elders met to consider this question </s>
<s> after much discussion  peter got up and addressed them   brothers  you know that some time ago god made a choice among you that the gentiles should hear from my lips the message of the gospel and believe </s>
<s> god  who knows the heart  showed that he accepted them by giving the holy spirit to them  just as he did to us </s>
<s> he did not discriminate between us and them  for he purified their hearts by faith </s>
<s> now then  why do you try to test god by putting on the necks of gentiles a yoke that neither we nor our ancestors have been able to bear </s>
<s> no  we believe it is through the grace of our lord jesus that we are saved  just as they are  </s>
<s> the whole assembly became silent as they listened to barnabas and paul telling about the signs and wonders god had done among the gentiles through them </s>
<s> when they finished  james spoke up   brothers   he said   listen to me </s>
<s> simon has described to us how god first intervened to choose a people for his name from the gentiles </s>
<s> the words of the prophets are in agreement with this  as it is written </s>
<s>   after this i will return and rebuild davids fallen tent  its ruins i will rebuild  and i will restore it </s>
<s> that the rest of mankind may seek the lord  even all the gentiles who bear my name  says the lord  who does these things  </s>
<s> things known from long ago </s>
<s>  it is my judgment  therefore  that we should not make it difficult for the gentiles who are turning to god </s>
<s> instead we should write to them  telling them to abstain from food polluted by idols  from sexual immorality  from the meat of strangled animals and from blood </s>
<s> for the law of moses has been preached in every city from the earliest times and is read in the synagogues on every sabbath  </s>
<s> then the apostles and elders  with the whole church  decided to choose some of their own men and send them to antioch with paul and barnabas  they chose judas  called barsabbas  and silas  men who were leaders among the believers </s>
<s> with them they sent the following letter </s>
<s> so the men were sent off and went down to antioch  where they gathered the church together and delivered the letter </s>
<s> the people read it and were glad for its encouraging message </s>
<s> judas and silas  who themselves were prophets  said much to encourage and strengthen the believers </s>
<s> after spending some time there  they were sent off by the believers with the blessing of peace to return to those who had sent them  </s>
<s> </s>
<s> but paul and barnabas remained in antioch  where they and many others taught and preached the word of the lord </s>
<s> some time later paul said to barnabas   let us go back and visit the believers in all the towns where we preached the word of the lord and see how they are doing  </s>
<s> barnabas wanted to take john  also called mark  with them </s>
<s> but paul did not think it wise to take him  because he had deserted them in pamphylia and had not continued with them in the work </s>
<s> they had such a sharp disagreement that they parted company  barnabas took mark and sailed for cyprus </s>
<s> but paul chose silas and left  commended by the believers to the grace of the lord </s>
<s> he went through syria and cilicia  strengthening the churches </s>
<s> paul came to derbe and then to lystra  where a disciple named timothy lived  whose mother was jewish and a believer but whose father was a greek </s>
<s> the believers at lystra and iconium spoke well of him </s>
<s> paul wanted to take him along on the journey  so he circumcised him because of the jews who lived in that area  for they all knew that his father was a greek </s>
<s> as they travelled from town to town  they delivered the decisions reached by the apostles and elders in jerusalem for the people to obey </s>
<s> so the churches were strengthened in the faith and grew daily in numbers </s>
<s> paul and his companions travelled throughout the region of phrygia and galatia  having been kept by the holy spirit from preaching the word in the province of asia </s>
<s> when they came to the border of mysia  they tried to enter bithynia  but the spirit of jesus would not allow them to </s>
<s> so they passed by mysia and went down to troas </s>
<s> during the night paul had a vision of a man of macedonia standing and begging him   come over to macedonia and help us  </s>
<s> after paul had seen the vision  we got ready at once to leave for macedonia  concluding that god had called us to preach the gospel to them </s>
<s> from troas we put out to sea and sailed straight for samothrace  and the next day we went on to neapolis </s>
<s> from there we travelled to philippi  a roman colony and the leading city of that district of macedonia  and we stayed there several days </s>
<s> on the sabbath we went outside the city gate to the river  where we expected to find a place of prayer  we sat down and began to speak to the women who had gathered there </s>
<s> one of those listening was a woman from the city of thyatira named lydia  a dealer in purple cloth  she was a worshipper of god  the lord opened her heart to respond to pauls message </s>
<s> when she and the members of her household were baptised  she invited us to her home   if you consider me a believer in the lord   she said   come and stay at my house   and she persuaded us </s>
<s> once when we were going to the place of prayer  we were met by a female slave who had a spirit by which she predicted the future  she earned a great deal of money for her owners by fortunetelling </s>
<s> she followed paul and the rest of us  shouting   these men are servants of the most high god  who are telling you the way to be saved  </s>
<s> she kept this up for many days  finally paul became so annoyed that he turned round and said to the spirit   in the name of jesus christ i command you to come out of her   at that moment the spirit left her </s>
<s> when her owners realised that their hope of making money was gone  they seized paul and silas and dragged them into the marketplace to face the authorities </s>
<s> they brought them before the magistrates and said   these men are jews  and are throwing our city into an uproar</s>
<s> by advocating customs unlawful for us romans to accept or practise  </s>
<s> the crowd joined in the attack against paul and silas  and the magistrates ordered them to be stripped and beaten with rods </s>
<s> after they had been severely flogged  they were thrown into prison  and the jailer was commanded to guard them carefully </s>
<s> when he received these orders  he put them in the inner cell and fastened their feet in the stocks </s>
<s> about midnight paul and silas were praying and singing hymns to god  and the other prisoners were listening to them </s>
<s> suddenly there was such a violent earthquake that the foundations of the prison were shaken  at once all the prison doors flew open  and everyones chains came loose </s>
<s> the jailer woke up  and when he saw the prison doors open  he drew his sword and was about to kill himself because he thought the prisoners had escaped </s>
<s> but paul shouted   dont harm yourself  we are all here  </s>
<s> the jailer called for lights  rushed in and fell trembling before paul and silas </s>
<s> he then brought them out and asked   sirs  what must i do to be saved  </s>
<s> they replied   believe in the lord jesus  and you will be saved  you and your household  </s>
<s> then they spoke the word of the lord to him and to all the others in his house </s>
<s> at that hour of the night the jailer took them and washed their wounds  then immediately he and all his household were baptised </s>
<s> the jailer brought them into his house and set a meal before them  he was filled with joy because he had come to believe in god  he and his whole household </s>
<s> when it was daylight  the magistrates sent their officers to the jailer with the order   release those men  </s>
<s> the jailer told paul   the magistrates have ordered that you and silas be released  now you can leave  go in peace  </s>
<s> but paul said to the officers   they beat us publicly without a trial  even though we are roman citizens  and threw us into prison  and now do they want to get rid of us quietly  no  let them come themselves and escort us out  </s>
<s> the officers reported this to the magistrates  and when they heard that paul and silas were roman citizens  they were alarmed </s>
<s> they came to appease them and escorted them from the prison  requesting them to leave the city </s>
<s> after paul and silas came out of the prison  they went to lydias house  where they met with the brothers and sisters and encouraged them  then they left </s>
<s> when paul and his companions had passed through amphipolis and apollonia  they came to thessalonica  where there was a jewish synagogue </s>
<s> as was his custom  paul went into the synagogue  and on three sabbath days he reasoned with them from the scriptures </s>
<s> explaining and proving that the messiah had to suffer and rise from the dead   this jesus i am proclaiming to you is the messiah   he said </s>
<s> some of the jews were persuaded and joined paul and silas  as did a large number of godfearing greeks and quite a few prominent women </s>
<s> but other jews were jealous  so they rounded up some bad characters from the marketplace  formed a mob and started a riot in the city  they rushed to jasons house in search of paul and silas in order to bring them out to the crowd </s>
<s> but when they did not find them  they dragged jason and some other believers before the city officials  shouting   these men who have caused trouble all over the world have now come here </s>
<s> and jason has welcomed them into his house  they are all defying caesars decrees  saying that there is another king  one called jesus  </s>
<s> when they heard this  the crowd and the city officials were thrown into turmoil </s>
<s> then they put jason and the others on bail and let them go </s>
<s> as soon as it was night  the believers sent paul and silas away to berea  on arriving there  they went to the jewish synagogue </s>
<s> now the berean jews were of more noble character than those in thessalonica  for they received the message with great eagerness and examined the scriptures every day to see if what paul said was true </s>
<s> as a result  many of them believed  as did also a number of prominent greek women and many greek men </s>
<s> but when the jews in thessalonica learned that paul was preaching the word of god at berea  some of them went there too  agitating the crowds and stirring them up </s>
<s> the believers immediately sent paul to the coast  but silas and timothy stayed at berea </s>
<s> those who escorted paul brought him to athens and then left with instructions for silas and timothy to join him as soon as possible </s>
<s> while paul was waiting for them in athens  he was greatly distressed to see that the city was full of idols </s>
<s> so he reasoned in the synagogue with both jews and godfearing greeks  as well as in the marketplace day by day with those who happened to be there </s>
<s> a group of epicurean and stoic philosophers began to debate with him  some of them asked   what is this babbler trying to say   others remarked   he seems to be advocating foreign gods   they said this because paul was preaching the good news about jesus and the resurrection </s>
<s> then they took him and brought him to a meeting of the areopagus  where they said to him   may we know what this new teaching is that you are presenting </s>
<s> you are bringing some strange ideas to our ears  and we would like to know what they mean  </s>
<s>  all the athenians and the foreigners who lived there spent their time doing nothing but talking about and listening to the latest ideas  </s>
<s> paul then stood up in the meeting of the areopagus and said   people of athens  i see that in every way you are very religious </s>
<s> for as i walked around and looked carefully at your objects of worship  i even found an altar with this inscription  to an unknown god  so you are ignorant of the very thing you worship  and this is what i am going to proclaim to you </s>
<s>  the god who made the world and everything in it is the lord of heaven and earth and does not live in temples built by human hands </s>
<s> and he is not served by human hands  as if he needed anything  rather  he himself gives everyone life and breath and everything else </s>
<s> from one man he made all the nations  that they should inhabit the whole earth  and he marked out their appointed times in history and the boundaries of their lands </s>
<s> god did this so that they would seek him and perhaps reach out for him and find him  though he is not far from any one of us </s>
<s>  for in him we live and move and have our being   as some of your own poets have said   we are his offspring  </s>
<s>  therefore since we are gods offspring  we should not think that the divine being is like gold or silver or stone  an image made by human design and skill </s>
<s> in the past god overlooked such ignorance  but now he commands all people everywhere to repent </s>
<s> for he has set a day when he will judge the world with justice by the man he has appointed  he has given proof of this to everyone by raising him from the dead  </s>
<s> when they heard about the resurrection of the dead  some of them sneered  but others said   we want to hear you again on this subject  </s>
<s> at that  paul left the council </s>
<s> some of the people became followers of paul and believed  among them was dionysius  a member of the areopagus  also a woman named damaris  and a number of others </s>
<s> after this  paul left athens and went to corinth </s>
<s> there he met a jew named aquila  a native of pontus  who had recently come from italy with his wife priscilla  because claudius had ordered all jews to leave rome  paul went to see them </s>
<s> and because he was a tentmaker as they were  he stayed and worked with them </s>
<s> every sabbath he reasoned in the synagogue  trying to persuade jews and greeks </s>
<s> when silas and timothy came from macedonia  paul devoted himself exclusively to preaching  testifying to the jews that jesus was the messiah </s>
<s> but when they opposed paul and became abusive  he shook out his clothes in protest and said to them   your blood be on your own heads  i am innocent of it  from now on i will go to the gentiles  </s>
<s> then paul left the synagogue and went next door to the house of titius justus  a worshipper of god </s>
<s> crispus  the synagogue leader  and his entire household believed in the lord  and many of the corinthians who heard paul believed and were baptised </s>
<s> one night the lord spoke to paul in a vision   do not be afraid  keep on speaking  do not be silent </s>
<s> for i am with you  and no one is going to attack and harm you  because i have many people in this city  </s>
<s> so paul stayed in corinth for a year and a half  teaching them the word of god </s>
<s> while gallio was proconsul of achaia  the jews of corinth made a united attack on paul and brought him to the place of judgment </s>
<s>  this man   they charged   is persuading the people to worship god in ways contrary to the law  </s>
<s> just as paul was about to speak  gallio said to them   if you jews were making a complaint about some misdemeanour or serious crime  it would be reasonable for me to listen to you </s>
<s> but since it involves questions about words and names and your own law  settle the matter yourselves  i will not be a judge of such things  </s>
<s> so he drove them off </s>
<s> then the crowd there turned on sosthenes the synagogue leader and beat him in front of the proconsul  and gallio showed no concern whatever </s>
<s> paul stayed on in corinth for some time  then he left the brothers and sisters and sailed for syria  accompanied by priscilla and aquila  before he sailed  he had his hair cut off at cenchreae because of a vow he had taken </s>
<s> they arrived at ephesus  where paul left priscilla and aquila  he himself went into the synagogue and reasoned with the jews </s>
<s> when they asked him to spend more time with them  he declined </s>
<s> but as he left  he promised   i will come back if it is gods will   then he set sail from ephesus </s>
<s> when he landed at caesarea  he went up to jerusalem and greeted the church and then went down to antioch </s>
<s> after spending some time in antioch  paul set out from there and travelled from place to place throughout the region of galatia and phrygia  strengthening all the disciples </s>
<s> meanwhile a jew named apollos  a native of alexandria  came to ephesus  he was a learned man  with a thorough knowledge of the scriptures </s>
<s> he had been instructed in the way of the lord  and he spoke with great fervour and taught about jesus accurately  though he knew only the baptism of john </s>
<s> he began to speak boldly in the synagogue  when priscilla and aquila heard him  they invited him to their home and explained to him the way of god more adequately </s>
<s> when apollos wanted to go to achaia  the brothers and sisters encouraged him and wrote to the disciples there to welcome him  when he arrived  he was a great help to those who by grace had believed </s>
<s> for he vigorously refuted his jewish opponents in public debate  proving from the scriptures that jesus was the messiah </s>
<s> while apollos was at corinth  paul took the road through the interior and arrived at ephesus  there he found some disciples</s>
<s> and asked them   did you receive the holy spirit when you believed   they answered   no  we have not even heard that there is a holy spirit  </s>
<s> so paul asked   then what baptism did you receive    johns baptism   they replied </s>
<s> paul said   johns baptism was a baptism of repentance  he told the people to believe in the one coming after him  that is  in jesus  </s>
<s> on hearing this  they were baptised in the name of the lord jesus </s>
<s> when paul placed his hands on them  the holy spirit came on them  and they spoke in tongues and prophesied </s>
<s> there were about twelve men in all </s>
<s> paul entered the synagogue and spoke boldly there for three months  arguing persuasively about the kingdom of god </s>
<s> but some of them became obstinate  they refused to believe and publicly maligned the way  so paul left them  he took the disciples with him and had discussions daily in the lecture hall of tyrannus </s>
<s> this went on for two years  so that all the jews and greeks who lived in the province of asia heard the word of the lord </s>
<s> god did extraordinary miracles through paul </s>
<s> so that even handkerchiefs and aprons that had touched him were taken to those who were ill  and their illnesses were cured and the evil spirits left them </s>
<s> some jews who went around driving out evil spirits tried to invoke the name of the lord jesus over those who were demonpossessed  they would say   in the name of the jesus whom paul preaches  i command you to come out  </s>
<s> seven sons of sceva  a jewish chief priest  were doing this </s>
<s> one day the evil spirit answered them   jesus i know  and paul i know about  but who are you  </s>
<s> then the man who had the evil spirit jumped on them and overpowered them all  he gave them such a beating that they ran out of the house naked and bleeding </s>
<s> when this became known to the jews and greeks living in ephesus  they were all seized with fear  and the name of the lord jesus was held in high honour </s>
<s> many of those who believed now came and openly confessed what they had done </s>
<s> a number who had practised sorcery brought their scrolls together and burned them publicly  when they calculated the value of the scrolls  the total came to fifty thousand drachmas </s>
<s> in this way the word of the lord spread widely and grew in power </s>
<s> after all this had happened  paul decided to go to jerusalem  passing through macedonia and achaia   after i have been there   he said   i must visit rome also  </s>
<s> he sent two of his helpers  timothy and erastus  to macedonia  while he stayed in the province of asia a little longer </s>
<s> about that time there arose a great disturbance about the way </s>
<s> a silversmith named demetrius  who made silver shrines of artemis  brought in a lot of business for the craftsmen there </s>
<s> he called them together  along with the workers in related trades  and said   you know  my friends  that we receive a good income from this business </s>
<s> and you see and hear how this fellow paul has convinced and led astray large numbers of people here in ephesus and in practically the whole province of asia  he says that gods made by human hands are no gods at all </s>
<s> there is danger not only that our trade will lose its good name  but also that the temple of the great goddess artemis will be discredited  and the goddess herself  who is worshipped throughout the province of asia and the world  will be robbed of her divine majesty  </s>
<s> when they heard this  they were furious and began shouting   great is artemis of the ephesians  </s>
<s> soon the whole city was in an uproar  the people seized gaius and aristarchus  pauls travelling companions from macedonia  and all of them rushed into the theatre together </s>
<s> paul wanted to appear before the crowd  but the disciples would not let him </s>
<s> even some of the officials of the province  friends of paul  sent him a message begging him not to venture into the theatre </s>
<s> the assembly was in confusion  some were shouting one thing  some another  most of the people did not even know why they were there </s>
<s> the jews in the crowd pushed alexander to the front  and they shouted instructions to him  he motioned for silence in order to make a defence before the people </s>
<s> but when they realised he was a jew  they all shouted in unison for about two hours   great is artemis of the ephesians  </s>
<s> the city clerk quietened the crowd and said   fellow ephesians  doesnt all the world know that the city of ephesus is the guardian of the temple of the great artemis and of her image  which fell from heaven </s>
<s> therefore  since these facts are undeniable  you ought to calm down and not do anything rash </s>
<s> you have brought these men here  though they have neither robbed temples nor blasphemed our goddess </s>
<s> if  then  demetrius and his fellow craftsmen have a grievance against anybody  the courts are open and there are proconsuls  they can press charges </s>
<s> if there is anything further you want to bring up  it must be settled in a legal assembly </s>
<s> as it is  we are in danger of being charged with rioting because of what happened today  in that case we would not be able to account for this commotion  since there is no reason for it  </s>
<s> after he had said this  he dismissed the assembly </s>
<s> when the uproar had ended  paul sent for the disciples and  after encouraging them  said goodbye and set out for macedonia </s>
<s> he travelled through that area  speaking many words of encouragement to the people  and finally arrived in greece </s>
<s> where he stayed three months  because some jews had plotted against him just as he was about to sail for syria  he decided to go back through macedonia </s>
<s> he was accompanied by sopater son of pyrrhus from berea  aristarchus and secundus from thessalonica  gaius from derbe  timothy also  and tychicus and trophimus from the province of asia </s>
<s> these men went on ahead and waited for us at troas </s>
<s> but we sailed from philippi after the festival of unleavened bread  and five days later joined the others at troas  where we stayed seven days </s>
<s> on the first day of the week we came together to break bread  paul spoke to the people and  because he intended to leave the next day  kept on talking until midnight </s>
<s> there were many lamps in the upstairs room where we were meeting </s>
<s> seated in a window was a young man named eutychus  who was sinking into a deep sleep as paul talked on and on  when he was sound asleep  he fell to the ground from the third storey and was picked up dead </s>
<s> paul went down  threw himself on the young man and put his arms round him   dont be alarmed   he said   hes alive  </s>
<s> then he went upstairs again and broke bread and ate  after talking until daylight  he left </s>
<s> the people took the young man home alive and were greatly comforted </s>
<s> we went on ahead to the ship and sailed for assos  where we were going to take paul aboard  he had made this arrangement because he was going there on foot </s>
<s> when he met us at assos  we took him aboard and went on to mitylene </s>
<s> the next day we set sail from there and arrived off chios  the day after that we crossed over to samos  and on the following day arrived at miletus </s>
<s> paul had decided to sail past ephesus to avoid spending time in the province of asia  for he was in a hurry to reach jerusalem  if possible  by the day of pentecost </s>
<s> from miletus  paul sent to ephesus for the elders of the church </s>
<s> when they arrived  he said to them   you know how i lived the whole time i was with you  from the first day i came into the province of asia </s>
<s> i served the lord with great humility and with tears and in the midst of severe testing by the plots of my jewish opponents </s>
<s> you know that i have not hesitated to preach anything that would be helpful to you but have taught you publicly and from house to house </s>
<s> i have declared to both jews and greeks that they must turn to god in repentance and have faith in our lord jesus </s>
<s>  and now  compelled by the spirit  i am going to jerusalem  not knowing what will happen to me there </s>
<s> i only know that in every city the holy spirit warns me that prison and hardships are facing me </s>
<s> however  i consider my life worth nothing to me  my only aim is to finish the race and complete the task the lord jesus has given me  the task of testifying to the good news of gods grace </s>
<s>  now i know that none of you among whom i have gone about preaching the kingdom will ever see me again </s>
<s> therefore  i declare to you today that i am innocent of the blood of any of you </s>
<s> for i have not hesitated to proclaim to you the whole will of god </s>
<s> keep watch over yourselves and all the flock of which the holy spirit has made you overseers  be shepherds of the church of god  which he bought with his own blood </s>
<s> i know that after i leave  savage wolves will come in among you and will not spare the flock </s>
<s> even from your own number men will arise and distort the truth in order to draw away disciples after them </s>
<s> so be on your guard  remember that for three years i never stopped warning each of you night and day with tears </s>
<s>  now i commit you to god and to the word of his grace  which can build you up and give you an inheritance among all those who are sanctified </s>
<s> i have not coveted anyones silver or gold or clothing </s>
<s> you yourselves know that these hands of mine have supplied my own needs and the needs of my companions </s>
<s> in everything i did  i showed you that by this kind of hard work we must help the weak  remembering the words the lord jesus himself said   it is more blessed to give than to receive   </s>
<s> when paul had finished speaking  he knelt down with all of them and prayed </s>
<s> they all wept as they embraced him and kissed him </s>
<s> what grieved them most was his statement that they would never see his face again  then they accompanied him to the ship </s>
<s> after we had torn ourselves away from them  we put out to sea and sailed straight to kos  the next day we went to rhodes and from there to patara </s>
<s> we found a ship crossing over to phoenicia  went on board and set sail </s>
<s> after sighting cyprus and passing to the south of it  we sailed on to syria  we landed at tyre  where our ship was to unload its cargo </s>
<s> we sought out the disciples there and stayed with them seven days  through the spirit they urged paul not to go on to jerusalem </s>
<s> when it was time to leave  we left and continued on our way  all of them  including wives and children  accompanied us out of the city  and there on the beach we knelt to pray </s>
<s> after saying goodbye to each other  we went aboard the ship  and they returned home </s>
<s> we continued our voyage from tyre and landed at ptolemais  where we greeted the brothers and sisters and stayed with them for a day </s>
<s> leaving the next day  we reached caesarea and stayed at the house of philip the evangelist  one of the seven </s>
<s> he had four unmarried daughters who prophesied </s>
<s> after we had been there a number of days  a prophet named agabus came down from judea </s>
<s> coming over to us  he took pauls belt  tied his own hands and feet with it and said   the holy spirit says   in this way the jewish leaders in jerusalem will bind the owner of this belt and will hand him over to the gentiles   </s>
<s> when we heard this  we and the people there pleaded with paul not to go up to jerusalem </s>
<s> then paul answered   why are you weeping and breaking my heart  i am ready not only to be bound  but also to die in jerusalem for the name of the lord jesus  </s>
<s> when he would not be dissuaded  we gave up and said   the lords will be done  </s>
<s> after this  we started on our way up to jerusalem </s>
<s> some of the disciples from caesarea accompanied us and brought us to the home of mnason  where we were to stay  he was a man from cyprus and one of the early disciples </s>
<s> when we arrived at jerusalem  the brothers and sisters received us warmly </s>
<s> the next day paul and the rest of us went to see james  and all the elders were present </s>
<s> paul greeted them and reported in detail what god had done among the gentiles through his ministry </s>
<s> when they heard this  they praised god  then they said to paul   you see  brother  how many thousands of jews have believed  and all of them are zealous for the law </s>
<s> they have been informed that you teach all the jews who live among the gentiles to turn away from moses  telling them not to circumcise their children or live according to our customs </s>
<s> what shall we do  they will certainly hear that you have come </s>
<s> so do what we tell you  there are four men with us who have made a vow </s>
<s> take these men  join in their purification rites and pay their expenses  so that they can have their heads shaved  then everyone will know there is no truth in these reports about you  but that you yourself are living in obedience to the law </s>
<s> as for the gentile believers  we have written to them our decision that they should abstain from food sacrificed to idols  from blood  from the meat of strangled animals and from sexual immorality  </s>
<s> the next day paul took the men and purified himself along with them  then he went to the temple to give notice of the date when the days of purification would end and the offering would be made for each of them </s>
<s> when the seven days were nearly over  some jews from the province of asia saw paul at the temple  they stirred up the whole crowd and seized him </s>
<s> shouting   fellow israelites  help us  this is the man who teaches everyone everywhere against our people and our law and this place  and besides  he has brought greeks into the temple and defiled this holy place  </s>
<s>  they had previously seen trophimus the ephesian in the city with paul and assumed that paul had brought him into the temple  </s>
<s> the whole city was aroused  and the people came running from all directions  seizing paul  they dragged him from the temple  and immediately the gates were shut </s>
<s> while they were trying to kill him  news reached the commander of the roman troops that the whole city of jerusalem was in an uproar </s>
<s> he at once took some officers and soldiers and ran down to the crowd  when the rioters saw the commander and his soldiers  they stopped beating paul </s>
<s> the commander came up and arrested him and ordered him to be bound with two chains  then he asked who he was and what he had done </s>
<s> some in the crowd shouted one thing and some another  and since the commander could not get at the truth because of the uproar  he ordered that paul be taken into the barracks </s>
<s> when paul reached the steps  the violence of the mob was so great he had to be carried by the soldiers </s>
<s> the crowd that followed kept shouting   get rid of him  </s>
<s> as the soldiers were about to take paul into the barracks  he asked the commander   may i say something to you    do you speak greek   he replied </s>
<s>  arent you the egyptian who started a revolt and led four thousand terrorists out into the wilderness some time ago  </s>
<s> paul answered   i am a jew  from tarsus in cilicia  a citizen of no ordinary city  please let me speak to the people  </s>
<s> after receiving the commanders permission  paul stood on the steps and motioned to the crowd  when they were all silent  he said to them in aramaic </s>
<s>  brothers and fathers  listen now to my defence  </s>
<s> when they heard him speak to them in aramaic  they became very quiet  then paul said </s>
<s>  i am a jew  born in tarsus of cilicia  but brought up in this city  i studied under gamaliel and was thoroughly trained in the law of our ancestors  i was just as zealous for god as any of you are today </s>
<s> i persecuted the followers of this way to their death  arresting both men and women and throwing them into prison </s>
<s> as the high priest and all the council can themselves testify  i even obtained letters from them to their associates in damascus  and went there to bring these people as prisoners to jerusalem to be punished </s>
<s>  about noon as i came near damascus  suddenly a bright light from heaven flashed around me </s>
<s> i fell to the ground and heard a voice say to me   saul  saul  why do you persecute me  </s>
<s>   who are you  lord   i asked    i am jesus of nazareth  whom you are persecuting   he replied </s>
<s> my companions saw the light  but they did not understand the voice of him who was speaking to me </s>
<s>   what shall i do  lord   i asked    get up   the lord said   and go into damascus  there you will be told all that you have been assigned to do  </s>
<s> my companions led me by the hand into damascus  because the brilliance of the light had blinded me </s>
<s>  a man named ananias came to see me  he was a devout observer of the law and highly respected by all the jews living there </s>
<s> he stood beside me and said   brother saul  receive your sight   and at that very moment i was able to see him </s>
<s>  then he said   the god of our ancestors has chosen you to know his will and to see the righteous one and to hear words from his mouth </s>
<s> you will be his witness to all people of what you have seen and heard </s>
<s> and now what are you waiting for  get up  be baptised and wash your sins away  calling on his name  </s>
<s>  when i returned to jerusalem and was praying at the temple  i fell into a trance</s>
<s> and saw the lord speaking to me   quick   he said   leave jerusalem immediately  because the people here will not accept your testimony about me  </s>
<s>   lord   i replied   these people know that i went from one synagogue to another to imprison and beat those who believe in you </s>
<s> and when the blood of your martyr stephen was shed  i stood there giving my approval and guarding the clothes of those who were killing him  </s>
<s>  then the lord said to me   go  i will send you far away to the gentiles   </s>
<s> the crowd listened to paul until he said this  then they raised their voices and shouted   rid the earth of him  hes not fit to live  </s>
<s> as they were shouting and throwing off their cloaks and flinging dust into the air </s>
<s> the commander ordered that paul be taken into the barracks  he directed that he be flogged and interrogated in order to find out why the people were shouting at him like this </s>
<s> as they stretched him out to flog him  paul said to the centurion standing there   is it legal for you to flog a roman citizen who hasnt even been found guilty  </s>
<s> when the centurion heard this  he went to the commander and reported it   what are you going to do   he asked   this man is a roman citizen  </s>
<s> the commander went to paul and asked   tell me  are you a roman citizen    yes  i am   he answered </s>
<s> then the commander said   i had to pay a lot of money for my citizenship    but i was born a citizen   paul replied </s>
<s> those who were about to interrogate him withdrew immediately  the commander himself was alarmed when he realised that he had put paul  a roman citizen  in chains </s>
<s> the commander wanted to find out exactly why paul was being accused by the jews  so the next day he released him and ordered the chief priests and all the members of the sanhedrin to assemble  then he brought paul and set him before them </s>
<s> paul looked straight at the sanhedrin and said   my brothers  i have fulfilled my duty to god in all good conscience to this day  </s>
<s> at this the high priest ananias ordered those standing near paul to strike him on the mouth </s>
<s> then paul said to him   god will strike you  you whitewashed wall  you sit there to judge me according to the law  yet you yourself violate the law by commanding that i be struck  </s>
<s> those who were standing near paul said   how dare you insult gods high priest  </s>
<s> paul replied   brothers  i did not realise that he was the high priest  for it is written   do not speak evil about the ruler of your people   </s>
<s> then paul  knowing that some of them were sadducees and the others pharisees  called out in the sanhedrin   my brothers  i am a pharisee  descended from pharisees  i stand on trial because of the hope of the resurrection of the dead  </s>
<s> when he said this  a dispute broke out between the pharisees and the sadducees  and the assembly was divided </s>
<s>  the sadducees say that there is no resurrection  and that there are neither angels nor spirits  but the pharisees believe all these things  </s>
<s> there was a great uproar  and some of the teachers of the law who were pharisees stood up and argued vigorously   we find nothing wrong with this man   they said   what if a spirit or an angel has spoken to him  </s>
<s> the dispute became so violent that the commander was afraid paul would be torn to pieces by them  he ordered the troops to go down and take him away from them by force and bring him into the barracks </s>
<s> the following night the lord stood near paul and said   take courage  as you have testified about me in jerusalem  so you must also testify in rome  </s>
<s> the next morning some jews formed a conspiracy and bound themselves with an oath not to eat or drink until they had killed paul </s>
<s> more than forty men were involved in this plot </s>
<s> they went to the chief priests and the elders and said   we have taken a solemn oath not to eat anything until we have killed paul </s>
<s> now then  you and the sanhedrin petition the commander to bring him before you on the pretext of wanting more accurate information about his case  we are ready to kill him before he gets here  </s>
<s> but when the son of pauls sister heard of this plot  he went into the barracks and told paul </s>
<s> then paul called one of the centurions and said   take this young man to the commander  he has something to tell him  </s>
<s> so he took him to the commander  the centurion said   paul  the prisoner  sent for me and asked me to bring this young man to you because he has something to tell you  </s>
<s> the commander took the young man by the hand  drew him aside and asked   what is it you want to tell me  </s>
<s> he said   some jews have agreed to ask you to bring paul before the sanhedrin tomorrow on the pretext of wanting more accurate information about him </s>
<s> dont give in to them  because more than forty of them are waiting in ambush for him  they have taken an oath not to eat or drink until they have killed him  they are ready now  waiting for your consent to their request  </s>
<s> the commander dismissed the young man with this warning   dont tell anyone that you have reported this to me  </s>
<s> then he called two of his centurions and ordered them   get ready a detachment of two hundred soldiers  seventy horsemen and two hundred spearmen to go to caesarea at nine tonight </s>
<s> provide horses for paul so that he may be taken safely to governor felix  </s>
<s> he wrote a letter as follows </s>
<s> so the soldiers  carrying out their orders  took paul with them during the night and brought him as far as antipatris </s>
<s> the next day they let the cavalry go on with him  while they returned to the barracks </s>
<s> when the cavalry arrived in caesarea  they delivered the letter to the governor and handed paul over to him </s>
<s> the governor read the letter and asked what province he was from  learning that he was from cilicia </s>
<s> he said   i will hear your case when your accusers get here   then he ordered that paul be kept under guard in herods palace </s>
<s> five days later the high priest ananias went down to caesarea with some of the elders and a lawyer named tertullus  and they brought their charges against paul before the governor </s>
<s> when paul was called in  tertullus presented his case before felix   we have enjoyed a long period of peace under you  and your foresight has brought about reforms in this nation </s>
<s> everywhere and in every way  most excellent felix  we acknowledge this with profound gratitude </s>
<s> but in order not to weary you further  i would request that you be kind enough to hear us briefly </s>
<s>  we have found this man to be a troublemaker  stirring up riots among the jews all over the world  he is a ringleader of the nazarene sect</s>
<s> and even tried to desecrate the temple  so we seized him  </s>
<s> </s>
<s> by examining him yourself you will be able to learn the truth about all these charges we are bringing against him  </s>
<s> the other jews joined in the accusation  asserting that these things were true </s>
<s> when the governor motioned for him to speak  paul replied   i know that for a number of years you have been a judge over this nation  so i gladly make my defence </s>
<s> you can easily verify that no more than twelve days ago i went up to jerusalem to worship </s>
<s> my accusers did not find me arguing with anyone at the temple  or stirring up a crowd in the synagogues or anywhere else in the city </s>
<s> and they cannot prove to you the charges they are now making against me </s>
<s> however  i admit that i worship the god of our ancestors as a follower of the way  which they call a sect  i believe everything that is in accordance with the law and that is written in the prophets </s>
<s> and i have the same hope in god as these men themselves have  that there will be a resurrection of both the righteous and the wicked </s>
<s> so i strive always to keep my conscience clear before god and man </s>
<s>  after an absence of several years  i came to jerusalem to bring my people gifts for the poor and to present offerings </s>
<s> i was ceremonially clean when they found me in the temple courts doing this  there was no crowd with me  nor was i involved in any disturbance </s>
<s> but there are some jews from the province of asia  who ought to be here before you and bring charges if they have anything against me </s>
<s> or these who are here should state what crime they found in me when i stood before the sanhedrin </s>
<s> unless it was this one thing i shouted as i stood in their presence   it is concerning the resurrection of the dead that i am on trial before you today   </s>
<s> then felix  who was well acquainted with the way  adjourned the proceedings   when lysias the commander comes   he said   i will decide your case  </s>
<s> he ordered the centurion to keep paul under guard but to give him some freedom and permit his friends to take care of his needs </s>
<s> several days later felix came with his wife drusilla  who was jewish  he sent for paul and listened to him as he spoke about faith in christ jesus </s>
<s> as paul talked about righteousness  selfcontrol and the judgment to come  felix was afraid and said   thats enough for now  you may leave  when i find it convenient  i will send for you  </s>
<s> at the same time he was hoping that paul would offer him a bribe  so he sent for him frequently and talked with him </s>
<s> when two years had passed  felix was succeeded by porcius festus  but because felix wanted to grant a favour to the jews  he left paul in prison </s>
<s> three days after arriving in the province  festus went up from caesarea to jerusalem </s>
<s> where the chief priests and the jewish leaders appeared before him and presented the charges against paul </s>
<s> they requested festus  as a favour to them  to have paul transferred to jerusalem  for they were preparing an ambush to kill him along the way </s>
<s> festus answered   paul is being held at caesarea  and i myself am going there soon </s>
<s> let some of your leaders come with me  and if the man has done anything wrong  they can press charges against him there  </s>
<s> after spending eight or ten days with them  festus went down to caesarea  the next day he convened the court and ordered that paul be brought before him </s>
<s> when paul came in  the jews who had come down from jerusalem stood round him  they brought many serious charges against him  but they could not prove them </s>
<s> then paul made his defence   i have done nothing wrong against the jewish law or against the temple or against caesar  </s>
<s> festus  wishing to do the jews a favour  said to paul   are you willing to go up to jerusalem and stand trial before me there on these charges  </s>
<s> paul answered   i am now standing before caesars court  where i ought to be tried  i have not done any wrong to the jews  as you yourself know very well </s>
<s> if  however  i am guilty of doing anything deserving death  i do not refuse to die  but if the charges brought against me by these jews are not true  no one has the right to hand me over to them  i appeal to caesar  </s>
<s> after festus had conferred with his council  he declared   you have appealed to caesar  to caesar you will go  </s>
<s> a few days later king agrippa and bernice arrived at caesarea to pay their respects to festus </s>
<s> since they were spending many days there  festus discussed pauls case with the king  he said   there is a man here whom felix left as a prisoner </s>
<s> when i went to jerusalem  the chief priests and the elders of the jews brought charges against him and asked that he be condemned </s>
<s>  i told them that it is not the roman custom to hand over anyone before they have faced their accusers and have had an opportunity to defend themselves against the charges </s>
<s> when they came here with me  i did not delay the case  but convened the court the next day and ordered the man to be brought in </s>
<s> when his accusers got up to speak  they did not charge him with any of the crimes i had expected </s>
<s> instead  they had some points of dispute with him about their own religion and about a dead man named jesus whom paul claimed was alive </s>
<s> i was at a loss how to investigate such matters  so i asked if he would be willing to go to jerusalem and stand trial there on these charges </s>
<s> but when paul made his appeal to be held over for the emperors decision  i ordered him to be held until i could send him to caesar  </s>
<s> then agrippa said to festus   i would like to hear this man myself   he replied   tomorrow you will hear him  </s>
<s> the next day agrippa and bernice came with great pomp and entered the audience room with the highranking military officers and the prominent men of the city  at the command of festus  paul was brought in </s>
<s> festus said   king agrippa  and all who are present with us  you see this man  the whole jewish community has petitioned me about him in jerusalem and here in caesarea  shouting that he ought not to live any longer </s>
<s> i found he had done nothing deserving of death  but because he made his appeal to the emperor i decided to send him to rome </s>
<s> but i have nothing definite to write to his majesty about him  therefore i have brought him before all of you  and especially before you  king agrippa  so that as a result of this investigation i may have something to write </s>
<s> for i think it is unreasonable to send a prisoner on to rome without specifying the charges against him  </s>
<s> then agrippa said to paul   you have permission to speak for yourself   so paul motioned with his hand and began his defence </s>
<s>  king agrippa  i consider myself fortunate to stand before you today as i make my defence against all the accusations of the jews </s>
<s> and especially so because you are well acquainted with all the jewish customs and controversies  therefore  i beg you to listen to me patiently </s>
<s>  the jewish people all know the way i have lived ever since i was a child  from the beginning of my life in my own country  and also in jerusalem </s>
<s> they have known me for a long time and can testify  if they are willing  that i conformed to the strictest sect of our religion  living as a pharisee </s>
<s> and now it is because of my hope in what god has promised our ancestors that i am on trial today </s>
<s> this is the promise our twelve tribes are hoping to see fulfilled as they earnestly serve god day and night  king agrippa  it is because of this hope that these jews are accusing me </s>
<s> why should any of you consider it incredible that god raises the dead </s>
<s>  i too was convinced that i ought to do all that was possible to oppose the name of jesus of nazareth </s>
<s> and that is just what i did in jerusalem  on the authority of the chief priests i put many of the lords people in prison  and when they were put to death  i cast my vote against them </s>
<s> many a time i went from one synagogue to another to have them punished  and i tried to force them to blaspheme  i was so obsessed with persecuting them that i even hunted them down in foreign cities </s>
<s>  on one of these journeys i was going to damascus with the authority and commission of the chief priests </s>
<s> about noon  king agrippa  as i was on the road  i saw a light from heaven  brighter than the sun  blazing around me and my companions </s>
<s> we all fell to the ground  and i heard a voice saying to me in aramaic   saul  saul  why do you persecute me  it is hard for you to kick against the goads  </s>
<s>  then i asked   who are you  lord     i am jesus  whom you are persecuting   the lord replied </s>
<s>  now get up and stand on your feet  i have appeared to you to appoint you as a servant and as a witness of what you have seen and will see of me </s>
<s> i will rescue you from your own people and from the gentiles  i am sending you to them</s>
<s> to open their eyes and turn them from darkness to light  and from the power of satan to god  so that they may receive forgiveness of sins and a place among those who are sanctified by faith in me  </s>
<s>  so then  king agrippa  i was not disobedient to the vision from heaven </s>
<s> first to those in damascus  then to those in jerusalem and in all judea  and then to the gentiles  i preached that they should repent and turn to god and demonstrate their repentance by their deeds </s>
<s> that is why some jews seized me in the temple courts and tried to kill me </s>
<s> but god has helped me to this very day  so i stand here and testify to small and great alike  i am saying nothing beyond what the prophets and moses said would happen </s>
<s> that the messiah would suffer and  as the first to rise from the dead  would bring the message of light to his own people and to the gentiles  </s>
<s> at this point festus interrupted pauls defence   you are out of your mind  paul   he shouted   your great learning is driving you insane  </s>
<s>  i am not insane  most excellent festus   paul replied   what i am saying is true and reasonable </s>
<s> the king is familiar with these things  and i can speak freely to him  i am convinced that none of this has escaped his notice  because it was not done in a corner </s>
<s> king agrippa  do you believe the prophets  i know you do  </s>
<s> then agrippa said to paul   do you think that in such a short time you can persuade me to be a christian  </s>
<s> paul replied   short time or long  i pray to god that not only you but all who are listening to me today may become what i am  except for these chains  </s>
<s> the king rose  and with him the governor and bernice and those sitting with them </s>
<s> after they left the room  they began saying to one another   this man is not doing anything that deserves death or imprisonment  </s>
<s> agrippa said to festus   this man could have been set free if he had not appealed to caesar  </s>
<s> when it was decided that we would sail for italy  paul and some other prisoners were handed over to a centurion named julius  who belonged to the imperial regiment </s>
<s> we boarded a ship from adramyttium about to sail for ports along the coast of the province of asia  and we put out to sea  aristarchus  a macedonian from thessalonica  was with us </s>
<s> the next day we landed at sidon  and julius  in kindness to paul  allowed him to go to his friends so they might provide for his needs </s>
<s> from there we put out to sea again and passed to the lee of cyprus because the winds were against us </s>
<s> when we had sailed across the open sea off the coast of cilicia and pamphylia  we landed at myra in lycia </s>
<s> there the centurion found an alexandrian ship sailing for italy and put us on board </s>
<s> we made slow headway for many days and had difficulty arriving off cnidus  when the wind did not allow us to hold our course  we sailed to the lee of crete  opposite salmone </s>
<s> we moved along the coast with difficulty and came to a place called fair havens  near the town of lasea </s>
<s> much time had been lost  and sailing had already become dangerous because by now it was after the day of atonement  so paul warned them </s>
<s>  men  i can see that our voyage is going to be disastrous and bring great loss to ship and cargo  and to our own lives also  </s>
<s> but the centurion  instead of listening to what paul said  followed the advice of the pilot and of the owner of the ship </s>
<s> since the harbour was unsuitable to winter in  the majority decided that we should sail on  hoping to reach phoenix and winter there  this was a harbour in crete  facing both southwest and northwest </s>
<s> when a gentle south wind began to blow  they saw their opportunity  so they weighed anchor and sailed along the shore of crete </s>
<s> before very long  a wind of hurricane force  called the  northeaster  swept down from the island </s>
<s> the ship was caught by the storm and could not head into the wind  so we gave way to it and were driven along </s>
<s> as we passed to the lee of a small island called cauda  we were hardly able to make the lifeboat secure </s>
<s> so the men hoisted it aboard  then they passed ropes under the ship itself to hold it together  because they were afraid they would run aground on the sandbars of syrtis  they lowered the sea anchor and let the ship be driven along </s>
<s> we took such a violent battering from the storm that the next day they began to throw the cargo overboard </s>
<s> on the third day  they threw the ships tackle overboard with their own hands </s>
<s> when neither sun nor stars appeared for many days and the storm continued raging  we finally gave up all hope of being saved </s>
<s> after they had gone a long time without food  paul stood up before them and said   men  you should have taken my advice not to sail from crete  then you would have spared yourselves this damage and loss </s>
<s> but now i urge you to keep up your courage  because not one of you will be lost  only the ship will be destroyed </s>
<s> last night an angel of the god to whom i belong and whom i serve stood beside me</s>
<s> and said   do not be afraid  paul  you must stand trial before caesar  and god has graciously given you the lives of all who sail with you  </s>
<s> so keep up your courage  men  for i have faith in god that it will happen just as he told me </s>
<s> nevertheless  we must run aground on some island  </s>
<s> on the fourteenth night we were still being driven across the adriatic sea  when about midnight the sailors sensed they were approaching land </s>
<s> they took soundings and found that the water was forty metres deep  a short time later they took soundings again and found it was thirty metres deep </s>
<s> fearing that we would be dashed against the rocks  they dropped four anchors from the stern and prayed for daylight </s>
<s> in an attempt to escape from the ship  the sailors let the lifeboat down into the sea  pretending they were going to lower some anchors from the bow </s>
<s> then paul said to the centurion and the soldiers   unless these men stay with the ship  you cannot be saved  </s>
<s> so the soldiers cut the ropes that held the lifeboat and let it drift away </s>
<s> just before dawn paul urged them all to eat   for the last fourteen days   he said   you have been in constant suspense and have gone without food  you havent eaten anything </s>
<s> now i urge you to take some food  you need it to survive  not one of you will lose a single hair from his head  </s>
<s> after he said this  he took some bread and gave thanks to god in front of them all  then he broke it and began to eat </s>
<s> they were all encouraged and ate some food themselves </s>
<s> altogether there were 276 of us on board </s>
<s> when they had eaten as much as they wanted  they lightened the ship by throwing the grain into the sea </s>
<s> when daylight came  they did not recognise the land  but they saw a bay with a sandy beach  where they decided to run the ship aground if they could </s>
<s> cutting loose the anchors  they left them in the sea and at the same time untied the ropes that held the rudders  then they hoisted the foresail to the wind and made for the beach </s>
<s> but the ship struck a sandbar and ran aground  the bow stuck fast and would not move  and the stern was broken to pieces by the pounding of the surf </s>
<s> the soldiers planned to kill the prisoners to prevent any of them from swimming away and escaping </s>
<s> but the centurion wanted to spare pauls life and kept them from carrying out their plan  he ordered those who could swim to jump overboard first and get to land </s>
<s> the rest were to get there on planks or on other pieces of the ship  in this way everyone reached land safely </s>
<s> once safely on shore  we found out that the island was called malta </s>
<s> the islanders showed us unusual kindness  they built a fire and welcomed us all because it was raining and cold </s>
<s> paul gathered a pile of brushwood and  as he put it on the fire  a viper  driven out by the heat  fastened itself on his hand </s>
<s> when the islanders saw the snake hanging from his hand  they said to each other   this man must be a murderer  for though he escaped from the sea  the goddess justice has not allowed him to live  </s>
<s> but paul shook the snake off into the fire and suffered no ill effects </s>
<s> the people expected him to swell up or suddenly fall dead  but after waiting a long time and seeing nothing unusual happen to him  they changed their minds and said he was a god </s>
<s> there was an estate near by that belonged to publius  the chief official of the island  he welcomed us to his home and showed us generous hospitality for three days </s>
<s> his father was ill in bed  suffering from fever and dysentery  paul went in to see him and  after prayer  placed his hands on him and healed him </s>
<s> when this had happened  the rest of those on the island who were ill came and were cured </s>
<s> they honoured us in many ways  and when we were ready to sail  they furnished us with the supplies we needed </s>
<s> after three months we put out to sea in a ship that had wintered in the island  it was an alexandrian ship with the figurehead of the twin gods castor and pollux </s>
<s> we put in at syracuse and stayed there three days </s>
<s> from there we set sail and arrived at rhegium  the next day the south wind came up  and on the following day we reached puteoli </s>
<s> there we found some brothers and sisters who invited us to spend a week with them  and so we came to rome </s>
<s> the brothers and sisters there had heard that we were coming  and they travelled as far as the forum of appius and the three taverns to meet us  at the sight of these people paul thanked god and was encouraged </s>
<s> when we got to rome  paul was allowed to live by himself  with a soldier to guard him </s>
<s> three days later he called together the local jewish leaders  when they had assembled  paul said to them   my brothers  although i have done nothing against our people or against the customs of our ancestors  i was arrested in jerusalem and handed over to the romans </s>
<s> they examined me and wanted to release me  because i was not guilty of any crime deserving death </s>
<s> the jews objected  so i was compelled to make an appeal to caesar  i certainly did not intend to bring any charge against my own people </s>
<s> for this reason i have asked to see you and talk with you  it is because of the hope of israel that i am bound with this chain  </s>
<s> they replied   we have not received any letters from judea concerning you  and none of our people who have come from there has reported or said anything bad about you </s>
<s> but we want to hear what your views are  for we know that people everywhere are talking against this sect  </s>
<s> they arranged to meet paul on a certain day  and came in even larger numbers to the place where he was staying  he witnessed to them from morning till evening  explaining about the kingdom of god  and from the law of moses and from the prophets he tried to persuade them about jesus </s>
<s> some were convinced by what he said  but others would not believe </s>
<s> they disagreed among themselves and began to leave after paul had made this final statement   the holy spirit spoke the truth to your ancestors when he said through isaiah the prophet </s>
<s>   go to this people and say   you will be ever hearing but never understanding  you will be ever seeing but never perceiving  </s>
<s> for this peoples heart has become calloused  they hardly hear with their ears  and they have closed their eyes  otherwise they might see with their eyes  hear with their ears  understand with their hearts and turn  and i would heal them  </s>
<s>  therefore i want you to know that gods salvation has been sent to the gentiles  and they will listen   </s>
<s> </s>
<s> for two whole years paul stayed there in his own rented house and welcomed all who came to see him </s>
<s> he proclaimed the kingdom of god and taught about the lord jesus christ  with all boldness and without hindrance </s>
<s> paul  a servant of christ jesus  called to be an apostle and set apart for the gospel of god </s>
<s> the gospel he promised beforehand through his prophets in the holy scriptures</s>
<s> regarding his son  who as to his earthly life was a descendant of david </s>
<s> and who through the spirit of holiness was appointed the son of god in power by his resurrection from the dead  jesus christ our lord </s>
<s> through him we received grace and apostleship to call all the gentiles to the obedience that comes from faith for his names sake </s>
<s> and you also are among those gentiles who are called to belong to jesus christ </s>
<s> to all in rome who are loved by god and called to be his holy people  grace and peace to you from god our father and from the lord jesus christ </s>
<s> first  i thank my god through jesus christ for all of you  because your faith is being reported all over the world </s>
<s> god  whom i serve in my spirit in preaching the gospel of his son  is my witness how constantly i remember you</s>
<s> in my prayers at all times  and i pray that now at last by gods will the way may be opened for me to come to you </s>
<s> i long to see you so that i may impart to you some spiritual gift to make you strong </s>
<s> that is  that you and i may be mutually encouraged by each others faith </s>
<s> i do not want you to be unaware  brothers and sisters  that i planned many times to come to you  but have been prevented from doing so until now  in order that i might have a harvest among you  just as i have had among the other gentiles </s>
<s> i am a debtor both to greeks and nongreeks  both to the wise and the foolish </s>
<s> that is why i am so eager to preach the gospel also to you who are in rome </s>
<s> for i am not ashamed of the gospel  because it is the power of god that brings salvation to everyone who believes  first to the jew  then to the gentile </s>
<s> for in the gospel the righteousness of god is revealed  a righteousness that is by faith from first to last  just as it is written   the righteous will live by faith  </s>
<s> the wrath of god is being revealed from heaven against all the godlessness and wickedness of people  who suppress the truth by their wickedness </s>
<s> since what may be known about god is plain to them  because god has made it plain to them </s>
<s> for since the creation of the world gods invisible qualities  his eternal power and divine nature  have been clearly seen  being understood from what has been made  so that people are without excuse </s>
<s> for although they knew god  they neither glorified him as god nor gave thanks to him  but their thinking became futile and their foolish hearts were darkened </s>
<s> although they claimed to be wise  they became fools</s>
<s> and exchanged the glory of the immortal god for images made to look like a mortal human being and birds and animals and reptiles </s>
<s> therefore god gave them over in the sinful desires of their hearts to sexual impurity for the degrading of their bodies with one another </s>
<s> they exchanged the truth about god for a lie  and worshipped and served created things rather than the creator  who is for ever praised  amen </s>
<s> because of this  god gave them over to shameful lusts  even their women exchanged natural sexual relations for unnatural ones </s>
<s> in the same way the men also abandoned natural relations with women and were inflamed with lust for one another  men committed shameful acts with other men  and received in themselves the due penalty for their error </s>
<s> furthermore  just as they did not think it worth while to retain the knowledge of god  so god gave them over to a depraved mind  so that they do what ought not to be done </s>
<s> they have become filled with every kind of wickedness  evil  greed and depravity  they are full of envy  murder  strife  deceit and malice  they are gossips </s>
<s> slanderers  godhaters  insolent  arrogant and boastful  they invent ways of doing evil  they disobey their parents </s>
<s> they have no understanding  no fidelity  no love  no mercy </s>
<s> although they know gods righteous decree that those who do such things deserve death  they not only continue to do these very things but also approve of those who practise them </s>
<s> you  therefore  have no excuse  you who pass judgment on someone else  for at whatever point you judge another  you are condemning yourself  because you who pass judgment do the same things </s>
<s> now we know that gods judgment against those who do such things is based on truth </s>
<s> so when you  a mere human being  pass judgment on them and yet do the same things  do you think you will escape gods judgment </s>
<s> or do you show contempt for the riches of his kindness  forbearance and patience  not realising that gods kindness is intended to lead you to repentance </s>
<s> but because of your stubbornness and your unrepentant heart  you are storing up wrath against yourself for the day of gods wrath  when his righteous judgment will be revealed </s>
<s> god  will repay each person according to what they have done  </s>
<s> to those who by persistence in doing good seek glory  honour and immortality  he will give eternal life </s>
<s> but for those who are selfseeking and who reject the truth and follow evil  there will be wrath and anger </s>
<s> there will be trouble and distress for every human being who does evil  first for the jew  then for the gentile </s>
<s> but glory  honour and peace for everyone who does good  first for the jew  then for the gentile </s>
<s> for god does not show favouritism </s>
<s> all who sin apart from the law will also perish apart from the law  and all who sin under the law will be judged by the law </s>
<s> for it is not those who hear the law who are righteous in gods sight  but it is those who obey the law who will be declared righteous </s>
<s>  indeed  when gentiles  who do not have the law  do by nature things required by the law  they are a law for themselves  even though they do not have the law </s>
<s> they show that the requirements of the law are written on their hearts  their consciences also bearing witness  and their thoughts sometimes accusing them and at other times even defending them  </s>
<s> this will take place on the day when god judges peoples secrets through jesus christ  as my gospel declares </s>
<s> now you  if you call yourself a jew  if you rely on the law and boast in god </s>
<s> if you know his will and approve of what is superior because you are instructed by the law </s>
