<s> if you are convinced that you are a guide for the blind  a light for those who are in the dark </s>
<s> an instructor of the foolish  a teacher of little children  because you have in the law the embodiment of knowledge and truth </s>
<s> you  then  who teach others  do you not teach yourself  you who preach against stealing  do you steal </s>
<s> you who say that people should not commit adultery  do you commit adultery  you who abhor idols  do you rob temples </s>
<s> you who boast in the law  do you dishonour god by breaking the law </s>
<s> as it is written   gods name is blasphemed among the gentiles because of you  </s>
<s> circumcision has value if you observe the law  but if you break the law  you have become as though you had not been circumcised </s>
<s> so then  if those who are not circumcised keep the laws requirements  will they not be regarded as though they were circumcised </s>
<s> the one who is not circumcised physically and yet obeys the law will condemn you who  even though you have the written code and circumcision  are a lawbreaker </s>
<s> a person is not a jew who is one only outwardly  nor is circumcision merely outward and physical </s>
<s> no  a person is a jew who is one inwardly  and circumcision is circumcision of the heart  by the spirit  not by the written code  such a persons praise is not from other people  but from god </s>
<s> what advantage  then  is there in being a jew  or what value is there in circumcision </s>
<s> much in every way  first of all  the jews have been entrusted with the very words of god </s>
<s> what if some were unfaithful  will their unfaithfulness nullify gods faithfulness </s>
<s> not at all  let god be true  and every human being a liar  as it is written   so that you may be proved right when you speak and prevail when you judge  </s>
<s> but if our unrighteousness brings out gods righteousness more clearly  what shall we say  that god is unjust in bringing his wrath on us   i am using a human argument  </s>
<s> certainly not  if that were so  how could god judge the world </s>
<s> someone might argue   if my falsehood enhances gods truthfulness and so increases his glory  why am i still condemned as a sinner  </s>
<s> why not say  as some slanderously claim that we say   let us do evil that good may result  their condemnation is just </s>
<s> what shall we conclude then  do we have any advantage  not at all  for we have already made the charge that jews and gentiles alike are all under the power of sin </s>
<s> as it is written   there is no one righteous  not even one </s>
<s> there is no one who understands  there is no one who seeks god </s>
<s> all have turned away  they have together become worthless  there is no one who does good  not even one  </s>
<s>  their throats are open graves  their tongues practise deceit    the poison of vipers is on their lips  </s>
<s>  their mouths are full of cursing and bitterness  </s>
<s>  their feet are swift to shed blood </s>
<s> ruin and misery mark their ways </s>
<s> and the way of peace they do not know  </s>
<s>  there is no fear of god before their eyes  </s>
<s> now we know that whatever the law says  it says to those who are under the law  so that every mouth may be silenced and the whole world held accountable to god </s>
<s> therefore no one will be declared righteous in gods sight by the works of the law  rather  through the law we become conscious of our sin </s>
<s> but now apart from the law the righteousness of god has been made known  to which the law and the prophets testify </s>
<s> this righteousness is given through faith in jesus christ to all who believe  there is no difference between jew and gentile </s>
<s> for all have sinned and fall short of the glory of god </s>
<s> and all are justified freely by his grace through the redemption that came by christ jesus </s>
<s> god presented christ as a sacrifice of atonement  through the shedding of his blood  to be received by faith  he did this to demonstrate his righteousness  because in his forbearance he had left the sins committed beforehand unpunished</s>
<s>  he did it to demonstrate his righteousness at the present time  so as to be just and the one who justifies those who have faith in jesus </s>
<s> where  then  is boasting  it is excluded  because of what law  the law that requires works  no  because of the  law that requires faith </s>
<s> for we maintain that a person is justified by faith apart from the works of the law </s>
<s> or is god the god of jews only  is he not the god of gentiles too  yes  of gentiles too </s>
<s> since there is only one god  who will justify the circumcised by faith and the uncircumcised through that same faith </s>
<s> do we  then  nullify the law by this faith  not at all  rather  we uphold the law </s>
<s> what then shall we say that abraham  our forefather according to the flesh  discovered in this matter </s>
<s> if  in fact  abraham was justified by works  he had something to boast about  but not before god </s>
<s> what does scripture say   abraham believed god  and it was credited to him as righteousness  </s>
<s> now to the one who works  wages are not credited as a gift but as an obligation </s>
<s> however  to the one who does not work but trusts god who justifies the ungodly  their faith is credited as righteousness </s>
<s> david says the same thing when he speaks of the blessedness of the one to whom god credits righteousness apart from works </s>
<s>  blessed are those whose transgressions are forgiven  whose sins are covered </s>
<s> blessed is the one whose sin the lord will never count against them  </s>
<s> is this blessedness only for the circumcised  or also for the uncircumcised  we have been saying that abrahams faith was credited to him as righteousness </s>
<s> under what circumstances was it credited  was it after he was circumcised  or before  it was not after  but before </s>
<s> and he received circumcision as a sign  a seal of the righteousness that he had by faith while he was still uncircumcised  so then  he is the father of all who believe but have not been circumcised  in order that righteousness might be credited to them </s>
<s> and he is then also the father of the circumcised who not only are circumcised but who also follow in the footsteps of the faith that our father abraham had before he was circumcised </s>
<s> it was not through the law that abraham and his offspring received the promise that he would be heir of the world  but through the righteousness that comes by faith </s>
<s> for if those who depend on the law are heirs  faith means nothing and the promise is worthless </s>
<s> because the law brings wrath  and where there is no law there is no transgression </s>
<s> therefore  the promise comes by faith  so that it may be by grace and may be guaranteed to all abrahams offspring  not only to those who are of the law but also to those who have the faith of abraham  he is the father of us all </s>
<s> as it is written   i have made you a father of many nations   he is our father in the sight of god  in whom he believed  the god who gives life to the dead and calls into being things that were not </s>
<s> against all hope  abraham in hope believed and so became the father of many nations  just as it had been said to him   so shall your offspring be  </s>
<s> without weakening in his faith  he faced the fact that his body was as good as dead  since he was about a hundred years old  and that sarahs womb was also dead </s>
<s> yet he did not waver through unbelief regarding the promise of god  but was strengthened in his faith and gave glory to god </s>
<s> being fully persuaded that god had power to do what he had promised </s>
<s> this is why  it was credited to him as righteousness  </s>
<s> the words  it was credited to him were written not for him alone </s>
<s> but also for us  to whom god will credit righteousness  for us who believe in him who raised jesus our lord from the dead </s>
<s> he was delivered over to death for our sins and was raised to life for our justification </s>
<s> therefore  since we have been justified through faith  we have peace with god through our lord jesus christ </s>
<s> through whom we have gained access by faith into this grace in which we now stand  and we boast in the hope of the glory of god </s>
<s> not only so  but we also glory in our sufferings  because we know that suffering produces perseverance </s>
<s> perseverance  character  and character  hope </s>
<s> and hope does not put us to shame  because gods love has been poured out into our hearts through the holy spirit  who has been given to us </s>
<s> you see  at just the right time  when we were still powerless  christ died for the ungodly </s>
<s> very rarely will anyone die for a righteous person  though for a good person someone might possibly dare to die </s>
<s> but god demonstrates his own love for us in this  while we were still sinners  christ died for us </s>
<s> since we have now been justified by his blood  how much more shall we be saved from gods wrath through him </s>
<s> for if  while we were gods enemies  we were reconciled to him through the death of his son  how much more  having been reconciled  shall we be saved through his life </s>
<s> not only is this so  but we also boast in god through our lord jesus christ  through whom we have now received reconciliation </s>
<s> therefore  just as sin entered the world through one man  and death through sin  and in this way death came to all people  because all sinned </s>
<s> to be sure  sin was in the world before the law was given  but sin is not charged against anyones account where there is no law </s>
<s> nevertheless  death reigned from the time of adam to the time of moses  even over those who did not sin by breaking a command  as did adam  who is a pattern of the one to come </s>
<s> but the gift is not like the trespass  for if the many died by the trespass of the one man  how much more did gods grace and the gift that came by the grace of the one man  jesus christ  overflow to the many </s>
<s> nor can the gift of god be compared with the result of one mans sin  the judgment followed one sin and brought condemnation  but the gift followed many trespasses and brought justification </s>
<s> for if  by the trespass of the one man  death reigned through that one man  how much more will those who receive gods abundant provision of grace and of the gift of righteousness reign in life through the one man  jesus christ </s>
<s> consequently  just as one trespass resulted in condemnation for all people  so also one righteous act resulted in justification and life for all people </s>
<s> for just as through the disobedience of the one man the many were made sinners  so also through the obedience of the one man the many will be made righteous </s>
<s> the law was brought in so that the trespass might increase  but where sin increased  grace increased all the more </s>
<s> so that  just as sin reigned in death  so also grace might reign through righteousness to bring eternal life through jesus christ our lord </s>
<s> what shall we say  then  shall we go on sinning  so that grace may increase </s>
<s> by no means  we are those who have died to sin  how can we live in it any longer </s>
<s> or dont you know that all of us who were baptised into christ jesus were baptised into his death </s>
<s> we were therefore buried with him through baptism into death in order that  just as christ was raised from the dead through the glory of the father  we too may live a new life </s>
<s> for if we have been united with him in a death like his  we will certainly also be united with him in a resurrection like his </s>
<s> for we know that our old self was crucified with him so that the body ruled by sin might be done away with  that we should no longer be slaves to sin </s>
<s> because anyone who has died has been set free from sin </s>
<s> now if we died with christ  we believe that we will also live with him </s>
<s> for we know that since christ was raised from the dead  he cannot die again  death no longer has mastery over him </s>
<s> the death he died  he died to sin once for all  but the life he lives  he lives to god </s>
<s> in the same way  count yourselves dead to sin but alive to god in christ jesus </s>
<s> therefore do not let sin reign in your mortal body so that you obey its evil desires </s>
<s> do not offer any part of yourself to sin as an instrument of wickedness  but rather offer yourselves to god as those who have been brought from death to life  and offer every part of yourself to him as an instrument of righteousness </s>
<s> for sin shall no longer be your master  because you are not under the law  but under grace </s>
<s> what then  shall we sin because we are not under the law but under grace  by no means </s>
<s> dont you know that when you offer yourselves to someone as obedient slaves  you are slaves of the one you obey  whether you are slaves to sin  which leads to death  or to obedience  which leads to righteousness </s>
<s> but thanks be to god that  though you used to be slaves to sin  you have come to obey from your heart the pattern of teaching that has now claimed your allegiance </s>
<s> you have been set free from sin and have become slaves to righteousness </s>
<s> i am using an example from everyday life because of your human limitations  just as you used to offer yourselves as slaves to impurity and to everincreasing wickedness  so now offer yourselves as slaves to righteousness leading to holiness </s>
<s> when you were slaves to sin  you were free from the control of righteousness </s>
<s> what benefit did you reap at that time from the things you are now ashamed of  those things result in death </s>
<s> but now that you have been set free from sin and have become slaves of god  the benefit you reap leads to holiness  and the result is eternal life </s>
<s> for the wages of sin is death  but the gift of god is eternal life in christ jesus our lord </s>
<s> do you not know  brothers and sisters  for i am speaking to those who know the law  that the law has authority over someone only as long as that person lives </s>
<s> for example  by law a married woman is bound to her husband as long as he is alive  but if her husband dies  she is released from the law that binds her to him </s>
<s> so then  if she has sexual relations with another man while her husband is still alive  she is called an adulteress  but if her husband dies  she is released from that law and is not an adulteress if she marries another man </s>
<s> so  my brothers and sisters  you also died to the law through the body of christ  that you might belong to another  to him who was raised from the dead  in order that we might bear fruit for god </s>
<s> for when we were in the realm of the flesh  the sinful passions aroused by the law were at work in us  so that we bore fruit for death </s>
<s> but now  by dying to what once bound us  we have been released from the law so that we serve in the new way of the spirit  and not in the old way of the written code </s>
<s> what shall we say  then  is the law sinful  certainly not  nevertheless  i would not have known what sin was had it not been for the law  for i would not have known what coveting really was if the law had not said   you shall not covet  </s>
<s> but sin  seizing the opportunity afforded by the commandment  produced in me every kind of coveting  for apart from the law  sin was dead </s>
<s> once i was alive apart from the law  but when the commandment came  sin sprang to life and i died </s>
<s> i found that the very commandment that was intended to bring life actually brought death </s>
<s> for sin  seizing the opportunity afforded by the commandment  deceived me  and through the commandment put me to death </s>
<s> so then  the law is holy  and the commandment is holy  righteous and good </s>
<s> did that which is good  then  become death to me  by no means  nevertheless  in order that sin might be recognised as sin  it used what is good to bring about my death  so that through the commandment sin might become utterly sinful </s>
<s> we know that the law is spiritual  but i am unspiritual  sold as a slave to sin </s>
<s> i do not understand what i do  for what i want to do i do not do  but what i hate i do </s>
<s> and if i do what i do not want to do  i agree that the law is good </s>
<s> as it is  it is no longer i myself who do it  but it is sin living in me </s>
<s> for i know that good itself does not dwell in me  that is  in my sinful nature  for i have the desire to do what is good  but i cannot carry it out </s>
<s> for i do not do the good i want to do  but the evil i do not want to do  this i keep on doing </s>
<s> now if i do what i do not want to do  it is no longer i who do it  but it is sin living in me that does it </s>
<s> so i find this law at work  although i want to do good  evil is right there with me </s>
<s> for in my inner being i delight in gods law </s>
<s> but i see another law at work in me  waging war against the law of my mind and making me a prisoner of the law of sin at work within me </s>
<s> what a wretched man i am  who will rescue me from this body that is subject to death </s>
<s> thanks be to god  who delivers me through jesus christ our lord  so then  i myself in my mind am a slave to gods law  but in my sinful nature a slave to the law of sin </s>
<s> therefore  there is now no condemnation for those who are in christ jesus </s>
<s> because through christ jesus the law of the spirit who gives life has set you free from the law of sin and death </s>
<s> for what the law was powerless to do because it was weakened by the flesh  god did by sending his own son in the likeness of sinful flesh to be a sin offering  and so he condemned sin in the flesh </s>
<s> in order that the righteous requirement of the law might be fully met in us  who do not live according to the flesh but according to the spirit </s>
<s> those who live according to the flesh have their minds set on what the flesh desires  but those who live in accordance with the spirit have their minds set on what the spirit desires </s>
<s> the mind governed by the flesh is death  but the mind governed by the spirit is life and peace </s>
<s> the mind governed by the flesh is hostile to god  it does not submit to gods law  nor can it do so </s>
<s> those who are in the realm of the flesh cannot please god </s>
<s> you  however  are not in the realm of the flesh but are in the realm of the spirit  if indeed the spirit of god lives in you  and if anyone does not have the spirit of christ  they do not belong to christ </s>
<s> but if christ is in you  then even though your body is subject to death because of sin  the spirit gives life because of righteousness </s>
<s> and if the spirit of him who raised jesus from the dead is living in you  he who raised christ from the dead will also give life to your mortal bodies because of his spirit who lives in you </s>
<s> therefore  brothers and sisters  we have an obligation  but it is not to the flesh  to live according to it </s>
<s> for if you live according to the flesh  you will die  but if by the spirit you put to death the misdeeds of the body  you will live </s>
<s> for those who are led by the spirit of god are the children of god </s>
<s> the spirit you received does not make you slaves  so that you live in fear again  rather  the spirit you received brought about your adoption to sonship  and by him we cry   abba  father  </s>
<s> the spirit himself testifies with our spirit that we are gods children </s>
<s> now if we are children  then we are heirs  heirs of god and coheirs with christ  if indeed we share in his sufferings in order that we may also share in his glory </s>
<s> i consider that our present sufferings are not worth comparing with the glory that will be revealed in us </s>
<s> for the creation waits in eager expectation for the children of god to be revealed </s>
<s> for the creation was subjected to frustration  not by its own choice  but by the will of the one who subjected it  in hope</s>
<s> that the creation itself will be liberated from its bondage to decay and brought into the freedom and glory of the children of god </s>
<s> we know that the whole creation has been groaning as in the pains of childbirth right up to the present time </s>
<s> not only so  but we ourselves  who have the firstfruits of the spirit  groan inwardly as we wait eagerly for our adoption to sonship  the redemption of our bodies </s>
<s> for in this hope we were saved  but hope that is seen is no hope at all  who hopes for what they already have </s>
<s> but if we hope for what we do not yet have  we wait for it patiently </s>
<s> in the same way  the spirit helps us in our weakness  we do not know what we ought to pray for  but the spirit himself intercedes for us through wordless groans </s>
<s> and he who searches our hearts knows the mind of the spirit  because the spirit intercedes for gods people in accordance with the will of god </s>
<s> and we know that in all things god works for the good of those who love him  who have been called according to his purpose </s>
<s> for those god foreknew he also predestined to be conformed to the image of his son  that he might be the firstborn among many brothers and sisters </s>
<s> and those he predestined  he also called  those he called  he also justified  those he justified  he also glorified </s>
<s> what  then  shall we say in response to these things  if god is for us  who can be against us </s>
<s> he who did not spare his own son  but gave him up for us all  how will he not also  along with him  graciously give us all things </s>
<s> who will bring any charge against those whom god has chosen  it is god who justifies </s>
<s> who then is the one who condemns  no one  christ jesus who died  more than that  who was raised to life  is at the right hand of god and is also interceding for us </s>
<s> who shall separate us from the love of christ  shall trouble or hardship or persecution or famine or nakedness or danger or sword </s>
<s> as it is written   for your sake we face death all day long  we are considered as sheep to be slaughtered  </s>
<s> i speak the truth in christ  i am not lying  my conscience confirms it through the holy spirit </s>
<s> i have great sorrow and unceasing anguish in my heart </s>
<s> for i could wish that i myself were cursed and cut off from christ for the sake of my people  those of my own race </s>
<s> the people of israel  theirs is the adoption to sonship  theirs the divine glory  the covenants  the receiving of the law  the temple worship and the promises </s>
<s> theirs are the patriarchs  and from them is traced the human ancestry of the messiah  who is god over all  for ever praised  amen </s>
<s> it is not as though gods word had failed  for not all who are descended from israel are israel </s>
<s> nor because they are his descendants are they all abrahams children  on the contrary   it is through isaac that your offspring will be reckoned  </s>
<s> in other words  it is not the children by physical descent who are gods children  but it is the children of the promise who are regarded as abrahams offspring </s>
<s> for this was how the promise was stated   at the appointed time i will return  and sarah will have a son  </s>
<s> not only that  but rebekahs children were conceived at the same time by our father isaac </s>
<s> yet  before the twins were born or had done anything good or bad  in order that gods purpose in election might stand </s>
<s> not by works but by him who calls  she was told   the older will serve the younger  </s>
<s> just as it is written   jacob i loved  but esau i hated  </s>
<s> what then shall we say  is god unjust  not at all </s>
<s> for he says to moses   i will have mercy on whom i have mercy  and i will have compassion on whom i have compassion  </s>
<s> one of you will say to me   then why does god still blame us  for who is able to resist his will  </s>
<s> but who are you  a human being  to talk back to god   shall what is formed say to the one who formed it   why did you make me like this   </s>
<s> does not the potter have the right to make out of the same lump of clay some pottery for special purposes and some for common use </s>
<s> what if god  although choosing to show his wrath and make his power known  bore with great patience the objects of his wrath  prepared for destruction </s>
<s> what if he did this to make the riches of his glory known to the objects of his mercy  whom he prepared in advance for glory </s>
<s> even us  whom he also called  not only from the jews but also from the gentiles </s>
<s> as he says in hosea   i will call them  my people  who are not my people  and i will call her  my loved one  who is not my loved one    in the very place where it was said to them   you are not my people   there they will be called  children of the living god     though the number of the israelites be like the sand by the sea  only the remnant will be saved </s>
<s> for the lord will carry out his sentence on earth with speed and finality    unless the lord almighty had left us descendants  we would have become like sodom  we would have been like gomorrah  </s>
<s> what then shall we say  that the gentiles  who did not pursue righteousness  have obtained it  a righteousness that is by faith </s>
<s> but the people of israel  who pursued the law as the way of righteousness  have not attained their goal </s>
<s> why not  because they pursued it not by faith but as if it were by works  they stumbled over the  stumbling stone  </s>
<s> as it is written   see  i lay in zion a stone that causes people to stumble and a rock that makes them fall  and the one who believes in him will never be put to shame  </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  my hearts desire and prayer to god for the israelites is that they may be saved </s>
<s> for i can testify about them that they are zealous for god  but their zeal is not based on knowledge </s>
<s> since they did not know the righteousness of god and sought to establish their own  they did not submit to gods righteousness </s>
<s> christ is the culmination of the law so that there may be righteousness for everyone who believes </s>
<s> moses writes this about the righteousness that is by the law   the person who does these things will live by them  </s>
<s> but the righteousness that is by faith says   do not say in your heart   who will ascend into heaven     that is  to bring christ down </s>
<s>  or  who will descend into the deep     that is  to bring christ up from the dead  </s>
<s> but what does it say   the word is near you  it is in your mouth and in your heart   that is  the message concerning faith that we proclaim </s>
<s> if you declare with your mouth   jesus is lord   and believe in your heart that god raised him from the dead  you will be saved </s>
<s> for it is with your heart that you believe and are justified  and it is with your mouth that you profess your faith and are saved </s>
<s> as scripture says   anyone who believes in him will never be put to shame  </s>
<s> for there is no difference between jew and gentile  the same lord is lord of all and richly blesses all who call on him </s>
<s> for   everyone who calls on the name of the lord will be saved  </s>
<s> how  then  can they call on the one they have not believed in  and how can they believe in the one of whom they have not heard  and how can they hear without someone preaching to them </s>
<s> and how can anyone preach unless they are sent  as it is written   how beautiful are the feet of those who bring good news  </s>
<s> but not all the israelites accepted the good news  for isaiah says   lord  who has believed our message  </s>
<s> consequently  faith comes from hearing the message  and the message is heard through the word about christ </s>
<s> but i ask  did they not hear  of course they did   their voice has gone out into all the earth  their words to the ends of the world    i will make you envious by those who are not a nation  i will make you angry by a nation that has no understanding    i was found by those who did not seek me  i revealed myself to those who did not ask for me    all day long i have held out my hands to a disobedient and obstinate people  </s>
<s> i ask then  did god reject his people  by no means  i am an israelite myself  a descendant of abraham  from the tribe of benjamin </s>
<s> god did not reject his people  whom he foreknew  dont you know what scripture says in the passage about elijah  how he appealed to god against israel </s>
<s>  lord  they have killed your prophets and torn down your altars  i am the only one left  and they are trying to kill me </s>
<s> and what was gods answer to him   i have reserved for myself seven thousand who have not bowed the knee to baal  </s>
<s> so too  at the present time there is a remnant chosen by grace </s>
<s> and if by grace  then it cannot be based on works  if it were  grace would no longer be grace </s>
<s> what then  what the people of israel sought so earnestly they did not obtain  the elect among them did  but the others were hardened </s>
<s> as it is written   god gave them a spirit of stupor  eyes that could not see and ears that could not hear  to this very day    may their table become a snare and a trap  a stumblingblock and a retribution for them </s>
<s> may their eyes be darkened so they cannot see  and their backs be bent for ever  </s>
<s> again i ask  did they stumble so as to fall beyond recovery  not at all  rather  because of their transgression  salvation has come to the gentiles to make israel envious </s>
<s> but if their transgression means riches for the world  and their loss means riches for the gentiles  how much greater riches will their full inclusion bring </s>
<s> i am talking to you gentiles  inasmuch as i am the apostle to the gentiles  i take pride in my ministry</s>
<s> in the hope that i may somehow arouse my own people to envy and save some of them </s>
<s> for if their rejection brought reconciliation to the world  what will their acceptance be but life from the dead </s>
<s> if the part of the dough offered as firstfruits is holy  then the whole batch is holy  if the root is holy  so are the branches </s>
<s> if some of the branches have been broken off  and you  though a wild olive shoot  have been grafted in among the others and now share in the nourishing sap from the olive root </s>
<s> do not consider yourself to be superior to those other branches  if you do  consider this  you do not support the root  but the root supports you </s>
<s> you will say then   branches were broken off so that i could be grafted in  </s>
<s> granted  but they were broken off because of unbelief  and you stand by faith  do not be arrogant  but tremble </s>
<s> for if god did not spare the natural branches  he will not spare you either </s>
<s> consider therefore the kindness and sternness of god  sternness to those who fell  but kindness to you  provided that you continue in his kindness  otherwise  you also will be cut off </s>
<s> and if they do not persist in unbelief  they will be grafted in  for god is able to graft them in again </s>
<s> after all  if you were cut out of an olive tree that is wild by nature  and contrary to nature were grafted into a cultivated olive tree  how much more readily will these  the natural branches  be grafted into their own olive tree </s>
<s> i do not want you to be ignorant of this mystery  brothers and sisters  so that you may not be conceited  israel has experienced a hardening in part until the full number of the gentiles has come in </s>
<s> and in this way all israel will be saved  as it is written   the deliverer will come from zion  he will turn godlessness away from jacob </s>
<s> and this is my covenant with them when i take away their sins  </s>
<s> as far as the gospel is concerned  they are enemies for your sake  but as far as election is concerned  they are loved on account of the patriarchs </s>
<s> for gods gifts and his call are irrevocable </s>
<s> just as you who were at one time disobedient to god have now received mercy as a result of their disobedience </s>
<s> so they too have now become disobedient in order that they too may now receive mercy as a result of gods mercy to you </s>
<s> for god has bound everyone over to disobedience so that he may have mercy on them all </s>
<s> oh  the depth of the riches of the wisdom and knowledge of god  how unsearchable his judgments  and his paths beyond tracing out </s>
<s>  who has known the mind of the lord  or who has been his counsellor  </s>
<s>  who has ever given to god  that god should repay them  </s>
<s> for from him and through him and for him are all things  to him be the glory for ever  amen </s>
<s> therefore  i urge you  brothers and sisters  in view of gods mercy  to offer your bodies as a living sacrifice  holy and pleasing to god  this is your true and proper worship </s>
<s> do not conform to the pattern of this world  but be transformed by the renewing of your mind  then you will be able to test and approve what gods will is  his good  pleasing and perfect will </s>
<s> for by the grace given me i say to every one of you  do not think of yourself more highly than you ought  but rather think of yourself with sober judgment  in accordance with the faith god has distributed to each of you </s>
<s> for just as each of us has one body with many members  and these members do not all have the same function </s>
<s> so in christ we  though many  form one body  and each member belongs to all the others </s>
<s> we have different gifts  according to the grace given to each of us  if your gift is prophesying  then prophesy in accordance with your faith </s>
<s> if it is serving  then serve  if it is teaching  then teach </s>
<s> if it is to encourage  then give encouragement  if it is giving  then give generously  if it is to lead  do it diligently  if it is to show mercy  do it cheerfully </s>
<s> love must be sincere  hate what is evil  cling to what is good </s>
<s> be devoted to one another in love  honour one another above yourselves </s>
<s> never be lacking in zeal  but keep your spiritual fervour  serving the lord </s>
<s> be joyful in hope  patient in affliction  faithful in prayer </s>
<s> share with the lords people who are in need  practise hospitality </s>
<s> bless those who persecute you  bless and do not curse </s>
<s> rejoice with those who rejoice  mourn with those who mourn </s>
<s> live in harmony with one another  do not be proud  but be willing to associate with people of low position  do not be conceited </s>
<s> do not repay anyone evil for evil  be careful to do what is right in the eyes of everyone </s>
<s> if it is possible  as far as it depends on you  live at peace with everyone </s>
<s> do not take revenge  my dear friends  but leave room for gods wrath  for it is written   it is mine to avenge  i will repay   says the lord </s>
<s> on the contrary   if your enemy is hungry  feed him  if he is thirsty  give him something to drink  in doing this  you will heap burning coals on his head  </s>
<s> let everyone be subject to the governing authorities  for there is no authority except that which god has established  the authorities that exist have been established by god </s>
<s> consequently  whoever rebels against the authority is rebelling against what god has instituted  and those who do so will bring judgment on themselves </s>
<s> for rulers hold no terror for those who do right  but for those who do wrong  do you want to be free from fear of the one in authority  then do what is right and you will be commended </s>
<s> for the one in authority is gods servant for your good  but if you do wrong  be afraid  for rulers do not bear the sword for no reason  they are gods servants  agents of wrath to bring punishment on the wrongdoer </s>
<s> therefore  it is necessary to submit to the authorities  not only because of possible punishment but also as a matter of conscience </s>
<s> this is also why you pay taxes  for the authorities are gods servants  who give their full time to governing </s>
<s> give to everyone what you owe them  if you owe taxes  pay taxes  if revenue  then revenue  if respect  then respect  if honour  then honour </s>
<s> let no debt remain outstanding  except the continuing debt to love one another  for whoever loves others has fulfilled the law </s>
<s> the commandments   you shall not commit adultery    you shall not murder    you shall not steal    you shall not covet   and whatever other command there may be  are summed up in this one command   love your neighbour as yourself  </s>
<s> love does no harm to a neighbour  therefore love is the fulfilment of the law </s>
<s> and do this  understanding the present time  the hour has already come for you to wake up from your slumber  because our salvation is nearer now than when we first believed </s>
<s> the night is nearly over  the day is almost here  so let us put aside the deeds of darkness and put on the armour of light </s>
<s> let us behave decently  as in the daytime  not in carousing and drunkenness  not in sexual immorality and debauchery  not in dissension and jealousy </s>
<s> rather  clothe yourselves with the lord jesus christ  and do not think about how to gratify the desires of the flesh </s>
<s> accept the one whose faith is weak  without quarrelling over disputable matters </s>
<s> one persons faith allows them to eat anything  but another  whose faith is weak  eats only vegetables </s>
<s> the one who eats everything must not treat with contempt the one who does not  and the one who does not eat everything must not judge the one who does  for god has accepted them </s>
<s> who are you to judge someone elses servant  to their own master  servants stand or fall  and they will stand  for the lord is able to make them stand </s>
<s> one person considers one day more sacred than another  another considers every day alike  each of them should be fully convinced in their own mind </s>
<s> whoever regards one day as special does so to the lord  whoever eats meat does so to the lord  for they give thanks to god  and whoever abstains does so to the lord and gives thanks to god </s>
<s> for none of us lives for ourselves alone  and none of us dies for ourselves alone </s>
<s> if we live  we live for the lord  and if we die  we die for the lord  so  whether we live or die  we belong to the lord </s>
<s> for this very reason  christ died and returned to life so that he might be the lord of both the dead and the living </s>
<s> you  then  why do you judge your brother or sister  or why do you treat them with contempt  for we will all stand before gods judgment seat </s>
<s> it is written    as surely as i live   says the lord   every knee will bow before me  every tongue will acknowledge god   </s>
<s> therefore let us stop passing judgment on one another  instead  make up your mind not to put any stumblingblock or obstacle in the way of a brother or sister </s>
<s> i am convinced  being fully persuaded in the lord jesus  that nothing is unclean in itself  but if anyone regards something as unclean  then for that person it is unclean </s>
<s> if your brother or sister is distressed because of what you eat  you are no longer acting in love  do not by your eating destroy someone for whom christ died </s>
<s> therefore do not let what you know is good be spoken of as evil </s>
<s> for the kingdom of god is not a matter of eating and drinking  but of righteousness  peace and joy in the holy spirit </s>
<s> because anyone who serves christ in this way is pleasing to god and receives human approval </s>
<s> let us therefore make every effort to do what leads to peace and to mutual edification </s>
<s> do not destroy the work of god for the sake of food  all food is clean  but it is wrong for a person to eat anything that causes someone else to stumble </s>
<s> it is better not to eat meat or drink wine or to do anything else that will cause your brother or sister to fall </s>
<s> so whatever you believe about these things keep between yourself and god  blessed is the one who does not condemn himself by what he approves </s>
<s> but whoever has doubts is condemned if they eat  because their eating is not from faith  and everything that does not come from faith is sin </s>
<s> we who are strong ought to bear with the failings of the weak and not to please ourselves </s>
<s> each of us should please our neighbours for their good  to build them up </s>
<s> for even christ did not please himself but  as it is written   the insults of those who insult you have fallen on me  </s>
<s> for everything that was written in the past was written to teach us  so that through the endurance taught in the scriptures and the encouragement they provide we might have hope </s>
<s> may the god who gives endurance and encouragement give you the same attitude of mind toward each other that christ jesus had </s>
<s> so that with one mind and one voice you may glorify the god and father of our lord jesus christ </s>
<s> accept one another  then  just as christ accepted you  in order to bring praise to god </s>
<s> for i tell you that christ has become a servant of the jews on behalf of gods truth  so that the promises made to the patriarchs might be confirmed</s>
<s> and  moreover  that the gentiles might glorify god for his mercy  as it is written   therefore i will praise you among the gentiles  i will sing the praises of your name    rejoice  you gentiles  with his people    praise the lord  all you gentiles  let all the peoples extol him    the root of jesse will spring up  one who will arise to rule over the nations  in him the gentiles will hope  </s>
<s> may the god of hope fill you with all joy and peace as you trust in him  so that you may overflow with hope by the power of the holy spirit </s>
<s> i myself am convinced  my brothers and sisters  that you yourselves are full of goodness  filled with knowledge and competent to instruct one another </s>
<s> yet i have written to you quite boldly on some points to remind you of them again  because of the grace god gave me</s>
<s> to be a minister of christ jesus to the gentiles  he gave me the priestly duty of proclaiming the gospel of god  so that the gentiles might become an offering acceptable to god  sanctified by the holy spirit </s>
<s> therefore i glory in christ jesus in my service to god </s>
<s> i will not venture to speak of anything except what christ has accomplished through me in leading the gentiles to obey god by what i have said and done </s>
<s> by the power of signs and wonders  through the power of the spirit of god  so from jerusalem all the way round to illyricum  i have fully proclaimed the gospel of christ </s>
<s> it has always been my ambition to preach the gospel where christ was not known  so that i would not be building on someone elses foundation </s>
<s> rather  as it is written   those who were not told about him will see  and those who have not heard will understand  </s>
<s> but now that there is no more place for me to work in these regions  and since i have been longing for many years to visit you </s>
<s> i plan to do so when i go to spain  i hope to see you while passing through and that you will assist me on my journey there  after i have enjoyed your company for a while </s>
<s> now  however  i am on my way to jerusalem in the service of the lords people there </s>
<s> for macedonia and achaia were pleased to make a contribution for the poor among the lords people in jerusalem </s>
<s> they were pleased to do it  and indeed they owe it to them  for if the gentiles have shared in the jews spiritual blessings  they owe it to the jews to share with them their material blessings </s>
<s> so after i have completed this task and have made sure that they have received this contribution  i will go to spain and visit you on the way </s>
<s> i know that when i come to you  i will come in the full measure of the blessing of christ </s>
<s> i urge you  brothers and sisters  by our lord jesus christ and by the love of the spirit  to join me in my struggle by praying to god for me </s>
<s> pray that i may be kept safe from the unbelievers in judea and that the contribution i take to jerusalem may be favourably received by the lords people there </s>
<s> so that i may come to you with joy  by gods will  and in your company be refreshed </s>
<s> the god of peace be with you all  amen </s>
<s> i commend to you our sister phoebe  a deacon  of the church in cenchreae </s>
<s> i ask you to receive her in the lord in a way worthy of his people and to give her any help she may need from you  for she has been the benefactor of many people  including me </s>
<s> greet priscilla and aquila  my fellow workers in christ jesus </s>
<s> they risked their lives for me  not only i but all the churches of the gentiles are grateful to them </s>
<s> greet also the church that meets at their house  greet my dear friend epenetus  who was the first convert to christ in the province of asia </s>
<s> greet mary  who worked very hard for you </s>
<s> greet andronicus and junia  my fellow jews who have been in prison with me  they are outstanding among the apostles  and they were in christ before i was </s>
<s> greet ampliatus  my dear friend in the lord </s>
<s> greet urbanus  our fellow worker in christ  and my dear friend stachys </s>
<s> greet apelles  whose fidelity to christ has stood the test  greet those who belong to the household of aristobulus </s>
<s> greet herodion  my fellow jew  greet those in the household of narcissus who are in the lord </s>
<s> greet tryphena and tryphosa  those women who work hard in the lord  greet my dear friend persis  another woman who has worked very hard in the lord </s>
<s> greet rufus  chosen in the lord  and his mother  who has been a mother to me  too </s>
<s> greet asyncritus  phlegon  hermes  patrobas  hermas and the other brothers and sisters with them </s>
<s> greet philologus  julia  nereus and his sister  and olympas and all the lords people who are with them </s>
<s> greet one another with a holy kiss  all the churches of christ send greetings </s>
<s> i urge you  brothers and sisters  to watch out for those who cause divisions and put obstacles in your way that are contrary to the teaching you have learned  keep away from them </s>
<s> for such people are not serving our lord christ  but their own appetites  by smooth talk and flattery they deceive the minds of nave people </s>
<s> everyone has heard about your obedience  so i rejoice because of you  but i want you to be wise about what is good  and innocent about what is evil </s>
<s> the god of peace will soon crush satan under your feet  the grace of our lord jesus be with you </s>
<s> timothy  my coworker  sends his greetings to you  as do lucius  jason and sosipater  my fellow jews </s>
<s> i  tertius  who wrote down this letter  greet you in the lord </s>
<s> gaius  whose hospitality i and the whole church here enjoy  sends you his greetings  erastus  who is the citys director of public works  and our brother quartus send you their greetings  </s>
<s> </s>
<s> now to him who is able to establish you in accordance with my gospel  the message i proclaim about jesus christ  in keeping with the revelation of the mystery hidden for long ages past </s>
<s> but now revealed and made known through the prophetic writings by the command of the eternal god  so that all the gentiles might come to the obedience that comes from faith </s>
<s> to the only wise god be glory for ever through jesus christ  amen </s>
<s> paul  called to be an apostle of christ jesus by the will of god  and our brother sosthenes </s>
<s> to the church of god in corinth  to those sanctified in christ jesus and called to be his holy people  together with all those everywhere who call on the name of our lord jesus christ  their lord and ours </s>
<s> grace and peace to you from god our father and the lord jesus christ </s>
<s> i always thank my god for you because of his grace given you in christ jesus </s>
<s> for in him you have been enriched in every way  with all kinds of speech and with all knowledge </s>
<s> god thus confirming our testimony about christ among you </s>
<s> therefore you do not lack any spiritual gift as you eagerly wait for our lord jesus christ to be revealed </s>
<s> he will also keep you firm to the end  so that you will be blameless on the day of our lord jesus christ </s>
<s> god is faithful  who has called you into fellowship with his son  jesus christ our lord </s>
<s> i appeal to you  brothers and sisters  in the name of our lord jesus christ  that all of you agree with one another in what you say and that there be no divisions among you  but that you be perfectly united in mind and thought </s>
<s> my brothers and sisters  some from chloes household have informed me that there are quarrels among you </s>
<s> what i mean is this  one of you says   i follow paul  another   i follow apollos  another   i follow cephas   still another   i follow christ  </s>
<s> is christ divided  was paul crucified for you  were you baptised in the name of paul </s>
<s> i thank god that i did not baptise any of you except crispus and gaius </s>
<s> so no one can say that you were baptised in my name </s>
<s>  yes  i also baptised the household of stephanas  beyond that  i dont remember if i baptised anyone else  </s>
<s> for christ did not send me to baptise  but to preach the gospel  not with wisdom and eloquence  lest the cross of christ be emptied of its power </s>
<s> for the message of the cross is foolishness to those who are perishing  but to us who are being saved it is the power of god </s>
<s> for it is written   i will destroy the wisdom of the wise  the intelligence of the intelligent i will frustrate  </s>
<s> where is the wise person  where is the teacher of the law  where is the philosopher of this age  has not god made foolish the wisdom of the world </s>
<s> for since in the wisdom of god the world through its wisdom did not know him  god was pleased through the foolishness of what was preached to save those who believe </s>
<s> jews demand signs and greeks look for wisdom </s>
<s> but we preach christ crucified  a stumblingblock to jews and foolishness to gentiles </s>
<s> but to those whom god has called  both jews and greeks  christ the power of god and the wisdom of god </s>
<s> for the foolishness of god is wiser than human wisdom  and the weakness of god is stronger than human strength </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  think of what you were when you were called  not many of you were wise by human standards  not many were influential  not many were of noble birth </s>
<s> but god chose the foolish things of the world to shame the wise  god chose the weak things of the world to shame the strong </s>
<s> god chose the lowly things of this world and the despised things  and the things that are not  to nullify the things that are </s>
<s> so that no one may boast before him </s>
<s> it is because of him that you are in christ jesus  who has become for us wisdom from god  that is  our righteousness  holiness and redemption </s>
<s> therefore  as it is written   let the one who boasts boast in the lord  </s>
<s> and so it was with me  brothers and sisters  when i came to you  i did not come with eloquence or human wisdom as i proclaimed to you the testimony about god </s>
<s> for i resolved to know nothing while i was with you except jesus christ and him crucified </s>
<s> i came to you in weakness with great fear and trembling </s>
<s> my message and my preaching were not with wise and persuasive words  but with a demonstration of the spirits power </s>
<s> so that your faith might not rest on human wisdom  but on gods power </s>
<s> we do  however  speak a message of wisdom among the mature  but not the wisdom of this age or of the rulers of this age  who are coming to nothing </s>
<s> no  we declare gods wisdom  a mystery that has been hidden and that god destined for our glory before time began </s>
<s> none of the rulers of this age understood it  for if they had  they would not have crucified the lord of glory </s>
<s> however  as it is written   what no eye has seen  what no ear has heard  and what no human mind has conceived  the things god has prepared for those who love him  the spirit searches all things  even the deep things of god </s>
<s> for who knows a persons thoughts except their own spirit within them  in the same way no one knows the thoughts of god except the spirit of god </s>
<s> what we have received is not the spirit of the world  but the spirit who is from god  so that we may understand what god has freely given us </s>
<s> this is what we speak  not in words taught us by human wisdom but in words taught by the spirit  explaining spiritual realities with spirittaught words </s>
<s> the person without the spirit does not accept the things that come from the spirit of god but considers them foolishness  and cannot understand them because they are discerned only through the spirit </s>
<s> the person with the spirit makes judgments about all things  but such a person is not subject to merely human judgments </s>
<s> for   who has known the mind of the lord so as to instruct him  </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  i could not address you as people who live by the spirit but as people who are still worldly  mere infants in christ </s>
<s> i gave you milk  not solid food  for you were not yet ready for it  indeed  you are still not ready </s>
<s> you are still worldly  for since there is jealousy and quarrelling among you  are you not worldly  are you not acting like mere humans </s>
<s> for when one says   i follow paul   and another   i follow apollos   are you not mere human beings </s>
<s> what  after all  is apollos  and what is paul  only servants  through whom you came to believe  as the lord has assigned to each his task </s>
<s> i planted the seed  apollos watered it  but god has been making it grow </s>
<s> so neither the one who plants nor the one who waters is anything  but only god  who makes things grow </s>
<s> the one who plants and the one who waters have one purpose  and they will each be rewarded according to their own labour </s>
<s> for we are fellow workers in gods service  you are gods field  gods building </s>
<s> by the grace god has given me  i laid a foundation as a wise builder  and someone else is building on it  but each one should build with care </s>
<s> for no one can lay any foundation other than the one already laid  which is jesus christ </s>
<s> if anyone builds on this foundation using gold  silver  costly stones  wood  hay or straw </s>
<s> their work will be shown for what it is  because the day will bring it to light  it will be revealed with fire  and the fire will test the quality of each persons work </s>
<s> if what has been built survives  the builder will receive a reward </s>
<s> if it is burned up  the builder will suffer loss but yet will be saved  even though only as one escaping through the flames </s>
<s> dont you know that you yourselves are gods temple and that gods spirit lives among you </s>
<s> if anyone destroys gods temple  god will destroy that person  for gods temple is sacred  and you together are that temple </s>
<s> do not deceive yourselves  if any of you think you are wise by the standards of this age  you should become  fools so that you may become wise </s>
<s> for the wisdom of this world is foolishness in gods sight  as it is written   he catches the wise in their craftiness </s>
<s> and again   the lord knows that the thoughts of the wise are futile  </s>
<s> so then  no more boasting about human leaders  all things are yours </s>
<s> whether paul or apollos or cephas or the world or life or death or the present or the future  all are yours </s>
<s> and you are of christ  and christ is of god </s>
<s> this  then  is how you ought to regard us  as servants of christ and as those entrusted with the mysteries god has revealed </s>
<s> now it is required that those who have been given a trust must prove faithful </s>
<s> i care very little if i am judged by you or by any human court  indeed  i do not even judge myself </s>
<s> my conscience is clear  but that does not make me innocent  it is the lord who judges me </s>
<s> therefore judge nothing before the appointed time  wait until the lord comes  he will bring to light what is hidden in darkness and will expose the motives of the heart  at that time each will receive their praise from god </s>
<s> now  brothers and sisters  i have applied these things to myself and apollos for your benefit  so that you may learn from us the meaning of the saying   do not go beyond what is written   then you will not be puffed up in being a follower of one of us over against the other </s>
<s> for who makes you different from anyone else  what do you have that you did not receive  and if you did receive it  why do you boast as though you did not </s>
<s> already you have all you want  already you have become rich  you have begun to reign  and that without us  how i wish that you really had begun to reign so that we also might reign with you </s>
<s> for it seems to me that god has put us apostles on display at the end of the procession  like those condemned to die in the arena  we have been made a spectacle to the whole universe  to angels as well as to human beings </s>
<s> we are fools for christ  but you are so wise in christ  we are weak  but you are strong  you are honoured  we are dishonoured </s>
<s> to this very hour we go hungry and thirsty  we are in rags  we are brutally treated  we are homeless </s>
<s> we work hard with our own hands  when we are cursed  we bless  when we are persecuted  we endure it </s>
<s> when we are slandered  we answer kindly  we have become the scum of the earth  the garbage of the world  right up to this moment </s>
<s> i am writing this not to shame you but to warn you as my dear children </s>
<s> even if you had ten thousand guardians in christ  you do not have many fathers  for in christ jesus i became your father through the gospel </s>
<s> therefore i urge you to imitate me </s>
<s> for this reason i have sent to you timothy  my son whom i love  who is faithful in the lord  he will remind you of my way of life in christ jesus  which agrees with what i teach everywhere in every church </s>
<s> some of you have become arrogant  as if i were not coming to you </s>
<s> but i will come to you very soon  if the lord is willing  and then i will find out not only how these arrogant people are talking  but what power they have </s>
<s> for the kingdom of god is not a matter of talk but of power </s>
<s> what do you prefer  shall i come to you with a rod of discipline  or shall i come in love and with a gentle spirit </s>
<s> it is actually reported that there is sexual immorality among you  and of a kind that even pagans do not tolerate  a man is sleeping with his fathers wife </s>
<s> and you are proud  shouldnt you rather have gone into mourning and have put out of your fellowship the man who has been doing this </s>
<s> for my part  even though i am not physically present  i am with you in spirit  as one who is present with you in this way  i have already passed judgment in the name of our lord jesus on the one who has been doing this </s>
<s> so when you are assembled and i am with you in spirit  and the power of our lord jesus is present </s>
<s> hand this man over to satan for the destruction of the flesh   so that his spirit may be saved on the day of the lord </s>
<s> your boasting is not good  dont you know that a little yeast leavens the whole batch of dough </s>
<s> get rid of the old yeast  so that you may be a new unleavened batch  as you really are  for christ  our passover lamb  has been sacrificed </s>
<s> therefore let us keep the festival  not with the old bread leavened with malice and wickedness  but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth </s>
<s> i wrote to you in my letter not to associate with sexually immoral people </s>
<s> not at all meaning the people of this world who are immoral  or the greedy and swindlers  or idolaters  in that case you would have to leave this world </s>
<s> but now i am writing to you that you must not associate with anyone who claims to be a brother or sister but is sexually immoral or greedy  an idolater or slanderer  a drunkard or swindler  do not even eat with such people </s>
<s> what business is it of mine to judge those outside the church  are you not to judge those inside </s>
<s> god will judge those outside   expel the wicked person from among you  </s>
<s> if any of you has a dispute with another  do you dare to take it before the ungodly for judgment instead of before the lords people </s>
<s> or do you not know that the lords people will judge the world  and if you are to judge the world  are you not competent to judge trivial cases </s>
<s> do you not know that we will judge angels  how much more the things of this life </s>
<s> therefore  if you have disputes about such matters  do you ask for a ruling from those whose way of life is scorned in the church </s>
<s> i say this to shame you  is it possible that there is nobody among you wise enough to judge a dispute between believers </s>
<s> but instead  one brother takes another to court  and this in front of unbelievers </s>
<s> the very fact that you have lawsuits among you means you have been completely defeated already  why not rather be wronged  why not rather be cheated </s>
<s> instead  you yourselves cheat and do wrong  and you do this to your brothers and sisters </s>
<s> or do you not know that wrongdoers will not inherit the kingdom of god  do not be deceived  neither the sexually immoral nor idolaters nor adulterers nor men who have sex with men</s>
<s> nor thieves nor the greedy nor drunkards nor slanderers nor swindlers will inherit the kingdom of god </s>
<s> and that is what some of you were  but you were washed  you were sanctified  you were justified in the name of the lord jesus christ and by the spirit of our god </s>
<s>  i have the right to do anything   you say  but not everything is beneficial   i have the right to do anything  but i will not be mastered by anything </s>
<s> you say   food for the stomach and the stomach for food  and god will destroy them both   the body  however  is not meant for sexual immorality but for the lord  and the lord for the body </s>
<s> by his power god raised the lord from the dead  and he will raise us also </s>
<s> do you not know that your bodies are members of christ himself  shall i then take the members of christ and unite them with a prostitute  never </s>
<s> do you not know that he who unites himself with a prostitute is one with her in body  for it is said   the two will become one flesh  </s>
<s> but whoever is united with the lord is one with him in spirit </s>
<s> flee from sexual immorality  all other sins a person commits are outside the body  but whoever sins sexually  sins against their own body </s>
<s> do you not know that your bodies are temples of the holy spirit  who is in you  whom you have received from god  you are not your own </s>
<s> you were bought at a price  therefore honour god with your bodies </s>
<s> now for the matters you wrote about   it is good for a man not to have sexual relations with a woman  </s>
<s> but since sexual immorality is occurring  each man should have sexual relations with his own wife  and each woman with her own husband </s>
<s> the husband should fulfil his marital duty to his wife  and likewise the wife to her husband </s>
<s> the wife does not have authority over her own body but yields it to her husband  in the same way  the husband does not have authority over his own body but yields it to his wife </s>
<s> do not deprive each other except perhaps by mutual consent and for a time  so that you may devote yourselves to prayer  then come together again so that satan will not tempt you because of your lack of selfcontrol </s>
<s> i say this as a concession  not as a command </s>
<s> i wish that all of you were as i am  but each of you has your own gift from god  one has this gift  another has that </s>
<s> now to the unmarried and the widows i say  it is good for them to stay unmarried  as i do </s>
<s> but if they cannot control themselves  they should marry  for it is better to marry than to burn with passion </s>
<s> to the married i give this command  not i  but the lord   a wife must not separate from her husband </s>
<s> but if she does  she must remain unmarried or else be reconciled to her husband  and a husband must not divorce his wife </s>
<s> to the rest i say this  i  not the lord   if any brother has a wife who is not a believer and she is willing to live with him  he must not divorce her </s>
<s> and if a woman has a husband who is not a believer and he is willing to live with her  she must not divorce him </s>
<s> for the unbelieving husband has been sanctified through his wife  and the unbelieving wife has been sanctified through her believing husband  otherwise your children would be unclean  but as it is  they are holy </s>
<s> but if the unbeliever leaves  let it be so  the brother or the sister is not bound in such circumstances  god has called us to live in peace </s>
<s> how do you know  wife  whether you will save your husband  or  how do you know  husband  whether you will save your wife </s>
<s> nevertheless  each person should live as a believer in whatever situation the lord has assigned to them  just as god has called them  this is the rule i lay down in all the churches </s>
<s> was a man already circumcised when he was called  he should not become uncircumcised  was a man uncircumcised when he was called  he should not be circumcised </s>
<s> circumcision is nothing and uncircumcision is nothing  keeping gods commands is what counts </s>
<s> each person should remain in the situation they were in when god called them </s>
<s> were you a slave when you were called  dont let it trouble you  although if you can gain your freedom  do so </s>
<s> for the one who was a slave when called to faith in the lord is the lords freed person  similarly  the one who was free when called is christs slave </s>
<s> you were bought at a price  do not become slaves of human beings </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  each person  as responsible to god  should remain in the situation they were in when god called them </s>
<s> now about virgins  i have no command from the lord  but i give a judgment as one who by the lords mercy is trustworthy </s>
<s> because of the present crisis  i think that it is good for a man to remain as he is </s>
<s> are you pledged to a woman  do not seek to be released  are you free from such a commitment  do not look for a wife </s>
<s> but if you do marry  you have not sinned  and if a virgin marries  she has not sinned  but those who marry will face many troubles in this life  and i want to spare you this </s>
<s> what i mean  brothers and sisters  is that the time is short  from now on those who have wives should live as if they do not </s>
<s> those who mourn  as if they did not  those who are happy  as if they were not  those who buy something  as if it were not theirs to keep </s>
<s> those who use the things of the world  as if not engrossed in them  for this world in its present form is passing away </s>
<s> i would like you to be free from concern  an unmarried man is concerned about the lords affairs  how he can please the lord </s>
<s> but a married man is concerned about the affairs of this world  how he can please his wife </s>
<s> and his interests are divided  an unmarried woman or virgin is concerned about the lords affairs  her aim is to be devoted to the lord in both body and spirit  but a married woman is concerned about the affairs of this world  how she can please her husband </s>
<s> i am saying this for your own good  not to restrict you  but that you may live in a right way in undivided devotion to the lord </s>
<s> if anyone is worried that he might not be acting honourably towards the virgin he is engaged to  and if his passions are too strong and he feels he ought to marry  he should do as he wants  he is not sinning  they should get married </s>
<s> but the man who has settled the matter in his own mind  who is under no compulsion but has control over his own will  and who has made up his mind not to marry the virgin  this man also does the right thing </s>
<s> so then  he who marries the virgin does right  but he who does not marry her does better </s>
<s> a woman is bound to her husband as long as he lives  but if her husband dies  she is free to marry anyone she wishes  but he must belong to the lord </s>
<s> in my judgment  she is happier if she stays as she is  and i think that i too have the spirit of god </s>
<s> now about food sacrificed to idols  we know that  we all possess knowledge   but knowledge puffs up while love builds up </s>
<s> those who think they know something do not yet know as they ought to know </s>
<s> but whoever loves god is known by god </s>
<s> so then  about eating food sacrificed to idols  we know that  an idol is nothing at all in the world and that  there is no god but one  </s>
<s> for even if there are socalled gods  whether in heaven or on earth  as indeed there are many  gods and many  lords  </s>
<s> yet for us there is but one god  the father  from whom all things came and for whom we live  and there is but one lord  jesus christ  through whom all things came and through whom we live </s>
<s> but not everyone possesses this knowledge  some people are still so accustomed to idols that when they eat sacrificial food they think of it as having been sacrificed to a god  and since their conscience is weak  it is defiled </s>
<s> but food does not bring us near to god  we are no worse if we do not eat  and no better if we do </s>
<s> be careful  however  that the exercise of your rights does not become a stumblingblock to the weak </s>
<s> for if someone with a weak conscience sees you  with all your knowledge  eating in an idols temple  wont that person be emboldened to eat what is sacrificed to idols </s>
<s> so this weak brother or sister  for whom christ died  is destroyed by your knowledge </s>
<s> when you sin against them in this way and wound their weak conscience  you sin against christ </s>
<s> therefore  if what i eat causes my brother or sister to fall into sin  i will never eat meat again  so that i will not cause them to fall </s>
<s> am i not free  am i not an apostle  have i not seen jesus our lord  are you not the result of my work in the lord </s>
<s> even though i may not be an apostle to others  surely i am to you  for you are the seal of my apostleship in the lord </s>
<s> this is my defence to those who sit in judgment on me </s>
<s> dont we have the right to food and drink </s>
<s> dont we have the right to take a believing wife along with us  as do the other apostles and the lords brothers and cephas </s>
<s> or is it only i and barnabas who lack the right to not work for a living </s>
<s> who serves as a soldier at his own expense  who plants a vineyard and does not eat its grapes  who tends a flock and does not drink the milk </s>
<s> do i say this merely on human authority  doesnt the law say the same thing </s>
<s> for it is written in the law of moses   do not muzzle an ox while it is treading out the grain   is it about oxen that god is concerned </s>
<s> surely he says this for us  doesnt he  yes  this was written for us  because whoever ploughs and threshes should be able to do so in the hope of sharing in the harvest </s>
<s> if we have sown spiritual seed among you  is it too much if we reap a material harvest from you </s>
<s> if others have this right of support from you  shouldnt we have it all the more  but we did not use this right  on the contrary  we put up with anything rather than hinder the gospel of christ </s>
<s> dont you know that those who serve in the temple get their food from the temple  and that those who serve at the altar share in what is offered on the altar </s>
<s> in the same way  the lord has commanded that those who preach the gospel should receive their living from the gospel </s>
<s> but i have not used any of these rights  and i am not writing this in the hope that you will do such things for me  for i would rather die than allow anyone to deprive me of this boast </s>
<s> for when i preach the gospel  i cannot boast  since i am compelled to preach  woe to me if i do not preach the gospel </s>
<s> if i preach voluntarily  i have a reward  if not voluntarily  i am simply discharging the trust committed to me </s>
<s> what then is my reward  just this  that in preaching the gospel i may offer it free of charge  and so not make full use of my rights as a preacher of the gospel </s>
<s> though i am free and belong to no one  i have made myself a slave to everyone  to win as many as possible </s>
<s> to the jews i became like a jew  to win the jews  to those under the law i became like one under the law  though i myself am not under the law   so as to win those under the law </s>
<s> to those not having the law i became like one not having the law  though i am not free from gods law but am under christs law   so as to win those not having the law </s>
<s> to the weak i became weak  to win the weak  i have become all things to all people so that by all possible means i might save some </s>
<s> i do all this for the sake of the gospel  that i may share in its blessings </s>
<s> do you not know that in a race all the runners run  but only one gets the prize  run in such a way as to get the prize </s>
<s> everyone who competes in the games goes into strict training  they do it to get a crown that will not last  but we do it to get a crown that will last for ever </s>
<s> therefore i do not run like someone running aimlessly  i do not fight like a boxer beating the air </s>
<s> no  i strike a blow to my body and make it my slave so that after i have preached to others  i myself will not be disqualified for the prize </s>
<s> for i do not want you to be ignorant of the fact  brothers and sisters  that our ancestors were all under the cloud and that they all passed through the sea </s>
<s> they were all baptised into moses in the cloud and in the sea </s>
<s> they all ate the same spiritual food</s>
<s> and drank the same spiritual drink  for they drank from the spiritual rock that accompanied them  and that rock was christ </s>
<s> nevertheless  god was not pleased with most of them  their bodies were scattered in the wilderness </s>
<s> now these things occurred as examples to keep us from setting our hearts on evil things as they did </s>
<s> do not be idolaters  as some of them were  as it is written   the people sat down to eat and drink and got up to indulge in revelry  </s>
<s> we should not commit sexual immorality  as some of them did  and in one day twentythree thousand of them died </s>
<s> we should not test christ  as some of them did  and were killed by snakes </s>
<s> and do not grumble  as some of them did  and were killed by the destroying angel </s>
<s> these things happened to them as examples and were written down as warnings for us  on whom the culmination of the ages has come </s>
<s> so  if you think you are standing firm  be careful that you dont fall </s>
<s> no temptation has overtaken you except what is common to mankind  and god is faithful  he will not let you be tempted beyond what you can bear  but when you are tempted  he will also provide a way out so that you can endure it </s>
<s> therefore  my dear friends  flee from idolatry </s>
<s> i speak to sensible people  judge for yourselves what i say </s>
<s> is not the cup of thanksgiving for which we give thanks a participation in the blood of christ  and is not the bread that we break a participation in the body of christ </s>
<s> because there is one loaf  we  who are many  are one body  for we all share the one loaf </s>
<s> consider the people of israel  do not those who eat the sacrifices participate in the altar </s>
<s> do i mean then that food sacrificed to an idol is anything  or that an idol is anything </s>
<s> no  but the sacrifices of pagans are offered to demons  not to god  and i do not want you to be participants with demons </s>
<s> you cannot drink the cup of the lord and the cup of demons too  you cannot have a part in both the lords table and the table of demons </s>
<s> are we trying to arouse the lords jealousy  are we stronger than he </s>
<s>  i have the right to do anything   you say  but not everything is beneficial   i have the right to do anything  but not everything is constructive </s>
<s> no one should seek their own good  but the good of others </s>
<s> eat anything sold in the meat market without raising questions of conscience </s>
<s> for   the earth is the lords  and everything in it  </s>
<s> if an unbeliever invites you to a meal and you want to go  eat whatever is put before you without raising questions of conscience </s>
<s> but if someone says to you   this has been offered in sacrifice   then do not eat it  both for the sake of the one who told you and for the sake of conscience </s>
<s> i am referring to the other persons conscience  not yours  for why is my freedom being judged by anothers conscience </s>
<s> if i take part in the meal with thankfulness  why am i denounced because of something i thank god for </s>
<s> so whether you eat or drink or whatever you do  do it all for the glory of god </s>
<s> do not cause anyone to stumble  whether jews  greeks or the church of god </s>
<s> even as i try to please everyone in every way  for i am not seeking my own good but the good of many  so that they may be saved </s>
<s> follow my example  as i follow the example of christ </s>
<s> i praise you for remembering me in everything and for holding to the traditions just as i passed them on to you </s>
<s> but i want you to realise that the head of every man is christ  and the head of the woman is man  and the head of christ is god </s>
<s> every man who prays or prophesies with his head covered dishonours his head </s>
<s> but every woman who prays or prophesies with her head uncovered dishonours her head  it is the same as having her head shaved </s>
<s> for if a woman does not cover her head  she might as well have her hair cut off  but if it is a disgrace for a woman to have her hair cut off or her head shaved  then she should cover her head </s>
<s> a man ought not to cover his head  since he is the image and glory of god  but woman is the glory of man </s>
<s> for man did not come from woman  but woman from man </s>
<s> neither was man created for woman  but woman for man </s>
<s> it is for this reason that a woman ought to have authority over her own head  because of the angels </s>
<s> nevertheless  in the lord woman is not independent of man  nor is man independent of woman </s>
<s> for as woman came from man  so also man is born of woman  but everything comes from god </s>
<s> judge for yourselves  is it proper for a woman to pray to god with her head uncovered </s>
<s> does not the very nature of things teach you that if a man has long hair  it is a disgrace to him </s>
<s> but that if a woman has long hair  it is her glory  for long hair is given to her as a covering </s>
<s> if anyone wants to be contentious about this  we have no other practice  nor do the churches of god </s>
