<s> in the following directives i have no praise for you  for your meetings do more harm than good </s>
<s> in the first place  i hear that when you come together as a church  there are divisions among you  and to some extent i believe it </s>
<s> no doubt there have to be differences among you to show which of you have gods approval </s>
<s> so then  when you come together  it is not the lords supper you eat </s>
<s> for when you are eating  some of you go ahead with your own private suppers  as a result  one person remains hungry and another gets drunk </s>
<s> dont you have homes to eat and drink in  or do you despise the church of god by humiliating those who have nothing  what shall i say to you  shall i praise you  certainly not in this matter </s>
<s> for i received from the lord what i also passed on to you  the lord jesus  on the night he was betrayed  took bread </s>
<s> and when he had given thanks  he broke it and said   this is my body  which is for you  do this in remembrance of me  </s>
<s> in the same way  after supper he took the cup  saying   this cup is the new covenant in my blood  do this  whenever you drink it  in remembrance of me  </s>
<s> for whenever you eat this bread and drink this cup  you proclaim the lords death until he comes </s>
<s> so then  whoever eats the bread or drinks the cup of the lord in an unworthy manner will be guilty of sinning against the body and blood of the lord </s>
<s> everyone ought to examine themselves before they eat of the bread and drink from the cup </s>
<s> for those who eat and drink without discerning the body of christ eat and drink judgment on themselves </s>
<s> that is why many among you are weak and ill  and a number of you have fallen asleep </s>
<s> but if we were more discerning with regard to ourselves  we would not come under such judgment </s>
<s> nevertheless  when we are judged in this way by the lord  we are being disciplined so that we will not be finally condemned with the world </s>
<s> so then  my brothers and sisters  when you gather to eat  you should all eat together </s>
<s> anyone who is hungry should eat something at home  so that when you meet together it may not result in judgment  and when i come i will give further instructions </s>
<s> now about the gifts of the spirit  brothers and sisters  i do not want you to be uninformed </s>
<s> you know that when you were pagans  somehow or other you were influenced and led astray to dumb idols </s>
<s> therefore i want you to know that no one who is speaking by the spirit of god says   jesus be cursed   and no one can say   jesus is lord   except by the holy spirit </s>
<s> there are different kinds of gifts  but the same spirit distributes them </s>
<s> there are different kinds of service  but the same lord </s>
<s> there are different kinds of working  but in all of them and in everyone it is the same god at work </s>
<s> now to each one the manifestation of the spirit is given for the common good </s>
<s> to one there is given through the spirit a message of wisdom  to another a message of knowledge by means of the same spirit </s>
<s> to another faith by the same spirit  to another gifts of healing by that one spirit </s>
<s> to another miraculous powers  to another prophecy  to another distinguishing between spirits  to another speaking in different kinds of tongues  and to still another the interpretation of tongues </s>
<s> all these are the work of one and the same spirit  and he distributes them to each one  just as he determines </s>
<s> just as a body  though one  has many parts  but all its many parts form one body  so it is with christ </s>
<s> for we were all baptised by one spirit so as to form one body  whether jews or gentiles  slave or free  and we were all given the one spirit to drink </s>
<s> and so the body is not made up of one part but of many </s>
<s> now if the foot should say   because i am not a hand  i do not belong to the body   it would not for that reason stop being part of the body </s>
<s> and if the ear should say   because i am not an eye  i do not belong to the body   it would not for that reason stop being part of the body </s>
<s> if the whole body were an eye  where would the sense of hearing be  if the whole body were an ear  where would the sense of smell be </s>
<s> but in fact god has placed the parts in the body  every one of them  just as he wanted them to be </s>
<s> if they were all one part  where would the body be </s>
<s> as it is  there are many parts  but one body </s>
<s> the eye cannot say to the hand   i dont need you   and the head cannot say to the feet   i dont need you  </s>
<s> on the contrary  those parts of the body that seem to be weaker are indispensable </s>
<s> and the parts that we think are less honourable we treat with special honour  and the parts that are unpresentable are treated with special modesty </s>
<s> while our presentable parts need no special treatment  but god has put the body together  giving greater honour to the parts that lacked it </s>
<s> so that there should be no division in the body  but that its parts should have equal concern for each other </s>
<s> if one part suffers  every part suffers with it  if one part is honoured  every part rejoices with it </s>
<s> now you are the body of christ  and each one of you is a part of it </s>
<s> and god has placed in the church first of all apostles  second prophets  third teachers  then miracles  then gifts of healing  of helping  of guidance  and of different kinds of tongues </s>
<s> are all apostles  are all prophets  are all teachers  do all work miracles </s>
<s> do all have gifts of healing  do all speak in tongues  do all interpret </s>
<s> now eagerly desire the greater gifts  and yet i will show you the most excellent way </s>
<s> if i speak in the tongues of men or of angels  but do not have love  i am only a resounding gong or a clanging cymbal </s>
<s> if i have the gift of prophecy and can fathom all mysteries and all knowledge  and if i have a faith that can move mountains  but do not have love  i am nothing </s>
<s> if i give all i possess to the poor and give over my body to hardship that i may boast  but do not have love  i gain nothing </s>
<s> love is patient  love is kind  it does not envy  it does not boast  it is not proud </s>
<s> it does not dishonour others  it is not selfseeking  it is not easily angered  it keeps no record of wrongs </s>
<s> love does not delight in evil but rejoices with the truth </s>
<s> it always protects  always trusts  always hopes  always perseveres </s>
<s> love never fails  but where there are prophecies  they will cease  where there are tongues  they will be stilled  where there is knowledge  it will pass away </s>
<s> for we know in part and we prophesy in part </s>
<s> but when completeness comes  what is in part disappears </s>
<s> when i was a child  i talked like a child  i thought like a child  i reasoned like a child  when i became a man  i put the ways of childhood behind me </s>
<s> for now we see only a reflection as in a mirror  then we shall see face to face  now i know in part  then i shall know fully  even as i am fully known </s>
<s> and now these three remain  faith  hope and love  but the greatest of these is love </s>
<s> follow the way of love and eagerly desire gifts of the spirit  especially prophecy </s>
<s> for anyone who speaks in a tongue does not speak to people but to god  indeed  no one understands them  they utter mysteries by the spirit </s>
<s> but the one who prophesies speaks to people for their strengthening  encouraging and comfort </s>
<s> anyone who speaks in a tongue edifies themselves  but the one who prophesies edifies the church </s>
<s> i would like every one of you to speak in tongues  but even more to prophesy  the one who prophesies is greater than the one who speaks in tongues  unless someone interprets  so that the church may be edified </s>
<s> now  brothers and sisters  if i come to you and speak in tongues  what good will i be to you  unless i bring you some revelation or knowledge or prophecy or word of instruction </s>
<s> even in the case of lifeless things that make sounds  such as the pipe or harp  how will anyone know what tune is being played unless there is a distinction in the notes </s>
<s> again  if the trumpet does not sound a clear call  who will get ready for battle </s>
<s> so it is with you  unless you speak intelligible words with your tongue  how will anyone know what you are saying  you will just be speaking into the air </s>
<s> undoubtedly there are all sorts of languages in the world  yet none of them is without meaning </s>
<s> if then i do not grasp the meaning of what someone is saying  i am a foreigner to the speaker  and the speaker is a foreigner to me </s>
<s> so it is with you  since you are eager for gifts of the spirit  try to excel in those that build up the church </s>
<s> for this reason the one who speaks in a tongue should pray that they may interpret what they say </s>
<s> for if i pray in a tongue  my spirit prays  but my mind is unfruitful </s>
<s> so what shall i do  i will pray with my spirit  but i will also pray with my understanding  i will sing with my spirit  but i will also sing with my understanding </s>
<s> otherwise when you are praising god in the spirit  how can someone else  who is now put in the position of an enquirer  say  amen to your thanksgiving  since they do not know what you are saying </s>
<s> you are giving thanks well enough  but no one else is edified </s>
<s> i thank god that i speak in tongues more than all of you </s>
<s> but in the church i would rather speak five intelligible words to instruct others than ten thousand words in a tongue </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  stop thinking like children  in regard to evil be infants  but in your thinking be adults </s>
<s> in the law it is written   with other tongues and through the lips of foreigners i will speak to this people  but even then they will not listen to me </s>
<s> tongues  then  are a sign  not for believers but for unbelievers  prophecy  however  is not for unbelievers but for believers </s>
<s> so if the whole church comes together and everyone speaks in tongues  and enquirers or unbelievers come in  will they not say that you are out of your mind </s>
<s> but if an unbeliever or an enquirer comes in while everyone is prophesying  they are convicted of sin and are brought under judgment by all </s>
<s> as the secrets of their hearts are laid bare  so they will fall down and worship god  exclaiming   god is really among you  </s>
<s> what then shall we say  brothers and sisters  when you come together  each of you has a hymn  or a word of instruction  a revelation  a tongue or an interpretation  everything must be done so that the church may be built up </s>
<s> if anyone speaks in a tongue  two  or at the most three  should speak  one at a time  and someone must interpret </s>
<s> if there is no interpreter  the speaker should keep quiet in the church and speak to himself and to god </s>
<s> two or three prophets should speak  and the others should weigh carefully what is said </s>
<s> and if a revelation comes to someone who is sitting down  the first speaker should stop </s>
<s> for you can all prophesy in turn so that everyone may be instructed and encouraged </s>
<s> the spirits of prophets are subject to the control of prophets </s>
<s> for god is not a god of disorder but of peace  as in all the congregations of the lords people </s>
<s> women should remain silent in the churches  they are not allowed to speak  but must be in submission  as the law says </s>
<s> if they want to enquire about something  they should ask their own husbands at home  for it is disgraceful for a woman to speak in the church </s>
<s> or did the word of god originate with you  or are you the only people it has reached </s>
<s> if anyone thinks they are a prophet or otherwise gifted by the spirit  let them acknowledge that what i am writing to you is the lords command </s>
<s> but if anyone ignores this  they will themselves be ignored </s>
<s> therefore  my brothers and sisters  be eager to prophesy  and do not forbid speaking in tongues </s>
<s> but everything should be done in a fitting and orderly way </s>
<s> now  brothers and sisters  i want to remind you of the gospel i preached to you  which you received and on which you have taken your stand </s>
<s> by this gospel you are saved  if you hold firmly to the word i preached to you  otherwise  you have believed in vain </s>
<s> for what i received i passed on to you as of first importance  that christ died for our sins according to the scriptures </s>
<s> that he was buried  that he was raised on the third day according to the scriptures </s>
<s> and that he appeared to cephas  and then to the twelve </s>
<s> after that  he appeared to more than five hundred of the brothers and sisters at the same time  most of whom are still living  though some have fallen asleep </s>
<s> then he appeared to james  then to all the apostles </s>
<s> and last of all he appeared to me also  as to one abnormally born </s>
<s> for i am the least of the apostles and do not even deserve to be called an apostle  because i persecuted the church of god </s>
<s> but by the grace of god i am what i am  and his grace to me was not without effect  no  i worked harder than all of them  yet not i  but the grace of god that was with me </s>
<s> whether  then  it is i or they  this is what we preach  and this is what you believed </s>
<s> but if it is preached that christ has been raised from the dead  how can some of you say that there is no resurrection of the dead </s>
<s> if there is no resurrection of the dead  then not even christ has been raised </s>
<s> and if christ has not been raised  our preaching is useless and so is your faith </s>
<s> more than that  we are then found to be false witnesses about god  for we have testified about god that he raised christ from the dead  but he did not raise him if in fact the dead are not raised </s>
<s> for if the dead are not raised  then christ has not been raised either </s>
<s> and if christ has not been raised  your faith is futile  you are still in your sins </s>
<s> then those also who have fallen asleep in christ are lost </s>
<s> if only for this life we have hope in christ  we are of all people most to be pitied </s>
<s> but christ has indeed been raised from the dead  the firstfruits of those who have fallen asleep </s>
<s> for since death came through a man  the resurrection of the dead comes also through a man </s>
<s> for as in adam all die  so in christ all will be made alive </s>
<s> but each in turn  christ  the firstfruits  then  when he comes  those who belong to him </s>
<s> then the end will come  when he hands over the kingdom to god the father after he has destroyed all dominion  authority and power </s>
<s> for he must reign until he has put all his enemies under his feet </s>
<s> the last enemy to be destroyed is death </s>
<s> for he  has put everything under his feet  now when it says that  everything has been put under him  it is clear that this does not include god himself  who put everything under christ </s>
<s> when he has done this  then the son himself will be made subject to him who put everything under him  so that god may be all in all </s>
<s> now if there is no resurrection  what will those do who are baptised for the dead  if the dead are not raised at all  why are people baptised for them </s>
<s> and as for us  why do we endanger ourselves every hour </s>
<s> i face death every day  yes  just as surely as i boast about you in christ jesus our lord </s>
<s> if i fought wild beasts in ephesus with no more than human hopes  what have i gained  if the dead are not raised   let us eat and drink  for tomorrow we die  </s>
<s> but someone will ask   how are the dead raised  with what kind of body will they come  </s>
<s> how foolish  what you sow does not come to life unless it dies </s>
<s> when you sow  you do not plant the body that will be  but just a seed  perhaps of wheat or of something else </s>
<s> but god gives it a body as he has determined  and to each kind of seed he gives its own body </s>
<s> not all flesh is the same  people have one kind of flesh  animals have another  birds another and fish another </s>
<s> there are also heavenly bodies and there are earthly bodies  but the splendour of the heavenly bodies is one kind  and the splendour of the earthly bodies is another </s>
<s> the sun has one kind of splendour  the moon another and the stars another  and star differs from star in splendour </s>
<s> so will it be with the resurrection of the dead  the body that is sown is perishable  it is raised imperishable </s>
<s> it is sown in dishonour  it is raised in glory  it is sown in weakness  it is raised in power </s>
<s> it is sown a natural body  it is raised a spiritual body  if there is a natural body  there is also a spiritual body </s>
<s> so it is written   the first man adam became a living being  the last adam  a lifegiving spirit </s>
<s> the spiritual did not come first  but the natural  and after that the spiritual </s>
<s> the first man was of the dust of the earth  the second man is of heaven </s>
<s> as was the earthly man  so are those who are of the earth  and as is the heavenly man  so also are those who are of heaven </s>
<s> and just as we have borne the image of the earthly man  so shall we bear the image of the heavenly man </s>
<s> i declare to you  brothers and sisters  that flesh and blood cannot inherit the kingdom of god  nor does the perishable inherit the imperishable </s>
<s> listen  i tell you a mystery  we will not all sleep  but we will all be changed </s>
<s> in a flash  in the twinkling of an eye  at the last trumpet  for the trumpet will sound  the dead will be raised imperishable  and we will be changed </s>
<s> for the perishable must clothe itself with the imperishable  and the mortal with immortality </s>
<s> when the perishable has been clothed with the imperishable  and the mortal with immortality  then the saying that is written will come true   death has been swallowed up in victory  </s>
<s>  where  o death  is your victory  where  o death  is your sting  </s>
<s> therefore  my dear brothers and sisters  stand firm  let nothing move you  always give yourselves fully to the work of the lord  because you know that your labour in the lord is not in vain </s>
<s> now about the collection for the lords people  do what i told the galatian churches to do </s>
<s> on the first day of every week  each one of you should set aside a sum of money in keeping with your income  saving it up  so that when i come no collections will have to be made </s>
<s> then  when i arrive  i will give letters of introduction to the men you approve and send them with your gift to jerusalem </s>
<s> if it seems advisable for me to go also  they will accompany me </s>
<s> after i go through macedonia  i will come to you  for i will be going through macedonia </s>
<s> perhaps i will stay with you for a while  or even spend the winter  so that you can help me on my journey  wherever i go </s>
<s> for i do not want to see you now and make only a passing visit  i hope to spend some time with you  if the lord permits </s>
<s> but i will stay on at ephesus until pentecost </s>
<s> because a great door for effective work has opened to me  and there are many who oppose me </s>
<s> when timothy comes  see to it that he has nothing to fear while he is with you  for he is carrying on the work of the lord  just as i am </s>
<s> no one  then  should treat him with contempt  send him on his way in peace so that he may return to me  i am expecting him along with the brothers </s>
<s> now about our brother apollos  i strongly urged him to go to you with the brothers  he was quite unwilling to go now  but he will go when he has the opportunity </s>
<s> be on your guard  stand firm in the faith  be courageous  be strong </s>
<s> do everything in love </s>
<s> you know that the household of stephanas were the first converts in achaia  and they have devoted themselves to the service of the lords people  i urge you  brothers and sisters </s>
<s> to submit to such people and to everyone who joins in the work and labours at it </s>
<s> i was glad when stephanas  fortunatus and achaicus arrived  because they have supplied what was lacking from you </s>
<s> for they refreshed my spirit and yours also  such men deserve recognition </s>
<s> the churches in the province of asia send you greetings  aquila and priscilla greet you warmly in the lord  and so does the church that meets at their house </s>
<s> all the brothers and sisters here send you greetings  greet one another with a holy kiss </s>
<s> i  paul  write this greeting in my own hand </s>
<s> if anyone does not love the lord  let that person be cursed  come  lord </s>
<s> the grace of the lord jesus be with you </s>
<s> my love to all of you in christ jesus  amen </s>
<s> paul  an apostle of christ jesus by the will of god  and timothy our brother  to the church of god in corinth  together with all his holy people throughout achaia </s>
<s> grace and peace to you from god our father and the lord jesus christ </s>
<s> praise be to the god and father of our lord jesus christ  the father of compassion and the god of all comfort </s>
<s> who comforts us in all our troubles  so that we can comfort those in any trouble with the comfort we ourselves receive from god </s>
<s> for just as we share abundantly in the sufferings of christ  so also our comfort abounds through christ </s>
<s> if we are distressed  it is for your comfort and salvation  if we are comforted  it is for your comfort  which produces in you patient endurance of the same sufferings we suffer </s>
<s> and our hope for you is firm  because we know that just as you share in our sufferings  so also you share in our comfort </s>
<s> we do not want you to be uninformed  brothers and sisters  about the troubles we experienced in the province of asia  we were under great pressure  far beyond our ability to endure  so that we despaired of life itself </s>
<s> indeed  we felt we had received the sentence of death  but this happened that we might not rely on ourselves but on god  who raises the dead </s>
<s> he has delivered us from such a deadly peril  and he will deliver us again  on him we have set our hope that he will continue to deliver us </s>
<s> as you help us by your prayers  then many will give thanks on our behalf for the gracious favour granted us in answer to the prayers of many </s>
<s> now this is our boast  our conscience testifies that we have conducted ourselves in the world  and especially in our relations with you  with integrity and godly sincerity  we have done so  relying not on worldly wisdom but on gods grace </s>
<s> for we do not write to you anything you cannot read or understand  and i hope that </s>
<s> as you have understood us in part  you will come to understand fully that you can boast of us just as we will boast of you in the day of the lord jesus </s>
<s> because i was confident of this  i wanted to visit you first so that you might benefit twice </s>
<s> i wanted to visit you on my way to macedonia and to come back to you from macedonia  and then to let you send me on my way to judea </s>
<s> was i fickle when i intended to do this  or do i make my plans in a worldly manner so that in the same breath i say both  yes  yes and  no  no </s>
<s> but as surely as god is faithful  our message to you is not  yes and  no </s>
<s> for the son of god  jesus christ  who was preached among you by us  by me  silas and timothy  was not  yes and  no  but in him it has always been  yes </s>
<s> for no matter how many promises god has made  they are  yes in christ  and so through him the  amen is spoken by us to the glory of god </s>
<s> now it is god who makes both us and you stand firm in christ  he anointed us </s>
<s> set his seal of ownership on us  and put his spirit in our hearts as a deposit  guaranteeing what is to come </s>
<s> i call god as my witness  and i stake my life on it  that it was in order to spare you that i did not return to corinth </s>
<s> not that we lord it over your faith  but we work with you for your joy  because it is by faith you stand firm </s>
<s> so i made up my mind that i would not make another painful visit to you </s>
<s> for if i grieve you  who is left to make me glad but you whom i have grieved </s>
<s> i wrote as i did  so that when i came i would not be distressed by those who should have made me rejoice  i had confidence in all of you  that you would all share my joy </s>
<s> for i wrote to you out of great distress and anguish of heart and with many tears  not to grieve you but to let you know the depth of my love for you </s>
<s> if anyone has caused grief  he has not so much grieved me as he has grieved all of you to some extent  not to put it too severely </s>
<s> the punishment inflicted on him by the majority is sufficient </s>
<s> now instead  you ought to forgive and comfort him  so that he will not be overwhelmed by excessive sorrow </s>
<s> i urge you  therefore  to reaffirm your love for him </s>
<s> another reason i wrote to you was to see if you would stand the test and be obedient in everything </s>
<s> anyone you forgive  i also forgive  and what i have forgiven  if there was anything to forgive  i have forgiven in the sight of christ for your sake </s>
<s> in order that satan might not outwit us  for we are not unaware of his schemes </s>
<s> now when i went to troas to preach the gospel of christ and found that the lord had opened a door for me </s>
<s> i still had no peace of mind  because i did not find my brother titus there  so i said goodbye to them and went on to macedonia </s>
<s> but thanks be to god  who always leads us as captives in christs triumphal procession and uses us to spread the aroma of the knowledge of him everywhere </s>
<s> for we are to god the pleasing aroma of christ among those who are being saved and those who are perishing </s>
<s> to the one we are an aroma that brings death  to the other  an aroma that brings life  and who is equal to such a task </s>
<s> unlike so many  we do not peddle the word of god for profit  on the contrary  in christ we speak before god with sincerity  as those sent from god </s>
<s> are we beginning to commend ourselves again  or do we need  like some people  letters of recommendation to you or from you </s>
<s> you yourselves are our letter  written on our hearts  known and read by everyone </s>
<s> you show that you are a letter from christ  the result of our ministry  written not with ink but with the spirit of the living god  not on tablets of stone but on tablets of human hearts </s>
<s> such confidence we have through christ before god </s>
<s> not that we are competent in ourselves to claim anything for ourselves  but our competence comes from god </s>
<s> he has made us competent as ministers of a new covenant  not of the letter but of the spirit  for the letter kills  but the spirit gives life </s>
<s> now if the ministry that brought death  which was engraved in letters on stone  came with glory  so that the israelites could not look steadily at the face of moses because of its glory  transitory though it was </s>
<s> will not the ministry of the spirit be even more glorious </s>
<s> if the ministry that brought condemnation was glorious  how much more glorious is the ministry that brings righteousness </s>
<s> for what was glorious has no glory now in comparison with the surpassing glory </s>
<s> and if what was transitory came with glory  how much greater is the glory of that which lasts </s>
<s> therefore  since we have such a hope  we are very bold </s>
<s> we are not like moses  who would put a veil over his face to prevent the israelites from seeing the end of what was passing away </s>
<s> but their minds were made dull  for to this day the same veil remains when the old covenant is read  it has not been removed  because only in christ is it taken away </s>
<s> even to this day when moses is read  a veil covers their hearts </s>
<s> but whenever anyone turns to the lord  the veil is taken away </s>
<s> now the lord is the spirit  and where the spirit of the lord is  there is freedom </s>
<s> and we all  who with unveiled faces contemplate the lords glory  are being transformed into his image with everincreasing glory  which comes from the lord  who is the spirit </s>
<s> therefore  since through gods mercy we have this ministry  we do not lose heart </s>
<s> rather  we have renounced secret and shameful ways  we do not use deception  nor do we distort the word of god  on the contrary  by setting forth the truth plainly we commend ourselves to everyones conscience in the sight of god </s>
<s> and even if our gospel is veiled  it is veiled to those who are perishing </s>
<s> the god of this age has blinded the minds of unbelievers  so that they cannot see the light of the gospel that displays the glory of christ  who is the image of god </s>
<s> for what we preach is not ourselves  but jesus christ as lord  and ourselves as your servants for jesus sake </s>
<s> for god  who said   let light shine out of darkness   made his light shine in our hearts to give us the light of the knowledge of gods glory displayed in the face of christ </s>
<s> but we have this treasure in jars of clay to show that this allsurpassing power is from god and not from us </s>
<s> we are hard pressed on every side  but not crushed  perplexed  but not in despair </s>
<s> persecuted  but not abandoned  struck down  but not destroyed </s>
<s> we always carry around in our body the death of jesus  so that the life of jesus may also be revealed in our body </s>
<s> for we who are alive are always being given over to death for jesus sake  so that his life may also be revealed in our mortal body </s>
<s> so then  death is at work in us  but life is at work in you </s>
<s> it is written   i believed  therefore i have spoken   since we have that same spirit of faith  we also believe and therefore speak </s>
<s> because we know that the one who raised the lord jesus from the dead will also raise us with jesus and present us with you to himself </s>
<s> all this is for your benefit  so that the grace that is reaching more and more people may cause thanksgiving to overflow to the glory of god </s>
<s> therefore we do not lose heart  though outwardly we are wasting away  yet inwardly we are being renewed day by day </s>
<s> for our light and momentary troubles are achieving for us an eternal glory that far outweighs them all </s>
<s> so we fix our eyes not on what is seen  but on what is unseen  since what is seen is temporary  but what is unseen is eternal </s>
<s> for we know that if the earthly tent we live in is destroyed  we have a building from god  an eternal house in heaven  not built by human hands </s>
<s> meanwhile we groan  longing to be clothed instead with our heavenly dwelling </s>
<s> because when we are clothed  we will not be found naked </s>
<s> for while we are in this tent  we groan and are burdened  because we do not wish to be unclothed but to be clothed instead with our heavenly dwelling  so that what is mortal may be swallowed up by life </s>
<s> now the one who has fashioned us for this very purpose is god  who has given us the spirit as a deposit  guaranteeing what is to come </s>
<s> therefore we are always confident and know that as long as we are at home in the body we are away from the lord </s>
<s> for we live by faith  not by sight </s>
<s> we are confident  i say  and would prefer to be away from the body and at home with the lord </s>
<s> so we make it our goal to please him  whether we are at home in the body or away from it </s>
<s> for we must all appear before the judgment seat of christ  so that each of us may receive what is due to us for the things done while in the body  whether good or bad </s>
<s> since  then  we know what it is to fear the lord  we try to persuade others  what we are is plain to god  and i hope it is also plain to your conscience </s>
<s> we are not trying to commend ourselves to you again  but are giving you an opportunity to take pride in us  so that you can answer those who take pride in what is seen rather than in what is in the heart </s>
<s> if we are  out of our mind   as some say  it is for god  if we are in our right mind  it is for you </s>
<s> for christs love compels us  because we are convinced that one died for all  and therefore all died </s>
<s> and he died for all  that those who live should no longer live for themselves but for him who died for them and was raised again </s>
<s> so from now on we regard no one from a worldly point of view  though we once regarded christ in this way  we do so no longer </s>
<s> therefore  if anyone is in christ  the new creation has come  the old has gone  the new is here </s>
<s> all this is from god  who reconciled us to himself through christ and gave us the ministry of reconciliation </s>
<s> that god was reconciling the world to himself in christ  not counting peoples sins against them  and he has committed to us the message of reconciliation </s>
<s> we are therefore christs ambassadors  as though god were making his appeal through us  we implore you on christs behalf  be reconciled to god </s>
<s> god made him who had no sin to be sin for us  so that in him we might become the righteousness of god </s>
<s> as gods fellow workers we urge you not to receive gods grace in vain </s>
<s> for he says   in the time of my favour i heard you  and in the day of salvation i helped you  </s>
<s> we put no stumblingblock in anyones path  so that our ministry will not be discredited </s>
<s> rather  as servants of god we commend ourselves in every way  in great endurance  in troubles  hardships and distresses </s>
<s> in beatings  imprisonments and riots  in hard work  sleepless nights and hunger </s>
<s> in purity  understanding  patience and kindness  in the holy spirit and in sincere love </s>
<s> in truthful speech and in the power of god  with weapons of righteousness in the right hand and in the left </s>
<s> through glory and dishonour  bad report and good report  genuine  yet regarded as impostors </s>
<s> known  yet regarded as unknown  dying  and yet we live on  beaten  and yet not killed </s>
<s> sorrowful  yet always rejoicing  poor  yet making many rich  having nothing  and yet possessing everything </s>
<s> we have spoken freely to you  corinthians  and opened wide our hearts to you </s>
<s> we are not withholding our affection from you  but you are withholding yours from us </s>
<s> as a fair exchange  i speak as to my children  open wide your hearts also </s>
<s> do not be yoked together with unbelievers  for what do righteousness and wickedness have in common  or what fellowship can light have with darkness </s>
<s> what harmony is there between christ and belial  or what does a believer have in common with an unbeliever </s>
<s> what agreement is there between the temple of god and idols  for we are the temple of the living god  as god has said   i will live with them and walk among them  and i will be their god  and they will be my people    come out from them and be separate  touch no unclean thing  and i will receive you    i will be a father to you  and you will be my sons and daughters </s>
<s> therefore  since we have these promises  dear friends  let us purify ourselves from everything that contaminates body and spirit  perfecting holiness out of reverence for god </s>
<s> make room for us in your hearts  we have wronged no one  we have corrupted no one  we have exploited no one </s>
<s> i do not say this to condemn you  i have said before that you have such a place in our hearts that we would live or die with you </s>
<s> i have spoken to you with great frankness  i take great pride in you  i am greatly encouraged  in all our troubles my joy knows no bounds </s>
<s> for when we came into macedonia  we had no rest  but we were harassed at every turn  conflicts on the outside  fears within </s>
<s> but god  who comforts the downcast  comforted us by the coming of titus </s>
<s> and not only by his coming but also by the comfort you had given him  he told us about your longing for me  your deep sorrow  your ardent concern for me  so that my joy was greater than ever </s>
<s> even if i caused you sorrow by my letter  i do not regret it  though i did regret it  i see that my letter hurt you  but only for a little while </s>
<s> yet now i am happy  not because you were made sorry  but because your sorrow led you to repentance  for you became sorrowful as god intended and so were not harmed in any way by us </s>
<s> godly sorrow brings repentance that leads to salvation and leaves no regret  but worldly sorrow brings death </s>
<s> see what this godly sorrow has produced in you  what earnestness  what eagerness to clear yourselves  what indignation  what alarm  what longing  what concern  what readiness to see justice done  at every point you have proved yourselves to be innocent in this matter </s>
<s> so even though i wrote to you  it was neither on account of the one who did the wrong nor on account of the injured party  but rather that before god you could see for yourselves how devoted to us you are </s>
<s> by all this we are encouraged  in addition to our own encouragement  we were especially delighted to see how happy titus was  because his spirit has been refreshed by all of you </s>
<s> i had boasted to him about you  and you have not embarrassed me  but just as everything we said to you was true  so our boasting about you to titus has proved to be true as well </s>
<s> and his affection for you is all the greater when he remembers that you were all obedient  receiving him with fear and trembling </s>
<s> i am glad i can have complete confidence in you </s>
<s> and now  brothers and sisters  we want you to know about the grace that god has given the macedonian churches </s>
<s> in the midst of a very severe trial  their overflowing joy and their extreme poverty welled up in rich generosity </s>
<s> for i testify that they gave as much as they were able  and even beyond their ability  entirely on their own </s>
<s> they urgently pleaded with us for the privilege of sharing in this service to the lords people </s>
<s> and they exceeded our expectations  they gave themselves first of all to the lord  and then by the will of god also to us </s>
<s> so we urged titus  just as he had earlier made a beginning  to bring also to completion this act of grace on your part </s>
<s> but since you excel in everything  in faith  in speech  in knowledge  in complete earnestness and in the love we have kindled in you  see that you also excel in this grace of giving </s>
<s> i am not commanding you  but i want to test the sincerity of your love by comparing it with the earnestness of others </s>
<s> for you know the grace of our lord jesus christ  that though he was rich  yet for your sake he became poor  so that you through his poverty might become rich </s>
<s> and here is my judgment about what is best for you in this matter  last year you were the first not only to give but also to have the desire to do so </s>
<s> now finish the work  so that your eager willingness to do it may be matched by your completion of it  according to your means </s>
<s> for if the willingness is there  the gift is acceptable according to what one has  not according to what one does not have </s>
<s> our desire is not that others might be relieved while you are hard pressed  but that there might be equality </s>
<s> at the present time your plenty will supply what they need  so that in turn their plenty will supply what you need  the goal is equality </s>
<s> as it is written   the one who gathered much did not have too much  and the one who gathered little did not have too little  </s>
<s> thanks be to god  who put into the heart of titus the same concern i have for you </s>
<s> for titus not only welcomed our appeal  but he is coming to you with much enthusiasm and on his own initiative </s>
<s> and we are sending along with him the brother who is praised by all the churches for his service to the gospel </s>
<s> what is more  he was chosen by the churches to accompany us as we carry the offering  which we administer in order to honour the lord himself and to show our eagerness to help </s>
<s> we want to avoid any criticism of the way we administer this liberal gift </s>
<s> for we are taking pains to do what is right  not only in the eyes of the lord but also in the eyes of man </s>
<s> in addition  we are sending with them our brother who has often proved to us in many ways that he is zealous  and now even more so because of his great confidence in you </s>
<s> as for titus  he is my partner and fellow worker among you  as for our brothers  they are representatives of the churches and an honour to christ </s>
<s> therefore show these men the proof of your love and the reason for our pride in you  so that the churches can see it </s>
<s> there is no need for me to write to you about this service to the lords people </s>
<s> for i know your eagerness to help  and i have been boasting about it to the macedonians  telling them that since last year you in achaia were ready to give  and your enthusiasm has stirred most of them to action </s>
<s> but i am sending the brothers in order that our boasting about you in this matter should not prove hollow  but that you may be ready  as i said you would be </s>
<s> for if any macedonians come with me and find you unprepared  we  not to say anything about you  would be ashamed of having been so confident </s>
<s> so i thought it necessary to urge the brothers to visit you in advance and finish the arrangements for the generous gift you had promised  then it will be ready as a generous gift  not as one grudgingly given </s>
<s> remember this  whoever sows sparingly will also reap sparingly  and whoever sows generously will also reap generously </s>
<s> each of you should give what you have decided in your heart to give  not reluctantly or under compulsion  for god loves a cheerful giver </s>
<s> and god is able to bless you abundantly  so that in all things at all times  having all that you need  you will abound in every good work </s>
<s> as it is written   they have freely scattered their gifts to the poor  their righteousness endures for ever  </s>
<s> this service that you perform is not only supplying the needs of the lords people but is also overflowing in many expressions of thanks to god </s>
<s> because of the service by which you have proved yourselves  others will praise god for the obedience that accompanies your confession of the gospel of christ  and for your generosity in sharing with them and with everyone else </s>
<s> and in their prayers for you their hearts will go out to you  because of the surpassing grace god has given you </s>
<s> thanks be to god for his indescribable gift </s>
<s> by the humility and gentleness of christ  i appeal to you  i  paul  who am  timid when face to face with you  but  bold towards you when away </s>
<s> i beg you that when i come i may not have to be as bold as i expect to be towards some people who think that we live by the standards of this world </s>
<s> for though we live in the world  we do not wage war as the world does </s>
<s> the weapons we fight with are not the weapons of the world  on the contrary  they have divine power to demolish strongholds </s>
<s> we demolish arguments and every pretension that sets itself up against the knowledge of god  and we take captive every thought to make it obedient to christ </s>
<s> and we will be ready to punish every act of disobedience  once your obedience is complete </s>
<s> you are judging by appearances  if anyone is confident that they belong to christ  they should consider again that we belong to christ just as much as they do </s>
<s> so even if i boast somewhat freely about the authority the lord gave us for building you up rather than tearing you down  i will not be ashamed of it </s>
<s> i do not want to seem to be trying to frighten you with my letters </s>
<s> for some say   his letters are weighty and forceful  but in person he is unimpressive and his speaking amounts to nothing  </s>
<s> such people should realise that what we are in our letters when we are absent  we will be in our actions when we are present </s>
<s> we do not dare to classify or compare ourselves with some who commend themselves  when they measure themselves by themselves and compare themselves with themselves  they are not wise </s>
<s> we  however  will not boast beyond proper limits  but will confine our boasting to the sphere of service god himself has assigned to us  a sphere that also includes you </s>
<s> we are not going too far in our boasting  as would be the case if we had not come to you  for we did get as far as you with the gospel of christ </s>
<s> neither do we go beyond our limits by boasting of work done by others  our hope is that  as your faith continues to grow  our sphere of activity among you will greatly expand </s>
<s> so that we can preach the gospel in the regions beyond you  for we do not want to boast about work already done in someone elses territory </s>
<s> but   let the one who boasts boast in the lord  </s>
<s> for it is not the one who commends himself who is approved  but the one whom the lord commends </s>
<s> i hope you will put up with me in a little foolishness  yes  please put up with me </s>
<s> i am jealous for you with a godly jealousy  i promised you to one husband  to christ  so that i might present you as a pure virgin to him </s>
<s> but i am afraid that just as eve was deceived by the snakes cunning  your minds may somehow be led astray from your sincere and pure devotion to christ </s>
<s> for if someone comes to you and preaches a jesus other than the jesus we preached  or if you receive a different spirit from the spirit you received  or a different gospel from the one you accepted  you put up with it easily enough </s>
<s> i do not think i am in the least inferior to those  superapostles </s>
<s> i may indeed be untrained as a speaker  but i do have knowledge  we have made this perfectly clear to you in every way </s>
<s> was it a sin for me to lower myself in order to elevate you by preaching the gospel of god to you free of charge </s>
<s> i robbed other churches by receiving support from them so as to serve you </s>
<s> and when i was with you and needed something  i was not a burden to anyone  for the brothers who came from macedonia supplied what i needed  i have kept myself from being a burden to you in any way  and will continue to do so </s>
<s> as surely as the truth of christ is in me  nobody in the regions of achaia will stop this boasting of mine </s>
<s> why  because i do not love you  god knows i do </s>
<s> and i will keep on doing what i am doing in order to cut the ground from under those who want an opportunity to be considered equal with us in the things they boast about </s>
<s> for such people are false apostles  deceitful workers  masquerading as apostles of christ </s>
<s> and no wonder  for satan himself masquerades as an angel of light </s>
<s> it is not surprising  then  if his servants also masquerade as servants of righteousness  their end will be what their actions deserve </s>
<s> i repeat  let no one take me for a fool  but if you do  then tolerate me just as you would a fool  so that i may do a little boasting </s>
<s> in this selfconfident boasting i am not talking as the lord would  but as a fool </s>
<s> since many are boasting in the way the world does  i too will boast </s>
<s> you gladly put up with fools since you are so wise </s>
<s> in fact  you even put up with anyone who enslaves you or exploits you or takes advantage of you or puts on airs or slaps you in the face </s>
<s> to my shame i admit that we were too weak for that  whatever anyone else dares to boast about  i am speaking as a fool  i also dare to boast about </s>
<s> are they hebrews  so am i  are they israelites  so am i  are they abrahams descendants  so am i </s>
<s> are they servants of christ   i am out of my mind to talk like this   i am more  i have worked much harder  been in prison more frequently  been flogged more severely  and been exposed to death again and again </s>
<s> five times i received from the jews the forty lashes minus one </s>
<s> three times i was beaten with rods  once i was pelted with stones  three times i was shipwrecked  i spent a night and a day in the open sea </s>
<s> i have been constantly on the move  i have been in danger from rivers  in danger from bandits  in danger from my fellow jews  in danger from gentiles  in danger in the city  in danger in the country  in danger at sea  and in danger from false believers </s>
<s> i have laboured and toiled and have often gone without sleep  i have known hunger and thirst and have often gone without food  i have been cold and naked </s>
<s> besides everything else  i face daily the pressure of my concern for all the churches </s>
<s> who is weak  and i do not feel weak  who is led into sin  and i do not inwardly burn </s>
<s> if i must boast  i will boast of the things that show my weakness </s>
<s> the god and father of the lord jesus  who is to be praised for ever  knows that i am not lying </s>
<s> in damascus the governor under king aretas had the city of the damascenes guarded in order to arrest me </s>
<s> but i was lowered in a basket from a window in the wall and slipped through his hands </s>
<s> i must go on boasting  although there is nothing to be gained  i will go on to visions and revelations from the lord </s>
<s> i know a man in christ who fourteen years ago was caught up to the third heaven  whether it was in the body or out of the body i do not know  god knows </s>
<s> and i know that this man  whether in the body or apart from the body i do not know  but god knows </s>
<s> was caught up to paradise and heard inexpressible things  things that no one is permitted to tell </s>
<s> i will boast about a man like that  but i will not boast about myself  except about my weaknesses </s>
<s> even if i should choose to boast  i would not be a fool  because i would be speaking the truth  but i refrain  so no one will think more of me than is warranted by what i do or say </s>
<s> or because of these surpassingly great revelations  therefore  in order to keep me from becoming conceited  i was given a thorn in my flesh  a messenger of satan  to torment me </s>
<s> three times i pleaded with the lord to take it away from me </s>
<s> but he said to me   my grace is sufficient for you  for my power is made perfect in weakness   therefore i will boast all the more gladly about my weaknesses  so that christs power may rest on me </s>
<s> that is why  for christs sake  i delight in weaknesses  in insults  in hardships  in persecutions  in difficulties  for when i am weak  then i am strong </s>
<s> i have made a fool of myself  but you drove me to it  i ought to have been commended by you  for i am not in the least inferior to the  superapostles  even though i am nothing </s>
<s> i persevered in demonstrating among you the marks of a true apostle  including signs  wonders and miracles </s>
<s> how were you inferior to the other churches  except that i was never a burden to you  forgive me this wrong </s>
<s> now i am ready to visit you for the third time  and i will not be a burden to you  because what i want is not your possessions but you  after all  children should not have to save up for their parents  but parents for their children </s>
<s> so i will very gladly spend for you everything i have and expend myself as well  if i love you more  will you love me less </s>
<s> be that as it may  i have not been a burden to you  yet  crafty fellow that i am  i caught you by trickery </s>
<s> did i exploit you through any of the men i sent to you </s>
<s> i urged titus to go to you and i sent our brother with him  titus did not exploit you  did he  did we not walk in the same footsteps by the same spirit </s>
<s> have you been thinking all along that we have been defending ourselves to you  we have been speaking in the sight of god as those in christ  and everything we do  dear friends  is for your strengthening </s>
<s> for i am afraid that when i come i may not find you as i want you to be  and you may not find me as you want me to be  i fear that there may be discord  jealousy  fits of rage  selfish ambition  slander  gossip  arrogance and disorder </s>
<s> i am afraid that when i come again my god will humble me before you  and i will be grieved over many who have sinned earlier and have not repented of the impurity  sexual sin and debauchery in which they have indulged </s>
<s> this will be my third visit to you   every matter must be established by the testimony of two or three witnesses  </s>
<s> i already gave you a warning when i was with you the second time  i now repeat it while absent  on my return i will not spare those who sinned earlier or any of the others </s>
<s> since you are demanding proof that christ is speaking through me  he is not weak in dealing with you  but is powerful among you </s>
<s> for to be sure  he was crucified in weakness  yet he lives by gods power  likewise  we are weak in him  yet by gods power we will live with him in our dealing with you </s>
<s> examine yourselves to see whether you are in the faith  test yourselves  do you not realise that christ jesus is in you  unless  of course  you fail the test </s>
<s> and i trust that you will discover that we have not failed the test </s>
<s> now we pray to god that you will not do anything wrong  not so that people will see that we have stood the test but so that you will do what is right even though we may seem to have failed </s>
<s> for we cannot do anything against the truth  but only for the truth </s>
<s> we are glad whenever we are weak but you are strong  and our prayer is that you may be fully restored </s>
<s> this is why i write these things when i am absent  that when i come i may not have to be harsh in my use of authority  the authority the lord gave me for building you up  not for tearing you down </s>
<s> finally  brothers and sisters  rejoice  strive for full restoration  encourage one another  be of one mind  live in peace  and the god of love and peace will be with you </s>
<s> greet one another with a holy kiss </s>
<s> all gods people here send their greetings </s>
<s> may the grace of the lord jesus christ  and the love of god  and the fellowship of the holy spirit be with you all </s>
<s> paul  an apostle  sent not from men nor by a man  but by jesus christ and god the father  who raised him from the dead </s>
<s> and all the brothers and sisters with me  to the churches in galatia </s>
<s> grace and peace to you from god our father and the lord jesus christ </s>
<s> who gave himself for our sins to rescue us from the present evil age  according to the will of our god and father </s>
<s> to whom be glory for ever and ever  amen </s>
<s> i am astonished that you are so quickly deserting the one who called you to live in the grace of christ and are turning to a different gospel </s>
<s> which is really no gospel at all  evidently some people are throwing you into confusion and are trying to pervert the gospel of christ </s>
<s> but even if we or an angel from heaven should preach a gospel other than the one we preached to you  let them be under gods curse </s>
<s> as we have already said  so now i say again  if anybody is preaching to you a gospel other than what you accepted  let them be under gods curse </s>
<s> am i now trying to win the approval of human beings  or of god  or am i trying to please people  if i were still trying to please people  i would not be a servant of christ </s>
<s> i want you to know  brothers and sisters  that the gospel i preached is not of human origin </s>
<s> i did not receive it from any man  nor was i taught it  rather  i received it by revelation from jesus christ </s>
<s> for you have heard of my previous way of life in judaism  how intensely i persecuted the church of god and tried to destroy it </s>
<s> i was advancing in judaism beyond many of my own age among my people and was extremely zealous for the traditions of my fathers </s>
<s> but when god  who set me apart from my mothers womb and called me by his grace  was pleased</s>
<s> to reveal his son in me so that i might preach him among the gentiles  my immediate response was not to consult any human being </s>
<s> i did not go up to jerusalem to see those who were apostles before i was  but i went into arabia  later i returned to damascus </s>
<s> then after three years  i went up to jerusalem to get acquainted with cephas and stayed with him fifteen days </s>
<s> i saw none of the other apostles  only james  the lords brother </s>
<s> i assure you before god that what i am writing to you is no lie </s>
<s> then i went to syria and cilicia </s>
<s> i was personally unknown to the churches of judea that are in christ </s>
<s> they only heard the report   the man who formerly persecuted us is now preaching the faith he once tried to destroy  </s>
<s> and they praised god because of me </s>
<s> then after fourteen years  i went up again to jerusalem  this time with barnabas  i took titus along also </s>
<s> i went in response to a revelation and  meeting privately with those esteemed as leaders  i presented to them the gospel that i preach among the gentiles  i wanted to be sure i was not running and had not been running my race in vain </s>
<s> yet not even titus  who was with me  was compelled to be circumcised  even though he was a greek </s>
<s> this matter arose because some false believers had infiltrated our ranks to spy on the freedom we have in christ jesus and to make us slaves </s>
<s> we did not give in to them for a moment  so that the truth of the gospel might be preserved for you </s>
<s> as for those who were held in high esteem  whatever they were makes no difference to me  god does not show favouritism  they added nothing to my message </s>
<s> on the contrary  they recognised that i had been entrusted with the task of preaching the gospel to the uncircumcised  just as peter had been to the circumcised </s>
<s> for god  who was at work in peter as an apostle to the circumcised  was also at work in me as an apostle to the gentiles </s>
<s> james  cephas and john  those esteemed as pillars  gave me and barnabas the right hand of fellowship when they recognised the grace given to me  they agreed that we should go to the gentiles  and they to the circumcised </s>
<s> all they asked was that we should continue to remember the poor  the very thing i had been eager to do all along </s>
<s> when cephas came to antioch  i opposed him to his face  because he stood condemned </s>
<s> for before certain men came from james  he used to eat with the gentiles  but when they arrived  he began to draw back and separate himself from the gentiles because he was afraid of those who belonged to the circumcision group </s>
<s> the other jews joined him in his hypocrisy  so that by their hypocrisy even barnabas was led astray </s>
<s> when i saw that they were not acting in line with the truth of the gospel  i said to cephas in front of them all   you are a jew  yet you live like a gentile and not like a jew  how is it  then  that you force gentiles to follow jewish customs </s>
<s>  we who are jews by birth and not sinful gentiles</s>
<s> know that a person is not justified by the works of the law  but by faith in jesus christ  so we  too  have put our faith in christ jesus that we may be justified by faith in christ and not by the works of the law  because by the works of the law no one will be justified </s>
<s>  but if  in seeking to be justified in christ  we jews find ourselves also among the sinners  doesnt that mean that christ promotes sin  absolutely not </s>
<s> if i rebuild what i destroyed  then i really would be a lawbreaker </s>
<s>  for through the law i died to the law so that i might live for god </s>
<s> i have been crucified with christ and i no longer live  but christ lives in me  the life i now live in the body  i live by faith in the son of god  who loved me and gave himself for me </s>
<s> i do not set aside the grace of god  for if righteousness could be gained through the law  christ died for nothing  </s>
<s> you foolish galatians  who has bewitched you  before your very eyes jesus christ was clearly portrayed as crucified </s>
<s> i would like to learn just one thing from you  did you receive the spirit by the works of the law  or by believing what you heard </s>
<s> are you so foolish  after beginning by means of the spirit  are you now trying to finish by means of the flesh </s>
<s> have you experienced so much in vain  if it really was in vain </s>
<s> so again i ask  does god give you his spirit and work miracles among you by the works of the law  or by your believing what you heard </s>
<s> so also abraham  believed god  and it was credited to him as righteousness  </s>
<s> understand  then  that those who have faith are children of abraham </s>
<s> scripture foresaw that god would justify the gentiles by faith  and announced the gospel in advance to abraham   all nations will be blessed through you  </s>
<s> so those who rely on faith are blessed along with abraham  the man of faith </s>
<s> for all who rely on the works of the law are under a curse  as it is written   cursed is everyone who does not continue to do everything written in the book of the law  </s>
<s> clearly no one who relies on the law is justified before god  because  the righteous will live by faith  </s>
<s> the law is not based on faith  on the contrary  it says   the person who does these things will live by them  </s>
<s> christ redeemed us from the curse of the law by becoming a curse for us  for it is written   cursed is everyone who is hung on a pole  </s>
<s> he redeemed us in order that the blessing given to abraham might come to the gentiles through christ jesus  so that by faith we might receive the promise of the spirit </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  let me take an example from everyday life  just as no one can set aside or add to a human covenant that has been duly established  so it is in this case </s>
<s> the promises were spoken to abraham and to his seed  scripture does not say  and to seeds  meaning many people  but  and to your seed  meaning one person  who is christ </s>
<s> what i mean is this  the law  introduced 430 years later  does not set aside the covenant previously established by god and thus do away with the promise </s>
<s> for if the inheritance depends on the law  then it no longer depends on the promise  but god in his grace gave it to abraham through a promise </s>
<s> why  then  was the law given at all  it was added because of transgressions until the seed to whom the promise referred had come  the law was given through angels and entrusted to a mediator </s>
<s> a mediator  however  implies more than one party  but god is one </s>
<s> is the law  therefore  opposed to the promises of god  absolutely not  for if a law had been given that could impart life  then righteousness would certainly have come by the law </s>
<s> but scripture has locked up everything under the control of sin  so that what was promised  being given through faith in jesus christ  might be given to those who believe </s>
<s> before the coming of this faith  we were held in custody under the law  locked up until the faith that was to come would be revealed </s>
<s> so the law was our guardian until christ came that we might be justified by faith </s>
<s> now that this faith has come  we are no longer under a guardian </s>
<s> so in christ jesus you are all children of god through faith </s>
<s> for all of you who were baptised into christ have clothed yourselves with christ </s>
<s> there is neither jew nor gentile  neither slave nor free  nor is there male and female  for you are all one in christ jesus </s>
<s> if you belong to christ  then you are abrahams seed  and heirs according to the promise </s>
<s> what i am saying is that as long as an heir is under age  he is no different from a slave  although he owns the whole estate </s>
<s> the heir is subject to guardians and trustees until the time set by his father </s>
<s> so also  when we were under age  we were in slavery under the elemental spiritual forces of the world </s>
<s> but when the set time had fully come  god sent his son  born of a woman  born under the law </s>
<s> to redeem those under the law  that we might receive adoption to sonship </s>
<s> because you are his sons  god sent the spirit of his son into our hearts  the spirit who calls out   abba  father  </s>
<s> so you are no longer a slave  but gods child  and since you are his child  god has made you also an heir </s>
<s> formerly  when you did not know god  you were slaves to those who by nature are not gods </s>
<s> but now that you know god  or rather are known by god  how is it that you are turning back to those weak and miserable forces  do you wish to be enslaved by them all over again </s>
<s> you are observing special days and months and seasons and years </s>
<s> i fear for you  that somehow i have wasted my efforts on you </s>
<s> i plead with you  brothers and sisters  become like me  for i became like you  you did me no wrong </s>
<s> as you know  it was because of an illness that i first preached the gospel to you </s>
<s> and even though my illness was a trial to you  you did not treat me with contempt or scorn  instead  you welcomed me as if i were an angel of god  as if i were christ jesus himself </s>
<s> where  then  is your blessing of me now  i can testify that  if you could have done so  you would have torn out your eyes and given them to me </s>
<s> have i now become your enemy by telling you the truth </s>
<s> those people are zealous to win you over  but for no good  what they want is to alienate you from us  so that you may have zeal for them </s>
<s> it is fine to be zealous  provided the purpose is good  and to be so always  not just when i am with you </s>
<s> my dear children  for whom i am again in the pains of childbirth until christ is formed in you </s>
<s> how i wish i could be with you now and change my tone  because i am perplexed about you </s>
<s> tell me  you who want to be under the law  are you not aware of what the law says </s>
<s> for it is written that abraham had two sons  one by the slave woman and the other by the free woman </s>
<s> his son by the slave woman was born according to the flesh  but his son by the free woman was born as the result of a divine promise </s>
<s> these things are being taken figuratively  the women represent two covenants  one covenant is from mount sinai and bears children who are to be slaves  this is hagar </s>
<s> now hagar stands for mount sinai in arabia and corresponds to the present city of jerusalem  because she is in slavery with her children </s>
<s> but the jerusalem that is above is free  and she is our mother </s>
<s> for it is written   be glad  barren woman  you who never bore a child  break forth and cry aloud  you who were never in labour  because more are the children of the desolate woman than of her who has a husband  </s>
<s> now you  brothers and sisters  like isaac  are children of promise </s>
<s> at that time the son born according to the flesh persecuted the son born by the power of the spirit  it is the same now </s>
<s> but what does scripture say   get rid of the slave woman and her son  for the slave womans son will never share in the inheritance with the free womans son  </s>
<s> therefore  brothers and sisters  we are not children of the slave woman  but of the free woman </s>
<s> it is for freedom that christ has set us free  stand firm  then  and do not let yourselves be burdened again by a yoke of slavery </s>
<s> mark my words  i  paul  tell you that if you let yourselves be circumcised  christ will be of no value to you at all </s>
<s> again i declare to every man who lets himself be circumcised that he is required to obey the whole law </s>
<s> you who are trying to be justified by the law have been alienated from christ  you have fallen away from grace </s>
<s> for through the spirit we eagerly await by faith the righteousness for which we hope </s>
<s> for in christ jesus neither circumcision nor uncircumcision has any value  the only thing that counts is faith expressing itself through love </s>
<s> you were running a good race  who cut in on you to keep you from obeying the truth </s>
<s> that kind of persuasion does not come from the one who calls you </s>
<s>  a little yeast works through the whole batch of dough  </s>
<s> i am confident in the lord that you will take no other view  the one who is throwing you into confusion  whoever that may be  will have to pay the penalty </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  if i am still preaching circumcision  why am i still being persecuted  in that case the offence of the cross has been abolished </s>
<s> as for those agitators  i wish they would go the whole way and emasculate themselves </s>
<s> you  my brothers and sisters  were called to be free  but do not use your freedom to indulge the flesh  rather  serve one another humbly in love </s>
<s> for the entire law is fulfilled in keeping this one command   love your neighbour as yourself  </s>
<s> if you bite and devour each other  watch out or you will be destroyed by each other </s>
<s> so i say  live by the spirit  and you will not gratify the desires of the flesh </s>
<s> for the flesh desires what is contrary to the spirit  and the spirit what is contrary to the flesh  they are in conflict with each other  so that you are not to do whatever you want </s>
<s> but if you are led by the spirit  you are not under the law </s>
<s> the acts of the flesh are obvious  sexual immorality  impurity and debauchery </s>
<s> idolatry and witchcraft  hatred  discord  jealousy  fits of rage  selfish ambition  dissensions  factions</s>
<s> and envy  drunkenness  orgies  and the like  i warn you  as i did before  that those who live like this will not inherit the kingdom of god </s>
<s> but the fruit of the spirit is love  joy  peace  forbearance  kindness  goodness  faithfulness </s>
<s> gentleness and selfcontrol  against such things there is no law </s>
<s> those who belong to christ jesus have crucified the flesh with its passions and desires </s>
<s> since we live by the spirit  let us keep in step with the spirit </s>
<s> let us not become conceited  provoking and envying each other </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  if someone is caught in a sin  you who live by the spirit should restore that person gently  but watch yourselves  or you also may be tempted </s>
<s> carry each others burdens  and in this way you will fulfil the law of christ </s>
<s> if anyone thinks they are something when they are not  they deceive themselves </s>
<s> each one should test their own actions  then they can take pride in themselves alone  without comparing themselves to someone else </s>
<s> for each one should carry their own load </s>
<s> nevertheless  the one who receives instruction in the word should share all good things with their instructor </s>
<s> do not be deceived  god cannot be mocked  a man reaps what he sows </s>
<s> whoever sows to please their flesh  from the flesh will reap destruction  whoever sows to please the spirit  from the spirit will reap eternal life </s>
<s> let us not become weary in doing good  for at the proper time we will reap a harvest if we do not give up </s>
<s> therefore  as we have opportunity  let us do good to all people  especially to those who belong to the family of believers </s>
<s> see what large letters i use as i write to you with my own hand </s>
<s> those who want to impress people by means of the flesh are trying to compel you to be circumcised  the only reason they do this is to avoid being persecuted for the cross of christ </s>
<s> not even those who are circumcised keep the law  yet they want you to be circumcised that they may boast about your circumcision in the flesh </s>
<s> may i never boast except in the cross of our lord jesus christ  through which the world has been crucified to me  and i to the world </s>
<s> neither circumcision nor uncircumcision means anything  what counts is the new creation </s>
<s> peace and mercy to all who follow this rule  to the israel of god </s>
<s> from now on  let no one cause me trouble  for i bear on my body the marks of jesus </s>
<s> the grace of our lord jesus christ be with your spirit  brothers and sisters  amen </s>
<s> paul  an apostle of christ jesus by the will of god  to gods holy people in ephesus  the faithful in christ jesus </s>
<s> grace and peace to you from god our father and the lord jesus christ </s>
<s> praise be to the god and father of our lord jesus christ  who has blessed us in the heavenly realms with every spiritual blessing in christ </s>
<s> for he chose us in him before the creation of the world to be holy and blameless in his sight  in love</s>
<s> he predestined us for adoption to sonship through jesus christ  in accordance with his pleasure and will </s>
<s> to the praise of his glorious grace  which he has freely given us in the one he loves </s>
<s> in him we have redemption through his blood  the forgiveness of sins  in accordance with the riches of gods grace</s>
<s> that he lavished on us  with all wisdom and understanding </s>
<s> he made known to us the mystery of his will according to his good pleasure  which he purposed in christ </s>
<s> to be put into effect when the times reach their fulfilment  to bring unity to all things in heaven and on earth under christ </s>
<s> in him we were also chosen  having been predestined according to the plan of him who works out everything in conformity with the purpose of his will </s>
<s> in order that we  who were the first to put our hope in christ  might be for the praise of his glory </s>
<s> and you also were included in christ when you heard the message of truth  the gospel of your salvation  when you believed  you were marked in him with a seal  the promised holy spirit </s>
<s> who is a deposit guaranteeing our inheritance until the redemption of those who are gods possession  to the praise of his glory </s>
<s> for this reason  ever since i heard about your faith in the lord jesus and your love for all gods people </s>
<s> i have not stopped giving thanks for you  remembering you in my prayers </s>
<s> i keep asking that the god of our lord jesus christ  the glorious father  may give you the spirit of wisdom and revelation  so that you may know him better </s>
<s> i pray that the eyes of your heart may be enlightened in order that you may know the hope to which he has called you  the riches of his glorious inheritance in his holy people </s>
<s> and his incomparably great power for us who believe  that power is the same as the mighty strength</s>
<s> he exerted when he raised christ from the dead and seated him at his right hand in the heavenly realms </s>
<s> far above all rule and authority  power and dominion  and every name that is invoked  not only in the present age but also in the one to come </s>
<s> and god placed all things under his feet and appointed him to be head over everything for the church </s>
<s> which is his body  the fullness of him who fills everything in every way </s>
<s> as for you  you were dead in your transgressions and sins </s>
<s> in which you used to live when you followed the ways of this world and of the ruler of the kingdom of the air  the spirit who is now at work in those who are disobedient </s>
<s> all of us also lived among them at one time  gratifying the cravings of our flesh and following its desires and thoughts  like the rest  we were by nature deserving of wrath </s>
<s> but because of his great love for us  god  who is rich in mercy </s>
<s> made us alive with christ even when we were dead in transgressions  it is by grace you have been saved </s>
<s> and god raised us up with christ and seated us with him in the heavenly realms in christ jesus </s>
<s> in order that in the coming ages he might show the incomparable riches of his grace  expressed in his kindness to us in christ jesus </s>
<s> for it is by grace you have been saved  through faith  and this is not from yourselves  it is the gift of god </s>
<s> not by works  so that no one can boast </s>
<s> for we are gods handiwork  created in christ jesus to do good works  which god prepared in advance for us to do </s>
<s> therefore  remember that formerly you who are gentiles by birth and called  uncircumcised by those who call themselves  the circumcision  which is done in the body by human hands  </s>
<s> remember that at that time you were separate from christ  excluded from citizenship in israel and foreigners to the covenants of the promise  without hope and without god in the world </s>
<s> but now in christ jesus you who once were far away have been brought near by the blood of christ </s>
<s> for he himself is our peace  who has made the two groups one and has destroyed the barrier  the dividing wall of hostility </s>
<s> by setting aside in his flesh the law with its commands and regulations  his purpose was to create in himself one new humanity out of the two  thus making peace </s>
<s> and in one body to reconcile both of them to god through the cross  by which he put to death their hostility </s>
<s> he came and preached peace to you who were far away and peace to those who were near </s>
<s> for through him we both have access to the father by one spirit </s>
<s> consequently  you are no longer foreigners and strangers  but fellow citizens with gods people and also members of his household </s>
<s> built on the foundation of the apostles and prophets  with christ jesus himself as the chief cornerstone </s>
<s> in him the whole building is joined together and rises to become a holy temple in the lord </s>
<s> and in him you too are being built together to become a dwelling in which god lives by his spirit </s>
<s> for this reason i  paul  the prisoner of christ jesus for the sake of you gentiles </s>
<s> surely you have heard about the administration of gods grace that was given to me for you </s>
<s> that is  the mystery made known to me by revelation  as i have already written briefly </s>
<s> in reading this  then  you will be able to understand my insight into the mystery of christ </s>
<s> which was not made known to people in other generations as it has now been revealed by the spirit to gods holy apostles and prophets </s>
<s> this mystery is that through the gospel the gentiles are heirs together with israel  members together of one body  and sharers together in the promise in christ jesus </s>
<s> i became a servant of this gospel by the gift of gods grace given me through the working of his power </s>
<s> although i am less than the least of all the lords people  this grace was given me  to preach to the gentiles the boundless riches of christ </s>
<s> and to make plain to everyone the administration of this mystery  which for ages past was kept hidden in god  who created all things </s>
<s> his intent was that now  through the church  the manifold wisdom of god should be made known to the rulers and authorities in the heavenly realms </s>
