<s> who gave himself for us to redeem us from all wickedness and to purify for himself a people that are his very own  eager to do what is good </s>
<s> these  then  are the things you should teach  encourage and rebuke with all authority  do not let anyone despise you </s>
<s> remind the people to be subject to rulers and authorities  to be obedient  to be ready to do whatever is good </s>
<s> to slander no one  to be peaceable and considerate  and always to be gentle towards everyone </s>
<s> at one time we too were foolish  disobedient  deceived and enslaved by all kinds of passions and pleasures  we lived in malice and envy  being hated and hating one another </s>
<s> but when the kindness and love of god our saviour appeared </s>
<s> he saved us  not because of righteous things we had done  but because of his mercy  he saved us through the washing of rebirth and renewal by the holy spirit </s>
<s> whom he poured out on us generously through jesus christ our saviour </s>
<s> so that  having been justified by his grace  we might become heirs having the hope of eternal life </s>
<s> this is a trustworthy saying  and i want you to stress these things  so that those who have trusted in god may be careful to devote themselves to doing what is good  these things are excellent and profitable for everyone </s>
<s> but avoid foolish controversies and genealogies and arguments and quarrels about the law  because these are unprofitable and useless </s>
<s> warn a divisive person once  and then warn them a second time  after that  have nothing to do with them </s>
<s> you may be sure that such people are warped and sinful  they are self condemned </s>
<s> as soon as i send artemas or tychicus to you  do your best to come to me at nicopolis  because i have decided to winter there </s>
<s> do everything you can to help zenas the lawyer and apollos on their way and see that they have everything they need </s>
<s> our people must learn to devote themselves to doing what is good  in order to provide for urgent needs and not live unproductive lives </s>
<s> everyone with me sends you greetings  greet those who love us in the faith  grace be with you all </s>
<s> paul  a prisoner of christ jesus  and timothy our brother  to philemon our dear friend and fellow worker </s>
<s> also to apphia our sister and archippus our fellow soldier  and to the church that meets in your home </s>
<s> grace and peace to you from god our father and the lord jesus christ </s>
<s> i always thank my god as i remember you in my prayers </s>
<s> because i hear about your love for all his holy people and your faith in the lord jesus </s>
<s> i pray that your partnership with us in the faith may be effective in deepening your understanding of every good thing we share for the sake of christ </s>
<s> your love has given me great joy and encouragement  because you  brother  have refreshed the hearts of the lords people </s>
<s> therefore  although in christ i could be bold and order you to do what you ought to do </s>
<s> yet i prefer to appeal to you on the basis of love  it is as none other than paul  an old man and now also a prisoner of christ jesus </s>
<s> that i appeal to you for my son onesimus  who became my son while i was in chains </s>
<s> formerly he was useless to you  but now he has become useful both to you and to me </s>
<s> i am sending him  who is my very heart  back to you </s>
<s> i would have liked to keep him with me so that he could take your place in helping me while i am in chains for the gospel </s>
<s> but i did not want to do anything without your consent  so that any favour you do would not seem forced but would be voluntary </s>
<s> perhaps the reason he was separated from you for a little while was that you might have him back for ever </s>
<s> no longer as a slave  but better than a slave  as a dear brother  he is very dear to me but even dearer to you  both as a fellow man and as a brother in the lord </s>
<s> so if you consider me a partner  welcome him as you would welcome me </s>
<s> if he has done you any wrong or owes you anything  charge it to me </s>
<s> i  paul  am writing this with my own hand  i will pay it back  not to mention that you owe me your very self </s>
<s> i do wish  brother  that i may have some benefit from you in the lord  refresh my heart in christ </s>
<s> confident of your obedience  i write to you  knowing that you will do even more than i ask </s>
<s> and one thing more  prepare a guest room for me  because i hope to be restored to you in answer to your prayers </s>
<s> epaphras  my fellow prisoner in christ jesus  sends you greetings </s>
<s> and so do mark  aristarchus  demas and luke  my fellow workers </s>
<s> the grace of the lord jesus christ be with your spirit </s>
<s> in the past god spoke to our ancestors through the prophets at many times and in various ways </s>
<s> but in these last days he has spoken to us by his son  whom he appointed heir of all things  and through whom also he made the universe </s>
<s> the son is the radiance of gods glory and the exact representation of his being  sustaining all things by his powerful word  after he had provided purification for sins  he sat down at the right hand of the majesty in heaven </s>
<s> so he became as much superior to the angels as the name he has inherited is superior to theirs </s>
<s> for to which of the angels did god ever say   you are my son  today i have become your father   i will be his father  and he will be my son   let all gods angels worship him    he makes his angels spirits  and his servants flames of fire    your throne  o god  will last for ever and ever  a sceptre of justice will be the sceptre of your kingdom </s>
<s> you have loved righteousness and hated wickedness  therefore god  your god  has set you above your companions by anointing you with the oil of joy    in the beginning  lord  you laid the foundations of the earth  and the heavens are the work of your hands </s>
<s> they will perish  but you remain  they will all wear out like a garment </s>
<s> you will roll them up like a robe  like a garment they will be changed  but you remain the same  and your years will never end    sit at my right hand until i make your enemies a footstool for your feet </s>
<s> we must pay the most careful attention  therefore  to what we have heard  so that we do not drift away </s>
<s> for since the message spoken through angels was binding  and every violation and disobedience received its just punishment </s>
<s> how shall we escape if we ignore so great a salvation  this salvation  which was first announced by the lord  was confirmed to us by those who heard him </s>
<s> god also testified to it by signs  wonders and various miracles  and by gifts of the holy spirit distributed according to his will </s>
<s> it is not to angels that he has subjected the world to come  about which we are speaking </s>
<s> but there is a place where someone has testified   what is mankind that you are mindful of them  a son of man that you care for him </s>
<s> you made them a little lower than the angels  you crowned them with glory and honour</s>
<s> and put everything under their feet   </s>
<s> in bringing many sons and daughters to glory  it was fitting that god  for whom and through whom everything exists  should make the pioneer of their salvation perfect through what he suffered </s>
<s> both the one who makes people holy and those who are made holy are of the same family  so jesus is not ashamed to call them brothers and sisters </s>
<s> he says   i will declare your name to my brothers and sisters  in the assembly i will sing your praises    i will put my trust in him    here am i  and the children god has given me  </s>
<s> since the children have flesh and blood  he too shared in their humanity so that by his death he might break the power of him who holds the power of death  that is  the devil </s>
<s> and free those who all their lives were held in slavery by their fear of death </s>
<s> for surely it is not angels he helps  but abrahams descendants </s>
<s> for this reason he had to be made like them  fully human in every way  in order that he might become a merciful and faithful high priest in service to god  and that he might make atonement for the sins of the people </s>
<s> because he himself suffered when he was tempted  he is able to help those who are being tempted </s>
<s> therefore  holy brothers and sisters  who share in the heavenly calling  fix your thoughts on jesus  whom we acknowledge as our apostle and high priest </s>
<s> he was faithful to the one who appointed him  just as moses was faithful in all gods house </s>
<s> jesus has been found worthy of greater honour than moses  just as the builder of a house has greater honour than the house itself </s>
<s> for every house is built by someone  but god is the builder of everything </s>
<s>  moses was faithful as a servant in all gods house   bearing witness to what would be spoken by god in the future </s>
<s> but christ is faithful as the son over gods house  and we are his house  if indeed we hold firmly to our confidence and the hope in which we glory </s>
<s> so  as the holy spirit says   today  if you hear his voice </s>
<s> do not harden your hearts as you did in the rebellion  during the time of testing in the wilderness </s>
<s> where your ancestors tested and tried me  though for forty years they saw what i did </s>
<s> that is why i was angry with that generation  i said   their hearts are always going astray  and they have not known my ways  </s>
<s> so i declared on oath in my anger   they shall never enter my rest   </s>
<s> see to it  brothers and sisters  that none of you has a sinful  unbelieving heart that turns away from the living god </s>
<s> but encourage one another daily  as long as it is called  today  so that none of you may be hardened by sins deceitfulness </s>
<s> we have come to share in christ  if indeed we hold our original conviction firmly to the very end </s>
<s> as has just been said   today  if you hear his voice  do not harden your hearts as you did in the rebellion  </s>
<s> who were they who heard and rebelled  were they not all those moses led out of egypt </s>
<s> and with whom was he angry for forty years  was it not with those who sinned  whose bodies perished in the wilderness </s>
<s> and to whom did god swear that they would never enter his rest if not to those who disobeyed </s>
<s> so we see that they were not able to enter  because of their unbelief </s>
<s> therefore  since the promise of entering his rest still stands  let us be careful that none of you be found to have fallen short of it </s>
<s> for we also have had the good news proclaimed to us  just as they did  but the message they heard was of no value to them  because they did not share the faith of those who obeyed </s>
<s> now we who have believed enter that rest  just as god has said   so i declared on oath in my anger   they shall never enter my rest   </s>
<s> therefore since it still remains for some to enter that rest  and since those who formerly had the good news proclaimed to them did not go in because of their disobedience </s>
<s> god again set a certain day  calling it  today  this he did when a long time later he spoke through david  as in the passage already quoted   today  if you hear his voice  do not harden your hearts  </s>
<s> for the word of god is alive and active  sharper than any doubleedged sword  it penetrates even to dividing soul and spirit  joints and marrow  it judges the thoughts and attitudes of the heart </s>
<s> nothing in all creation is hidden from gods sight  everything is uncovered and laid bare before the eyes of him to whom we must give account </s>
<s> therefore  since we have a great high priest who has ascended into heaven  jesus the son of god  let us hold firmly to the faith we profess </s>
<s> for we do not have a high priest who is unable to feel sympathy for our weaknesses  but we have one who has been tempted in every way  just as we are  yet he did not sin </s>
<s> let us then approach gods throne of grace with confidence  so that we may receive mercy and find grace to help us in our time of need </s>
<s> every high priest is selected from among the people and is appointed to represent the people in matters related to god  to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins </s>
<s> he is able to deal gently with those who are ignorant and are going astray  since he himself is subject to weakness </s>
<s> this is why he has to offer sacrifices for his own sins  as well as for the sins of the people </s>
<s> and no one takes this honour on himself  but he receives it when called by god  just as aaron was </s>
<s> in the same way  christ did not take on himself the glory of becoming a high priest  but god said to him   you are my son  today i have become your father    you are a priest for ever  in the order of melchizedek  </s>
<s> during the days of jesus life on earth  he offered up prayers and petitions with fervent cries and tears to the one who could save him from death  and he was heard because of his reverent submission </s>
<s> son though he was  he learned obedience from what he suffered</s>
<s> and  once made perfect  he became the source of eternal salvation for all who obey him</s>
<s> and was designated by god to be high priest in the order of melchizedek </s>
<s> we have much to say about this  but it is hard to make it clear to you because you no longer try to understand </s>
<s> in fact  though by this time you ought to be teachers  you need someone to teach you the elementary truths of gods word all over again  you need milk  not solid food </s>
<s> anyone who lives on milk  being still an infant  is not acquainted with the teaching about righteousness </s>
<s> but solid food is for the mature  who by constant use have trained themselves to distinguish good from evil </s>
<s> therefore let us move beyond the elementary teachings about christ and be taken forward to maturity  not laying again the foundation of repentance from acts that lead to death  and of faith in god </s>
<s> instruction about cleansing rites  the laying on of hands  the resurrection of the dead  and eternal judgment </s>
<s> and god permitting  we will do so </s>
<s> it is impossible for those who have once been enlightened  who have tasted the heavenly gift  who have shared in the holy spirit </s>
<s> who have tasted the goodness of the word of god and the powers of the coming age</s>
<s> and who have fallen away  to be brought back to repentance  to their loss they are crucifying the son of god all over again and subjecting him to public disgrace </s>
<s> land that drinks in the rain often falling on it and that produces a crop useful to those for whom it is farmed receives the blessing of god </s>
<s> but land that produces thorns and thistles is worthless and is in danger of being cursed  in the end it will be burned </s>
<s> even though we speak like this  dear friends  we are convinced of better things in your case  the things that have to do with salvation </s>
<s> god is not unjust  he will not forget your work and the love you have shown him as you have helped his people and continue to help them </s>
<s> we want each of you to show this same diligence to the very end  so that what you hope for may be fully realized </s>
<s> we do not want you to become lazy  but to imitate those who through faith and patience inherit what has been promised </s>
<s> when god made his promise to abraham  since there was no one greater for him to swear by  he swore by himself </s>
<s> saying   i will surely bless you and give you many descendants  </s>
<s> and so after waiting patiently  abraham received what was promised </s>
<s> people swear by someone greater than themselves  and the oath confirms what is said and puts an end to all argument </s>
<s> because god wanted to make the unchanging nature of his purpose very clear to the heirs of what was promised  he confirmed it with an oath </s>
<s> god did this so that  by two unchangeable things in which it is impossible for god to lie  we who have fled to take hold of the hope set before us may be greatly encouraged </s>
<s> we have this hope as an anchor for the soul  firm and secure  it enters the inner sanctuary behind the curtain </s>
<s> where our forerunner  jesus  has entered on our behalf  he has become a high priest for ever  in the order of melchizedek </s>
<s> this melchizedek was king of salem and priest of god most high  he met abraham returning from the defeat of the kings and blessed him </s>
<s> and abraham gave him a tenth of everything  first  the name melchizedek means  king of righteousness  then also   king of salem means  king of peace </s>
<s> without father or mother  without genealogy  without beginning of days or end of life  resembling the son of god  he remains a priest for ever </s>
<s> just think how great he was  even the patriarch abraham gave him a tenth of the plunder </s>
<s> now the law requires the descendants of levi who become priests to collect a tenth from the people  that is  from their fellow israelites  even though they also are descended from abraham </s>
<s> this man  however  did not trace his descent from levi  yet he collected a tenth from abraham and blessed him who had the promises </s>
<s> and without doubt the lesser is blessed by the greater </s>
<s> in the one case  the tenth is collected by people who die  but in the other case  by him who is declared to be living </s>
<s> one might even say that levi  who collects the tenth  paid the tenth through abraham </s>
<s> because when melchizedek met abraham  levi was still in the body of his ancestor </s>
<s> if perfection could have been attained through the levitical priesthood  and indeed the law given to the people established that priesthood  why was there still need for another priest to come  one in the order of melchizedek  not in the order of aaron </s>
<s> for when the priesthood is changed  the law must be changed also </s>
<s> he of whom these things are said belonged to a different tribe  and no one from that tribe has ever served at the altar </s>
<s> for it is clear that our lord descended from judah  and in regard to that tribe moses said nothing about priests </s>
<s> and what we have said is even more clear if another priest like melchizedek appears </s>
<s> one who has become a priest not on the basis of a regulation as to his ancestry but on the basis of the power of an indestructible life </s>
<s> for it is declared   you are a priest for ever  in the order of melchizedek  </s>
<s> the former regulation is set aside because it was weak and useless</s>
<s>  for the law made nothing perfect   and a better hope is introduced  by which we draw near to god </s>
<s> and it was not without an oath  others became priests without any oath </s>
<s> but he became a priest with an oath when god said to him   the lord has sworn and will not change his mind   you are a priest for ever   </s>
<s> now there have been many of those priests  since death prevented them from continuing in office </s>
<s> but because jesus lives for ever  he has a permanent priesthood </s>
<s> therefore he is able to save completely those who come to god through him  because he always lives to intercede for them </s>
<s> such a high priest truly meets our need  one who is holy  blameless  pure  set apart from sinners  exalted above the heavens </s>
<s> unlike the other high priests  he does not need to offer sacrifices day after day  first for his own sins  and then for the sins of the people  he sacrificed for their sins once for all when he offered himself </s>
<s> for the law appoints as high priests men in all their weakness  but the oath  which came after the law  appointed the son  who has been made perfect for ever </s>
<s> now the main point of what we are saying is this  we do have such a high priest  who sat down at the right hand of the throne of the majesty in heaven </s>
<s> and who serves in the sanctuary  the true tabernacle set up by the lord  not by a mere human being </s>
<s> every high priest is appointed to offer both gifts and sacrifices  and so it was necessary for this one also to have something to offer </s>
<s> if he were on earth  he would not be a priest  for there are already priests who offer the gifts prescribed by the law </s>
<s> they serve at a sanctuary that is a copy and shadow of what is in heaven  this is why moses was warned when he was about to build the tabernacle   see to it that you make everything according to the pattern shown you on the mountain  </s>
<s> but in fact the ministry jesus has received is as superior to theirs as the covenant of which he is mediator is superior to the old one  since the new covenant is established on better promises </s>
<s> for if there had been nothing wrong with that first covenant  no place would have been sought for another </s>
<s> but god found fault with the people and said   the days are coming  declares the lord  when i will make a new covenant with the people of israel and with the people of judah </s>
<s> it will not be like the covenant i made with their ancestors when i took them by the hand to lead them out of egypt  because they did not remain faithful to my covenant  and i turned away from them </s>
<s> this is the covenant i will establish with the people of israel after that time  declares the lord  i will put my laws in their minds and write them on their hearts  i will be their god  and they will be my people </s>
<s> no longer will they teach their neighbours  or say to one another   know the lord   because they will all know me  from the least of them to the greatest </s>
<s> for i will forgive their wickedness and will remember their sins no more  </s>
<s> by calling this covenant  new  he has made the first one obsolete  and what is obsolete and outdated will soon disappear </s>
<s> now the first covenant had regulations for worship and also an earthly sanctuary </s>
<s> a tabernacle was set up  in its first room were the lampstand and the table with its consecrated bread  this was called the holy place </s>
<s> behind the second curtain was a room called the most holy place </s>
<s> which had the golden altar of incense and the goldcovered ark of the covenant  this ark contained the gold jar of manna  aarons staff that had budded  and the stone tablets of the covenant </s>
<s> above the ark were the cherubim of the glory  overshadowing the atonement cover  but we cannot discuss these things in detail now </s>
<s> when everything had been arranged like this  the priests entered regularly into the outer room to carry on their ministry </s>
<s> but only the high priest entered the inner room  and that only once a year  and never without blood  which he offered for himself and for the sins the people had committed in ignorance </s>
<s> the holy spirit was showing by this that the way into the most holy place had not yet been disclosed as long as the first tabernacle was still functioning </s>
<s> this is an illustration for the present time  indicating that the gifts and sacrifices being offered were not able to clear the conscience of the worshipper </s>
<s> they are only a matter of food and drink and various ceremonial washings  external regulations applying until the time of the new order </s>
<s> but when christ came as high priest of the good things that are now already here  he went through the greater and more perfect tabernacle that is not made with human hands  that is to say  is not a part of this creation </s>
<s> he did not enter by means of the blood of goats and calves  but he entered the most holy place once for all by his own blood  so obtaining eternal redemption </s>
<s> the blood of goats and bulls and the ashes of a heifer sprinkled on those who are ceremonially unclean sanctify them so that they are outwardly clean </s>
<s> how much more  then  will the blood of christ  who through the eternal spirit offered himself unblemished to god  cleanse our consciences from acts that lead to death  so that we may serve the living god </s>
<s> for this reason christ is the mediator of a new covenant  that those who are called may receive the promised eternal inheritance  now that he has died as a ransom to set them free from the sins committed under the first covenant </s>
<s> in the case of a will  it is necessary to prove the death of the one who made it </s>
<s> because a will is in force only when somebody has died  it never takes effect while the one who made it is living </s>
<s> this is why even the first covenant was not put into effect without blood </s>
<s> when moses had proclaimed every command of the law to all the people  he took the blood of calves  together with water  scarlet wool and branches of hyssop  and sprinkled the scroll and all the people </s>
<s> he said   this is the blood of the covenant  which god has commanded you to keep  </s>
<s> in the same way  he sprinkled with the blood both the tabernacle and everything used in its ceremonies </s>
<s> in fact  the law requires that nearly everything be cleansed with blood  and without the shedding of blood there is no forgiveness </s>
<s> it was necessary  then  for the copies of the heavenly things to be purified with these sacrifices  but the heavenly things themselves with better sacrifices than these </s>
<s> for christ did not enter a sanctuary made with human hands that was only a copy of the true one  he entered heaven itself  now to appear for us in gods presence </s>
<s> nor did he enter heaven to offer himself again and again  the way the high priest enters the most holy place every year with blood that is not his own </s>
<s> otherwise christ would have had to suffer many times since the creation of the world  but he has appeared once for all at the culmination of the ages to do away with sin by the sacrifice of himself </s>
<s> just as people are destined to die once  and after that to face judgment </s>
<s> so christ was sacrificed once to take away the sins of many  and he will appear a second time  not to bear sin  but to bring salvation to those who are waiting for him </s>
<s> the law is only a shadow of the good things that are coming  not the realities themselves  for this reason it can never  by the same sacrifices repeated endlessly year after year  make perfect those who draw near to worship </s>
<s> otherwise  would they not have stopped being offered  for the worshippers would have been cleansed once for all  and would no longer have felt guilty for their sins </s>
<s> but those sacrifices are an annual reminder of sins </s>
<s> it is impossible for the blood of bulls and goats to take away sins </s>
<s> therefore  when christ came into the world  he said   sacrifice and offering you did not desire  but a body you prepared for me </s>
<s> with burnt offerings and sin offerings you were not pleased </s>
<s> then i said   here i am  it is written about me in the scroll  i have come to do your will  my god   </s>
<s> day after day every priest stands and performs his religious duties  again and again he offers the same sacrifices  which can never take away sins </s>
<s> but when this priest had offered for all time one sacrifice for sins  he sat down at the right hand of god </s>
<s> and since that time he waits for his enemies to be made his footstool </s>
<s> for by one sacrifice he has made perfect for ever those who are being made holy </s>
<s> the holy spirit also testifies to us about this  first he says </s>
<s>  this is the covenant i will make with them after that time  says the lord  i will put my laws in their hearts  and i will write them on their minds    their sins and lawless acts i will remember no more  </s>
<s> and where these have been forgiven  sacrifice for sin is no longer necessary </s>
<s> therefore  brothers and sisters  since we have confidence to enter the most holy place by the blood of jesus </s>
<s> by a new and living way opened for us through the curtain  that is  his body </s>
<s> and since we have a great priest over the house of god </s>
<s> let us draw near to god with a sincere heart and with the full assurance that faith brings  having our hearts sprinkled to cleanse us from a guilty conscience and having our bodies washed with pure water </s>
<s> let us hold unswervingly to the hope we profess  for he who promised is faithful </s>
<s> and let us consider how we may spur one another on towards love and good deeds </s>
<s> not giving up meeting together  as some are in the habit of doing  but encouraging one another  and all the more as you see the day approaching </s>
<s> if we deliberately keep on sinning after we have received the knowledge of the truth  no sacrifice for sins is left </s>
<s> but only a fearful expectation of judgment and of raging fire that will consume the enemies of god </s>
<s> anyone who rejected the law of moses died without mercy on the testimony of two or three witnesses </s>
<s> how much more severely do you think someone deserves to be punished who has trampled the son of god underfoot  who has treated as an unholy thing the blood of the covenant that sanctified them  and who has insulted the spirit of grace </s>
<s> for we know him who said   it is mine to avenge  i will repay   and again   the lord will judge his people  </s>
<s> it is a dreadful thing to fall into the hands of the living god </s>
<s> remember those earlier days after you had received the light  when you endured in a great conflict full of suffering </s>
<s> sometimes you were publicly exposed to insult and persecution  at other times you stood side by side with those who were so treated </s>
<s> you suffered along with those in prison and joyfully accepted the confiscation of your property  because you knew that you yourselves had better and lasting possessions </s>
<s> so do not throw away your confidence  it will be richly rewarded </s>
<s> you need to persevere so that when you have done the will of god  you will receive what he has promised </s>
<s> for   in just a little while  he who is coming will come and will not delay    but my righteous one will live by faith  and i take no pleasure in the one who shrinks back  </s>
<s> now faith is confidence in what we hope for and assurance about what we do not see </s>
<s> this is what the ancients were commended for </s>
<s> by faith we understand that the universe was formed at gods command  so that what is seen was not made out of what was visible </s>
<s> by faith abel brought god a better offering than cain did  by faith he was commended as righteous  when god spoke well of his offerings  and by faith abel still speaks  even though he is dead </s>
<s> by faith enoch was taken from this life  so that he did not experience death   he could not be found  because god had taken him away   for before he was taken  he was commended as one who pleased god </s>
<s> and without faith it is impossible to please god  because anyone who comes to him must believe that he exists and that he rewards those who earnestly seek him </s>
<s> by faith noah  when warned about things not yet seen  in holy fear built an ark to save his family  by his faith he condemned the world and became heir of the righteousness that is in keeping with faith </s>
<s> by faith abraham  when called to go to a place he would later receive as his inheritance  obeyed and went  even though he did not know where he was going </s>
<s> by faith he made his home in the promised land like a stranger in a foreign country  he lived in tents  as did isaac and jacob  who were heirs with him of the same promise </s>
<s> for he was looking forward to the city with foundations  whose architect and builder is god </s>
<s> and by faith even sarah  who was past childbearing age  was enabled to bear children because she considered him faithful who had made the promise </s>
<s> and so from this one man  and he as good as dead  came descendants as numerous as the stars in the sky and as countless as the sand on the seashore </s>
<s> all these people were still living by faith when they died  they did not receive the things promised  they only saw them and welcomed them from a distance  admitting that they were foreigners and strangers on earth </s>
<s> people who say such things show that they are looking for a country of their own </s>
<s> if they had been thinking of the country they had left  they would have had opportunity to return </s>
<s> instead  they were longing for a better country  a heavenly one  therefore god is not ashamed to be called their god  for he has prepared a city for them </s>
<s> by faith abraham  when god tested him  offered isaac as a sacrifice  he who had embraced the promises was about to sacrifice his one and only son </s>
<s> even though god had said to him   it is through isaac that your offspring will be reckoned  </s>
<s> abraham reasoned that god could even raise the dead  and so in a manner of speaking he did receive isaac back from death </s>
<s> by faith isaac blessed jacob and esau in regard to their future </s>
<s> by faith jacob  when he was dying  blessed each of josephs sons  and worshipped as he leaned on the top of his staff </s>
<s> by faith joseph  when his end was near  spoke about the exodus of the israelites from egypt and gave instructions concerning the burial of his bones </s>
<s> by faith moses parents hid him for three months after he was born  because they saw he was no ordinary child  and they were not afraid of the kings edict </s>
<s> by faith moses  when he had grown up  refused to be known as the son of pharaohs daughter </s>
<s> he chose to be illtreated along with the people of god rather than to enjoy the fleeting pleasures of sin </s>
<s> he regarded disgrace for the sake of christ as of greater value than the treasures of egypt  because he was looking ahead to his reward </s>
<s> by faith he left egypt  not fearing the kings anger  he persevered because he saw him who is invisible </s>
<s> by faith he kept the passover and the application of blood  so that the destroyer of the firstborn would not touch the firstborn of israel </s>
<s> by faith the people passed through the red sea as on dry land  but when the egyptians tried to do so  they were drowned </s>
<s> by faith the walls of jericho fell  after the army had marched round them for seven days </s>
<s> by faith the prostitute rahab  because she welcomed the spies  was not killed with those who were disobedient </s>
<s> and what more shall i say  i do not have time to tell about gideon  barak  samson and jephthah  about david and samuel and the prophets </s>
<s> who through faith conquered kingdoms  administered justice  and gained what was promised  who shut the mouths of lions </s>
<s> quenched the fury of the flames  and escaped the edge of the sword  whose weakness was turned to strength  and who became powerful in battle and routed foreign armies </s>
<s> women received back their dead  raised to life again  there were others who were tortured  refusing to be released so that they might gain an even better resurrection </s>
<s> some faced jeers and flogging  and even chains and imprisonment </s>
<s> they were put to death by stoning  they were sawn in two  they were killed by the sword  they went about in sheepskins and goatskins  destitute  persecuted and illtreated </s>
<s> the world was not worthy of them  they wandered in deserts and mountains  living in caves and in holes in the ground </s>
<s> these were all commended for their faith  yet none of them received what had been promised </s>
<s> since god had planned something better for us so that only together with us would they be made perfect </s>
<s> therefore  since we are surrounded by such a great cloud of witnesses  let us throw off everything that hinders and the sin that so easily entangles  and let us run with perseverance the race marked out for us </s>
<s> fixing our eyes on jesus  the pioneer and perfecter of faith  for the joy that was set before him he endured the cross  scorning its shame  and sat down at the right hand of the throne of god </s>
<s> consider him who endured such opposition from sinners  so that you will not grow weary and lose heart </s>
<s> in your struggle against sin  you have not yet resisted to the point of shedding your blood </s>
<s> and have you completely forgotten this word of encouragement that addresses you as a father addresses his son  it says   my son  do not make light of the lords discipline  and do not lose heart when he rebukes you </s>
<s> because the lord disciplines the one he loves  and he chastens everyone he accepts as his son  </s>
<s> endure hardship as discipline  god is treating you as his children  for what children are not disciplined by their father </s>
<s> if you are not disciplined  and everyone undergoes discipline  then you are not legitimate  not true sons and daughters at all </s>
<s> moreover  we have all had human fathers who disciplined us and we respected them for it  how much more should we submit to the father of spirits and live </s>
<s> they disciplined us for a little while as they thought best  but god disciplines us for our good  in order that we may share in his holiness </s>
<s> no discipline seems pleasant at the time  but painful  later on  however  it produces a harvest of righteousness and peace for those who have been trained by it </s>
<s> therefore  strengthen your feeble arms and weak knees </s>
<s>  make level paths for your feet   so that the lame may not be disabled  but rather healed </s>
<s> make every effort to live in peace with everyone and to be holy  without holiness no one will see the lord </s>
<s> see to it that no one falls short of the grace of god and that no bitter root grows up to cause trouble and defile many </s>
<s> see that no one is sexually immoral  or is godless like esau  who for a single meal sold his inheritance rights as the oldest son </s>
<s> afterwards  as you know  when he wanted to inherit this blessing  he was rejected  even though he sought the blessing with tears  he could not change what he had done </s>
<s> you have not come to a mountain that can be touched and that is burning with fire  to darkness  gloom and storm </s>
<s> to a trumpet blast or to such a voice speaking words that those who heard it begged that no further word be spoken to them </s>
<s> because they could not bear what was commanded   if even an animal touches the mountain  it must be stoned to death  </s>
<s> the sight was so terrifying that moses said   i am trembling with fear  </s>
<s> but you have come to mount zion  to the city of the living god  the heavenly jerusalem  you have come to thousands upon thousands of angels in joyful assembly </s>
<s> to the church of the firstborn  whose names are written in heaven  you have come to god  the judge of all  to the spirits of the righteous made perfect </s>
<s> to jesus the mediator of a new covenant  and to the sprinkled blood that speaks a better word than the blood of abel </s>
<s> see to it that you do not refuse him who speaks  if they did not escape when they refused him who warned them on earth  how much less will we  if we turn away from him who warns us from heaven </s>
<s> at that time his voice shook the earth  but now he has promised   once more i will shake not only the earth but also the heavens  </s>
<s> the words  once more indicate the removing of what can be shaken  that is  created things  so that what cannot be shaken may remain </s>
<s> therefore  since we are receiving a kingdom that cannot be shaken  let us be thankful  and so worship god acceptably with reverence and awe </s>
<s> for our  god is a consuming fire  </s>
<s> keep on loving one another as brothers and sisters </s>
<s> do not forget to show hospitality to strangers  for by so doing some people have shown hospitality to angels without knowing it </s>
<s> continue to remember those in prison as if you were together with them in prison  and those who are illtreated as if you yourselves were suffering </s>
<s> marriage should be honoured by all  and the marriage bed kept pure  for god will judge the adulterer and all the sexually immoral </s>
<s> keep your lives free from the love of money and be content with what you have  because god has said   never will i leave you  never will i forsake you    the lord is my helper  i will not be afraid  what can mere mortals do to me  </s>
<s> remember your leaders  who spoke the word of god to you  consider the outcome of their way of life and imitate their faith </s>
<s> jesus christ is the same yesterday and today and for ever </s>
<s> do not be carried away by all kinds of strange teachings  it is good for our hearts to be strengthened by grace  not by eating ceremonial foods  which is of no benefit to those who do so </s>
<s> we have an altar from which those who minister at the tabernacle have no right to eat </s>
<s> the high priest carries the blood of animals into the most holy place as a sin offering  but the bodies are burned outside the camp </s>
<s> and so jesus also suffered outside the city gate to make the people holy through his own blood </s>
<s> let us  then  go to him outside the camp  bearing the disgrace he bore </s>
<s> for here we do not have an enduring city  but we are looking for the city that is to come </s>
<s> through jesus  therefore  let us continually offer to god a sacrifice of praise  the fruit of lips that openly profess his name </s>
<s> and do not forget to do good and to share with others  for with such sacrifices god is pleased </s>
<s> have confidence in your leaders and submit to their authority  because they keep watch over you as those who must give an account  do this so that their work will be a joy  not a burden  for that would be of no benefit to you </s>
<s> pray for us  we are sure that we have a clear conscience and desire to live honourably in every way </s>
<s> i particularly urge you to pray so that i may be restored to you soon </s>
<s> now may the god of peace  who through the blood of the eternal covenant brought back from the dead our lord jesus  that great shepherd of the sheep </s>
<s> equip you with everything good for doing his will  and may he work in us what is pleasing to him  through jesus christ  to whom be glory for ever and ever  amen </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  i urge you to bear with my word of exhortation  for in fact i have written to you quite briefly </s>
<s> i want you to know that our brother timothy has been released  if he arrives soon  i will come with him to see you </s>
<s> greet all your leaders and all the lords people  those from italy send you their greetings </s>
<s> grace be with you all </s>
<s> james  a servant of god and of the lord jesus christ  to the twelve tribes scattered among the nations  greetings </s>
<s> consider it pure joy  my brothers and sisters  whenever you face trials of many kinds </s>
<s> because you know that the testing of your faith produces perseverance </s>
<s> let perseverance finish its work so that you may be mature and complete  not lacking anything </s>
<s> if any of you lacks wisdom  you should ask god  who gives generously to all without finding fault  and it will be given to you </s>
<s> but when you ask  you must believe and not doubt  because the one who doubts is like a wave of the sea  blown and tossed by the wind </s>
<s> that person should not expect to receive anything from the lord </s>
<s> such a person is doubleminded and unstable in all they do </s>
<s> believers in humble circumstances ought to take pride in their high position </s>
<s> but the rich should take pride in their humiliation  since they will pass away like a wild flower </s>
<s> for the sun rises with scorching heat and withers the plant  its blossom falls and its beauty is destroyed  in the same way  the rich will fade away even while they go about their business </s>
<s> blessed is the one who perseveres under trial because  having stood the test  that person will receive the crown of life that the lord has promised to those who love him </s>
<s> when tempted  no one should say   god is tempting me   for god cannot be tempted by evil  nor does he tempt anyone </s>
<s> but each person is tempted when they are dragged away by their own evil desire and enticed </s>
<s> then  after desire has conceived  it gives birth to sin  and sin  when it is fullgrown  gives birth to death </s>
<s> dont be deceived  my dear brothers and sisters </s>
<s> every good and perfect gift is from above  coming down from the father of the heavenly lights  who does not change like shifting shadows </s>
<s> he chose to give us birth through the word of truth  that we might be a kind of firstfruits of all he created </s>
<s> my dear brothers and sisters  take note of this  everyone should be quick to listen  slow to speak and slow to become angry </s>
<s> because human anger does not produce the righteousness that god desires </s>
<s> therefore  get rid of all moral filth and the evil that is so prevalent  and humbly accept the word planted in you  which can save you </s>
<s> do not merely listen to the word  and so deceive yourselves  do what it says </s>
<s> anyone who listens to the word but does not do what it says is like someone who looks at his face in a mirror</s>
<s> and  after looking at himself  goes away and immediately forgets what he looks like </s>
<s> but whoever looks intently into the perfect law that gives freedom and continues in it  not forgetting what they have heard but doing it  they will be blessed in what they do </s>
<s> those who consider themselves religious and yet do not keep a tight rein on their tongues deceive themselves  and their religion is worthless </s>
<s> religion that god our father accepts as pure and faultless is this  to look after orphans and widows in their distress and to keep oneself from being polluted by the world </s>
<s> my brothers and sisters  believers in our glorious lord jesus christ must not show favouritism </s>
<s> suppose a man comes into your meeting wearing a gold ring and fine clothes  and a poor man in filthy old clothes also comes in </s>
<s> if you show special attention to the man wearing fine clothes and say   heres a good seat for you   but say to the poor man   you stand there or  sit on the floor by my feet  </s>
<s> have you not discriminated among yourselves and become judges with evil thoughts </s>
<s> listen  my dear brothers and sisters  has not god chosen those who are poor in the eyes of the world to be rich in faith and to inherit the kingdom he promised those who love him </s>
<s> but you have dishonoured the poor  is it not the rich who are exploiting you  are they not the ones who are dragging you into court </s>
<s> are they not the ones who are blaspheming the noble name of him to whom you belong </s>
<s> if you really keep the royal law found in scripture   love your neighbour as yourself   you are doing right </s>
<s> but if you show favouritism  you sin and are convicted by the law as lawbreakers </s>
<s> for whoever keeps the whole law and yet stumbles at just one point is guilty of breaking all of it </s>
<s> for he who said   you shall not commit adultery   also said   you shall not murder   if you do not commit adultery but do commit murder  you have become a lawbreaker </s>
<s> speak and act as those who are going to be judged by the law that gives freedom </s>
<s> because judgment without mercy will be shown to anyone who has not been merciful  mercy triumphs over judgment </s>
<s> what good is it  my brothers and sisters  if someone claims to have faith but has no deeds  can such faith save them </s>
<s> suppose a brother or a sister is without clothes and daily food </s>
<s> if one of you says to them   go in peace  keep warm and well fed   but does nothing about their physical needs  what good is it </s>
<s> in the same way  faith by itself  if it is not accompanied by action  is dead </s>
<s> but someone will say   you have faith  i have deeds   show me your faith without deeds  and i will show you my faith by my deeds </s>
<s> you believe that there is one god  good  even the demons believe that  and shudder </s>
<s> you foolish person  do you want evidence that faith without deeds is useless </s>
<s> was not our father abraham considered righteous for what he did when he offered his son isaac on the altar </s>
<s> you see that his faith and his actions were working together  and his faith was made complete by what he did </s>
<s> and the scripture was fulfilled that says   abraham believed god  and it was credited to him as righteousness   and he was called gods friend </s>
<s> you see that a person is considered righteous by what they do and not by faith alone </s>
<s> in the same way  was not even rahab the prostitute considered righteous for what she did when she gave lodging to the spies and sent them off in a different direction </s>
<s> as the body without the spirit is dead  so faith without deeds is dead </s>
<s> not many of you should become teachers  my fellow believers  because you know that we who teach will be judged more strictly </s>
<s> we all stumble in many ways  anyone who is never at fault in what they say is perfect  able to keep their whole body in check </s>
<s> when we put bits into the mouths of horses to make them obey us  we can turn the whole animal </s>
<s> or take ships as an example  although they are so large and are driven by strong winds  they are steered by a very small rudder wherever the pilot wants to go </s>
<s> likewise  the tongue is a small part of the body  but it makes great boasts  consider what a great forest is set on fire by a small spark </s>
<s> the tongue also is a fire  a world of evil among the parts of the body  it corrupts the whole body  sets the whole course of ones life on fire  and is itself set on fire by hell </s>
<s> all kinds of animals  birds  reptiles and sea creatures are being tamed and have been tamed by mankind </s>
<s> but no human being can tame the tongue  it is a restless evil  full of deadly poison </s>
<s> with the tongue we praise our lord and father  and with it we curse human beings  who have been made in gods likeness </s>
<s> out of the same mouth come praise and cursing  my brothers and sisters  this should not be </s>
<s> can both fresh water and salt water flow from the same spring </s>
<s> my brothers and sisters  can a figtree bear olives  or a grapevine bear figs  neither can a salt spring produce fresh water </s>
<s> who is wise and understanding among you  let them show it by their good life  by deeds done in the humility that comes from wisdom </s>
<s> but if you harbour bitter envy and selfish ambition in your hearts  do not boast about it or deny the truth </s>
<s> such  wisdom does not come down from heaven but is earthly  unspiritual  demonic </s>
<s> for where you have envy and selfish ambition  there you find disorder and every evil practice </s>
<s> but the wisdom that comes from heaven is first of all pure  then peaceloving  considerate  submissive  full of mercy and good fruit  impartial and sincere </s>
<s> peacemakers who sow in peace reap a harvest of righteousness </s>
<s> what causes fights and quarrels among you  dont they come from your desires that battle within you </s>
<s> you desire but do not have  so you kill  you covet but you cannot get what you want  so you quarrel and fight  you do not have because you do not ask god </s>
<s> when you ask  you do not receive  because you ask with wrong motives  that you may spend what you get on your pleasures </s>
<s> you adulterous people  dont you know that friendship with the world means enmity against god  therefore  anyone who chooses to be a friend of the world becomes an enemy of god </s>
<s> or do you think scripture says without reason that he jealously longs for the spirit he has caused to dwell in us </s>
<s> but he gives us more grace  that is why scripture says   god opposes the proud but shows favour to the humble  </s>
<s> submit yourselves  then  to god  resist the devil  and he will flee from you </s>
<s> come near to god and he will come near to you  wash your hands  you sinners  and purify your hearts  you doubleminded </s>
<s> grieve  mourn and wail  change your laughter to mourning and your joy to gloom </s>
<s> humble yourselves before the lord  and he will lift you up </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  do not slander one another  anyone who speaks against a brother or sister or judges them speaks against the law and judges it  when you judge the law  you are not keeping it  but sitting in judgment on it </s>
<s> there is only one lawgiver and judge  the one who is able to save and destroy  but you  who are you to judge your neighbour </s>
<s> now listen  you who say   today or tomorrow we will go to this or that city  spend a year there  carry on business and make money  </s>
<s> why  you do not even know what will happen tomorrow  what is your life  you are a mist that appears for a little while and then vanishes </s>
<s> instead  you ought to say   if it is the lords will  we will live and do this or that  </s>
<s> as it is  you boast in your arrogant schemes  all such boasting is evil </s>
<s> if anyone  then  knows the good they ought to do and doesnt do it  it is sin for them </s>
<s> now listen  you rich people  weep and wail because of the misery that is coming on you </s>
<s> your wealth has rotted  and moths have eaten your clothes </s>
<s> your gold and silver are corroded  their corrosion will testify against you and eat your flesh like fire  you have hoarded wealth in the last days </s>
<s> look  the wages you failed to pay the workers who mowed your fields are crying out against you  the cries of the harvesters have reached the ears of the lord almighty </s>
<s> you have lived on earth in luxury and selfindulgence  you have fattened yourselves in the day of slaughter </s>
<s> you have condemned and murdered the innocent one  who was not opposing you </s>
<s> be patient  then  brothers and sisters  until the lords coming  see how the farmer waits for the land to yield its valuable crop  patiently waiting for the autumn and spring rains </s>
<s> you too  be patient and stand firm  because the lords coming is near </s>
<s> dont grumble against one another  brothers and sisters  or you will be judged  the judge is standing at the door </s>
<s> brothers and sisters  as an example of patience in the face of suffering  take the prophets who spoke in the name of the lord </s>
<s> as you know  we count as blessed those who have persevered  you have heard of jobs perseverance and have seen what the lord finally brought about  the lord is full of compassion and mercy </s>
<s> above all  my brothers and sisters  do not swear  not by heaven or by earth or by anything else  all you need to say is a simple  yes or  no  otherwise you will be condemned </s>
<s> is anyone among you in trouble  let them pray  is anyone happy  let them sing songs of praise </s>
<s> is anyone among you ill  let them call the elders of the church to pray over them and anoint them with oil in the name of the lord </s>
<s> and the prayer offered in faith will make the ill person well  the lord will raise them up  if they have sinned  they will be forgiven </s>
<s> therefore confess your sins to each other and pray for each other so that you may be healed  the prayer of a righteous person is powerful and effective </s>
<s> elijah was a human being  even as we are  he prayed earnestly that it would not rain  and it did not rain on the land for three and a half years </s>
<s> again he prayed  and the heavens gave rain  and the earth produced its crops </s>
<s> my brothers and sisters  if one of you should wander from the truth and someone should bring that person back </s>
<s> remember this  whoever turns a sinner from the error of their way will save them from death and cover over a multitude of sins </s>
<s> peter  an apostle of jesus christ  to gods elect  exiles  scattered throughout the provinces of pontus  galatia  cappadocia  asia and bithynia </s>
<s> who have been chosen according to the foreknowledge of god the father  through the sanctifying work of the spirit  to be obedient to jesus christ and sprinkled with his blood  grace and peace be yours in abundance </s>
<s> praise be to the god and father of our lord jesus christ  in his great mercy he has given us new birth into a living hope through the resurrection of jesus christ from the dead </s>
<s> and into an inheritance that can never perish  spoil or fade  this inheritance is kept in heaven for you </s>
<s> who through faith are shielded by gods power until the coming of the salvation that is ready to be revealed in the last time </s>
<s> in all this you greatly rejoice  though now for a little while you may have had to suffer grief in all kinds of trials </s>
<s> these have come so that the proven genuineness of your faith  of greater worth than gold  which perishes even though refined by fire  may result in praise  glory and honour when jesus christ is revealed </s>
<s> though you have not seen him  you love him  and even though you do not see him now  you believe in him and are filled with an inexpressible and glorious joy </s>
<s> for you are receiving the end result of your faith  the salvation of your souls </s>
<s> concerning this salvation  the prophets  who spoke of the grace that was to come to you  searched intently and with the greatest care </s>
<s> trying to find out the time and circumstances to which the spirit of christ in them was pointing when he predicted the sufferings of the messiah and the glories that would follow </s>
<s> it was revealed to them that they were not serving themselves but you  when they spoke of the things that have now been told you by those who have preached the gospel to you by the holy spirit sent from heaven  even angels long to look into these things </s>
<s> therefore  with minds that are alert and fully sober  set your hope on the grace to be brought to you when jesus christ is revealed at his coming </s>
<s> as obedient children  do not conform to the evil desires you had when you lived in ignorance </s>
<s> but just as he who called you is holy  so be holy in all you do </s>
<s> for it is written   be holy  because i am holy  </s>
<s> since you call on a father who judges each persons work impartially  live out your time as foreigners here in reverent fear </s>
<s> for you know that it was not with perishable things such as silver or gold that you were redeemed from the empty way of life handed down to you from your ancestors </s>
<s> but with the precious blood of christ  a lamb without blemish or defect </s>
<s> he was chosen before the creation of the world  but was revealed in these last times for your sake </s>
<s> through him you believe in god  who raised him from the dead and glorified him  and so your faith and hope are in god </s>
<s> now that you have purified yourselves by obeying the truth so that you have sincere love for each other  love one another deeply  from the heart </s>
<s> for you have been born again  not of perishable seed  but of imperishable  through the living and enduring word of god </s>
<s> for   all people are like grass  and all their glory is like the flowers of the field  the grass withers and the flowers fall </s>
<s> but the word of the lord endures for ever  </s>
<s> therefore  rid yourselves of all malice and all deceit  hypocrisy  envy  and slander of every kind </s>
<s> like newborn babies  crave pure spiritual milk  so that by it you may grow up in your salvation </s>
<s> now that you have tasted that the lord is good </s>
<s> as you come to him  the living stone  rejected by humans but chosen by god and precious to him </s>
<s> you also  like living stones  are being built into a spiritual house to be a holy priesthood  offering spiritual sacrifices acceptable to god through jesus christ </s>
<s> for in scripture it says   see  i lay a stone in zion  a chosen and precious cornerstone  and the one who trusts in him will never be put to shame    the stone the builders rejected has become the cornerstone    a stone that causes people to stumble and a rock that makes them fall  </s>
<s> but you are a chosen people  a royal priesthood  a holy nation  gods special possession  that you may declare the praises of him who called you out of darkness into his wonderful light </s>
<s> once you were not a people  but now you are the people of god  once you had not received mercy  but now you have received mercy </s>
<s> dear friends  i urge you  as foreigners and exiles  to abstain from sinful desires  which wage war against your soul </s>
<s> live such good lives among the pagans that  though they accuse you of doing wrong  they may see your good deeds and glorify god on the day he visits us </s>
<s> submit yourselves for the lords sake to every human authority  whether to the emperor  as the supreme authority </s>
<s> or to governors  who are sent by him to punish those who do wrong and to commend those who do right </s>
<s> for it is gods will that by doing good you should silence the ignorant talk of foolish people </s>
<s> live as free people  but do not use your freedom as a coverup for evil  live as gods slaves </s>
<s> show proper respect to everyone  love the family of believers  fear god  honour the emperor </s>
<s> slaves  in reverent fear of god submit yourselves to your masters  not only to those who are good and considerate  but also to those who are harsh </s>
<s> for it is commendable if someone bears up under the pain of unjust suffering because they are conscious of god </s>
<s> but how is it to your credit if you receive a beating for doing wrong and endure it  but if you suffer for doing good and you endure it  this is commendable before god </s>
<s> to this you were called  because christ suffered for you  leaving you an example  that you should follow in his steps </s>
<s>  he committed no sin  and no deceit was found in his mouth  </s>
<s> wives  in the same way submit yourselves to your own husbands so that  if any of them do not believe the word  they may be won over without words by the behaviour of their wives </s>
<s> when they see the purity and reverence of your lives </s>
<s> your beauty should not come from outward adornment  such as elaborate hairstyles and the wearing of gold jewellery or fine clothes </s>
<s> rather  it should be that of your inner self  the unfading beauty of a gentle and quiet spirit  which is of great worth in gods sight </s>
<s> for this is the way the holy women of the past who put their hope in god used to adorn themselves  they submitted themselves to their own husbands </s>
<s> like sarah  who obeyed abraham and called him her lord  you are her daughters if you do what is right and do not give way to fear </s>
<s> husbands  in the same way be considerate as you live with your wives  and treat them with respect as the weaker partner and as heirs with you of the gracious gift of life  so that nothing will hinder your prayers </s>
<s> finally  all of you  be likeminded  be sympathetic  love one another  be compassionate and humble </s>
<s> do not repay evil with evil or insult with insult  on the contrary  repay evil with blessing  because to this you were called so that you may inherit a blessing </s>
<s> for   whoever would love life and see good days must keep their tongue from evil and their lips from deceitful speech </s>
<s> they must turn from evil and do good  they must seek peace and pursue it </s>
<s> for the eyes of the lord are on the righteous and his ears are attentive to their prayer  but the face of the lord is against those who do evil  </s>
<s> who is going to harm you if you are eager to do good </s>
<s> but even if you should suffer for what is right  you are blessed   do not fear their threats  do not be frightened  </s>
<s> but in your hearts revere christ as lord  always be prepared to give an answer to everyone who asks you to give the reason for the hope that you have  but do this with gentleness and respect </s>
<s> keeping a clear conscience  so that those who speak maliciously against your good behaviour in christ may be ashamed of their slander </s>
<s> for it is better  if it is gods will  to suffer for doing good than for doing evil </s>
<s> for christ also suffered once for sins  the righteous for the unrighteous  to bring you to god  he was put to death in the body but made alive in the spirit </s>
<s> after being made alive  he went and made proclamation to the imprisoned spirits </s>
<s> to those who were disobedient long ago when god waited patiently in the days of noah while the ark was being built  in it only a few people  eight in all  were saved through water </s>
<s> and this water symbolises baptism that now saves you also  not the removal of dirt from the body but the pledge of a clear conscience towards god  it saves you by the resurrection of jesus christ </s>
<s> who has gone into heaven and is at gods right hand  with angels  authorities and powers in submission to him </s>
<s> therefore  since christ suffered in his body  arm yourselves also with the same attitude  because whoever suffers in the body has finished with sin </s>
<s> as a result  they do not live the rest of their earthly lives for evil human desires  but rather for the will of god </s>
<s> for you have spent enough time in the past doing what pagans choose to do  living in debauchery  lust  drunkenness  orgies  carousing and detestable idolatry </s>
<s> they are surprised that you do not join them in their reckless  wild living  and they heap abuse on you </s>
<s> but they will have to give account to him who is ready to judge the living and the dead </s>
<s> for this is the reason the gospel was preached even to those who are now dead  so that they might be judged according to human standards in regard to the body  but live according to god in regard to the spirit </s>
<s> the end of all things is near  therefore be alert and of sober mind so that you may pray </s>
<s> above all  love each other deeply  because love covers over a multitude of sins </s>
<s> offer hospitality to one another without grumbling </s>
<s> each of you should use whatever gift you have received to serve others  as faithful stewards of gods grace in its various forms </s>
<s> if anyone speaks  they should do so as one who speaks the very words of god  if anyone serves  they should do so with the strength god provides  so that in all things god may be praised through jesus christ  to him be the glory and the power for ever and ever  amen </s>
<s> dear friends  do not be surprised at the fiery ordeal that has come on you to test you  as though something strange were happening to you </s>
<s> but rejoice inasmuch as you participate in the sufferings of christ  so that you may be overjoyed when his glory is revealed </s>
<s> if you are insulted because of the name of christ  you are blessed  for the spirit of glory and of god rests on you </s>
<s> if you suffer  it should not be as a murderer or thief or any other kind of criminal  or even as a meddler </s>
<s> however  if you suffer as a christian  do not be ashamed  but praise god that you bear that name </s>
<s> for it is time for judgment to begin with gods household  and if it begins with us  what will the outcome be for those who do not obey the gospel of god </s>
<s> and   if it is hard for the righteous to be saved  what will become of the ungodly and the sinner  </s>
<s> so then  those who suffer according to gods will should commit themselves to their faithful creator and continue to do good </s>
<s> to the elders among you  i appeal as a fellow elder and a witness of christs sufferings who also will share in the glory to be revealed </s>
<s> be shepherds of gods flock that is under your care  watching over them  not because you must  but because you are willing  as god wants you to be  not pursuing dishonest gain  but eager to serve </s>
<s> not lording it over those entrusted to you  but being examples to the flock </s>
<s> and when the chief shepherd appears  you will receive the crown of glory that will never fade away </s>
<s> in the same way  you who are younger  submit yourselves to your elders  all of you  clothe yourselves with humility towards one another  because   god opposes the proud but shows favour to the humble  </s>
<s> be alert and of sober mind  your enemy the devil prowls around like a roaring lion looking for someone to devour </s>
<s> resist him  standing firm in the faith  because you know that the family of believers throughout the world is undergoing the same kind of sufferings </s>
<s> and the god of all grace  who called you to his eternal glory in christ  after you have suffered a little while  will himself restore you and make you strong  firm and steadfast </s>
<s> to him be the power for ever and ever  amen </s>
<s> with the help of silas  whom i regard as a faithful brother  i have written to you briefly  encouraging you and testifying that this is the true grace of god  stand fast in it </s>
<s> she who is in babylon  chosen together with you  sends you her greetings  and so does my son mark </s>
<s> greet one another with a kiss of love  peace to all of you who are in christ </s>
<s> simon peter  a servant and apostle of jesus christ  to those who through the righteousness of our god and saviour jesus christ have received a faith as precious as ours </s>
<s> grace and peace be yours in abundance through the knowledge of god and of jesus our lord </s>
<s> his divine power has given us everything we need for a godly life through our knowledge of him who called us by his own glory and goodness </s>
<s> through these he has given us his very great and precious promises  so that through them you may participate in the divine nature  having escaped the corruption in the world caused by evil desires </s>
<s> for this very reason  make every effort to add to your faith goodness  and to goodness  knowledge </s>
<s> and to knowledge  selfcontrol  and to selfcontrol  perseverance  and to perseverance  godliness </s>
<s> and to godliness  mutual affection  and to mutual affection  love </s>
<s> for if you possess these qualities in increasing measure  they will keep you from being ineffective and unproductive in your knowledge of our lord jesus christ </s>
<s> but whoever does not have them is shortsighted and blind  forgetting that they have been cleansed from their past sins </s>
<s> therefore  my brothers and sisters  make every effort to confirm your calling and election  for if you do these things  you will never stumble </s>
<s> and you will receive a rich welcome into the eternal kingdom of our lord and saviour jesus christ </s>
<s> so i will always remind you of these things  even though you know them and are firmly established in the truth you now have </s>
<s> i think it is right to refresh your memory as long as i live in the tent of this body </s>
<s> because i know that i will soon put it aside  as our lord jesus christ has made clear to me </s>
<s> and i will make every effort to see that after my departure you will always be able to remember these things </s>
<s> for we did not follow cleverly devised stories when we told you about the coming of our lord jesus christ in power  but we were eyewitnesses of his majesty </s>
<s> he received honour and glory from god the father when the voice came to him from the majestic glory  saying   this is my son  whom i love  with him i am well pleased  </s>
<s> we ourselves heard this voice that came from heaven when we were with him on the sacred mountain </s>
<s> we also have the prophetic message as something completely reliable  and you will do well to pay attention to it  as to a light shining in a dark place  until the day dawns and the morning star rises in your hearts </s>
<s> above all  you must understand that no prophecy of scripture came about by the prophets own interpretation of things </s>
<s> for prophecy never had its origin in the human will  but prophets  though human  spoke from god as they were carried along by the holy spirit </s>
<s> but there were also false prophets among the people  just as there will be false teachers among you  they will secretly introduce destructive heresies  even denying the sovereign lord who bought them  bringing swift destruction on themselves </s>
<s> many will follow their depraved conduct and will bring the way of truth into disrepute </s>
<s> in their greed these teachers will exploit you with fabricated stories  their condemnation has long been hanging over them  and their destruction has not been sleeping </s>
<s> for if god did not spare angels when they sinned  but sent them to hell  putting them in chains of darkness to be held for judgment </s>
<s> if he did not spare the ancient world when he brought the flood on its ungodly people  but protected noah  a preacher of righteousness  and seven others </s>
<s> if he condemned the cities of sodom and gomorrah by burning them to ashes  and made them an example of what is going to happen to the ungodly </s>
<s> and if he rescued lot  a righteous man  who was distressed by the depraved conduct of the lawless</s>
<s>  for that righteous man  living among them day after day  was tormented in his righteous soul by the lawless deeds he saw and heard  </s>
<s> if this is so  then the lord knows how to rescue the godly from trials and to hold the unrighteous for punishment on the day of judgment </s>
<s> this is especially true of those who follow the corrupt desire of the flesh and despise authority  bold and arrogant  they are not afraid to heap abuse on celestial beings </s>
<s> yet even angels  although they are stronger and more powerful  do not heap abuse on such beings when bringing judgment on them from the lord </s>
<s> but these people blaspheme in matters they do not understand  they are like unreasoning animals  creatures of instinct  born only to be caught and destroyed  and like animals they too will perish </s>
<s> they will be paid back with harm for the harm they have done  their idea of pleasure is to carouse in broad daylight  they are blots and blemishes  revelling in their pleasures while they feast with you </s>
<s> with eyes full of adultery  they never stop sinning  they seduce the unstable  they are experts in greed  an accursed brood </s>
<s> they have left the straight way and wandered off to follow the way of balaam son of bezer  who loved the wages of wickedness </s>
<s> but he was rebuked for his wrongdoing by a donkey  an animal without speech  who spoke with a human voice and restrained the prophets madness </s>
<s> these people are springs without water and mists driven by a storm  blackest darkness is reserved for them </s>
<s> for they mouth empty  boastful words and  by appealing to the lustful desires of the flesh  they entice people who are just escaping from those who live in error </s>
<s> they promise them freedom  while they themselves are slaves of depravity  for  people are slaves to whatever has mastered them  </s>
<s> if they have escaped the corruption of the world by knowing our lord and saviour jesus christ and are again entangled in it and are overcome  they are worse off at the end than they were at the beginning </s>
<s> it would have been better for them not to have known the way of righteousness  than to have known it and then to turn their backs on the sacred command that was passed on to them </s>
<s> of them the proverbs are true   a dog returns to its vomit   and   a sow that is washed returns to her wallowing in the mud  </s>
<s> dear friends  this is now my second letter to you  i have written both of them as reminders to stimulate you to wholesome thinking </s>
<s> i want you to recall the words spoken in the past by the holy prophets and the command given by our lord and saviour through your apostles </s>
<s> above all  you must understand that in the last days scoffers will come  scoffing and following their own evil desires </s>
<s> they will say   where is this   coming he promised  ever since our ancestors died  everything goes on as it has since the beginning of creation  </s>
<s> but they deliberately forget that long ago by gods word the heavens came into being and the earth was formed out of water and by water </s>
<s> by these waters also the world of that time was deluged and destroyed </s>
<s> by the same word the present heavens and earth are reserved for fire  being kept for the day of judgment and destruction of the ungodly </s>
<s> but do not forget this one thing  dear friends  with the lord a day is like a thousand years  and a thousand years are like a day </s>
<s> the lord is not slow in keeping his promise  as some understand slowness  instead he is patient with you  not wanting anyone to perish  but everyone to come to repentance </s>
<s> but the day of the lord will come like a thief  the heavens will disappear with a roar  the elements will be destroyed by fire  and the earth and everything done in it will be laid bare </s>
<s> since everything will be destroyed in this way  what kind of people ought you to be  you ought to live holy and godly lives</s>
<s> as you look forward to the day of god and speed its coming  that day will bring about the destruction of the heavens by fire  and the elements will melt in the heat </s>
<s> but in keeping with his promise we are looking forward to a new heaven and a new earth  where righteousness dwells </s>
<s> so then  dear friends  since you are looking forward to this  make every effort to be found spotless  blameless and at peace with him </s>
<s> bear in mind that our lords patience means salvation  just as our dear brother paul also wrote to you with the wisdom that god gave him </s>
<s> he writes the same way in all his letters  speaking in them of these matters  his letters contain some things that are hard to understand  which ignorant and unstable people distort  as they do the other scriptures  to their own destruction </s>
<s> therefore  dear friends  since you have been forewarned  be on your guard so that you may not be carried away by the error of the lawless and fall from your secure position </s>
<s> but grow in the grace and knowledge of our lord and saviour jesus christ  to him be glory both now and for ever  amen </s>
<s> that which was from the beginning  which we have heard  which we have seen with our eyes  which we have looked at and our hands have touched  this we proclaim concerning the word of life </s>
<s> the life appeared  we have seen it and testify to it  and we proclaim to you the eternal life  which was with the father and has appeared to us </s>
<s> we proclaim to you what we have seen and heard  so that you also may have fellowship with us  and our fellowship is with the father and with his son  jesus christ </s>
<s> we write this to make our joy complete </s>
<s> this is the message we have heard from him and declare to you  god is light  in him there is no darkness at all </s>
<s> if we claim to have fellowship with him and yet walk in the darkness  we lie and do not live out the truth </s>
<s> but if we walk in the light  as he is in the light  we have fellowship with one another  and the blood of jesus  his son  purifies us from all sin </s>
<s> if we claim to be without sin  we deceive ourselves and the truth is not in us </s>
<s> if we confess our sins  he is faithful and just and will forgive us our sins and purify us from all unrighteousness </s>
<s> if we claim we have not sinned  we make him out to be a liar and his word is not in us </s>
